 uṣā evamādyā vājasaneyi brāhmaṇa alpa granthā vṛttiḥ ārabhyate saṃsāra vyāvivṛtsubhyaḥ saṃsāra hetu nivṛtti sādhana ekatva pratipattaye śabdha vācyā tatparāṇām hetoḥ saṃsārasya atyanta avasādanāt upaniṣūvasya sadeḥ artha tādarthyād granthaḥ ucyate adhyāyī anūcyamāna āraṇya kambṛ hat parimāṇataḥ bṛhadāraṇyakam kāṇḍena sambandhaḥ abhidhīyate anumānābhyām anavagata iṣṭa aniṣṭa prāpti parihāra upāya prakāśana puruṣām nisargata prāpti parihārayoḥ iṣṭa dṛṣṭa viṣaye ceṣṭā aniṣṭaṣṭa prāpti parihāra upāya jñānasya anumānābhyām sidda at āgama anveṣaṇā asati janma antara sambandhyātma astitva janma antara sambandhyātma astitva janma antara iṣṭā aniṣṭaṣṭa prāpti parihāra icchā svabhāva vādi darśanāt janmāntara sambandhyātma astitve janma antara iṣṭa aniṣṭaṣṭa prāpti parihāra upāya viśeṣe śāstram pravartate prete mānuṣye upakramya upalabdhavyaḥ evamādi nirṇaya darśanāt maraṇam upakramya prapadyante tvāya dehinaḥ sthāṇum anusaṃyanti yathākarma yathāśrutam svayan upakramya karmaṇi samanvāram puṇena upakramya vyatirikta astitvam viṣayam vādi vipratipatti darśanāt deha antara sambandhina pratyakṣeṇa astitva lokāyatikā bauddhāḥ pratikūlāḥ syunā ghaṭa ādau viṣaye vipratipadyate ghaṭa sthāṇu ādau ādi darśanāt nirūpite sthāṇu ādau vipratipattiḥ vaināśikāḥ pratyaye jāyamāne deha antara vyatiriktasya astitvam pratijānate viṣaya vailakṣaṇyāt pratyakṣāt astitva siddhiḥ anumānāt śrutyā astitve liṅgasya darśi liṅgasya viṣaya janma antara sambandhasya agrahaṇāt āgamena astitve avagate pradarśita laukika liṅga viśeṣaiḥ anusāriṇaḥ mīmāṃsakāḥ tārkikāḥ pratyaya liṅgāni vaidikāni ati prabhavāṇi kalpayantaḥ pratyakṣaḥ anumeyaḥ sarvathā deha antara sambandhī pratipattuḥ deha antara gata iṣṭa aniṣṭa prāpti parihāra upāya viśeṣa arthinaḥ viśeṣa jñāpanāya kāṇḍam ārabdham ātmana iṣṭa aniṣṭa prāpti parihāra icchā kāraṇam viṣayam ajñānam kartṛ bhoktṛ svarūpa abhimāna lakṣaṇam viparīta svarūpa apanītam apanīyate phala rāga dveṣa ādi svābhāvika doṣa prayuktaḥ śāstra vihita pratiṣiddhā atikrameṇa vartamānaḥ kāyaiḥ dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa aniṣṭa sādhanāni adharma saṃjñakāni upacinoti bāhulyena svābhāvika doṣa balīyaḥ sthāvaranta adhogatiḥ kadācid śāstra kṛta saṃskāra balīyaḥ manaā ādibhiḥ iṣṭa sādhanam bāhulyena upacinoti ākhyam dvividham jñāna pūrvakam kevalañca kevalam ādi prāpti phalam jñāna pūrvakam ādi prāpti phalam śāstram yāji śreyān ityādi smṛtiḥ dvividham vaidikam ityādyā sāmye adharmayoḥ manuṣyatva prāptiḥ andyā sthāvara antā svābhāvika avidyā ādi doṣavatī adharma sādhana saṃsāra āśrayā sādhya sādhana jagat utpatteḥ avyākṛtam bīja aṅkura ādivat avidyā saṃsāra kriyā kāraka phala adhyāra upalakṣaṇaḥ anādiḥ anantaḥ anarthaḥ viraktasya avidyā nivṛttaye viparīta pratipatti artha upaniṣadā ārabhyate sambandhinaḥ vijñānasya prayojanam yepām aśvamedhe adhikāraḥ phala prāptiḥ evamādi śrutibhyaḥ viṣaya vijñānasya aśvamedhena ya vikalpa prakaraṇe āmnānāt antare sampādana darśanāt phala prāptiḥ avagamyate samaṣṭi vyaṣṭi prāpti phalava prārambha āmnānam saṃsāra viṣayatva pradarśana darśayiṣyati phalam aśanāya amṛtyu bhāvam nityānām saṃsāra viṣaya phala phala upasaṃhāra sambaddham jayā nisargata kāmya darśayitvā apara phalam darśayitvā ātmaka upasaṃhariṣyati tarmaṇām phalam saṃsāra prāk utpatteḥ avyākṛtam vaśāt vyākriyate bījāt vyākṛta avyākṛta saṃsāraḥ avidyā viṣayaḥ kriyā kāraka phala ātmaka tvena adhyāropitaḥ mūrta amūrta vāsanā ātmakaḥ vilakṣaṇaḥ anāma ātmakaḥ advayaḥ nitya śuddha mukta svabhāvaḥ kriyā kāraka phala bheda ādi viparyayeṇa avabhāsate kriyā kāraka phala bheda svarūpa āt sādhya sādhana rūpāt viraktasya ādi doṣa bīja avidyā nivṛttaye rajjvām sarpa apanayāya ārabhyate auṣā aityādi viṣayam darśanam ucyate prādhānyāt prādhānyam aṅkita kratoḥ uṣā brāhmaḥ muhūrta vaiśabdaḥ smaraṇa arthaḥ prasiddham smārayati prādhānyāt pradhānam avayavānām medhā arhasya yajñiyasya upāḥ sambandhaḥ aṅgasya paśoḥ saṃskartavya kāla ādi dṛṣṭayaḥ śira ādiṣu kṣipyante dṛṣṭi adhyāropaṇāt kāla ātva adhyāropaṇam prajāpatitva karaṇam paśoḥ evaṃrūpaḥ viṣṇatva ādi karaṇam pratimā ādau śirasaḥ anantara adhidaivata svābhāvyāt vivṛtam vaiśvānara rḥ vaiśvānara viśeṣaṇarm vivṛtam arthaḥ mukhasya daivata saṃvatsara māsaḥ trayodaśa māsaḥ vāātma aśarīram kāla avayavānām madhyam aṣām sarvatra anupaṅga punarvacanam ūrdhvatva sāmānyāt suṣiratva sāmānyāt pādasyam varṇa vyatyayena pāda āsana arthaḥ catasraḥ pārśvena sambandhāt pārśvayoḥ saṅkhyā vaiṣamyāt ayuktam mukhatva upapatteḥ pārśvābhyām sambandhāt adoṣaḥ diśa āgneyī ādyāḥ pārśva saṃvatsara avayava sādharmyāt ahorātrāṇi bahuvacanāt daiva pitrya mānuṣāṇi ahorātraiḥ kāla pādaiḥ śuklatva sāmānyāt sthā meghā antarīkṣasya udaratva ukteḥ udaka rudhira secana sāmānyāt udara stham jīrṇam sikatā viśliṣṭa avayavatva sāmānyāt syandana annadyaḥ gudā bahuvacanāt caklomānaḥ adhasthāt dakṣiṇa uttarau khaṇḍau klomāna nityam bahuvacanam kāṭhinyāt ucchrita sthāvarā mahāntaḥ yathāsambhavam udyann udgacchan savitā āmadhyāhnāt nāmeḥ arthaḥ nimlocat nastam nā madhyāhnāt apara aparatva sādharmyāt gātrāṇi vināmayati vikṣipati vidyotanam mukha ghana vidāraṇa sāmānyāt gātrāṇi kampayati garjana śabdha sāmānyāt mūtram varṣaṇam secana sāmānyāt śabda kalpanā arthaḥ aharvā sāvarṇa rājatau mahima ākhyau grahau agratas sthāpyete viṣayam darśanam sauvarṇaḥ dīpti sāmānyāt aharaśvam vajāyata āt ityādi lakṣaṇaḥ ahnā lakṣyate lakṣayitvā sauvarṇaḥ yadvat grahasya vibhakti vyatyayena āsādana rātrī rājate varṇa sāmānyāt jaghanyatva sāmānyāt pṛṣṭataḥ vibhūtiḥ sauvarṇaḥ rājataḥ grahau sthāpyete mahima ākhyau grahau sambabhūva tuḥ lakṣaṇau sambhūtau mahatva yukta punarvacanam stuti ityādi stuti hinoteḥ gati viśiṣṭa arthaḥ jāta viśeṣaḥ voḍhā nindā vāhana doṣaḥ vāhana svābhāvikam svābhāvika ucchrāya prāptiḥ ādi sambandhaḥ stutiḥ vājyādayaḥ jāti viśeṣāḥ anuṣaṅgaḥ samudra paramātmā bandhu bandhanam badhyate kāraṇam utpattim śuddha śuddha stūyate prasiddha adhyāye brāhmaṇam upayogikasya utpattiḥ ucyate viṣaya darśana vivakṣayā utpattiḥ stuti arthā kiñcana agra saṃsāra kiñcana pravibhakta viśeṣam prāk utpatteḥ manādeḥ śūnyam kiñcana kāryam kāraṇam utpatteḥ utpadyate ghaṭaḥ prāk utpatteḥ ghaṭasya nāstitvam nanu kāraṇasya astitvam mṛd piṇḍa ādi darśanāt upalabhyate astitā kāryasya kāraṇasya upalampamāna prāk utpatteḥ sarvānupalambhāt anupalabdhiḥ abhāva hetuḥ jagataḥ prāk utpatteḥ kāraṇam kāryam upalabhyate abhāvaḥ āvriyate āvriyate avakṣyat amṛtyunā gagana kusuma vandhyā bravīti amṛtyunā kāraṇena kāryam prāk utpatteḥ prāmāṇyāt anumeya anumīyate prāk utpatteḥ kārya kāraṇayoḥ astitvam kāryasya jāyamānasya kāraṇe sati utpatti darśanāt asati adarśanāt jagataḥ prāk utpatteḥ kāraṇa astitvam anumīyate ghaṭa ādi kāraṇāḥ titvavat ghaṭa ādi kāraṇasya asattvam anupamṛdya mṛd piṇḍa ādikam ghaṭa ādi anutpatteḥ mṛd ādeḥ kāraṇa mṛd suvarṇa ādi kāraṇam ghaṭa rucaka ādeḥ piṇḍa ākāra viśeṣaḥ abhāve bhāvāt asatī piṇḍa ākāra viśeṣe mṛd suvarṇa ādi kāraṇa dravya mātrāt ghaṭa rucaka ādi kārya utpattiḥ dṛśyate piṇḍa ākāra viśeṣe ghaṭa rucaka ādi kāraṇam asati mṛd suvarṇa ādi dravye ghaṭa rucaka ādiḥ jāyata mṛd suvarṇa ādi dravyam kāraṇam piṇḍa ākāra viśeṣaḥ kāraṇam kāryam utpādayat utpannasya kāryasya tirodhānam kurvat kārya utpādayati kāraṇe yugapad aneka kārya virodhāt kārya upama marde kāraṇasya sva upamarde piṇḍa ādi upamarde kārya utpatti darśanam ahetuḥ prāk utpatteḥ kāraṇa asattveḥ piṇḍa ādi vyatirekeṇa mṛdā ādera sattvāt ayuktam piṇḍa ādi kārya upamarde mṛdādi kāraṇam upamṛdyate ghaṭa ādi kārya antare anuvartate ayuktam piṇḍa ghaṭa ādi vyatirekeṇa mṛdādi kāraṇasya anupalambhāt mṛd ādi kāraṇānām ghaṭa ādi utpattau piṇḍa ādi nivṛttau anuvṛtti darśanāt sādṛśyāt anvaya darśanam kāraṇa anuvṛtteḥ piṇḍa ādi gatānām mṛd ādi avayavānām ghaṭa ādau tve anumāna ābhāsāt sādṛśya ādi kalpanā anupapatteḥ anumānayoḥ viruddha avi abhicārita apratyakṣa pūrvaka anumānasya sarvatra anāśvāsa prasaṅgāt kṣaṇikam gamyamānam buddheḥ anya buddhi apekṣa tve anya buddhi apekṣa anavasthāyām sadṛśam asyā buddheḥ mṛpātvāt tra anāśvāsa idambuddhyoḥ kartṛ abhāve sambandha anupapattiḥ sādṛśyāt sambandha ambuddhyoḥ ita retara viṣayatva anupapatteḥ asati itaretara viṣaya tve sādṛśya grahaṇa anupapattiḥ asati sādṛśye buddhiḥ idambuddhyoḥ sādṛśya buddhivat viṣayatva prasaṅgāt viṣaya buddhīnām buddhi buddheḥ viṣayatva prasaṅgāt buddhīnām mṛṣā tve asatya buddhi anupapatteḥ sādṛśyāt buddhiḥ siddhaḥ prāk kārya utpatteḥ kāraṇa sadbhāvaḥ kāryasya abhivyakti liṅga kāryasya sadbhāvaḥ prāk utpatteḥ siddhaḥ abhivyakti liṅga abhivyakti abhivyaktiḥ ālambanatva prāptiḥ prāvṛtam tama ādinā ghaṭa ādi vastu āloka ādinā prāvaraṇa tiraskāreṇa viṣaya prāpnuvat prāk sadbhāvam vyabhicarati jagat prāk utpatteḥ avagacchāmaḥ avidyamānaḥ ghaṭa udite upalabhyate avidyamānatva abhāvāt upalabhyeta ghaṭa ādi kāryam kadācid avidyamānam udite upalabhyeta mṛd piṇḍe asannihite ādi āvaraṇe asati vidyamāna dvividha āvaraṇasya ghaṭa ādi kāryasya dvividham āvaraṇam mṛdā dāra vibhaktasya kuḍya ādi prāk mṛdaḥ abhivyakteḥ mṛdā ādi avayavānām piṇḍa ādi kārya antara saṃsthānam prāk utpatteḥ vidyamānasya ghaṭa ādi kāryasya āvṛta anupalabdhiḥ naṣṭa utpanna bhāva abhāva śabda pratyaya bhedaḥ abhivyākta tirobhāvayoḥ dvividhatva apekṣaḥ piṇḍaka pāla ādeḥ āvaraṇa vailakṣaṇyāt ayuktam kuḍya ādi ghaṭa ādi āvaraṇam ghaṭa ādi bhinna deśam ghaṭa ādi bhinna deśe piṇḍa kapāle piṇḍa kapāla saṃsthānayoḥ vidyamānasya ghaṭasya āvṛta anupalabdhiḥ ayuktam āvaraṇa vailakṣaṇyāt kṣīra udaka ādeḥ kṣīra ādi āvaraṇena deśatva darśanāt ghaṭa ādi kārye kapāla cūrṇa ādi avayavānām antarbhāvāt anāvaraṇa vibhaktānām kārya antara āvaraṇatva upapatteḥ āvaraṇa abhāva yatnaḥ kartavya piṇḍa kapāla avasthayoḥ vidyamānam ghaṭa ādi kāryam āvṛta ubhalabhyata ghaṭa ādi kārya arthinā āvaraṇa vināśa yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ ghaṭa ādi utpattau ayuktam vidyamānasya āvṛta anupalabdhiḥ aniyamāt vināśa mātra prayatnāt ghaṭa ādi abhivyaktiḥ niyatā ādya āvṛte ghaṭa ādau pradīpa ādi utpattau prayatna darśanāt nāśāya dīpa ādi utpattau prayatnaḥ tiraskaraṇāya aṣṭe ghaṭaḥ upalabhyate ādhīyate prakāśavataḥ ghaṭasya upalabhyamāna prakāśa viśiṣṭaḥ ghaṭa upalabhyate pradīpa karaṇāt tiraskārāya pradīpa karaṇam prakāśavat tvaya prakāśavat tvena upalabhyamāna kvacid āvaraṇa vināśe yatnaḥ kuḍya ādi vināśe niyamaḥ abhivyaktarthina āvaraṇa vināśa yatnaḥ kārya niyama ātmarthavat kāraṇe vartamānam kāryam kārya antarāṇām āvaraṇam avocāma abhivyaktasya kāryasya piṇḍasya vyavahitasya kapālasya vināśa yatnaḥ kriyeta vidala cūrṇa ādi kāryam āvṛtaḥ ghaṭaḥ upalabhyata prayatna antara pekṣā ghaṭa ādi abhivyakti arthinaḥ niyata kārakavyā pāror athavān prāk utpatteḥ kāryam atitānāgata pratyaya bhedāt atītaḥ ghaṭaḥ anāgataḥ ghaṭa etayoḥ pratyayoḥ vartamāna ghaṭa pratyayavat nirviṣaya yuktam anāgata arthi pravṛtteḥ asati arthitayā pravṛttiḥ dṛṣṭā yoginām atīta anāgata jñānasya asanśced ghaṭa aiśvaram ghaṭa viṣayam jñānam mithyā pratyakṣam upacaryate ghaṭa sadbhā va ihi anumānam avocāma vipratiṣedhāt ghaṭaḥ bhaviṣyati kulāla ādiṣu vyāpriyamāṇeṣu ghaṭa pramāṇena niścitam kālena ghaṭasya sambandhaḥ bhaviṣyati ucyate ghaṭaḥ asan vipratiṣiddham abhidhīyate bhaviṣyana ghaṭaḥ asan bhaviṣyati arthaḥ ghaṭaḥ vartata yadvat prāk utpatteḥ ghaṭaḥ asan ucyeta ghaṭa artha pravṛtteṣu kulāla ādiṣu vyāpāra vartamānāḥ kulāla ādayaḥ ghaṭaḥ vartata śabdasya arthaḥ virudhyate ghaṭaḥ vartate piṇḍasya vartamāna kapālasya ghaṭasya ghaṭasya kulāla ādi vyāpāra vartam āna tāyām prāk utpatteḥ ghaṭaḥ asan virudhyate ghaṭasya bhaviṣyattā kārya pratipidhyeta pratipedhe virodhaḥ pratiṣedhati kriyāvatām kārakāṇām vartamāna caturvidhānām abhāvānām ghaṭasya itaretara abhāvaḥ ghaṭāt ghaṭa abhāvaḥ paṭa ādiḥ ghaṭa svarūpam ghaṭa abhāvaḥ sanpaṭaḥ abhāva ātmakaḥ bhāva ghaṭasya prāk pradhvaṃsa atyantā bhāvanām ghaṭāt anya ghaṭena vyapadiśyamāna ghaṭasya itara itara abhāvavat bhāva ātmaka bhāvānām sati ghaṭasya prāgabhāva ghaṭa svarūpam prāk utpatteḥ ghaṭasya prāgabhāva ghaṭasya svarūpam ucyeta ghaṭasya vyapadeśa anupapattiḥ kalpayitvā vyapadiśyeta śilāputrakasya yadvat ghaṭasya prāgabhāva kalpitasya abhāvasya ghaṭena vyapadeśaḥ ghaṭa svarūpasya artha ghaṭāt ghaṭasya abhāva uttaram prāk utpatteḥ śaśa viṣāṇavat abhāva ghaṭasya sva kāraṇa sattā sambandha anupapattiḥ dvi niṣṭha sambandhasya ayutasiddhānām adoṣa bhāva abhāvayoḥ ayuta siddhatva anupapatteḥ bhāva abhūtayoḥ yuta siddha ayuta siddha bhāva abhāvayoḥ abhāvayoḥ kāryam prāk utpatteḥ siddham kin lakṣaṇena ata aśitum icchā lakṣaṇam lakṣitena mṛtyu nāśanāyayā ucyate prasiddham hetum avat yotayati aśitum icchati aśanāya jantūn lakṣyate buddhi buddhi avasthaḥ hiraṇyagarbhaḥ ucyate kāryam piṇḍa avasthayā mṛdā ghaṇṭā ādaya syuḥ tadvat nirdeśaḥ prakṛtaḥ vakṣyamāṇa kārya sisṛkṣayā kārya ālocana kṣamam śabda vācyam saṃkalpa ādi lakṣaṇam antaḥkaraṇa makuruta kṛtavān abhiprāyeṇa ucyate ātmavān bhaveyam manasvī abhiprāyaḥ abhivyaktena manaskaḥ sannarcan arcayan pūjayan kṛtārthaḥ caraṇam pūjayata ātmikāḥ pūjā bhūtā utpannāḥ prabhṛtīnām trayāṇām utpatti vaktavyam śruti antara sāmarthyāt vikalpa asambhavāt sṛṣṭi kramasya pūjām kurvate mahyam kamudakam hetoḥ arkasya kratva aupayogikasya tve hetuḥ arthaḥ arkanāma nirvacanam etet arcanāt sukha hetu pūjā karaṇāt apsambandhāt gauṇam ya yathoktam arkasya kamudakam sukham sāmānyāt avatāraṇa arthau ucyate arcanā bhūtāḥ arkasya hetu pratiṣiṭhita tāsām aprakaraṇāt prakaraṇam dadhna maṇḍa saṅgātam āpadyata tejasā bāhya pacyamānam liṅga vyatyayena aṣām saṃghātaḥ tābhyaḥ adbhayaḥ aṇḍam abhinirvṛttam arthaḥ utpāditāyām mṛtyu śrama yuktaḥ kārya prajāpataḥ catat kāryam sargaḥ ucyate khinnasya teja sāraḥ niṣkrānta arthaḥ niṣkrānta aṇḍasya jaḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghātavān śarīri prathamaḥ smaraṇāt prakāram kārya karaṇa saṃghātam vyabhajat apekṣayā trayāṇām pūraṇam akurutā anuvartate apekṣayā apekṣayā draṣṭavyam sāmarthyasya tulya trayāṇām saṃkhyā āpūraṇa tve viśeṣataḥ mṛtyvātmanā vibhaktaḥ svarūpa upamardanena jasya upayogikasya arkasya virājaḥ citya ātmakasya darśanam ucyate utpattiḥ stuti artha avocāmaittham śuddha janma viśiṣṭatva sāmānyāt aiśāni āgneyyau īrmau īrayateḥ gati jaghanyaḥ bhāgaḥ prāṅmukhasya pratyak sambandhāt vāyavya nairṛtyau sakthyausakthinī pṛṣṭha koṇatva sāmānyāt pārśe ubhaya sambandha sāmānyāt pūrvavat adhobhāga sāmānyāt ādi ātmakaḥ lokā apsvantaḥ kka kasmiṃścid sthitim labhate uktam pratiṣṭhita agnevidvān guṇa phalam abādi krameṇa aṇḍasya kārya karaṇa saṃghātavantam virājam akurutā uktam kiṃvyāpāraḥ ucyate kāmitavān śarīrī utpadyeta kāmayitvā utpannena lakṣaṇām dvandva bhāvam sambhavanam kṛtavān trayīmāla ucitavān vihitam sṛṣṭi kramam anvālocayat arthaḥ lakṣitaḥ uktam parāmṛśati prasaṅgaḥ reta mithune reta śarīriṇaḥ utpattau kāraṇam bījam jñāna trayya ālocanāyām dṛṣṭavān janma antara bhāva bhāvitaḥ bījena aṇḍa garbhībhūtaḥ saṃvatsara kāla nirmātā saṃvatsara kāla nirmātuḥ nāsa saṃvatsara kāla nirmātāram garbha prasiddhaḥ kāla saṃvatsara parimāṇam abibhaḥ bhṛtavān saṃvatsara prasiddhaḥ kṛtavān saṃvatsara mātrasya parastād sṛṣṭavān aṇḍam abhinaditi arthaḥ śarīriṇam aśanāyavat abhivyādadān mukha vidāraṇam kṛtavān bhītaḥ svābhāvikyā yuktaḥ bhāṇiti śabdam bhītam kṛta ravam īkṣitavān aśanāyāvān kadācid apimaṃsye abhipūrva umanyatiḥ hiṃsā arthaḥ hiṃsiṣya arthaḥ alpam kariṣya īkṣitvā bhakṣaṇāt kartavyam dīrgha kāla bhakṣaṇāya bhakṣaṇe bīja bhakṣaṇa sasya abhāvaḥ evamprayojanam bāhulyam ālocya tayyā trayyā uktayā mithunībhāvam ālocanam upagamya upagamya sthāvaram jaṅgamam kiñcayat kiñcā gāyatri ādīdīni stotra śastra ādi bhūtān trividhān mantrān ādi chandaḥ viśiṣṭān sādhyān kartrīḥ grāmyān āraṇyān sādhana bhūtān nanu trayyā mithunībhūtayā uktam ādīn eha doṣaḥ avyaktaḥ mithunībhāvaḥ trayyā bāhyaḥ ādīnām vidyamānānām karmasu viniyoga bhāvena vyaktībhāvaḥ sarga vṛddhim buddhvā kriyā sādhanam phalam bhakṣayitum dhṛtavān kṛtsnam nāmnaḥ prasiddham mantraḥ aditiḥ dyaiḥ aditiḥ aditiḥ ityādiḥ jagataḥ āttā evabhavati anyathā virodhāt dṛśyatetasmāt arthaḥ ata attuḥ upapadyate ya uktam adanādaditi phalam aśvamedhayoḥ nirvacana mahatā bhūyas yajñeya janma antara karaṇa apekṣayā bhūyas janmāntare aśvamedhena ayajata bhāva bhāvita kalpa ādau vyāvartata kriyā kāraka phala tvena nirvṛttaḥ kāryam kāmayitvā lokavat pūrvavat padārtham ādayaḥ hetu sukhyātiḥ lakṣaṇam utkrāntavat vīrya niṣkrānteṣu ucchūna bhāvam gantum adhriyatā amedhyam nirgatasya mana kasyacid priye viṣaye gatasya tadvat gata manāḥ ucyate medhā arha yajñiyam vyātmavān śarīreṇa śarīravān prāviveśa viyogāt gatayaśoḥ aśvad aśvayat nāmā stūyate praveśāt gata vīrya amedhyam nāmnaḥ kratoḥ aśvamedhanāmalābhaḥ kriyā kāraka phala ātmakaḥ stūyate kratu nirvartakasya āśvasya pajāpati uktam auṣā medhasya aityādinā svarūpasya uktasya kratu phala samasya upāsanam vidhātavyam ārabhyate pūrvatra kriyā apadasya vidhāyakasya aśruta kriyā apekṣa prakaraṇasya arthaḥ avagamyate kratum ya arkam yathoktam vakṣyamāṇena samāsena padarśyamānena viśeṣaṇena viśiṣṭam veditavya arthaḥ paśu viṣayam darśanam kāmayitvā paśum kalpayitvā paśum ana varudhyā utsṛṣṭam paśum avarodham akṛtya mukta pragraham amanyatā acintayat devatāka tvena ālambham kṛtavān anyān grāmyān āraṇyān abhyaḥ daivatam pratigamitavān uktena vidhinā paśum kalpayitvā devatyaḥ prokṣyamāṇa ālabhyamānaḥ mad devatya anya grāmya āraṇyā daivatam anya abhyaḥ devatābhya ālabhyante mad avayava bhūtābhya ata yājñikāḥ aevam ya paśu sādhanakaḥ phala bhūtaḥ nirdiśyata ya savitā jagat avabhāsayati tejasā kratu phala kāla viśeṣaḥ nirvartya kratvā sādhya phalasya kratutva nirdeśaḥ pārthivaḥ sādhana bhūtaḥ arkasya kratau cityasya aḥ ayopya avayavāḥ vyākhyātaṃ atasya diaḥ aityādinā ādityau viśeṣitau kratu phale pārthivaḥ sākṣātkratu kriyā ātmakaḥ kratoḥ sādhya nirdeśaḥ kratu sādhya phalasya kratu nirdeśa sādhya esādhanau kratu phala bhūtau ādityau bhūya kriyā sādhana phala bhedāya vibhaktā uktam kriyā nirvṛtti uttara phala ekām mad rūpā sādhana sādhya maraṇam mṛtvā maraṇāya jāyata arthaḥ apajitaḥ āśaṅkya evaṃvida phala sanne tāsām phalam adhyāye brāhmaṇam dvayā ādyasya sambandhaḥ jñāna sahitānām uktā mṛtyvātma bhāvaḥ gati uktyā mṛtyvātma bhāva sādhana bhūtayoḥ jñān ayoḥ yata udbhavaḥ prakāśana artha mudgītha brāhmaṇam ārabhyate nanu mṛtyvātma bhāvaḥ pūrvatra jñāna karmaṇoḥ phalam uktam udgītha jñāna uḥ tumṛtyvā bhāva atikramaṇam phalam bhinna viṣaya phalasya jñāna udbhava prakāśana doṣaḥ agnyāt bhāva udgītha phalasya pūrvatra phalam uktam aetāsām nanu amṛtyum aityādi viruddham svābhāvika papma āsaṅga viṣaya atikramaṇasya svābhāvikaḥ papma āsaṅgaḥ kutaḥ udbhavaḥ atikramaṇam arthasya prakāśanāya ākhyāyikā ārabhate dvayā dvi prakārāḥ vṛttāvadya udakaḥ nipātaḥ vartamāna pradāpateḥ janmani avat yodayati vṛtta janma avasthasya apatyāni prāṇā ādayaḥ asura ucyate śāstra janita jñāna bhāvitā dyodanāt devā ta svābhāvika anumāna janita dṛṣṭa prayojana jñāna bhāvitā asuṣu ramaṇāt surebhyaḥ devobhyaḥ anya dṛṣṭa prayojana jñāna bhāvitā kānīyāṃsa sva arthe aṇi vṛddhiḥ kanīyāṃsaḥ alpā jyāyasā asura ājyāyānasaḥ svābhāvikī jñāna pravṛttiḥ mahattarā śāstra janitāyāḥ jñāna pravṛtteḥ dṛṣṭa prayojana ata śāstra janita pravṛtteḥ alpa atyanta yatnasādhyā sthā nimitta svābhāvika itara jñāna sādhyeṣu spardhā kṛtavantaḥ asurāṇām vṛtti udbhava abhibhavau spardhā kadācid śāstra janita jñāna bhāvanā rūpā vattiḥ udbhavati udbhavati dṛṣṭa prayojanā anumāna janita jñāna bhāvanā rūpā vṛttiḥ āsurī abhibhūyate jayaḥ asurāṇām parājayaḥ kadācid viparyayeṇa vṛttiḥ abhibhūyata āsuryā udbhavaḥ asurāṇām jayaḥ parājayaḥ jaye utkarṣa prajāpatitva prāpteḥ asura jaye adharma apakarṣa sthāvaratva prāpteḥ ubhaya sāmye manuṣyatva prāptiḥ ta abhibhūyamānā asuraiḥ devā bāhulyāt asurāṇām kṛtavantaḥ ucyate asuraiḥ abhibhūyamānā uktavantaḥ jyotiṣṭome udgītha padārtha kartṛ svarūpa āśrayaṇena ātyayāmā atigacchāmaḥ asura anabhibhūya bhāvam śāstra prakāśitam pratipatyāmaha uktavantaḥ anyonyam udgītha padārtha kartṛ svarūpa āśrayaṇam jñāna karmabhyām vakṣyamāṇam mantra japa lakṣaṇam vidhitsyamānam jñānam nirūpyamāṇam nanu abhyāroha japa viśeṣoḥ athavā ādau jñāna nirūpaṇa aya vacanāt udgītha prastāve purākalpa śravaṇāt udgītha vidhi aprakaraṇāt udgīthasya vihita prakara abhyāroha japasya anitya viprayojyatva at vijñānasya nityavat śravaṇāt ādīnām śuddhi aśuddhi vacanāt anyupāsyate śuddhi vacanam ādīnām upānyastānām aśuddhi vacanam ādi nindayā mukhya stutiḥ abhipretā upapadyate amṛtyum aityādi phala vacanam svarūpa āpatteḥ phalam ādi ādi bhāvaḥ bhavatu upāsanam viśuddhi ādi guṇavat nanu śrutatva at upāsya tve stuti arthatva upapatteḥ viparīta artha pratipatteḥ prāpti upapatteḥ lokavat aviparītam aniṣṭāt nivartate viparīta artha pratipattyā śrauta śabda janita artha pratipattau prāptiḥ upapannā viparyaye upāsana artha śruta śabda uttha viṣayasya ayathārtha tve pramāṇam vijñānasya apavādaḥ śrūyate prāpti darśanāt yathārtha pratipadyām viparyaye anartha prāpti darśanāt viparyayeṇa sthāṇuḥ amitram mitram anartham prāpnuvan dṛśyate īśvara ādīnām ayathārthānām grahaṇam śrutitaḥ anartha prāpti śāstram prāpnuyāt lokavat yathābhūtān īśvara ādīn grāhayati upāsana śāstram ādau dṛṣṭi darśanāt ayuktam sphuṭam ādeḥ abrahma dṛṣṭim sthāṇba ādau dṛṣṭim viparītām grāhayat śāstram dṛśyate yathārtham śāstrataḥ pratipatteḥ uktam pratimā avat bheda pratipatteḥ nāmādavabrahmaṇi dṛṣṭim viparītām grāhayati śāstram sthāṇba ādau dṛṣṭim kasmtāt bhedena ādi vastu pratipannasya ādau vidhīyate dṛṣṭiḥ pratimādau viṣṇu dṛṣṭiḥ ālambana tvena ādi pratipattiḥ pratima ādivat ādi anirjñāte sthāṇuḥ viparītam ādau dṛṣṭiḥ viparītā dṛṣṭiḥ kevalā brama pratimā brāhmaṇa ādiṣu viṣṇu ādi ādi dṛṣṭīnām tulya ṛś ādiṣu ādi dṛṣṭi darśanāt vidyamāna ādi vastu dṛṣṭīnām ādi viṣaye kṣepa darśanāt sāmānyān ādiṣu ādi dṛṣṭīnām vidyamāna ādi viṣayatva siddhiḥ pratimā brāhmaṇa ādiṣu viṣṇu ādi ādi buddhīnām vastu viṣayatva siddhiḥ mukhya apekṣa gauṇa ādiṣu agnitva ādeḥ gauṇa mukhya ādi sadbhāvavat ādiṣu bahma gauṇa mukhya sadbhāva upapattiḥ kriyā arthaiḥ aviśeṣāt arthānām darśa paurṇamāsa ādi kriyet amphalā viśiṣṭā kartavyatākā evaṅkrama prayukta aṅgā alaukikam vastu ādi viṣayam tathābhūtam vākyaiḥ jñāpyate paramātma īśvara ādi vastu asthūla ādi dharmakam aśanāya ādi atītam evamādi viśiṣṭam vākyaiḥ jñāpyate alaukika tathābhūtam bhavitum kriyā arthaiḥ vākyaiḥ jñāna vākyānām buddhi utpātaka tve viśeṣaḥ aniścitā viparyastā paramātma ādi vastu viṣayā buddhiḥ utpadyate anuṣṭheya abhāvāt ayuktam kriyā arthaiḥ vākyaiḥ aṃśa abhāvanā anuṣṭheyā jñāpyate alaukikī paramātma īśvara ādi anuṣṭheyam kiñcitasti kriyā arthaiḥ sādharmyam ayuktam jñānasya tathābhūta artha viṣaya anuṣṭheya pramāṇa samadhigata viṣayāyā buddheḥ anuṣṭheya viṣaya artha vākya janita vākya adhigatasya vastunaḥ tve sati anuṣṭheyatva viśiṣṭham anutiṣṭhati anuṣṭheyatva viśiṣṭham ananuṣṭheya tve vākya pramāṇatva anupapattiḥ anuṣṭheye asati padānām sahatiḥ upapadyate anuṣṭheya tve sati tādarthyena padāni saṃhanyante anuṣṭheya niṣṭham vākyam pramāṇam kartavyam prakārāṇām śatānām vākya akuryāt kriyeta kartavyam bhavet pañcamam evamādīnām anyatame asati paramātma īśvara ādīnām avākya pramāṇa padārtha tve pramāṇa antara viṣaya aasti meruḥ varṇa catuṣṭaya upetaḥ evamādi ananuṣṭheye vākya darśanāt ameruḥ varṇa catuṣṭaya upetaḥ ādi vākya śravaṇe meru ādau anuṣṭheyatva buddhiḥ utpadyate sahitānām paramātma īśvara ādi pratipādaka vākya padānām viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvena saṃhatiḥ vāryate meru ādi jñānavat jñāne prayojana abhāvāt ayuktam bhidyate hṛdaya granthiḥ phala śravaṇāt saṃsāra bīja avidyā ādi doṣa nivṛtti darśanāt ananya śeṣa jñānasya juhvām phala artha vādatva anupapatti pratiṣiddha aniṣṭa phala sambandhaḥ vedāt anuṣṭheyaḥ pratiṣiddha viṣaye pravṛtta kriyasya akaraṇāt anuṣṭheyam akartavya jñāna niṣṭhatā paramārthataḥ pratiṣedha vidhīnām kṣudhā ārtasya pratiṣedha jñāna saṃskṛtasya abhakṣye abhojye pratyupasthite kalajjā abhiśasta at nādau aidam bhakṣya madaḥ bhojyam jñānam utpannam viṣayayā pratiṣedha jñāna smṛtyā bādhyate mṛgatṛṣṇikāyām peya jñānam viṣaya yāthātmya bādhite snābha āvika nartha karītat bhakṣaṇa bhojana pravṛttiḥ viparīta jñāna nimittāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ nivṛttiḥ yatnaḥ kāryaḥ abhāve pratiṣedha vidhīnām vastu yāthātmya jñāna niṣṭhatā vyāpāra niṣṭhata āgandhaḥ paramātma ādi yāthātmya jñāna vidhīnām mātra paryavāsana saṃskṛtasya viparīta artha jñāna nimittānām pravṛttīnām anartha artha tvena jñāyamāna paramātma ādi yāthātmya jñāna smṛtyā svābhāvike nimitta bādhite abhāvaḥ nanu kalañja ādi bhakṣaṇa ādeḥ anartha arthatva vastu yāthātmya jñāna smṛtyā svābhāvike bhakṣyatva ādi viṣaya viparīta jñāne nivartite bhakṣaṇa ādi anartha pravṛtti abhāvavat apratiṣedha viṣaya śāstra vihita pravṛtti abhāvaḥ yukta viparīta jñāna nimittatva anartha artha tvābhyām tulya kalañja bhakṣaṇa ādi pravṛtteḥ mithyājñāna nimitta anartha artha śāstra vihita pravṛttīnām paramātma yāthātmya vijñānavataḥ śāstra vihita pravṛttīnām mithyājñāna nimitta tvena anartha artha tvena tulya paramātma jñānena viparīta jñāne nivartite yukta abhāvaḥ nanu yuktaḥ nityānām kevala śāstra nimitta anartha arthatva abhāvat abhāvaḥ yukta avidyā rāga dveṣa ādi doṣavataḥ vihita svarga ādi doṣavataḥ darśa pūrṇamāsa ādīni kāmyāni vihitāni anartha bīja avidyā ādi doṣavataḥ janita iṣṭā aniṣṭa prāpti parihāra rāga dveṣa ādi doṣavataḥ prerita aviśeṣa pravṛtteḥ iṣṭa aniṣṭa prāpti parihāra arthinaḥ nityāni vidhīyante kevalam śāstra nimittāni agnihotra darśa pūrṇamāsa cāturmāsya paśu bandha somānām svatas kāmya nityatva viveka usti kartṛ gatena svarga ādi doṣeṇa artha avidyā ādi doṣavataḥ svabhāva prāpta iṣṭa aniṣṭa prāpti parihāra arthinaḥ arthāni nityāni yuktam vihita paramātma yāthātmya vijñānavataḥ śama upāya vyatirekeṇa vihitam ubhalabhyate nimitta ādi sādhana upamardena jñānam vidhīyate upamardita kriyā kāraka ādi vijñānasya pravṛttiḥ upapadyate viśiṣṭa kriyā sādhana ādi jñāna pūrvaka kriyā pravṛtteḥ deśa kāla ādi anavacchinnā sthūla dvaya ādi patyaya dhāriṇaḥ avasaraḥ bhojana ādi pravṛtti avasara vatsyāt avidyā ādi kevala doṣa nimitta bhojana ādi pravṛtteḥ āvaśyakatva anupapatteḥ aniyatam kadācid kriyate kadācid kriyate nityam upapadyate kevala doṣa nimitta bhojana ādi aniyata doṣa udbhava abhibhavayoḥ aniyata kāmānām kāmyeṣu śāstra nimitta kāla ādi apekṣa nityānām aniyatatva anupapattiḥ doṣa nimitta tve sati kāmya agnihotrasya śāstra vihita sāyaṃprātar kāla ādi apekṣa bhojanādipa vṛttau niyama vatsyāt niyama sākriyatvāt kriyāyāḥ caprayojaka jñānasya apavāda karaḥ paramātmāya athātmya jñāna vidheḥ viparīta sthūla dvaita ādi jñāna nivartaka sāmarthyāt pratiṣedha vidhi artha sampadyate pravṛtti abhāvasya tulya pratiṣedha viṣaye pratiṣedha vidhivat vastu pratipādanam paratvam siddham śāstrasya viniścitya abhimāninīm m ucuḥ uktavantaḥ asmabhyam audgātram kuruṣva vāgdevatā nirvartti amaugātram kama dṛṣṭavantaḥ japa mantra abhidhāyām upāsanāyāḥ kartṛ tvena ādaya vivakṣyante paramārthataḥ kartṛkaḥ viṣaya jñāna saṃvyavahāraḥ kartṛkatva abhāvam vistarataḥ ṣaṣṭe adyāya upasaṃhariṣyati avyākṛta ādi kriyā kāraka phala avidyā viṣayam avyākṛtāt paramātma ākhyam viṣayam anāma ātmakam itara pratyākhyānena upasaṃhariṣyati ādi samāhāra upādhi parikalpitaḥ saṃsārya ādi samāhāra pakṣa pātinam darśayiṣyati yuktā ādīnām jñāna kartṛtva phala prāpti vivakṣā devaiḥ uktā vāktebhyaḥ arthibhyor aya udakāyat udgānam kṛtavatī devebhyor aya udgāna nirvartitaḥ kārya viśeṣaḥ ucyate vācī nimitta bhūtāyām ādi samudāyasya ya upakāraḥ niṣpadyate vadana ādi vyāpāreṇa vadana abhinirvṛttaḥ phalam bhogam tṛṣu pavamāneṣu avaśiṣṭeṣu navasu stotreṣu vācanikam phalam śobhanam varṇān abhinirvartayati mahyam asādhāraṇam vāgdevatāyāḥ samyak varṇānām uccāraṇam viśeṣyate vadana kāryam saṃghāta upakāra ātmakam yājamānam kalyāṇa vadana sambandha asaṅga avasaram randhram pratilamya vidura surāḥ udgātrānaḥ svābhāvikam jñānam abhibhūya ati itya śāstra janita jñāna udgātra ati eṣvanti atigamiṣyanti samudgātāram abhigamya āsaṅga lakṣaṇena vidhyan tāḍitavantaḥ saṃyojitavanta arthaḥ janma avasthasya kṣiptaḥ pratyakṣīkriyate ananurūpam śāstra pratiṣiddham prayuktaḥ asabhya bībhatsā anṛtā adyanicchan kāryeṇa apratirūpa vadanena anugamyamānaḥ kārya bhūtāsu prajāsu vartate apratirūpa vadanena anumitaḥ gataḥ kāraṇa anuvidhāyi kāryam ghrāṇa ādi udgītha nirvarta japa mantra prakāśyā upāsyāḥ kameṇa parīkṣitavantaḥ niścitam ādi kameṇa parīkṣyamāṇāḥ kalyāṇa viṣaya viśeṣa sambandha āsaṅga hetoḥ āsura saṃsargāt udgītha nirvartanā samarthāḥ anabhidheyāḥ anupāsyāḥ aśuddha itara avyāpaka anuktā ādi kalyāṇā kalyāṇa akārya darśanāt ādideva avidhi viddhavanta uktam saṃsargam kṛtavanta ādi upāsīnā mṛti ati gamanāya aśaraṇāḥ krameṇa abhinaya pradarśana bhavam mukha bila stham śaraṇam upagatebhyaḥ mukhya ityādi pūrvavat pāpmanāvivyat sanvedhanam kartum iṣṭavantaḥ doṣa asaṃsargiṇam mukhyam āsaṅga doṣeṇa ādiṣu labdha prasarāḥ abhyāsa anuvṛttyā saṃsrakṣyamāṇā vinaṣṭā vidhvastāḥ dṛṣṭānta ucyate dṛṣṭāntaḥ pāṣāṇam pāṃsu pāṣāṇa cūrṇanāya aśmani nikṣiptaḥ vistraṃseta vicūrṇībhavet dṛṣṭānta vidhvaṃsamānā viśeṣeṇa dhvaṃsamānā anāgatayaḥ vinaṣṭā āsuravināśāt devatva pratibandha svābhāvika āsaṅga janita pāpmabhyaḥ viyogāt asaṃsarga dharmi mukhya āśraya balāt ādayaḥ prakṛtā ādi ātmakam vakṣyamāṇam aṣi ādi ātmana svābhāvikena tiraskṛta vijñānāḥ piṇḍa mātra abhimānā āsan viyogāt ujjhitvā piṇḍa mātra abhimānam śāstra samarpita ādi ādi abhimānā arthaḥ pratipakṣa bhūtā parābhavan anuvartate parābhūtā vinaṣṭā arthaḥ kalpena varṇitaḥ atikrānta kālikaḥ ākhyāyikā rūpām śrutim krameṇa ādi parīkṣya apohya āsaṅga āspada doṣavat tvena adoṣa āspadam mukhyam tvena upagamya ādyādhyātmika piṇḍa mātra paricchinna abhimānam hitvā vairāja piṇḍa abhimānam ādi ādi viṣayam vartamāna śāstra prakāśitam pratipannaḥ vidhinā svarūpeṇa asyā prajāpatitva pratipakṣa bhūtaḥ adveṣṭā bharata ādi tulyaḥ indriya viṣaya āsaṅga janitaḥ dveṣṭā pāramārthika svarūpa tiḥ atiraskaraṇa hetu parābhavati viśīryate loṣṭavāt pariṣvaṅgāt phalam ya uktam tvena yajamānavat arthaḥ phalam upasaṃhṛtya adhunā khyāyikā aśriti hetoḥ ādīn muktā mukhya tvena āśrayitavyaḥ upapatti nirūpaṇāya ādīnām piṇḍa ādīnām sādhāraṇa ākhyāyikayā darśayanti śrutiḥ prāṇā mukhyena pariprāpita svarūpā uktavantaḥ phala avasthāḥ vitarke asakta sañjitavān bhāvam tvena upagamitavān smaranti kenacid upakṛtā upakāriṇam lokavat smarantaḥ vicārayamāṇāḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghāte upalabdhavantaḥ ayamāsye mukhe ya antarayam pratyakṣaḥ vartata vicārya adhyavasyati antarākāśe ādi tvena viśeṣam anāśritya vartamāna upalabdhaḥ devaiḥ viśeṣa āśrayāt asakta sañjitavān ādīn ata aṅgirasa kārya karaṇānām prasiddham kārya karaṇa lakṣaṇānām sāra arthaḥ apāye śoṣa prāpteḥ vakṣyāmaḥ viśeṣām āśrita kārya karaṇānām sādhāraṇa viśuddhaḥ ādīn apāsya tvena āśrayitavya vākya arthaḥ tvena upagantavyaḥ aviparīta bodhāt prāpteḥ viparyaye sva aniṣṭa prāpti darśanāt viśuddhiḥ asiddhā nanu parihṛtam ādīnām kalyāṇa vadana ādi āsaṅgavat āsaṅga āspadatva abhāvena vāḍham aṅgira satvena ādīnām ātmatva uktyā ādi dvāreṇa śava sṛṣṭi aśuddha śaṅkyate śuddha dūrnāma loṣṭavat vidhvastā parāmṛśati vartamāna yajamāna sthā devaiḥ nirdhāritā ayamāsye upāsana kriyāyāḥ bhāvena guṇa dūrnāma dūriti khyātā khyāpana paryāyaḥ prasiddha āsyā viśuddhi dūrna dūrna dūreḥ āsaṅga lakṣaṇaḥ asaṃśleṣa dharmi samīpa sthāsya dūra dūriti khyātiḥ viśuddhiḥ jñāpitā viduṣaḥ phalam ucyate ya prakṛtam viśuddhi guṇa upetam arthaḥ upāsanam upāsya artha vāde ādi svarūpam śrutyā jñāpyate upagamya cintanam laukika pratyaya avyavadhānena ādi svarūpa abhimāna abhivyaktiḥ laukika abhimānavat kindevataḥ diśyasi evamādi śrutibhyaḥ uktam ucyate evaṃvidtva virodhāt indriya viṣaya saṃsarga āsaṅga jaḥ abhimāninaḥ virudhyate ādi viśeṣa abhimāna hetu svābhāvika ajñāna hetu śāstra janitaḥ abhimānaḥ yuktam virodhāt pradarśayati ādīnām svābhāvika ajñāna prayukta indriya viṣaya saṃsarga āsaṅga janitena abhimāna mātra apahantā ucyate virodhāt gataḥ ucyate prācyādīnām avasānam gamayāñcakāra gamanam kṛtavān nanu gamitavān ucyate śrauta vijñānavat jana avadhi nimitta kalpita virodhi jana avyuṣita deśa vaditi doṣaḥ pāpmana dvitīyā bahuvacanam vividham nyagbhāvena dadhāt sthāpitavatī abhimāna śūnyeṣu antyajaneṣu sāmarthyāt indriya saṃsarga jaḥ āśrayatā avagamyate antyam īyān gacchet sambhāṣaṇa darśana ādibhiḥ saṃsṛjet saṃsarge saṃsargaḥ āśrayaḥ jana nivāsam śabda vācyam jana śūnyam deśa viyuktam abhiprāyaḥ nediti paribhaya arthe nipātaḥ jana saṃsarge ava anugaccheyam bhītaḥ ceyāt pūrveṇa sambandhaḥ jñāna phalam ādīnām ādi ucyate enā ādhyātmika pariccheda karaḥ vijñānenapahataḥ apahantā enā ādi prakṛtam atītya prāpayat aparicchinnam ādi devātātma pradhānām udgītha karmaṇi itara karaṇa apekṣayā sādhakatama prādhānyam vahanam kṛtavān mṛtyumatī tyoḍhāyāḥ ucyate atyam ucyatā atītyāmucyata mocitā asogniḥ mṛtyu viyoge viśeṣaḥ mṛtyu viyoge soyam prāk mokṣāt mṛtyu pratibaddhaḥ adhyātma dīptimān mṛtyu viyogāt ghrāṇam prācya ādi vibhāgena avasthitāḥ candramā ādi ādi bhāvena vartamāna ādi ādi bhāvena ādi pañcaka viśiṣṭam ādibhiḥ āgānam mukhyaḥ phalam āgānam pamāneṣu śiṣṭeṣu navasu stotreṣu ādyam kartuḥ saṃyogaḥ vācanika uktam āgītam gamyate hetum sāmānya mātra parāmarśa arthaḥ hetau prāṇibhiḥ kiñcit adyatebhakṣyate ana ākhyā prasiddhā śakaṭa vācī paryāyaḥ adyata arthaḥ kevalam adyata ākāra pariṇate annādya āgītam annādanam ādiṣu kalyāṇa saṅga japa nanu avadhāraṇam ayuktam adyata ādīnām nimitta upakāra darśanāt doṣaḥ dvāra upakārasya dvārakaḥ kṛtau ādīnām upakāra pradarśayan ādayaḥ sva viṣaya dyotanāt uktavantaḥ mukhyam at adhikam smaraṇa arthaḥ karam ātmana āgītavān āgānena ātmasātkṛtam arthaḥ sthātum utsāmahe usmān arthe ābhājayasva ṇicaḥ aśravaṇam chāndasam bhāginaḥ itara yūyam arthinaḥ samantatas ābhimukhyena niviśata uktavati pariveṣṭya niviṣṭavanta arthaḥ niviṣṭānām anujñayā ādyamānam karam tṛpti karam svātantryeṇa yuktam avadhāraṇam adyata āśraya anujñayā abhisanniviṣṭā ādi annena etā ādyāḥ ādi āśrayam ādayaḥ āśrayā svā jñātasya ādaya jñātīnām āśrayaṇīyaḥ abhiprāyaḥ abhisanniviṣṭānām prāṇavat ādīnām sva annena agrata etā gantā ādīnām annādaḥ anāmayāvi arthaḥ adhiṣṭhāya pālayitā svatantraḥ prāṇavat ādīnām ya uktam phalam ya evaṃvidham vidam jñātīnām madhye pratikūlaḥ pratispardhī bhavitum icchati sosurā pratispardhinaḥ paryāptaḥ bharaṇīyebhyaḥ bhartum arthaḥ ya jñātīnām madhye ādaya anugataḥ anuvartayan ātmīyān bhartum icchati ādayaḥ anuvṛtti bubhūrṣava āsan paryāptaḥ bharaṇīyebhyaḥ bhartum svatantraḥ guṇa phalam uktam kārya karaṇānām ātmatva pratipādanāya aṅgira upanyastam ayāsya āṅgirasa hetoḥ āṅgirasa āṅgirasa tve hetuḥ uktaḥ hetu siddhi ārabhyate hetu siddhi āyattam kāryāṇa ātmatva ādīnām adhīna uktā upapādanīyā ayāsya āṅgirasa ityādi upanyastam upādīyate uttara aprāṇaḥ vākyam yathāvyākhya smārayati aprāṇaḥ aprāṇaḥ prasiddhau prasiddham ādīnām yuktam smāraṇam prasiddha ata śabda upasaṃhāra artha tvena sambadhyate avayavāt anukta viśeṣāt kutaścid avayavāt aviśeṣitāt apasarpati aṅgam nīrasam śoṣam upaiti upasaṃhāraḥ kārya karaṇānām siddham apāye śeṣaḥ maraṇam jīvanti prāṇinaḥ apāsya ādīn upāsya samudāya arthaḥ kevalam kārya karaṇayoḥ bhūtayoḥ sāmnām ātmaka stuvan mahīkaroti upāsya tvāya prakṛta ucyate bṛhati icchandaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśat akṣarā bṛhatyām chandasi yuktam prasiddhavat vaktum bṛhatyām antarbhavanti saṃstuta ṛca śruti antarāt carcā antarbhāvaḥ bṛhatyā ṛca nirvartaka kauṣṭhyā prerita māruta nirvartyā pālanāt pālyate aprāṇasya śabda uccāraṇa sāmarthya abhāvāt tasmā ṛcām arthaḥ yajuṣām viśeṣa brahmaṇa pūrvavat avagamyate rṛc yajuṣṭvam anyārtha ucyate sāmāna adhikaraṇya nirdeśāt avāc avāc samāna adhikaraṇayoḥ yajuṣṭvam yuktam pariśeṣāt sāmni abhihite yajuṣī pariśiṣṭe viśeṣa viśeṣaḥ yajuṣī samāna adhikaraṇa yuktā aviśeṣa prasaṅgāt udgītha spaṣṭam viśeṣa abhidhāna śabdayoḥ viśeṣa abhidhāna yuktam anyathā anirdhārita viśeṣayoḥ ānarthakī āpatteḥ viśeṣa abhidhānasya mātra tve ubhayatra paunaruktyāt udgītha śrutiṣu evaṅkrama darśanāt kiñcit śabda abhidheyam śabda abhidheya vastu viṣayaḥ paiṃsnāni āpnoṣi śruti antarāt abhidhāna bhūtaḥ nirvartya ādi samudāya mātram gitiḥ abhidhīyate vyatirekeṇa nāmā varṇa ādeḥ nirvartya tantra ātmakam cāmaḥ gīti rūpabhya ādi samudāyasya pragītam bhuvi tulyaḥ vakṣyamāṇena prakāreṇa sambandhaḥ śabda lābha nimitta prakāra antara nirdeśa sāmarthya labhyaḥ prakāreṇa tulya ucyate puttikā śarīreṇa maśaka śarīreṇa śarīreṇa sama trailokya śarīreṇa prājāpatyena jagat hairaṇyagarbheṇa puttikā ādi śarīreṣu gaḥtva ādivat kārtsnyena parisamāpta sama mātra parimāṇena amūrta gata ghaṭa prāsāda ādi pradīpavat saṃkoca vikāsitayā mātram sama ta gatasya parimāṇa vṛtti lābhaḥ virudhyate samatvāt ākhyam śrati prakāśita mahacvam taspa phalam vyāpnoti yugbhāvam samāna deha indriya abhimāna sālokyam samāna lopha bhāvanā viśeṣataḥ ya uktam abhimāna abhivyakteḥ arthaḥ avayavaḥ bhakti viśeṣaḥ udgānam adhikārāt utprāṇena jagat stabdham uttambhitam vidhṛtam arthaḥ uttabdha artha avadyotakaḥ ucchabdaḥ guṇa abhidhāyakaḥ utprāṇaḥ śabda viśeṣa udgītha bhakteḥ gāyateḥ śabda artha udgītha bhakteḥ śabda vyatirekeṇa utprekṣyate yuktam avadhāraṇam ucca tantrā ekena abhidhīyate ukter athe hāpya ākhyāyikā śrūtaye hasma nāmataḥ cikitānasya apatyam caikitānaḥ apatyam yuvā camasasthaḥ bhakṣyamāṇaḥ anṛta vādinaḥ vispaṣṭam pātayatu torayam tātaṅṅādeśaḥ āśipi loṭ anṛta vādī arthaḥ anṛta vāditva prāptiḥ ucyate yadīta prakṛtāt saṃyuktāt mukhya abhidhāyakena ayāsya āṅgirasa abhidhīyate viśvasṛjām satre udrātāsaḥ vyatiriktena udgānam kṛtavān anṛta vādī viparīta pratipattuḥ vipātayatu śapatham pratyaya dārḍhya kartavyatām darśayati ākhyāyikā nirdhāritam vacasā śrutiḥ pradhānayā svasya bhūtena ayāsya āṅgirasa eṣor athaḥ nirdhāritaḥ śapathena prakṛtam abhisamvadhnāti mukhyam vyapadiśati abhinayena śabda vācyasya prāṇasyayaḥ dhanam hāsya phalena pralobhya abhimukhīkṛtya śuśrūṣave kaṇṭha gatam mādhuryam vibhūṣaṇam bhūṣitam ṛdhimat lakṣya ta audgānam ṛtvij udgānam viṣaye āśritam dhanavat svareṇa cikīrṣuḥ prāsaṅgikaṃvidhīyate sausvaryeṇa svaravat vapratyayeka rtavye icchā mātreṇa sausvaryam danta dhāvana taila pāna ādi sāmarthyāt kartavyam arthaḥ saṃskṛtayā sva bhūtaḥ bhūṣitam svaravanta mudgātāram didṛkṣanta draṣṭum icchanta dhaninām ava laukikāḥ prasiddham athaḥ dhanam dhaninam siddhasya guṇa phala sambandhasya upasaṃhāraḥ kriyate hāsya ya guṇaḥ suvarṇavattā lakṣaṇaḥ vidhīyate sausvaryam viśeṣaḥ kaṇṭha gata mādhuryam lākṣaṇikam suvarṇa śabda vācyam hāsya suvarṇa śabda sāmānyāt suvarṇayoḥ lokikam guṇa phalam arthaḥ hāsya ya pūrvavat guṇam vidhitsan aktām guṇam guṇa yuktam pūrvavat phalena pratilobhitāya pratilobhitāya śuśrūpave mūlīya ādīnām sthānānām ākhyā mūlīya ādiṣuhi gānam gīti bhāvam āpadyate gīyata yuktam anindita ekīya pakṣasya vikalpena guṇa patiṣṭhā vijñānavataḥ japa vidhitsyate vijñānavataḥ japa karmaṇi adhikāraḥ uktam viduṣā prayujyamānam bhāvāya abhyāroha phalam japa vidhīyata udgītha sambandhāt sarvatra prāptau vacanāt pavamāneṣu kartavyatāyām prāptāyām kāla saṃkocam prārabheta kāla japa karmaṇa ākhyā abhyāroha ābhimukhyena ārohati japa bhāva bahuvacanāt dvitīyā nirdeśāt brāhmaṇa utpanna yathāpaṭhita prayoktavyaḥ māntraḥ yājamānam japa aasataḥ aatamasaḥ amṛtya ūrmā mantrām arthaḥ tirohitaḥ vyācaṣṭe brāhmaṇam mantra mantraḥ uktavān arthaḥ ucyate aasataḥ svābhāvika ucyete asad atyanta bhauva hetutvāt śāstrīya agaraṇa hetu ajñānāt śāstrīya bhāva sādhana bhāvam āpādaya arthaḥ vākya etadāha ajñānam āvaraṇa ātmakatva āt maraṇa hetu viparītam svarūpam prakāśa ātmaka jñānam avināśa ātmaka pūrvavat mṛtya ūḥ ityādi phala bhāvam āpādaya arthaḥ mantraḥ asādhana svabhāvāt sādhana bhāvam āpādaya sādhana bhāvāt ajñāna rūpāt sādhya bhāvam āpādaya pūrvayoḥ mantrayoḥ samucitor athaḥ tṛtīyena mantreṇa ucyata prasiddha artha tṛtīye mantre antarhitam artha pūrvayoḥ mantrayoḥ yathāśruta arthaḥ yājamānam udgānam pavamāneṣu śiṣṭāni bhūtaḥ prāṇavat uktam vetti prāṇavat sādhayitum samarthaḥ stotreṣu prayujyamāneṣu prārthayeta śabdāt prāk sambadhyate icchati āgānena sādhayati jñāna karmabhyām āpattiḥ uktam apāye āpattiḥ āśaṅkate nivṛtti etaloka hatat darśanam viyuktam kevalam sādhanam ālokya aloka arha tvāya āśaṃsanam prārthanam utpanna abhimānasya prāpti āśaṃsanam grāma kadā grāmam prāpnutām araṇya stha āśāste asannikṛṣṭa viṣaye anātmani āśaṃsanam sva aśāsti kadācid bhāvam prapadyeyam ya uktam nirdhāritamahimānam indriya viṣaya āsaṅgaiḥ āsuraiḥ adharṣaṇīyaḥ viśuddhaḥ ādi pañcakam mad āśraya ādi svābhāvika uttha indriya viṣaya āsaṅga janita asura doṣa viyuktam mad āśrayāt upayoga bandhanam āṅgira satvāt udgītha bhūtāyāḥ vāca vayā āpteḥ nirvartaka gīti bhāvam āpadyamānasya dhanam bhūṣaṇam sausvaryam āntaram sauvarṇya lākṣaṇikam sausvaryam gīti bhāvam āpadyamānasya kaṇṭha ādi sthānāni guṇa puttikā ādi śarīreṣu kārtsnyena parisamāptaḥ amūrta gata abhimāna abhivyakteḥ arthaḥ adhyāye tṛtīya mudgītha brāhmaṇam jñāna karmabhyām samucitābhyām prajāpatitva prāptiḥ vyākhyātā kevala ataddha aitya ādinā phala sṛṣṭi saṃhāreṣu jagataḥ svātantrya ādi vibhūti upavarṇanena jñāna karmaṇoḥ vaidikayoḥ phala utkarṣaḥ varṇayitavya ārabhyate kāṇḍa vihita jñāna stutiḥ bhavet sāmarthyāt vivakṣitam jñāna phalam saṃsāra bhaya arati ādi yuktatva śravaṇāt kārya karaṇa lakṣaṇa sthūla vyakta anitya viṣaya vidyāyāḥ kevalāyāḥ vakṣyamāṇāyāḥ mokṣa hetu uttara saṃsāra viṣayāt sādhya sādhana ādi bheda lakṣaṇāt aviraktasya ekatva jñāna viṣaye adhikāraḥ atṛṣitasya pāne jñāna phala utkarṣa upavarṇanam uttara ityādi prathamaḥ aṇḍajaḥ śarīrī abhidhīyate vaidika jñāna phala bhūtaḥ bheda śarīreṇa avibhaktam antara utpatteḥ prakāraḥ ādi lakṣaṇaḥ prathamaḥ sambhūtaḥ anvālocanam kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ vastu piṇḍa kārya karaṇa rūpān dadarśa kevalam janma śrauta saṃskṛtaḥ vyāhṛtavān jñāna saṃskārāt abhyadhāt upaniṣadam śruti pradarśitam kāraṇe kārya prāṇiṣu kāla uktaḥ aha m agra kāraṇa abhidhānena abhidhāya viśeṣa jijñāsave viśeṣa piṇḍa abhidhānam devadattaḥ yajñadattaḥ prabūte kathayati viśeṣa piṇḍasya kathayati atikrānta janmani samyak jñāna bhāvanā anuṣṭhānaiḥ sādhaka avasthāyām jñāna bhāvanā anuṣṭhānaiḥ pratipitsūnām prathamaḥ prajāpatitva pratipitsu samudāyāt ādau auṣada dahat āsaṅga ajñāna lakṣaṇān prajāpatitva pratibandha kāraṇa bhūtān oṣitvā prativandhakān jñāna bhāvanā anuṣṭhāna vahninā kevalam jñāna balāt vauṣati bhasmīkaroti viduṣaḥ prathamaḥ bhavitum icchati arthaḥ darśayati ya sāmarthyāt jñāna bhāvanā prakarṣavān nanu anarthāya pratipipsā dahyate doṣaḥ jñāna bhāvanā utkarṣa abhāvāt prajāpatitva pratipattya bhāva mātra dāhasya utkṛṣṭa sādhanaḥ prāpnuvan nyūna sādhanaḥ dahati ucyate pratyakṣam utkṛṣṭa sādhanena dahyate āji sṛtām mājim upasarpati dagdhā apahṛta sāmarthyā tadvat tuṣṭu uṣitam kāṇḍa vihita jñāna phalam lakṣaṇam saṃsāra viṣayam atyakrāma ditīmam artha pradarśayiṣyan yoyam prathamaḥ śarīri vyākhyātaḥ bhītavān asmad ādivat karaṇavān nāśavi parīta darśanava tvād sāmānya ādadya tve asmad ādivat bhaya hetu viparīta darśana apanoda kāraṇam yathābhūta darśanam i īkṣaṇam kṛtavān mad ta unyat vyatirekeṇa vastu pratidvandībhūtam vināśa hetu abhāve yathābhūta darśa nāt vispaṣṭam apagatavat kevala avidyā nimittam artha darśane anupapannam bhītavān paramārtha nirūpaṇāyām anupapannam abhiprāyaḥ dvitīya dvaḥ antaraddhi vastu avidyā pratyupasthāpitam adṛśyamānam bhaya janmanaḥ hetuḥ mohaḥ śokaḥ anupaśyataḥ mantra varṇāt ekatva apanunoda yuktam vastu antarāt ekatva dvitīya darśanam apanītam codayanti ekatva darśanam upadideśa anupadiṣṭam prādurabhūt asmad ādeḥ prasaṅgaḥ janma antara kṛta saṃskāra hetukam ekatva darśana ānarthakya prasaṅgaḥ atikrānta janma avasthasya ekatva darśanam vidyamānam avidyā bandha kāraṇam apaninye avidyā saṃyukta ekatva darśana ānarthakyam antyam nivartakam pūrvavat prasaṅgena anaikāntyāt anarthakam ekatva darśanam doṣaḥ utkṛṣṭa hetu udbhava lokavat udbhavaiḥ viviktaiḥ kārya karaṇaiḥ saṃyukte janmani sati medhā smṛti vaiśāradyam jñāna vairāgya aiśvarya viparīta hetu dāhāt viśuddhaiḥ kārya karaṇaiḥ saṃyuktam utkṛṣṭam janma udbhavam anupadiṣṭam yuktam ekatva darśanam smṛtiḥ jñānam agratidham vairāgyam jagatpateḥ aiśvaryam siddham catuṣṭayam siddha tve bhaya anupapattiḥ tama anyān upadiṣṭa artha siddha vākyasya śraddhātātparya praṇipāta ādīnām ahetutvam śraddhāvān labhate jñānam saṃyata indriyaḥ viddhi praṇipātena evamādīnām śruti smṛti vihitānām jñāna hetūnām ahetu janma antara kṛta hetu tve jñānasya nimitta vikalpa samuccaya guṇavat aguṇavattva bheda upapatteḥ naimittikānām kāryāṇām nimitta bhedaḥ anekadhā vikalpate nimitta samuccayaḥ vikalpitānām samuccitānām guṇavat aguṇavattva bhedaḥ jñāna naimittike kārye vinā ālokena cakṣū sannikarṣaḥ naktañcarāṇām jñāne nimittam mana kevalam jñāna nimittam yogīnām asmākam sannikarṣa ālokābhyām ādi āloka bhedaiḥ samuccitā nimitta bhedā āloka viśeṣa guṇavat aguṇavat tvena bhedāḥ syuḥ ekatva jñāne kvacid janma antara kārma nimittam kvacid nimittam vijijñāsasva kvacid śraddhāvān labhate jñānam viddhi praṇipātena ācāryāt ityādi śruti smṛtibhya ekānta jñāna lābha nimitta prabhṛtīnām adharma ādi nimitta viyoga hetu vedānta śravaṇa manana nididhyāsanānām jñeya viṣaya ādi pratibandha kṣaye manasoḥ artha jñāna nimitta svābhāvyāt ahetu jñānasya praṇipāta ādīnām saṃsāra viṣaya prājāpati prāpatiḥ ratim anvabhavat aratya āviṣṭaḥ arthaḥ ādideva ekākitva ādi dharmavat ratim ratiḥ iṣṭā artha saṃyoga jā krīḍā prasaṃgina iṣṭa viyogāt ākulībhāvaḥ aratiḥ ucyate arateḥ apanodāya aratya paghāta samartham strīvastu gṛddhim viṣayam gṛdhyataḥ pariṣvaktasya bhāvaḥ īpsu parimāṇa kiṃparimāṇaḥ arati apanodāya parimāṇau syātām parimāṇau arthaḥ parimāṇam dvi prakāram pātitavān avadhāraṇam mūla kāraṇāt virājaḥ viśeṣaṇa kṣīrasya upamardena bhāva āpattivat upamardena etā ān vyavasthitasya virājaḥ saṃkalpa vyatiriktam strīpuṃsa pariṣvakta parisāṇam tathābhūtaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyāt pātanāt patitaḥ dampatyoḥ nirvacanam laukikayoḥ ata ātmana bhū toyeyam mānor adhabṛgalam ardham vidalam vidalam arthaḥ prākḥ udvahanāt ucyate sva ātmana uktavān valkaḥ vaktā yajñavalkaḥ apatyam daiva arthaḥ vāpatyam śūnyaḥ udvahanāt ardhena sampuṭīkaraṇena vidala manu ākhyaḥ śatarūpa ākhyām duhitaram tvena kalpitām maithunam upagatavān upagamanāt manuṣyā utpannāḥ śatarūpā duhitṛ gamane smārtam pratiṣedham anusmarantī kṣāñcake akṛtyam ātmana utpādya apyayam nirghṛṇaḥ tiraḥ jāti tiraskṛtā bhavāni īkṣitvā utpādya codyamānāyāḥ matiḥ śatarūpāyāḥ manoḥ ṛṣabha sameva ābhat ityādi pūrvavat baḍa vetarā vṛṣa gardabhī gardabha baḍavā vṛṣa ādīnām saṅgamāt ekagvuram aśvatara gardabha ākhyam vastaḥ chāga aviritarā meṣa sameva vīpsā ajām aviñcetisamabhavat arthaḥ ayaḥ kiṃñca srīpuṃsa lakṣaṇam dvandam pipīlikābhiḥ nyāyena jagat sṛṣṭavān jagat āvāham sṛjyate sṛṣṭam jagat ucyate sṛṣṭam jagat mada bheda mattaḥ vyatiricyate kuta jagat sṛṣṭavān arthaḥ sṛṣṭi abhyadhāt sṛṣṭi nāmā jagati hāsya prajāpategetasyām jagati prajāpativat sraṣṭā sva ananya jagataḥ ya prajāpativat uktam sva ananya jagat sādhya ādi adhidaivam jagat jagat mithuna ātmakam sṛṣṭā ādi varṇa niyanvardevatāḥ sisṛkṣuḥ ādau ayā śabda dvayam abhinaya pradarśana prakāreṇa mukhe prakṣityā abhyamanyat ābhimukhyena manyana pakarot devatyaḥ mukha vīryaḥ śruti smṛti siddham bala āśrayābhyām bāhubhyām balabhid ādikam kṣanni ati niyantarām kṣanniyam aindram bāhu śrutau smṛtau avagatam ūruta īhā ceṣṭā āśrayāt ādi lakṣaṇam viśaḥ niyantāram kṛṣi ādi ādi devatyaḥ pṛthvī daivatam śūdram padbhyām paricaraṇa kṣamam śruti smṛti prasiddheḥ kṣatra ādi sargam anuktam vakṣyamāṇamam uktavat sṛṣṭi sākalya anukīrtyai śrutiḥ vyavasthitā niścitor athaḥ sraṣṭuḥ ananya sṛṣṭānām prajāpatinā sṛṣṭa prakaraṇa arthe vyavasthite stuti abhiprāyeṇa avidvat matā antara nindā upanyāsaḥ anya nindā ani astutaye prakaraṇe kevala yājñikā yāga vaca aamum yajāsum indram aityādi śastra stotra ādi bhinna bhinnam ādidevam manyamānā abhiprāyaḥ bhedaḥ hiraṇyagarbhe saṃsārī mantra varṇāt indram mitram varuṇam smṛteḥ manum atīndriyaḥ agrāhyaḥ sūkṣmaḥ avyaktaḥ m ayaḥ acintyaḥ udbabhau saṃsāri sarvain pāpmana aupat asaṃsāriṇaḥ dāha prasaṅgaḥ bhaya arati saṃyoga śravaṇāt hiraṇyagarbham jāyamānam mantra varṇāt smṛteḥ vipāka prakriyāyām viśvasṛjaḥ avyaktam uttamām sātvikīm gatim manīṣiṇaḥ viruddha artha anupapatteḥ prāmāṇya vyāghāta kalpanā antara upapatteḥ avirodhāt upādhi viśeṣa sambandhāt viśeṣa kalpanā upapadyate vrajati śayānaḥ madāmadam pakṣasya ijyamānaḥ āttṛ agnīṣoma ātmakam jagat tvena paśyanta kenacid doṣeṇa atiśayā praśasyatarān sakāśāt atiśayā ata maraṇa sannamṛtāna maraṇa dharmiṇaḥ jñāna vahninā pāpmana oṣitvā ati sṛṣṭim bhūtām ati prajāpativat sraṣṭā vaidikam sādhanam jñāna lakṣaṇam kartṛ ādi aneka kāraka apekṣam prajāpatitva phala avasānam sādhyam jagat saṃsāraḥ sādhya sādhana lakṣaṇasya vyākṛtasya jagataḥ vyākaraṇāt bīja avasthā nirdidijñati aṅkura ādi kārya anumitām vṛkṣasya bījaḥ avidyā kṣetraḥ saṃsāra mūla uddhartavya uddharaṇe artha parisamāptiḥ uktam mūlaḥ avāc śākhaḥ kāṭhake gītāsu śākham purāṇe brahmavṛkṣaḥ bīja avastham jagat prāk utpatteḥ parokṣatva asarva abhidhānena abhidhīyate kāla sambandhi avyākṛta bhāvinaḥ jagataḥ sukha grahaṇa aitihya prayogaḥ ucyamāne sukham parokṣām jagataḥ bīja avasthām yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ukte yadvat vyākṛta ātmakam sādhya sādhana lakṣaṇam yathāvarṇitam abhidhīyate idaṃśabdayoḥ avastha jagat vācakayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyāt prata yakṣa avasthasya jagataḥ avagamyate avyākṛtam sati asata utpattiḥ vināśaḥ kāryasya avadhṛtam evambhūtam jagat avyākṛtam kartṛ prayogāt akriyata vispaṣṭam viśeṣa avadhāraṇa maryādam vyaktībhāvam āpadyata sāmarthyāt ākṣipta niyantṛ kartṛ sādhana kriyā nimittam asaunāma viśeṣa abhidhānena mātram vyapadiśati devadattaḥ yajñadatta asaunāmāyam śukla kṛṣṇa ādīnām aviśeṣaḥ avyākṛtam vastu vyākriyate asaunāmāyam arthaḥ śāstra ārambhaḥ svābhāvikyā kartṛ kriyā phala adhyāropaṇā kṛta kāraṇam jagataḥ ātmake salilāt acchān malam phenam avyākṛte vyākriyete vilakṣaṇaḥ svatas nitya śuddha mukta svabhāvaḥ avyākṛte bhūte vyākurvan ādi stamba paryanteṣu deheṣu phala āśrayeṣu aśanāya ādimatsu nanu avyākṛtam uktam ucyate avyākṛtam vyākurvan praviṣṭa doṣaḥ parasya avyākṛta jagat tvena vivakṣita ākṣipta niyantṛ kartṛ kriyā nimittam jagat avyākṛtam avocāma idaṃśabda sāmānā adhikaraṇyāt avyākṛta śabdasya jagat niyantra ādi aneka kāraka nimitta ādi viśeṣavat aparityakta anyatama viśeṣavat avyākṛtam vyākṛta avyākṛta mātram viśeṣaḥ vivakṣātaḥ śabda prayogaḥ grāma āgataḥ grāmaḥ śūnya kadācid grāma nivāsa mātra vivakṣāyām grāmaḥ śūnya śabda prayogaḥ kadācid nivāsi jana vivakṣāyām grāma āgata kadācid ubhaya vivakṣāyām grāma śabda prayogaḥ grāmam praviśet tadvat jagat avyākṛtam abheda vivakṣāyām ātmānātmanoḥ vyapadeśaḥ jagat utpatti vināśa ātmakam kevala jaga t vayapadeśaḥ asthūlaḥ anaṇuḥ ityādi kevala vyapadeśaḥ nanu vyākartrā vyāptam jagat parikalpyate apraviṣṭaḥ paricchinnena praveṣṭum śakyate puruṣeṇa grāma ādiḥ ākāśena nitya praviṣṭa pāṣāṇa sarpa ādivat stha upajāyate praviṣṭa upacaryate pāṣāṇe sahajaḥ antaḥsthaḥ sarpaḥ nālikere toyam anuprāviśat sraṣṭā bhāva anāpanna kāryam prāviśat śrūyate bhuktvā bhujigami kriyayoḥ apara kālayoḥ itaretara vicchedaḥ aviśiṣṭaḥ tadvat sthasya bhāva antara upajanana sthāna viyujya sthāna antara saṃyoga lakṣaṇaḥ praveśaḥ niravayavasya aparicchinnasya sāvayava praveśa śravaṇāt ṭha divyaḥ amūrtaḥ niṣkalam niṣkriyam ityādi śrutibhyaḥ vyapadeśya viśeṣa pratiṣedha śrutibhyaḥ pratibimba praveśavat vastu viprakarṣa anupapatteḥ dravye guṇa praveśavat anāśrita nitya paratantrasya āśritasya guṇasya dravye praveśa upacaryate svātantrya śravaṇāt praveśa upapadyate phale bījavat avayavatva vṛddhi kṣaya utpatti vināśa ādi dharmavattva prasaṅgāt dharmavat ityādi śruti nyāya virodhāt anya saṃsārī paricchinna praviṣṭa daivatā ārabhya ṭanāma vyākaravāṇi praveśa vyākaraṇa kartṛtva atat anuprāviśat asa sīmānam vidārya dvārā prāpadyata asarvāṇi vicitya abhivadan kumāra kumārī jīrṇaḥ daṇḍena vañcasi ta mantra varṇān parādanyasya praveśaḥ praviṣṭānām itaretara bhedāt parān ekatvam
