duḥkhi ādi darśanāt duḥkhena bāhyaḥ ādi virodhāt ayuktam upādhi āśraya janita viśeṣa viṣaya prakṣa ādeḥ vijñāta āram avijñātam ityādi śrutibhyaḥ viṣayam buddhi ādi upādhi praticchāyā viṣayam sukhitaḥ duḥkhitaḥ evamādi viṣayeṇa viṣayiṇaḥ sāmāna adhikaraṇya upacārāt draṣṭrṛ anya pratiṣedhāt deha avayava viśeṣya sukha duḥkhayoḥ viṣaya arthaḥ aśruteḥ yukta avidyā viṣaya arthatva abhyupagamāt kiñcana mohaḥ śokaḥ anupaśyataḥ ityādinā viṣaye pratiṣedhāt tārkika samaya virodhāt ayuktam yuktyā duḥkhitvā anupapatteḥ duḥkhena viṣayeṇa viśeṣya aviṣaya śabda guṇavat tvavat duḥkhi pratyaya viṣayatva anupapatteḥ sukha grāhakeṇa viṣayeṇa pratyayena nitya anumeyasya viṣayīkaraṇām upapadyate viṣayīkaraṇe ātmana viṣayya bhāva prasaṅgaḥ ekasya viṣaya viṣayi dīpavat yuga sambhavātātmani aṃśa anupapatteḥ vijñānasya grāhya grāhaka pratyuktam anumāna viṣayayoḥ duḥkha ātmanoḥ guṇa guṇi tve anumānam duḥkhasya nityam viṣaya ādi sāmāna adhikaraṇyāt saṃyoga ja tve duḥkhasya sāvayavatva vikriyāvattva anityatva prasaṅgāt avikṛtya saṃyogi dravyam guṇaḥ upayannapayan kvacid niravayavam vikriyamāṇam kvacid anitya guṇa āśrayam nityam āgama vādibhiḥ nityatayā abhyupagamyate dṛṣṭāntaḥ vikriyamāṇam pratyaya anivṛtteḥ nityam dravyasya avayavān yathātva vyatirekeṇa vikriyā anupapatteḥ sāvayava tve nitya avayavasya avayava saṃyoga pūrvaka tve sati vibhāga upapatteḥ vajra ādiṣu adarśanāt anumeya saṃyoga duḥkha ādi nitya guṇa āśrayatva upapattiḥ parasya aduḥkhi tve anyasya duḥkhinaḥ abhāve duḥkha upaśamanāya śāstra ārambhānarthakyam avidyā adhyāropita duḥkhitva bhrama apoha artha prakṛta saṅkhyā pūraṇa bhrama apohavat kalpita duḥkhya abhyupagamāt jala ādi pratibimbavat gra va īśaḥ pratibimbavat vyākṛte kārya upalabhya prāk utpatteḥ anupalabdha kārye sṛṣṭa vyākṛte buddheḥ upalabhyamānaḥ ādi pratibimbavat jala ādau kāryam praviṣṭa lakṣyamāṇaḥ nirdiśyate anuprāviśata sīmānam vidārya dvārā prāpadyata jīvena evamādibhiḥ gatasya niravayavasya deśa kāla antara apakramaṇa prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ praveśaḥ kadācid upapadyate parāda ityādi avocāma upalabdhi artha sṛṣṭi praveśa apyaya vākyānām upalabdheḥ arthatva śravaṇāt bahma ciram ityādi śrutibhyaḥ tattvataḥ jñātvā viśate prāpyate ityādi smṛtibhyaḥ bheda darśana apavādāt sṛṣṭi ādi vākyānām ekatva darśana artha paratva upapattiḥ kārya sthasya upalabhya praveśa upacaryate ānakha agra maryādam caitanyam upalabhyate ādhāne dhīyate dhānam āpita upaskara ādhāne antaḥstha upalabhyate praveśitaḥ viśvasya bharaṇāt nīḍe kāṣṭhāda ahitaḥ anuvartate mathyamāna upalabhyate dhāna deśe avasthitaḥ kāṣṭha ādau vyāpya avasthitaḥ sāmānyatas viśeṣataḥ deham saṃvyāpya avasthita prāṇana ādi kriyāvān darśana ādi kriyāvān upalabhyate praviṣṭham prāṇana ādi kriyā viśiṣṭam upalabhante nanu aprāpta pratiṣedhaḥ darśanasya aprakṛta doṣaḥ sṛṣṭi ādi vākyānām ekatva pratipatti artha prakṛtam darśanam cakṣaṇāya mantra varṇāt prāṇana ādi kriyā viśiṣṭasya adarśane hetum asamastaḥ prāṇana ādi kriyā viśiṣṭaḥ akṛtsna ucyate prāṇana kriyām kurvan samākhyaḥ abhidhānaḥ prāṇana kriyā kartṛ prāṇatī ucyate kriyām kurvan lāvakaḥ pācaka kriyā antara viśiṣṭasya anupasaṃhārāt vadana kriyām kurvan vakti caṣṭa ābhyām kriyāśakti udbhavaḥ pradarśitaḥ ābhyām śakti udbhavaḥ pradarśyate viṣaya śakteḥ cakṣuṣī vijñānasya sādhane sādhanam vyatiriktam vijñeyam upalambhe karaṇam kriyā sādhyā samavāyinī āśrayāyā abhivyaktaḥ vākkaraṇam pāṇi pāda pāyu upaśtha ākhyāni upalakṣaṇa arthā manuta jñāna śakti vikāsānām karaṇam mana ucyate ādīn i jāni vastu mātra viṣayāṇi kṛtsnā ātmavastu avadyotakāni prāṇana ādi kriyayā kriyā janita ādi vyākriyamāṇaḥ avadyotyamānaḥ prāṇana ādi kriyā samudāyāt viśiṣṭam anupasaṃhṛta itara viśiṣṭa kriyā ātmakam cintayati nasa asamāptaḥ prāṇana ādi samudāyāt pravibhakta viśeṣaṇena viśiṣṭa itara antara anupasaṃhārāt śṛṇomi spṛśāmi svabhāva pravṛtti viśiṣṭam kṛtsnam ādīni viśeṣaṇāni uktāni āpnuvan ucyate viśeṣola saṃhārī sankṛtsnaḥ vastu mātra ādi upādhi viśeṣa kriyā janitāni viśeṣaṇāni vyāpnoti vastu gṛhyamāṇaḥ āśaṅkya nirupādhika jala pratibimba bhedā ādi tve ādi upādhi viśeṣāḥ ādikarma janāma abhidheyā yadyā uktā abhinnatām apūrva vidhiḥ pakṣe prāpta katama evamādi pratipādana parābhiḥ śrutibhiḥ viṣayam utpāditam svarūpa viṣayān abhimāna buddhiḥ kāraka ādi kriyā phala adhyāropaṇa ātmikā avidyā nivartitā nivartitāyām ādi doṣa anupapatteḥ āna cintā anupapattiḥ upāsanam pakṣe vidhātavyam prāpta tiṣṭhasu pākṣikya upāsana prāptiḥ nityā apūrva vidhiḥ jñāna upāsanayoḥ ekatve prāpta prastutya abhidhānāt upāsana śabdayoḥ ekārtha avagamyate t ityādi śrutibhyaḥ upāsanam aprāpta vidhi arha svarūpa anvākhyāne pravṛttiḥ upapadyate apūrva vidhiḥ vidhi sāmānyāt yajeta ityādayaḥ vidhayaḥ taiḥ ādi upāsana vidheḥ viśeṣaḥ avagamyate mānasa kriyā vijñānasya yasyai haviḥ dhyāyet vaṣaṭkariṣyan ityādyā mānasī kriyā vidhīyate ityādyā kriyā vidhīyate jñāna ātmikā avocāma upāsana śabdayoḥ ekārtha bhāvāna aṃśa traya upapatteḥ yajeta bhāvanāyām bhāvya ādi ākāṅkṣa apanaya kāraṇam aṃśa avagamyate bhāvanāyām vidhīyamānāyām ākāṅkṣāyām tyāga brahmacarya śama dama uparama titikṣā ādi kartavya saṃyuktaḥ ityādīśāstreṇa samarthyate aśa kṛtsnasya darśa pūrṇamāsa ādi prakaraṇasya darśa pūrṇamāsa ādi vidhi uddeśa tvena upayogaḥ aupaniṣadām upāsana prakaraṇasya upāsana prakaraṇasya upāsana vidhi uddeśa tvena upayogaḥ asthūlam advitīyam aśanāya ādi atītaḥ evamādi vākyānām upāsyātma svarūpa viśeṣa samarpaṇena upayogaḥṣa phalam mokṣaḥ avidyā nivṛttiḥ varṇayanti upāsanena viṣayam viśiṣṭam bhāvayet jñāyate avidyā nivartakam viṣayam vākya janitam arthe vacanāni anveṣṭavyaḥ vijijñāsitavyaḥ ityādīni artha antara abhāvāt apūrva vidhiḥ svarūpa kathanān pratiṣedha vākya janita vyatirekeṇa mānasasya bāhyasya abhāvāt vidheḥ sāphalyam vidhi vākya śravaṇa mātra janita vyatirekeṇa pravṛttiḥ gamyate darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām svarga yajeta evamādau darśa pūrṇamāsa vidhi vākya janita darśa uṣṭhānam adhikāra ādi apekṣā anubhāvi ādi pratipādaka vākya janita vyatirekeṇa darśa pūrṇamāsa ādivat vyāpāraḥ vyāpāra upaśama hetu vākya janita vijñānasya udāsīna pravṛtti abrahma anātma nivartaka advitīyam evamādi vākyānām nivṛttau pravṛttiḥ upapadyate virodhāt vākya janita mātra abrahma anātma nivṛttiḥ tattvam advitīyam draṣṭaḥ viddhi ityādi vākyānām vādi draṣṭavya vidheḥ viṣaya samarpakāṇi artha antara abhāvāt uttaratvāt vastu svarūpa samarpakaiḥ vākyaiḥ ityādibhiḥ śravaṇa kāla darśanasya kṛta draṣṭavya vidheḥ anuṣṭhāna kartavyam uttaram svarūpa anvākhyāna mātreṇa vidhim pravartata vādi vākya vijñānasya janita bhaḥ kṛtasya karaṇam śravaṇe pravartata anavasthā prasaṅgāt vādi vākya artha śravaṇe vidhim pravartate vidhi vākya artha śravaṇe vidhim pravartiṣyata vidhi antara apekṣā artha śravaṇe anavasthā prasajyeta vākya janita jñāna smṛti saṃtateḥ śravaṇa mātrāt artha antara artha prāpta pratipādaka vākya śravaṇāt viṣayam utpadyate unpadya gānam viṣayam utpadyate unpadya gānam viṣayam mithyājñānam nivartayat utpadyate viṣaya mithyā jñāna nivṛttau prabhavāḥ smṛtayaḥ svābhāvikyaḥ anātma vastu bheda viṣayāḥ anarthatva avagateḥ avagatau satyām vastu anartha tvena ām agamyate anitya duḥkha aśuddhi ādi doṣavat vastunaḥ vilakṣaṇa anātma smṛtīnām avagateḥ abhāva prāptiḥ pāriśeṣyāt ekatva smṛti santateḥ arthata bhāvān vidheya bhaya āyāsa ādi duḥkha doṣa nivartaka smṛteḥ viparīta jñāna prabhavaḥ ādi doṣaḥ mohaḥ vidvāṃma kutaścana praptaḥ bhidyate hṛdaya granthiḥ ityādi śrutayaḥ nirodhaḥ artha citta vṛtti nirodhasya vākya janita artha antara tantra antareṣu kartavya avagata vidheya mokṣa sādhana tvena anavagamāt vedānteṣu artha sādhana tvena ām agamyate ciram evamādi śruti śatebhyaḥ ananya sādhana nirodhasya smṛti santāna vyatirekeṇa citta vṛtti nirodhasya sādhanam abhyupagamya it am uktam vyatirekeṇa mokṣa sādhanam avagamyate ākāṅkṣā bhāvāt bhāvanā bhāvaḥ uktam yajeta ādau bhāvanā kāṅkṣāyām phala sādhana kartavyatābhiḥ ākāṅkṣa apanayanam tadvat vidhau upapadyata advitīyam ityādi vākya artha sama ākāṅkṣā vinivṛtteḥ vākya artha vidhi prayuktaḥ pravartate vidhi antara prayuktau anavasthā doṣam avocāma advitīyam ityādi vākyeṣu vidhiḥ avagamyate svarūpa anvākhyānena avasita vastu svarūpa anvākhyāna mātra aprāmāṇyam arodīdyat ara udīt rudrasya rudra evamādau vastu svarūpa anvākhyāna mātra aprāmāṇyam artha vākyānām viśeṣāt vākyasya vastu anvākhyānam kriyā anvākhyānam prāmāṇya aprāmāṇya kāraṇam niścita phalavat utpādaka pramāṇam vākyam apramāṇam kiṃñca bhaḥ pṛcchāmaḥ svarūpa anvākhyāna pareṣu vākyeṣu phalavat niścitam utpadyate utpadyate aprāmāṇyam paśyasi avidyā bhaya ādi saṃsāra bīja doṣa nivṛttim phalam śṛṇopi mohaḥ anupaśyataḥ mantra bhagayaḥ śocāmi śokasya pāram śocāmi tārayatu evamādi vākya śatāni arodīt ādiṣu niścitam phalavat aprāmāṇyam aprāmāṇye phalavat niścita utpādakasya aprāmāṇyam aprāmāṇye ta darśa pūrṇamāsa ādi vākyeṣu viśrambhaḥ nanu darśa pūrṇamāsa ādi vākyānām pravṛtti utpādaka prāmāṇyam vākyeṣu doṣaḥ prāmāṇaya kāraṇa upapatteḥ prāmāṇya kāraṇam uktam alaṅkāraḥ pravṛtti bīja virodha phalavat avijñāna utpādaka pratipādaka vākyānām aprāmāṇya kāraṇam uktam ityādi vacanānām vākya artha vyatirekeṇa upāsana artha kintu apūrva vidhi artha pakṣe prāptasya niyama artha upāsanasya pakṣa prāptiḥ yāvatā pāriśeṣyāt smṛti santatiḥ nityā abhihitam bāḍham ārambhā niyata phala samyak jñāna prāptau avaśyambhāvinī pravṛttiḥ kāyānām labdha vṛtteḥ balīyaḥ mukteṣu ādi pravṛttivat pakṣe prāptam jñāna pravṛtti daurbalyam tyāga vairāgya ādi sādhana bala avalambena smṛti santatiḥ niyantavyā apūrvā kartavyā prāpta avecāma prāpta smṛti santāna niyama vidhi arthāni ityādi vākyāni anya artha asambhavāt nanu anātma upāsanam śabda prayogāt ādau ādi guṇā upāsyāḥ ādi guṇavat ādi upāsyam śabda prayogāt guṇavat ana vastu upāsyam gamyate upāsyatva vākya vailakṣaṇyāt vākye upāsya tvena abhipretaḥ dvitīya aśravaṇāt dvitīyā śrūyate ātmeni upāsya guṇaḥ anya avagamyate vākī aśeṣa ātmana upāsya tvena avagamāt vākyasya śeṣe upāsya tvena avagamyate praviṣṭasya darśana pratiṣedhāt anupāsya praveśa uktaḥ darśanam vāryate prakṛta upādānāt anupāsya it akṛt snatva doṣāt darśana pratiṣedhaḥ akṛtsnatva doṣa abhiprāyeṇa upāsya tvaṃpratiṣedhāya prāṇana ādi kriyā viśiṣṭa tvena viśeṣaṇāt upāsya anabhipetam prāṇana ādi ekaika kriyā viśiṣṭasya akṛtsnatva vacanam anarthakam ata anekaika viśiṣṭaḥ upāsya siddham śabdasya prayogaḥ śabda pratyayoḥ tattvasya paramārtha taḥ aviṣayatva jñāna anyathā avakṣyat arthāt śabda pratyayau anujñātau syātām aniṣṭam arekena avijñātam nivartante aprāpya ityādi śrutibhyaḥ anātma upāsana prasaṅga nivṛtti vākya anirjñātatva sāmānyāt jñātavyaḥ anātmā upāsane yatna āsthīyate itara ucyate prakṛtam gamanīyam nirdhāraṇa arthā ṣaṣṭhī sarvasmin arthaḥ tattvam vijñātavyam jñātavya tve jñāna apekṣata jñānāt jñātena anātma samastam nanu anya jñānena jñāyata parihāram ādi granthena vakṣyāmaḥ ucyate gavā ādi khura aṅkitaḥ ucyate naṣṭam vivitsitam paśum anveṣamāṇaḥ labheta labdhe anulabhata arthaḥ nanu jñāte jñāyata jñāne prakṛte lābhaḥ aprakṛta ucyata jñāna lābhayoḥ ekārtha vivakṣita alābhaḥ ajñānam jñānam lābhaḥ lābhavat aprāpta prāpti lakṣaṇa lābhaḥ labdhṛ labdha vyayarbheda abhāvāt anātmā labdhā labdhavyaḥ anātmā aprāpta utpādya ādi kriyā vyavahitaḥ kāraka viśeṣa upādānena kriyā viśeṣam utpādya labdhavyaḥ aprāpta prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ anityaḥ mithyājñāna janita kriyā prabhava putrādi lābhavat viparīta utpādya ādi kriyā vyavahitaḥ nitya labdha svarūpa tve mātram vyavadhānam gṛhyamāṇāyāḥ śuktikāyāḥ viparyayeṇa rajata ābhāsāyāḥ agrahaṇam viparīta jñāna vyavadhāna mātram grahaṇam jñāna mātram viparīta jñāna vyavadhāna apoha artha jñānasya alābhaḥ avidyā mātra vyavadhānam apohana mātram lābhaḥ kadācid upapadyate lābhe jñānāt artha antara sādhanasya ānarthakyam vakṣyāmaḥ nirāśaṅkam jñāna lābhayoḥ artha vivakṣan jñānam prakṛtya vindateḥ lābha artha guṇa phalam ucyate anupraveśena khyātim gata ityādi ādi saṃhatim prāptavān khyātim saṅghātam iṣṭaiḥ labhate uktam vastu mumukṣūṇām apekṣitam kīrti śabditam aikya jñānam phalam śloka śabditām muktim mukhyam phalam tattvam jñeyam anāhatyā tattvam priyataram prasiddhaḥ priyataram niratiśaya darśayati hiraṇya ādeḥ anyasya adyat tvena prasiddham arthaḥ tattvam priyataram ādi ucyate bāhyāt ādeḥ piṇḍa samudāyaḥ abhyantaraḥ sannikṛṣṭa antarāt tattvam niratiśaya prayatnena labdhavyaḥ laukika priyebhyaḥ priyatamaḥ lābhe yatna āsthena arthaḥ karttavyatā prāptam anya lābhe yatnam ujjhitvā ātmānātma priyayoḥ anyatara hānena itara upādāna prāptau upādānena itara hānam kriyate viparyayaḥ ucyate anātmamamamama viśeṣam ādikam priyataram brūvāṇam vādī abhimatam ādi lakṣaṇam āvaraṇam saṃrodham prāpsyati vinaṅkṣyati bravīti samarthaḥ paryāptaḥ vaktum uktam saṃrodham prāpsyati yathābhūta vādī vaktum īśvara kṣipra vācī kecid bhavet prasiddhiḥ ujjhitvā ya laukikam niścitya cintayati pramaraṇa śīlam nitya anuvāda mātram anyasya priyasya apriyasya abhāvāt grahaṇa stuti guṇa phala vidhāna manda darśinaḥ tāt śīlya pratyaya upādānāt sūtritā artha kṛtasnā sūtrasya vyācikhyāsuḥ prayojana abhidhitsayā upojjighāṃsati vakṣyamāṇam anantara vākye avadyotyam vastu brāhmaṇā vividiṣavaḥ janma jarā maraṇa prabandha cakra bhramaṇa kṛta āyāsa duḥkha udaka āpāra mahodadhi plava gurum āsādya tīram uttitīrṣavaḥ adharma sādhana phala lakṣaṇāt sādhya sādhana rūpān nirviṇṇāḥ vilakṣaṇa nitya niratiśaya pratipitsavaḥ paramātmā niravaśeṣam bhaviṣyāma manuṣyā grahaṇam viśeṣataḥ adhikāra jñāpana manuṣyā viśeṣataḥ abhyudaya niḥśreyasa sādhane adhikṛtā abhiprāyaḥ viṣaye phala prāptim dhruvām karmabhyaḥ vidyāyāḥ bhāva phala prāptim dhruvām prāmāṇyasya ubhayatra aviśeṣāt vipratiṣiddham vastu lakṣyate pṛcchāmaḥ manuṣyā avedyasmāt śrūyate avijñāya sādhya phalena tulyam anityatva prasaṅgaḥ bhāvasya phalasya anavasthā doṣaḥ catat sarevam avijñāya śāstra artha vairūpya doṣāt phala anityatva doṣaḥ doṣoḥ viśeṣa upapatteḥ pṛcchāmaḥ brahmāvet codite doṣān āgandhitam prativacanam brahmāparam bhāvasya sādhyatva upapatteḥ parasya bhāva āpattiḥ sādhyā sādhyān bhāva āpattiḥ sādhyā sādhyān bhāva āpattim atasmāt agra bhavitum adhikārāt bhāvī asarvam manuṣyā prakṛtāḥ abhyudaya niḥśreyasa sādhane viśeṣataḥ adhikāra uktam parasya aparasya dvaita ekatva apara sahitayā apara bhāvam upasampannaḥ bhojyāt apāvṛttaḥ prāptyā ucchinna bandhanaḥ bhāvī hetoḥ abhidhīyate bhāvinīm vṛttim āśritya śabda prayogaḥ aodanam pacati śāstre aparivrājakaḥ abhaya aityādi kecid bhāvī vyācakṣate bhāva āpatteḥ anityatva doṣāt paramārtha taḥ nimitta vaśāt bhāva āpadyate nimitta bhāva āpattiḥ nityā viruddham anitya tve phala tulya uktaḥ doṣaḥ avidyā kṛta asarvatva nivṛttim bhāva āpattim phalam manyase bhāvi kalpanā vyarthā prāk jantu nityam bhāva āpannaḥ paramārthataḥ abrahma asarva adhyāropitam śuktikāyām rajatam vyomni tala malavattva ādi brahmaṇi adhyoropitam abrahma asarva nivartyata manyase yuktam paramārtha ta śabdasya mukhya artha abrahma agra vākye ucyate vaktum artha vādi vedasya kalpanā yuktā śabda artha viparītaḥ bhāvī ucyata śruta hānya śruta kalpanāyā anyāyya mahattare prayojana antare asati avidyā kṛta vyatirekeṇa abrahma asarva vidyata apoha anupapatteḥ kvacid vastu apoḍhrī dṛṣṭā kartrī avidyāya aḥ sarvatra nivartikā dṛśyate abrahma asarva avidyā nivartyatām pāramārthikam vastu kartum nivartayitum vyarthā śruta hānya śruta kalpanā brahmaṇi avidyā anupapattiḥ brahmaṇi vidhānāt śuktikāyām rajata adhyāropaṇe asati śuktikā jñāpyate gocara āpannāyām śuktikā rajatam abrahma brahmaṇi ekatva vidhātavyam brahmaṇi avidyā adhyāropaṇāyām asatyām brūmaḥ śuktikāyām brahmaṇi atad adhyāropaṇā sva atad adhyāropanimittam avidyā kartṛ bhavatu avidyā kartṛ bhrāntam kiṃntu abrahma avidyā cetanaḥ bhrāntaḥ anya iṣyate ityādi śrutibhyaḥ smṛtibhyaḥ guḍākeśa śuni śvapāke ityādibhyaḥ mantra varṇāt nanu śāstra upadeśa ānarthakyam bāḍham avagate ānarthakyam avagamanarthakyam anavagama nivṛtteḥ dṛṣṭa nivṛtteḥ anupapattiḥ ekatva dṛṣṭa virodhāt dṛśyate ekatva anavagama nivṛttiḥ dṛśyamānam anupapannam bruvataḥ dṛṣṭa virodhaḥ dṛṣṭa virodhaḥ kenacid abhyupagamyate anupapannam dṛṣṭa darśana anupapattiḥ yuktiḥ evamādi śruti smṛti nyāyebhyaḥ parasmāt vilakṣaṇaḥ saṃsāri avagamyate vilakṣaṇaḥ aśanāyāt yatyeti ya vijaraḥ vimṛtyuḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ kaṇā akṣa pāda ādi tarka śāstreṣu saṃsāra vilakṣaṇa īśvara upapattitaḥ sādhyate saṃsāra duḥkha apanaya arthitva pravṛtti darśanāt sphuṭam anya īśvarāt saṃsāriṇaḥ avagamyate avākyanādaraḥ pārtha śrutibhyaḥ anveṣṭavyaḥ vijijñāsitavyaḥ gārgya praṇavaḥ lakṣyam ucyate ādi kartṛ nirdeśāt mumukṣoḥ gati mārga viśeṣa deśa upadeśāt asati bhede kutaḥ abhāve dakṣiṇa uttara mārga viśeṣa anupapattiḥ gantavya deśa anupapattiḥ bhinnasya parasmāt upapannam jñāna sādhana upadeśāt saṃsārī yuktaḥ pratyabhyudaya niḥśreyasādhanayoḥ jñānayoḥ upadeśaḥ īśvarasya yuktam bhāvī ucyata upadeśa anarthakya prasaṅgāt saṃsārī bhāvya saṃsārya bhāvasya phalasya siddha upadeśasya ānarthakyam prāptam vijñānasya kvacid artha sādhane aviniyāgāt saṃsāriṇa brahmatva sampādana artha upadeśa anirjñāte svarūpe sampādayet nirjñāta lakṣaṇe brahmaṇi śakyā sampad kartum cat ya prakṛtya sahasraśas śabdayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyāt artha avagamyate anyasya anya tve sampad kriyate ekatve prakṛtasya draṣṭavyasya ātmana darśayati brahmatva sampad upapattiḥ prayojanam upadeśasya gamyate āpatti śravaṇāt sampattiḥ tadāpattiḥ anyasyāmi abhāva upapadyate vacanāt sampatteḥ bhāva āpattiḥ sampatteḥ pratyaya mātra vijñānasya mithyājñāna nivartakatva vyatirekeṇa ākāraka avocāma vacanam vastunaḥ sāmarthya jñāpakam śāstram kārakam ityādi vākyeṣu parasya praveśa bhāvi kalpanā sādhvī iṣṭa artha bādhanāt dhanavat sarvasyām upaniṣadi pratipipādayiṣitor athaḥ kāṇḍa dvaye avadhāraṇāt avagamyate śākhā upaniṣatsu ekatva niścitor athaḥ saṃsārī anya aved kalpyeta iṣṭasya arthasya adhanam śāstram upakrama upasaṃhārayoḥ virodhāt asamañjasam kalpitam vyapadeśa anupapatteḥ saṃsārī kalpyeta vyapadeśaḥ aved saṃsāriṇa vedyatva upapatteḥ vedituḥ ucyata viśeṣaṇāt vedyaḥ viśeṣyeta viśeṣaṇāt aved avadhāraṇāt niścitam avagamyate sati upapannaḥ vyapadeśaḥ anyathā saṃsāri anyathā brahmatva abrahmatve ekasya upapanne paramārthataḥ prakāśau bhānoḥ viruddha ubhaya nimitta tve niścitaḥ vyapadeśaḥ yuktam tattva jñāna vivakṣāyām saṃśayaḥ niścitam jñānam artha sādhanam iṣyate ddhā saṃśaya vinaśyati śruti smṛtibhyām saṃśayitaḥ vākya arthaḥ vācyaḥ hita arthinā brahmaṇi sādhakatva kalpanā asmad ādiṣu apeśalā atadātmānam śāstra upālambhāt kalpanā śāstra śāstrasya upālambhaḥ brahmaṇa cikīrṣuṇā śāstra viparīta kalpanā sva artha parityāgaḥ kāryaḥ etāvatī akṣamā yuktā brahmaṇi kalpitam kiñcana advitīyam ityādi vākya śatebhyaḥ vyavahāraḥ brahmaṇi kalpitaḥ arthaḥ atyalpam ucyate aiyam kalpanā apeśalā praviṣṭam sraṣṭrṛ vaiśabdaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ stham pratibodhāt kintva pratibodhāt abrahma asarvam adhyāropāt akartā kriyāvān bhoktā sukhī duḥkhaḥ saṃsārī adhyāropayati paramārthataḥ vilakṣaṇam kathañcid ācāryeṇa dayālunā pratibodhitam anāsi saṃsārī aitya avetsvābhāvikam avidyā adhyāropita viśeṣa varjitam śabdasya arthaḥ svābhāvikaḥ viditavat nanu smarasya darśitaḥ ya praviśya prāṇityapān vyāniti udān samāniti nanu aasau vyapadiśyate bhavatā pratyakṣam darśayasi nanu darśana ādi kriyā kartuḥ svarūpam pratyakṣam darśayasi gamiḥ gantuḥ svarūpam chidiḥ chettuḥ nanu viśeṣaḥ draṣṭari dṛṣṭardraṣṭā ghaṭasya sarvathā draṣṭavya viśeṣam ghaṭasya viśeṣa upapatteḥ viśeṣaḥ dṛṣṭim kadācid dṛṣṭiḥ dṛśyate dṛṣṭyā nityayā bhavitavyam anityā dṛṣṭiḥ dṛśyā dṛṣṭiḥ kadācid dṛśyeta anityayā dṛṣṭyā ghaṭa ādi vastu tadvat kadācid dṛṣṭim dṛṣṭī nityā adṛśyā anyā anityā dṛśyā bāḍham prasiddhā anityā dṛṣṭiḥ andha anandhatva darśanāt nityā anandha draṣṭaḥ nityā dṛṣṭiḥ anumānāt andhasya ghaṭa ādi ābhāsa viṣayā dṛṣṭiḥ upalabhyate itara dṛṣṭi nāśe dṛṣṭiḥ avipariluptayā nityayā dṛṣṭyā svarūpa bhūtayā svayan samākhyathetām anityām dṛṣṭim vuddha antayoḥ vāsanā pratyaya rūpām nityam evaḥ sati dṛṣṭiḥ svarūpam auṣṇyavat kāṇādānām dṛṣṭi vyatiriktaḥ cetanaḥ nitya dṛś adhyāropita anitya dṛṣṭi ādi varjitam avedviditavat nanu vipratiṣiddham vijñātevijñātāram vipratiṣedhaḥ vijñāyata anya jñāna anapekṣa nitya dṛṣṭiḥ draṣṭri viṣayām dṛṣṭim ākāṅkṣate nivartate draṣṭu viṣaya dṛṣṭi ākāṅkṣā asambhavāt avidyamāne viṣaya ākāṅkṣā kasyacid upajāyate dṛśyā dṛṣṭiḥ viṣayīkartum utsahate ākāṅkṣeta sva viṣaya ākhāṅkṣāsu ajñāna adhyāropaṇa nivṛttiḥ aatmānam uktamna viṣayīkaraṇam bhavāmi antara aśanāya ādi atītaḥ asthūla manaṇu evamādi lakṣaṇam saṃsārī yuktam manuṣyā bhaviṣyāma pṛṣṭam akimu aved nirṇītam abrahma agra avedaham madhye pratibuddhvā anātmānam uktena rpīṇām madhye ityādi dṛṣṭi apekṣayā brahmatva buddhyā ucyate apuraḥ sarvatra anupraviṣṭam ityādi ucyate paramārthataḥ agra pratibodhāt ādi īśvanī athā vibhāvyamānam vidyāyāḥ bhāva āpattiḥ phalam arthasya draḍhimne mantrān udāharati śrutiḥ aaham darśanāt ṛṣṭiḥ vāmadeva ākhyaḥ pratipannavān mantrān dadarśa aaham aityādīn parāmṛśyate aaham suryaḥ aityādinā bhāva āpattim phalam parāmṛśati bhāvam phalam pratipeda prayogāt sahāya sādhana sādhyam mokṣam darśayati bhuñjānaḥ tṛpyati yadvat bhāva āpattiḥ mahatām ādīnām vīrya atiśayāt ida ānīmaidaṃyugīnānām viśeṣataḥ alpa vīrya kasyacid buddhiḥ utthāpanāya prakṛtam anupraviṣṭam dṛṣṭi kriyā ādi vartamāna vyāvṛtta bāhya autsukya aaham apohya upādhi janita bhrānti adhyāropitān viśeṣān saṃsāra dharmānāgandhitam brahyeva kevalam avidyā kṛta asarvatva nivṛtteḥ braha avijhānāt vīryeṣu vāma ḍheva ādiṣu hīna vīryeṣu vārtamānikeṣu iṣu brahyaṇaḥ viśeṣaḥ vijhānasya vārtamānikeṣu puruṣeṣu bahya phale anaikāntika śaḍkyata ata brahya vijhātuḥ utkena vidhinā vīryāḥ abhūtatyaa bhavanāya brahyā āvasya paryāptāḥ brahya avidyā phala prāpyau vidhna karaṇe ādaya īśata śaḍkā ucyate ādīn ṛṇavat brahya caryeṇa ṛpibhyaḥ yajhena devabhyaḥ jāyamānam ṛṇavantam darśayati śrutiḥ paśu ni darśanāt athaḥ ityāt vṛtti paripipālayiṣayā adhamarṇānivam paratantrāt pratyamṛtatva prāptim vidhnam kuryuḥ nyāyyā śaḍkā sva sva śarīrāṇi rakṣanti mahattarām vṛttim adhīnām darśayṣyati ādīnām paśu samatayā ekaikasya depām manudhyā hahi brahya āviśve pārārthya nivṛtteḥ sva paśu tvañca ami prāyaḥ apriya ariṣṭi vacanābhyām avagamyate brahya avidaḥ brahya phalaṛprāpta kuryuḥ vidhnam prabhāvavantaḥ nanu sati anyāsu phala prāpti pudevānām vidhna karaṇaṃpeya pāna āvisrambhaḥ abhyudaya niḥśreyasa sādhanā nuṣṭhāneṣu īśvarasya acintaya śakti tvādvidhna karaṇe prabhu kāla mantra oṣadhi tapasām phala sampatti vipatti hetu śāstre prasidvam anāśvāsaḥ śāstra artha anuṣṭhāne padārthānām niyata nimitta upādānāt jagat vaicitrya darśanāt svabhāva pakṣe ubhaya anupapatteḥ asukha duḥkha ādi phala nimittam pakṣe sthite smṛti nyāya parigṛhīte īśvara kālāḥ phala viparyāsa kartāraḥ kāṅkṣita kāraka śubha aśubham puruṣāṇām kāla īśvara ādi kārakam anapekṣya labhate labdha ātmakam phala dāne asamartham kriyāyāḥ kāraka ādi aneka nimitta upādāna sva abhāvyāt kriyā anuguṇā deveśvara ādaya karmasu phala prāptim pratyavisrambhaḥ vaśa aniga kvacid sva sāmarthyasya apraṇodya kāla daiva dravya ādi svabhāvānām guṇa pradhāna bhāvaḥ aniyataḥ durvijñeyaḥ mohaḥ kārakam phala prāptau kecitaṃ kāla dravya ādi svabhāva kecit saṃhatā prādhānyam aṅgīkṛtya smṛti vādāḥ ityādayaḥ sva viṣaye kasyacid prādhānya udbhava itareṣām kālīna prādhānya śakti stambhaḥ phala prāptim pratyanaikāntika śāstra nyāya nirdhārita prādhānyasya apagama mātra prāpti phalasya uktam prāpti phalam vighnam kuryuḥ vighna karaṇe sāmarthyam kāla anantarita prāpti phalasya cakṣuṣa ālokena saṃyogaḥ kāla abhivyaktiḥ viṣayam kāla viṣaya jñāna tirobhāvaḥ satyām avidyā kārya anupapatteḥ pradīpa kāryasya vighnam kuryuḥ svarūpam dhyeyam śāstraiḥ vijñeyam sama avidyā mātra vyavadhāna apagamāt śuktikāyāḥ rajata ābhāsāyāḥ śuktikā avocāma pratikūla tve prayatnaḥ anātma phalam deśa kāla nimitta antaritam anātma viṣaye saphalaḥ prayatnaḥ vighna ācaraṇāya sama kāla bhūte deśa kāla nimitta antarite avasara anupapatteḥ pratyaya santatyabhāvāt viparīta pratyaya kāryayoḥ darśanāt antya pratyayaḥ avidyā nivartakaḥ prathamena anaikāntika viṣayaḥ pratyayaḥ nivartayati antyaḥ tulya viṣaya santatas avidyā nivartakaḥ vicchinna jīvana ādau sati santati anupapatteḥ jīvana ādi hetuke pratyaye sati pratyaya santatiḥ upapadyate virodhāt jīvana ādi pratyaya tiraskaraṇena āmaraṇa antāt āsantatiḥ pratyayeyattā samantānānavadhāraṇāt śāstra artha avadhāraṇa doṣāt iyatām pratyayānām santatiḥ avidyāyā nivartikā anavadhāraṇāt śāstra arthaḥ avadhriyeta aniṣṭam santati mātra tve avadhārita ādi antayoḥ aviśeṣāt prathamā pratyaya santatiḥ maraṇa kāla antā viśeṣa abhāvāt ādi antayoḥ pratyayoḥ uktau doṣau prasajyeyātām anivartaka bhidyate hṛdaya granthiḥ mohaḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ arthavāda śākhā pramita viṣaya parihāra avidyā bhaya ādi doṣa nivṛtteḥ uktaḥ parihāraḥ ādyaḥ antyaḥ santatas asantatas cetyacodyam avidyā ādi doṣa nivṛtti phala avasāna vidhāyāḥ ya avidyā ādi doṣa nivṛtti phala pratyaya ādyaḥ antyaḥ santatas asantatas abhyupagamāt codyasya avatāra gandhaḥ uktam viparīta pratyaya kāryayoḥ darśanāt śeṣa hetu ārabdham viparīta pratyaya doṣa nimitta tathābhūtasya viparīta pratyaya doṣa saṃyuktasya phala dāne sāvarthyam pātaḥ phala upabhoga viparīta pratyayam rāga ādi doṣam mātram ākṣipati mukta iṣuvat pravṛtta phala hetukasya nivartukā avirodhāt sva āśrayāt sva virodhya kāryam utpitsu niruṇāddhi anāgata atītam itarat viparīta pratyayaḥ vidyāvata utpadyate nirviṣaya anavadhṛta viṣaya viśeṣa svarūpam sāmānya mātram āśritya viparīta pratyaya utpadyamāna utpadyate śuktikāyām rajatam viṣaya viśeṣa avadhāraṇavataḥ aśeṣa viparīta pratyaya āśrayasya upamardita pūrvavat śuktikā ādau samyak pratyayāt pattau punagdarśanāt kvacid vidyāyāḥ utpanna viparīta pratyaya janita saṃskārebhyaḥ viparīta pratyaya avabhāsāḥ smṛtayaḥ jāyamānā viparīta pratyaya bhrāntim akasmāt vijñāta vibhāgasya akasmāt viparyaya vibhramaḥ samyak jñānavataḥ pūrvavat viparīta pratyaya utpadyate samyak jñāne avisrambhāt śāstra artha ādau pravṛttiḥ asamañjasā pramāṇam apramāṇam sampadyeta pramāṇa apramāṇayoḥ viśeṣa anupapatteḥ asamyak jñāna pāta abhāvaḥ parihṛtam jñāna utpatteḥ prāk kāla janma antara sañcitānām vināśaḥ siddhaḥ phala prāpti vighna niṣedha ciram pāpmānaḥ pradrūyante tarataḥ kṛta akṛte tapataḥ kutaścana ityādi śrutibhyaḥ jñāna bhasmasāt ityādi smṛtibhyaḥ ṛṇaiḥ pratibadhyata avidyāvat vipaya avidyāvān ṛṇī kartṛtva ādi upapatteḥ ayatra ananyat vastu ākhyam avidyāyām satyām anya divasyāt timira kṛta dvitīya candravat avidyā kṛta aneka kāraka apekṣam darśana ādi phalam darśayati ityādinā satyām avidyā kṛta anekatva bhrama prahāṇam asambhavam darśayati avidyāvat viṣaya ṛṇi sambhavāt nā itaratra uttaratra vyācikhyāsiṣyamāṇaiḥ vākyaiḥ vistareṇa pradarśayiṣyāmaḥ abrahma vyatiriktām kāñcid stuti namaskāra yāga bali upahāra praṇidhāna ādinā anātmā mattaḥ adhikṛtaḥ ṛṇivat pratikartavyam pratyayaḥ tattvam kevalam evaṃbhūtaḥ avidvān avidyā doṣavān gavādiḥ vāhana dohana ādi upakāraiḥ upabhujyate ijyā ādi aneka upakāraiḥ upabhoktavya ādīnām artheṣu karmasu adhikṛta arthaḥ aviduṣaḥ varṇa āśrama ādi pravibhāgavataḥ adhikṛtasya sahitasya kevalasya śāstra uktasya kāryam manuṣyatva ādikaḥ brahmānta utkarṣaḥ śāstra viparītasya svābhāvikasya kāryam manuṣyatva ādika sthāvara apakarṣaḥ ityādinā vakṣyāmaḥ kṛtsnena adhyāya śeṣeṇa vidyayāḥ kāryam bhāva āpattiḥ saṅkṣepataḥ darśitam sarvāhi avidyā vibhāga pradarśanena upakṣīṇā eṣor athaḥ kṛtsnasya śāstrasya pradarśayiṣyāmaḥ avidyāvantam īśata vighnam kartum anugraham darśayati gaḥ ādayaḥ svāminam adhiṣṭhātāram pālayeyuḥ paśu sthānīya avidvān ādi upalakṣaṇa pālayati ima ādayaḥ mattaḥ īśita āraḥ bhṛtya stuti namaskāra ijyā ādinā ārādhanam abhyudayam niḥśreyasam prattaṃphalam prāpsyāmi abhisandhiḥ paśumataḥ paśāvādīyamāne vyāghra ādinā apahiyamāṇe paśu sthānīya paśu bhāvāt vyuttiṣṭhati citram paśu haraṇa kuṭuṃbinaḥ tattvam kathañcana manuṣyā vijānīyuḥ smaraṇam anugītāsu bhagavataḥ vyāsasya kriyāvadbhiḥ kaunteya samāvṛtaḥ maryaiḥ vartanam vyāghra ādibhyaḥ vighnam ācikīrṣanti asmad upabhogya māvyuttiṣṭheyuḥ mumocayiṣanti ādibhiḥ yokṣyanti viparītam ādibhiḥ mumukṣuḥ ārādhana bhakti praṇaya apramādī prāptim ati kākva pradarśitam apriya vākyena sūtritaḥ śāsra arthaḥ vyāci khya asitasya sārtha vādena ityādinā sambandha prayojane abhihite avidyāyāḥ saṃsāra adhikāra kāraṇa uktam ityādinā avidvānṛṇī paśavat ādi kartavya paratantra uktam ādi karmavya tvenimittam varṇā āśramāḥ varṇāḥ ataidam ārabhyate nimitta sambaddheṣu paratantra adhikṛtaḥ saṃsārī arthasya pradarśanāya sarga ādi sargaḥ uktaḥ sargaḥ sṛṣṭi paripūraṇāya pradarśitaḥ ādi sargaḥ śeṣa āmidhīyate aviduṣaḥ adhikāra hetu pradarśanāya agra rūpāpannam brāhmaṇa jātyam i mānād abhidhīyate kṣatra ādit abhinnam kṣatra ādi bhedaḥ kṣatra ādi paripālayitra ādi śūnyam sadam vibhūtavat arthaḥ abrāhmaṇaḥ kartavyam brāhmaṇa jāti nimittam cikīrṣu kartṛtva vibhūtyai praśasta ati atiśayena sṛṣṭavat sṛṣṭam kṣatriya jātiḥ vyakti bhedena pradarśayati prasiddhāni jāti ākhyāyām pakṣe bahuvacana smaraṇāt vyakti bahutvāt bheda upacāreṇa bahuvacanam kāni abhipiktā viśeṣataḥ nirdiśyante yādasām ādīnām mṛtyu roga ādīnām bhāsām evamādīni iṣu tadanu ādi kṣatra adhiṣṭhitāni purūravaḥ prabhṛtīni draṣṭavyāni artha devakṣatra sargaḥ prastutaḥ atiśayena sṛṣṭam brāhmaṇa jāteḥ niyansṛ kāraṇa bhātaḥ kṣatriyasya vyavasthitaḥ uparisthitam kka kṣatra ātmīyam khyāti sthāpayati rājasūya abhiṣiktena āsandyām sthitena brahman ṛtvij abhidhīyate kṣatra prakṛtā yati rājasūya abhiṣeka guṇam brāhmaṇa jāti medha parisamāptau upanikṣayati āśrayati purohitam nidhatta arthaḥ bala abhimānāt brāhmaṇa jātim brāhmaṇam ya hiṃsati nyagbhāvena svāma ātmāyām prasavam vicchinatti vināśayati prasavam vicchinatti vināśayati taraḥ krūra prasava hiṃsayā sutarām praśastataram paribhūya taraḥ tadvat sṛṣṭe navī upārjayituḥ abhāvāt sādhana upārjanāya viṣ sva arthe niṣṭhā ya jāti bhedā arthaḥ gaṇam gaṇam kathyante gaṇa prāyā viśaḥ prāyeṇa saṃhatā upārjane samarthāḥ ekaikaśas saṅkhyaḥ viśvedeva asrayodaśa viśvāyā apatyāni gaṇāḥ paricāraka bhāvāt śūdra śaudraḥ sva arthe aṇi vṛddhiḥ śaudraḥ sṛṣṭaḥ puṇyati viśeṣataḥ nirdiśati pūpā nirvacanam caturaḥ varṇān aniyata āśaṅkayā sṛṣṭam niyantṛ ugrāt niyantṛ niyamyante ucyate athaḥ abalīyān durbala taraḥ balavattaram jetum balena balavattamena kuṭumbikaḥ siddham balavattara niyantṛ vyavahāra lakṣaṇaḥ laukikaiḥ vyavahriyamāṇaḥ astra artha anuṣṭhīyamānaḥ nāmā śāstra artha tvena jñāyamānaḥ yathāśāstram vyavahāra kāla samīpa sthā ubhaya viveka jñāḥ prasiddham laukikam nyāyam viparyayeṇa laukikam vyavahāram śāstrāt anapetam uktam jñāyamānam anuṣṭhīyamānam jñāna anuṣṭānalakṣaṇaḥ śāstra jñāna nitarān niyamayati abhimānaḥ avidvān viśeṣa anuṣṭhānāya kṣatra śūdra nimitta viśeṣam abhimanyate nisargata adhikāra nimittāni cāturvarṇyam sṛṣṭam śūdra uttara upasaṃhāraḥ sraṣṭṛ agninaivana brāhmaṇa jātiḥ brāhmaṇā brāhmaṇa svarūpeṇa itareṣu varṇeṣu vikāra ādi adhiṣṭhitaḥ kṣatra ādiṣu vikāra āpannam brāhmaṇa e avikṛtam sraṣṭṛ madhye phalam sambaddham arthaḥ adhikaraṇa tvena vyavasthitam phalam prārthayanta upapannam madhye phala icchāyām ādi nimitta kriyā apekṣā jāti mātra svarūpa pratilambhena artha siddhiḥ adhīnā artha siddhiḥ ādi sambaddha kriyā apekṣā smṛteḥ japyena saṃsidhyet saṃśayaḥ maitraḥ brāhmaṇa ucyate pārivrājya darśanāt brahmaṇatva phalam brāhmaṇa kartṛ adhi karaṇa sraṣṭṛ paramātma kecid avidyā adhikāre adhikāra varṇa vibhāgasya prastuta viśeṣaṇa at ya di ātmocyeta viśeṣaṇam anarthakam asvam adṛṣṭvā sva vyatiriktaḥ adhīna prārthyamānaḥ prakṛtaḥ yuktam viśeṣaṇam prakṛta nivṛtti artha sva tvena avyabhicārāt paramātma avidyā kṛtānām svatva vyabhicārāt bravīti kṛtānām vyabhicāram akṣīyata sṛṣṭā varṇāḥ ākhyam kartavya niyantṛ artha sādhanam va paramātma ākhyaḥ aviditaḥ prāpyate padanīya tvena kriyata ata pakṣa vinivṛtti arthaḥ saṃsāri kāmakarma hetukāt adhīna abhimāna brāhmaṇa jāti mātra abhimāna āgantukāt asvabhūtāt ākhyam tvena avyabhicāri adṛṣṭā aaham aviditaḥ vyavahitaḥ asva ajñātaḥ saṅkhyā pūraṇa laukika pālayati bhaya ādi doṣa apanayena ananuktaḥ anadhītaḥ ādi avabodhaka tvena laukikam kṛṣi ādi akṛtam sva anabhivyañjitam ātmīya phala pradānena nitya svarūpeṇa anabhivyañjitaḥ avidyā ādi prahāṇena nanu sva darśana nimitta paripālanena phala prāpti dhrauvyāt iṣṭa phala nimittasya bāhulyāt nimittam pālanam akṣayam bhaviṣyati kṛtasya kṣayavat saṃsāre adbhutavat mahātmā anevaṃvid uktena vidhinā avidvān ādi iṣṭa phalam nairantaryeṇa aanena ānantyam bhaviṣyati hāsya avidyāvataḥ avidyā janita hetu darśana vibhrama udbhūta vibhūtivat antataḥ phala upabhogasya kṣīyata kāraṇayoḥ avidyā kāmayoḥ cala kṛta kṣaya ghnauvya upapattiḥ phala pālana ānanti ata aātmānam asvam aityasmin arthe prakṛta sva śabdasya aprayogāt ya ucyate hāsya abhāvāt nitya anuvādaḥ viduṣaḥ kṣaya lakṣaṇam saṃsāra santatam evana vidyata arthaḥ mithilāyām pradīptāyām dahyati kiñcana yadvat sva upāsakasya viduṣaḥ saṃyogāt kṣīyata varṣayanti śabda samavāyinam dvidhā parikalpayanti vyākṛta avasthā āśrayaḥ hairaṇyagarbha ākhyaḥ samavāyinam paricchinnam ya paricchinnam ya paricchinna darśinaḥ samavāyinam avyākṛta avastham kāraṇa āpādya aparicchinna darśi aparicchinna darśi kṣīyata śobhanā kalpanā śrautī sva prakṛtasya paramātmanaḥ abhihita prastutya sva śabdam vihāya śabda prakṣepeṇa pratinirdeśāt samavāyi kalpanāyā anavasara kevala viṣayeṇa viśeṣaṇāt kariṣyāmaḥ ātmāyam ithi apara kṛtebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ viśinaṣṭi aayam hāsya kenacana mīyata taiḥ viśeṣaṇaiḥ vākyatā yuktā viśeṣaṇa darśanāt kāmayata ayuktam paramātmā upāsanāt sthite sṛjata ithi prāpti vyatirekeṇa phala vacanam ayuktam sva upāsana stuti paratvat svasmāt sampadyata arthaḥ anyadataḥ prārthanīyam ātmataḥ ātmataḥ ityādi śruti antare bhāva pradarśana arthaḥ pūrvavat sampadyate yuktaḥ śabda prayogaḥ svasmāt prakṛtāt arthaḥ anyathā aavyākṛta avasthāt viśeṣaṇam avakṣyāt prakṛta paramātma vyāvṛttaye vyākṛta avasthā vyāvṛttaye prakṛte viśeṣite aśru antarāla ava sthā pratipattum śakyate athaḥ avidvān varṇa āśrama ādi abhimānaḥ niyamyamānaḥ ādi kartavya paśuvat paratantra uktam kāni kartavya paśuvat paratantraḥ ādayaḥ paśuvat upakaroti prapañcayati athaḥ vākya upanyāsa arthaḥ prakṛtaḥ gṛhī adhikṛtaḥ avidvān indriya saṅghāta ādi viśiṣṭaḥ piṇḍa ucyate varṇa āśrama ādi vihitaiḥ upakāri kaiḥ viśeṣaiḥ upakurvan keṣāṃ viśeṣāṇām ucyate gṛhī yāgaḥ uddiśya svatva parityāgaḥ parityāgaḥ āsecana adhikaḥ homaḥ homa yāga lakṣaṇena vaśya kartavya tvena paśuvat paratantra tvena pratibaddha svādhyāyam adhīte ahara hastena piṇḍa udaka ādi icchati udyamam icchā utpatti upalakṣaṇa arthā utpādayati arthaḥ vaśya kartavya tvena pitṛṇām bhogya tvena paratantraḥ vasadbhyaḥ avasadbhyaḥ arthibhyaḥ lambhayati ya dasya śvāpadā pipīlikābhiḥ kaṇa bali bhāṇḍa kṣālana ādi kurvan upakaroti ādibhyaḥ svāpya svasmai dehāya ariṣṭam avināśam svatva bhāva apracyutim svatva bhāva pracyuti bhayāt poṣaṇa rakṣaṇa ādibhiḥ paripālayet asarva bhogyaḥ prakāreṇa avaśyam ṛṇivat pratikartavyam parikalpitavate ādīni uktāni avināśam svatva apracyutyai saṃrakṣanti kuṭumbina uktam uktānām ṛṇavat avaśya kartavya mahāyajña prakaraṇe kartavya vicāritam avadāna prakaraṇe paśu bhāvāt kartavya bandhana rūpāt pratimucyate kāritaḥ vandhana adhikāre avaśa pravartate vimokṣṇa upāye adhikāra nanu uktam rakṣanti bāḍham adhikāra sva gocara ārūḍhān rakṣanti anyathā akṛta abhyāgama kṛta nāśa prasaṅgāt sāmānyam mātram viśiṣṭa adhikārān ārūḍham bhavitavyam preritaḥ avaśa bahirmukhaḥ svasmāt nanu avidyāsā avidyāvānihi bahirmukhībhūtaḥ pravartate pravartikā vastu svarūpāvarṇa ātmikā pravartaka bīja andha garta ādi patana pravṛtti hetuḥ ucyatām pravṛtti hetuḥ abhidhīyate asvābhāvikyām avidyāyām vartamānā bālāḥ parācaḥ anuyanti kāṭhaka śrutau smṛtau ityādi mānave pravṛttiḥ hetukī eṣor athaḥ vistaraḥ pradarśyata adhyāya parisamāpteḥ agra svābhāvikaḥ avidvān kārya karaṇa saṅghāta lakṣaṇaḥ varṇī dāra sambandhātātmā abhidhīyate kāmyamānam ādi bheda ādi bīja bhūtāḥ vidyāvān svābhāvikyā sva kartṛ ādi kāraka kriyā phala ātmaka dhyāra upalakṣaṇayā avidyā vāsanayā vāsitaḥ kāmitavān adhikāra hetu bhūtā kartuḥ vinā anadhikṛta karmaṇi adhikāra sampattaye bhavet utpadyeya sādhanam gavā ādi lakṣaṇam abhyudaya niḥśreyasa sādhanam anṛṇī ādīnām kāmyāni svarga ādi sādhanāni viṣaya paricchinna arthaḥ kāmayitavyaḥ viṣayaḥ sādhana lakṣaṇa phala bhūtāḥ sādhana ekaiva satyeṣaṇā sādhana apekṣā dvidhā avadhārayiṣyati phala artha ārambhasya eṣaṇa artha prāptā uktā avadhriyate bhojane abhihite tṛptiḥ abhidheyā artha bhojanasya sādhya sādhana lakṣaṇe prayuktaḥ avidvān avaśa kośakāravat veṣṭayati mārga praṇidadhat bahirmukhībhūtaḥ pratijānāti taittirīyake agnimugdhaḥ dhūma tāntaḥ pratijānāti avadhāryate kāmānām anantā āśaṅkya hetum phala sādhana lakṣaṇāt adhikāram labheta phala sādhana vyatiriktam adṛṣṭam labdhavyam labdhavyaviṣayaḥ vyatirekeṇa abhāvāt yuktam vaktum aetāvān uktam dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa artha sādhya sādhana lakṣaṇam avidyāvat adhikāra viṣayam dvayam viduṣā vyutthātavyam avidvān kāmayāmāsa pūrvataraḥ sargam prayukta ekākyaramamāṇaḥ upaghātāya sargaḥ uktam sṛṣṭau kāla dāra kriyātaḥ vākyam sampādayan ādīn uktānām ādīnām asampūrṇaḥ pāriśeṣyāt samastān sampādayati śaknoti sampādayitum kṛtsnatva sampādanāya ākṛtsna abhimāninaḥ kārya karaṇa saṅghātaḥ pravibhajyate anuvṛtti itarat kārya karaṇa jñātam pradhānatva ādīnām kuṭumba anukāri jāya ādi catuṣṭi mana parikalpate anuvṛttitva sāmānyāt codana ādi lakṣaṇaḥ dvāreṇa avadhāryate prasṛjyate manasābhyām pati sthānīyābhyām prasūyate ceṣṭā ādi lakṣaṇam dvividham itarat viśinaṣṭi itara nivṛtti artha gavā ādi sambandhi grāhyam sādhanam sthānīyam sambandhāt grāhyam gavā ādi upalabhata arthaḥ itarat viṣaya vijñānasya sampatti viṣayam ādi antaiḥ nirvartya ucyate ucyate sthānīyaḥ hetu hetu śarīreṇa ākṛt snatva abhimānina sampannā bāhyā ādi lakṣaṇā pañcabhiḥ nirvṛttaḥ darśana mātra nirvṛttaḥ akarmiṇaḥ pañcatva sampatti mātreṇa yajña ucyate bāhyaḥ paśu sādhyaḥ pāṅkta manaa ādi pañcatva yogāt paśu garva ādiḥ paśu tve adhikṛta tvena viśeṣaḥ grahaṇam bahunā sādhanam phalam sampādayat jagat tvena ya adhyāye sṛṣṭi ādi brāhmaṇam avidyā prastutā avidvān aanyaḥ varṇa āśrama abhimānaḥ kartavya niyataḥ ādi prayuktaḥ ādīnām upakurvan uktam sva ekena bhūtaiḥ bhojya tvena sṛṣṭaḥ ādi pāṅkta jagat bhojya tvena asṛjat sva ānurūpyeṇa jagataḥ bhoktā bhojyam kāryam arthaḥ prakaraṇe madhuvidyāyām vakṣyāmaḥ asarvam kāryam aitya ekatva ityādinā pāṅktena kāmyena bhojya tvena jagat jagat saptadhā pravibhajyamānam kārya kāraṇa tvena bhojyatva at annānām annānām viniyogānām sūtra bhūtāḥ saṅkṣepataḥ prakāśaka mantrāḥ kriyā viśeṣaṇam prajñayā jñāna medhā śabda vācye prakṛta nā medhā tapasī aprakaraṇāt ādi sādhanam aya jñānam prakṛtam prasiddhayoḥ medhā tapasoḥ kārya jñāna karmabhyām janitavān prakāśayiṣyāma vākya śeṣaḥ mantrāṇām arthaḥ rohita tvātt prāyeṇa durvijñeyaḥ artha vyākhyānāya brāhmaṇam pravartate ayat ajana aityasya kor ucyate ithi vyācaṣṭe prasiddha artha avadyotakena prasiddhaḥ mantrasya artha arthaḥ anuvāda svarūpeṇa mantreṇa prasiddha artha prakāśitā brāhmaṇam aviśaṅkyā amedhayā ajana nanu prasiddhātāsya arthasya ucyate ādi karmāntānām phala sādhanānām pratyakṣam abhihitam ajāyā aityādinā phala sādhanam sraṣṭṛ abhihitam vakṣyamāṇam prasiddham yuktam vaktum ityādi phala viṣayā prasiddhā ādi uktam aetāvān viṣaye anupapatteḥ āśāstrīya tapobhyām svābhāvikābhyām jagatsraṣṭṛ uktam sthāvara antasya aniṣṭa phalasya nimitta vivakṣitaḥ śāstrīya sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ vidhitsayā vairāgyasya vivakṣita am vyakta avyakta lakṣaṇaḥ saṃsāraḥ asuddhaḥ anityaḥ sādhya sādhana duḥkhaḥ avidyā viṣaya viraktasya ārabdhavyā annānām vibhāgena viniyoga ucyate aekam sādhāraṇma mantra vyākhyānam aidam tasma ādhāraṇam uttkam bhottkṛsamudāyasya bhujyate prāṇibhiḥ ahani ahani tasma ādhāraṇam bhoktṛ akalpayat ya karam bhujyamānam arthaḥ upāsanam tātparya agurum arājānam aitya ādau arthat upabhoga pradhāna ūna adṛṣṭa artha pradhāna arthaḥ bhūtaḥ adharma dvaya āvartate vimucyata mantra mogham annaṃvindate ityādiḥ smṛtiḥ artha pācayet apradāya bhūṅkte stena āde mārṣṭi ityādiḥ etasmarseṣām apravibhaktam prāṇibhiḥ bhujyate bhojyat pāt mukhe prakṣipyamāṇaḥ grāsaḥ parasya pīḍā karaḥ dṛśyate amama prativadvā pīḍaytvā grasitum śakyate duṣkṛtam ityādi smaraṇāt gṛhiṇā vaiśvadeva ākhyam ahani ahani nirūpyata kecid bhotta kṛsā dhāraṇa vaiśvadeva ākhyasya annasya bhujyamānān navat pratyakṣam ayat idamadyate karmavat svabhāva jugupsitam śiṣṭa nirvartya akaraṇe pratyavāya śravaṇāt itaratra pratyavāya upapatteḥ adantam āṅmi mantra varṇāt mantra ucyate havanam bali haraṇam huta prahute gṛhiṇaḥ dvebhyaḥ huta prahutayoḥ śrautayoḥ darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ prasiddhataram mantra prakāśita guṇa pradhāna prāptau pradhāne prathamatarā avagatiḥ darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ prādhānyam huta prahuta apekṣayā grahaṇam yuktam adve devātam prakḷpte darśa pūrṇamāsa ākhye arthatva avighātāya iṣṭi yājuka iṣṭi yajana śīlaḥ iṣṭi kāmyā iṣṭayaḥ śātapathīyam prasiddhiḥ tāt śīlya pratyaya prayogāt kāmya iṣṭi yajana pradhāne arthaḥ paśubhya paśubhya avagamyate annasya svāminaḥ ata ucitam atapaḥ aanyathā niyamena upajīveyuḥ ucyate annena vartante adyatve ādau viniyogaḥ bālam traivarṇikā jātakarmaṇi jātarūpa saṃyuktam pāyayanti sambhavam dhāpayanti manuṣyebhyaḥ akiyat pramāṇaḥ pṛṣṭā atṛṇāda tṛṇam bālaḥ vartata arthaḥ jātakarma ādau paya sarvathā paya vikāra saptamam paśu caturtha tvena vyākhyāyate sādhana sādhana āśrayam hotra ādi sādhanam sādhyam vakṣyamāṇasya trayasya sādhyasya darśa pūrṇamāsau uktau pakṣa piṇḍīkṛtya upadeśaḥ sādhanatva aviśeṣāt artha sambandhāt ānantaryam akāraṇam avyākhyāne pratipatti saukaryāt sukham nairantaryeṇa vyākhyātu śakyante vyākhyātāni sukham pratīyante kor athaḥ ucyate paśu adhyātma adhibhūta adhida lakṣaṇam kṛtsnam jagat veṣṭāvat sthānaram śaila ādi prasiddha avadyotakena vyākhyātam kāraṇatva apapatteḥ kāraṇa agnihotra ādi samavāyi agnihotra ādi āhuti vipariṇām ātmakam jagat kṛtsnam śruti smṛti vādāḥ śataśas vyavasthitāḥ yuktam vyākhyānam brāhmaṇa antareṣu saṃvatsareṇa ṣaṣṭi śatāni āhutīnām śatāni viṃśatiḥ yājuṣmatīriṣṭakā abhisampadyamānāḥ ahorātrāṇi āpnuvanti sambhūtaḥ mriyata arthaḥ brāhmaṇa vādā draṣṭavyam saṃvatsara abhyāsam apekṣate uktam paya āhuti vipariṇām ātmaka ekena āhvā jagat ucyate maraṇam mṛtvā āviddhān śarīreṇa viyujya maraṇāya paricchinnam arthaḥ hetuḥ āptyā ucyate samastam ādyam sāyaṃprātara āhuti prakṣepeṇa yuktam āhuti m devaiḥ bhāvam ayaḥ mriyata uktam brāhmaṇena svayambhū tapasi ānantyam juhavāni śraiṣṭhyam svārājyagādhipatyam paryet bhoktṛbhiḥ gānāni nimitta sthiteḥ nairantaryeṇa kṛta kṣaya upapatteḥ yuktaḥ kṣayaḥ kṣīyamāṇāni jagataḥ avibhraṣṭa avasthāna darśanāt bhavitavyam akṣaya kāraṇena kṣīyanta praśnaḥ prativacanam apuriṣaḥ annānām sraṣṭā ādi sambandhena pāṅkta bhoktā yebhyaḥ dattāni annānām bhoktāraḥ pitara janayanti abhidhīyate annānām bhoktā akṣaya hetuḥ ākṣiti ucyate bhujyamānam saptavidham kārya karaṇa lakṣaṇam kriyā phala ātmakam janayata utpādayati kāla bhāvinyā prajñayā kāya veṣṭitaiḥ saptavidham uktam kṣaṇa mātram prajñayā vicchidyeta bhujyamāna sātatyena bhoktā annānām nairantaryeṇa yathāprajñe yathākarma sātatyena kartṛ bhujyamānāni kṣīyanta arthaḥ kriyā lakṣaṇa prabandha ārūḍhaḥ sādhya sādhana lakṣaṇaḥ kriyā phala ātmakaḥ saṃhata aneka vāsanā santāna avaṣṭabdha kṣaṇikaḥ aśuddhaḥ asāraḥ nadī srotaḥ pradīpa santāna kalpaḥ kadalī stambhavat asāraḥ phena māyā marīci ambhaḥ ādi gata dṛṣṭīnāma vikīryamāṇaḥ sāravān lakṣyate vairāgya ucyate viraktānām ārabdhavyā caturtha pramukheṇa kṣitim vakṣyamāṇāni ani avasare vyakhyātāni yāthātmya phalam upasaṃhriyate akṣaya hetum uktam annamatti artha ucyate mukhya prādhānyam prādhānya annānām pituḥ ākṣiti annamatti guṇa bhūtaḥ ājñaḥ anāya bhūtaḥ bhoktā bhojyatām āpādyate bhāvam uktam apūrva arthaḥ pāṅktasya phala upakṣiptāni kāryatvāt vistīrṇa viṣaya pūrvabhyaḥ annebhyaḥ utkṛṣṭāni vyākhyāna artha uttaraḥ grantha brāhmaṇa parisamāpteḥ artha ucyate prāṇā kṛtavān ādau saṃśaya ata ādi bāhya karaṇa vyatiriktam yata prasiddham bāhya karaṇa viṣaya sambandhe sati abhimukhībhūtam viṣayam akim dṛṣṭavān uktaḥ aanyatra gatam mana anyatramanā āsam ādarśam aidam śrutavān madīyam uktaḥ aanyatramanā śrutavān asmiaiti asannidhau ādi grahaṇa samarthasya ādeḥ sva sva viṣaya sambandhe aśabda ādi jñānam bhāve antaḥkaraṇam kāraṇa viṣaya yogi avagabhyate lokām vayagra tve darśana ādi abhāvāt astitve sidve svarūpa ucyatekāmaḥ cyati kara ābhīlāṣa ādiḥ pratyupasthita vipaya vikalpanam śukla nīla ādi bhedena saṃśaya jñānam śradvā adṛṣṭa artheṣu karmasvāstikya vudvidaivaya ādi pu aśradvā viparītā vudviḥ dhāraṇam deha ādi avasāde uttambhan viparyayaḥ lajjā bhayma evamādikam mana antaḥkaraṇasya astitvam pratyanyat kāraṇam ucyate astayantaḥ karaṇam agocare pṛṣṭhaptaḥ upaspṛṣṭhaḥ kenicid hastasya sparśaḥ jāneḥ vivekena viveka mātreṇa kutaḥ viveka pratipattiḥ svarūpam apādhi gatam phala ākhyāni adhpa ātmam adhidaivam vyāci khyāsitāni ādhyātmikānām vyākhyātam idārnīvāgvattkavyā āraṃmaḥ dhavanistālvādi vyaṅgyaḥ prāṇibhiḥ varṇa ādi lakṣaṇa vāditra medhā ādi nimittaḥ dhvaniḥ svarūpam uttkam kāryam ucyate abhidheya avasānam abhidheya nirṇayam anugatā abhidheyavat prakāśyā abhidheya prakāśikā ev prakāśa ātmaka pradīpa ādivat pradīpa ādi prakāśaḥ prakāśa prakāśyate tadvat prakāśikā prakāśya anavasthām śrutiḥ pariharati prakāśyā prakāśaka kāryam arthaḥ ucyate mukha nāsikā sañcāryā hṛdaya vṛttiḥ praṇayanāt apanayanāt mūtra purīṣa ādeḥ apānanaḥ vṛttiḥ ānābhisthānaḥ vyānanaḥ vyāyamana karmā apānayoḥ sandhiḥ vīryavat hetuḥ udāna utkarṣa gamana ādi hetuḥ āpāda tala mastaka sthāna vṛttiḥ nayanāt bhuktasya pītasya koṣṭha sthānaḥ paktā ana vṛtti viśeṣāṇām sāmānya bhūtā sāmānya deha ceṣṭā abhisambandhinī vṛttiḥ uktam ādi vṛtti ithi vṛttimān ādhyātmikaḥ ana uktaḥ vṛtti bheda pradarśanena vyākhyātam vyākhyātāni ādhyātmikāni ākhyāni maya vikāraḥ prājāpatyaiḥ ārabdhaḥ atham kārya karaṇa saṅghāta piṇḍa svarūpa tvena abhimataḥ avivekibhiḥ aviśeṣeṇa maya uktasya viśeṣeṇa maya sphuṭīkaraṇam prājāpatyānām annānām ādhibhautikaḥ vistāraḥ abhidhīyate traya lokā eta vedā ityādīni vākyāni ṛju arthāni avijñātam eta viśeṣaḥ vispaṣṭam jñātam hetunā vāgdhi prakāśa ātmaka avijñātā bhavet vijñāpayadi viśeṣa vida phalam ucyate vibhūti vidam pālayati vijñāta bhojyatām pratipadyata arthaḥ vispaṣṭam yasma āsyam mad vibhūti phalam mana vijijñāsya sva āpadyate avijñātam agocaram sandihyamānam avijñātaḥ anirukta vijñāta vijijñāsyā vijñāta bhedena vibhāge sthite lokā ityādayaḥ vācanikā sarvatra vijñāta ādi darśanāt vacanāt niyamaḥ smartavyaḥ avijñāta arthaḥ śiṣya ādibhiḥ sandihyamāna avijñāta upakārā ācārya ādayā dṛśyante prāṇayoḥ sandihyamāna avijñātayoḥ annatva upapattiḥ vyākhyātaḥ ādhibhautikaḥ vistāraḥ ayamādhidaivikārya ārambhaḥ tvena prastutāyāḥ ādhāraḥ jyotīrūpam prakāśa ātmakam karaṇam ādheyam prakāśaḥ parimāṇā adhyātma adhibhūta bheda bhinnā sarvatra ādhāra tvena vyavasthitā kārya ādheyaḥ karaṇa jyoti anupraviṣṭaḥ uttaram prājāpatyāt uktasya kāryam ādhāraḥ jyotīrūpam karaṇam ādheyaḥ parimāṇam vistārā parimāṇā jyotīrūpasya karaṇasya ādhāra tvena vyavasthitā jyotīrūpam karaṇam ādheyam avagni ādityau ādhidaivike bhātā pitarau maithunyam itaretara saṃsarga samagacchetām amanasā prabhūtam mātrā prakāśitam kariṣyāmi rodasyoḥ saṅgamanāt ajñāyata parispandāya parameśvaraḥ kevalam āsapatnaḥ avidyamānaḥ sapatnanaḥ pratipakṣa tvena upagataḥ ucyate dvitīya tve sati bhajete guṇa bhāva upagate prāsaṅgi phalam āsya viduṣaḥ pratipakṣaḥ ya uktam asapatnam prakṛtasya prajāpatyā annasya uktasya antara nirdiṣṭasya kāryam karaṇa ādhāraḥ pūrvavat jayotīrūpam yāvaneva parimāṇaḥ adhyātma ādi bhedeṣu vyāptimatya parimāṇāḥ abādheyaḥ tāsu karaṇa bhūtaḥ vyāptimān pāṅktena ākhyāni jagat samastam vyāptam atiriktam kārya ātmakam karaṇa ātmakam samastāni ta tulyā vyāptimantaḥ gocaram adhya vyāpya vyavasthitāḥ ata anantā saṃsāra bhāvinanaḥ kārya karaṇa pratyākhyānena saṃsāraḥ avagamyate kārya karaṇa ātmakā ta uktam anantavataḥ paricchinnān adhyātma adhibhūta adhibhūta upāsana anurūpam phalam paricchinna bhūtaḥ arthaḥ ātmakān bhūtān aparicchinna anupāste pāṅktena arthaṅkara uditi uktam pāṅkta phala vyākhyātāni pāṅktata avagamyate karmaṇamoḥ sambhavāt agnī divā ādityau amanayoḥ vyākhyātam sambhāvayitavye ārambhaḥ asa prakṛtaḥ saṃvatsara viśeṣataḥ nirdiśyate avayavā saṃvatsara akāla kāla rātraya ahorātrāṇi tithaya arthaḥ nityā vyavasthitā ṣoḍaśānām pūraṇī tithibhiḥ uktābhiḥ āpūryate apakṣīyate pratipadādyābhiḥ śukla pakṣa āpūryate kalābhiḥ upacīyamānābhiḥ sampūrṇa maṇḍalaḥ paurṇamāsyām apacīyamānābhiḥ kalābhiḥ apakṣīyate kṛṣṇa pakṣe vyavasthitā amāvāsyāyām rātriṃrātrau vyavasthitā uktā pibati aupadhīraśnāti oṣadhi vyāpya avasthāya aparedyus jñāyate dvitīyayā saṃyuktaḥ pāṅkta ātmakaḥ divā ādityau pṛthivyagnaḥ jñāyā cāndramasyaḥ tithayaḥ upacaya apacaya dharmi vittavat tāsām kalānām kāla avayavānām jagat pariṇāma hetu eṣaṇa anurūpa pāṅktasya phala bhūtaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ kāraṇa anuvidhāyi kāryam rātriṃ anupraviṣṭaḥ dhruvayā vartate hetoḥ rātriṃ prāṇinaḥ prāṇinam pramāpayet kṛkalāsaḥ svabhāvena hiṃsyate prāṇibhiḥ amaṅgala bāḍham pratiṣiddhā amāvāsyāyāḥ pratiprasava vacanam hiṃsāyāḥ kṛkalāsa viṣaye pūjā abhihitaḥ atyantam parokṣaḥ upalabhyate yathektam ātmakam vetti sāmānyena ucyate gavā ādi upacaya apacaya dharmi at sādhyam piṇḍa viduṣaḥ dhruva sthānīyā candravat āpūryate apakṣīyate prasiddham nābhyai nābhim pradhirvittam parivāra sthānīyam āranemi ādi jyā niṃ sva apaharaṇam hīyate glānim cakra nābhi sthānīyena bāhyena parivāreṇa kṣīṇaḥ cakramara nemi vimuktam jīvan ara nemi sthānīyena upacīyata abhiprāyaḥ pāṅktena daiva saṃyuktena ātmakaḥ vyākhyātam ādi parivāra sthānīyam uktam apara prāpti sādhanatva mātram sāmānyena avagatam ādīnā prāpti phalam viśeṣa sambandha niyamaḥ ādīnām sādhanānām sādhya viśeṣa sambandhaḥ vaktavya uttarakaṇḍikā praṇīyate vākya upanyāsa arthaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ traya śāstra sādhana arhā nyūnā adhikā ucyate deloke sādhanena jetavyaḥ sādhyaḥ jetavyaḥ uttaratra vakṣyāmaḥ vākya śeṣaḥ agnihotra ādi lakṣaṇena kevalena jetavyaḥ trayāṇām praśasyatamaḥ sādhana sādhya traya phala bhedena viniyuktāni ākhyāni sādhanāni artha sādhanam abhihitā sādhana sādhanam karmaṇoḥ jaya hetu sva pratilābhena prasiddham putrasya akriyā ātmaka prakāreṇa jaya hetutvam jñāyate vaktavyam ārabhyate sampratiḥ sampradānam vakṣyamāṇasya sva vyāpāra sampradānam prakāreṇa sampratti saṃjñakam kartavyam praiṣyan mariṣyan mariṣyāmi apariṣṭa ādi āhūya uktaḥ kartavyam ithi vākya arthaḥ tirohita manvānā śrutiḥ vyākhyānāya pravartate avaśiṣṭam adhītam anadhītam adhyayana vyāpāraḥ kartavya viṣayaḥ ita tvad kartṛkaḥ arthaḥ yajñā anuṣṭheyāḥ anuṣṭhitāḥ ananuṣṭhitāḥ yajña mad kartṛkā yajñā ya āsan ita tvad kartṛkā arthaḥ lokā jetavyāḥ jitā ajitāḥ ita adhyayana yajña jaya kartavya samarpitaḥ muktaḥ kartavyatā bandhana viṣayāt kratoḥ pratipannavān anuśiṣṭa pituḥ abhiprāyam manvānā ācaṣṭa śrutiḥ parimāṇam gṛhiṇā kartavyam vedā adhyetavyāḥ yajñā yaṣṭavyāḥ jetavyāḥ bhāram mad adhīnam mattaḥ apacchidya ātamani nidhāya abhunajat pālayiṣyati ḷḍarthe laṅ chandasi kāla niyama abhāvāt sampannaḥ kartavyatā bandhanataḥ mocayiṣyati pituḥ ata lokyaḥ samarpita kartavya tākratuḥ paiti tadaibhiḥ prakṛtaiḥ vyāpnoti adhyātma pariccheda hetu apagamāt pituḥ ādhidaivikena ādi bhinna ghaṭa pradīpa prakāśavat taiḥ ati bhāvi pituḥ anantā prāṇā adhyātma ādi bheda vistārā bhāvitaḥ anuvṛtti pituḥ yuktam uktam āviśatīt putrasya uktam pituḥ vartate mantavya arthaḥ śruti antare itara puṇyebhyaḥ karmabhyaḥ pratidhīyate nirvacanam kadācid akṣṇyā koṇa chidrataḥ akṛtam kartavyam kartavyatā rūpāt akṛtāt prāpti pratibandha rūpāt mocayati anutiṣṭhan pūraṇena putrasya pituḥ chidram evaṃvidhena karmabhyām sva lābha sattā mātreṇa sva lābha vyatirekeṇa putravat vyāpāra antara apekṣayā jaya hetu pratipadyete kṛta samprattikam ādayaḥ prāṇā daivā hairaṇyagarbhā amaraṇa dharmāṇa ityādi apara lokadeva sādhya artha pradarśitā śrutyā kecid vāvadu uktāḥ śruti viśeṣa viniyoga upasahāreṇa ṛṇa śrutiḥ avi dvat viṣayā paramātma vidviṣaya siddham kariṣyāmaḥ ātmāyam kecid jayaḥ lokābhyām vyāvṛttiḥ apara vidyābhiḥ samucitya anuṣṭhitābhiḥ tribhya lokebhyaḥ vyāvṛttaḥ paramātma mokṣam adhigacchati paramparayā mokṣa arthāni ādi sādhanāni mukha apidhānāya śrutiḥ uttarā kṛta samprattikasya putriṇaḥ karmiṇaḥ phala pradarśanāya pravṛttā phalam mokṣa phalam śakyam vaktum sambandhāt medhā kārya annānām apunar darśanāt ayat kṣaya śravaṇāt jyotīrūpam kārya karaṇatva upapatteḥ atrayam ātmaka tvena upasaṃhārāt sādhana saṃhatam kasyacid mokṣa kasyacid phalam vākyāt avagantu śakyam ādi sādhanānām phala upakṣīṇa vākyasya adhidaiva ātmikā kṛta samprattikam vāca upādāna bhūtāḥ pṛthi vī lakṣaṇā ādhyātmikā saṅga ādi doṣaiḥ niruddhā viduṣaḥ doṣa apagame āvaraṇa bhaṅga udaka pradīpa prakāśavat vyāpnoti ucyat anṛta ādi doṣa rahitā śuddhā daivyā parasmai amoghā apratibaddhā vāgbhavati arthaḥ mana svabhāva nirmalatva at ānandya sukhī athaḥ ādi nimitta asaṃyogāti adbhayaḥ kin lakṣaṇaḥ ucyate sañcaran bhedeṣu sañcaran samaṣṭivya ṣṭi athavā sañcarana jaṅgameṣu asañcaran sthāvareṣu duḥkha nimittena duḥkha athaḥ ata aitya viśeṣeṇa upāsanam uktam anyatama gataḥ veśeṣa uktaḥ pratipattavyam vicāryamāṇe viśeṣaḥ upāsanam pratita pattum śakyate ucyate upāsana vicāraṇā arthaḥ tvena dhārayitavyam pravartate arthe karaṇāni ādīni athāni sṛṣṭavān ādīni karaṇāni arthaḥ anyonyena itaretaram spardhām saṃgharṣam cakruḥ sva vyāpārāt vadanāt anuparata dhṛtavatī mad sva vyāpārāt anuparantum śaktaḥ darśayatva karaṇāni yathākarma yathākarma karaṇāni mārakaḥ śrama rūpī sañjagrāha karaṇāni sva vyāpāre pravṛttāni āpna ut śrama darśitavān avarodham kṛtavān sva karmabhyaḥ pracyāvitavān arthaḥ adyatve vadane sva karmaṇi pravṛttā śrāmya tvena śrama rūpiṇā saṃyuktā sva karmataḥ pracyavate mukhyam āpna unna prāptavān śrama rūpī tve aśrānta sva karmaṇi pravartate karaṇāni dhṛtavanti asmākam madhye praśasyatamaḥ abhyadhikaḥ sañcaran asañcaran athaḥ asāma tvena pratipadyemahi viniścitya tvena pratipannāḥ asmad vratāni vāraṇāya paryāptāni rūpavanti karaṇāni calana prakāśa calana ātmakatva upapattiḥ calana vyāpāra pūrvakāṇi sva vyāpāreṣu lakṣyante ādaya abhidhānena abhidhīyante prāṇā ya ātmatām karaṇānām vetti śabda abhidheya viduṣā laukikāḥ vidvat prathitam amuṣyadam tāpatya ya uktam ādīnām ākhya phalam darśinā pratipakṣī śoṣam śoṣam sahasā anupadrutaḥ uktam darśanam upasaṃhāraḥ adhidaivata pradarśana arthaḥ viṣayam darśanam ucyate viśeṣasya dhāraṇam mīmāsyate adhyātmavat anyā śabdasya yor athaḥ śabdasya śabda sāmānya mātram viśeṣāṇām kāraṇam upādānam lavaṇa kaṇānām acalaḥ sāmānyāt yajñadattaḥ devadatta evamādi pravibhāgāni utpadyante pravibhajyante lavaṇa acalāt lavaṇa kaṇāḥ kāryam kāraṇena avyatiriktam viśeṣāṇām sāmānye antarbhāvāt sāmānya viśeṣa bhāva śabda sāmānyam viśeṣāṇām sama sāmānyam arthaḥ viśeṣaiḥ lābha aviśeṣāt viśeṣāṇām lābhaḥ apravibhaktaḥ ghaṭa ādīnām mṛdā viśeṣāṇām lābhaḥ vāca ucyate yata chabda vācyam vastu lābhaḥ śabda vyatirikta svarūpa anupapatteḥ pratipādayati śabda sāmānyam śabda viśeṣān dhārayati sva pradānena kārya kāraṇatva upapatteḥ sāmānya viśeṣa upapatteḥ pradāna upapattaḥ viśeṣāṇām śabda mātra siddhā uttarayoḥ yojyam uktam sita asita prabhṛtīnām viṣaya sāmānyam śabda abhidheyam sāmānyam prakāśya mātram abhidhīyate ittiṣṭhanti sarvai rūpeḥ viśeṣāṇām manana darśana ātmakānām calana ātmakānām kriyā sāmānya antarbhāva ucyate viśeṣāṇām sāmānyam ucyate aātmanā śarīreṇa uktam abhivyajyat tātsthyāt śabdam sāmānya mātram ityādi pūrvavat uktam itaretara āśrayam itaretara abhivyakti kāraṇam itaretara pralayam saṃhatam tridaṇḍa viṣṭambhavat ekatvam ucyate kārya karaṇa saṅghātaḥ traye vyākhyātaḥ aetat aityādinā avyākṛtam kārya karaṇa saṅghātaḥ adhyātma adhibhūta adhidaiva bhāvena vyavasthitam vakṣyamāṇam satyenacchannam vākyasya karaṇa ātmakaḥ upaṣṭambhaka bhūtaḥ abhūtaḥ kārya ātmake avasthe kriyā ātmakaḥ upaṣṭambhakaḥ bāhy bāhy ābhyām ātmakābhyām upajana apāya dharmibhyām martyābhyām aprakāśīkṛtaḥ saṃsāra sata avidyā viṣayam pradarśitam ata viṣaya adhigantavya ithi ārabhyate adhyāye ṣaṣṭham brāhmaṇam ādhḥYāYā anveṣaṇe anviṣṭam cā atma tattvam anveṣṭavyam avedaham tattvam viṣayaḥ bheda dṛṣṭi viṣayaḥ avidyā viṣayaḥ ya anā evamādibhiḥ pravibhatkau viṣayau upaniṣatsu avidyā viṣayaḥ sādhya sādhana ādi bheda viśeṣa viniyogena vyākhyātaḥ tṛtīya adhyāya parisamāpteḥ vyākhyātaḥ avidyā viṣayaḥ dvi prakāraḥ upaṣṭambha gṛhasi stambha ādi lakṣaṇaḥ prakāśakaḥ bāhyaḥ kārya lakṣaṇaḥ aprakāśaka upajana apāya dharmakaḥ kuśa mṛttikā gṛhasi śabda vācyaḥ śabda vācyaḥ channa upasaṃhratam bāhya ādhāra medeṣu anekadhā vistṛtaḥ ucyate bāhyaḥ piṇḍa sādhāraṇaḥ vaiśvānara hiraṇyagarbha ityādibhiḥ piṇḍa pradhānaiḥ śabdaiḥ ākhyāyate ādi pravibhakta karaṇaḥ anekam paramasti pratyekam bhedeṣu parisamāptam cetanāvat kartṛ bhoktṛ avidyā viṣayam tvena upagataḥ vaktā upasthāpyate viparīta dṛga jāta śatruḥ pakṣa siddhānta ākhyāyikā samarpyamāṇoḥ athaḥ cittasya vaśam viparyaye tarka śāstravat kevala artha anugama vākyaiḥ samarpyamāṇaḥ durvijñeyaḥ atyanta sūkṣma vastunaḥ kāṭhake śravaṇāya labhyaḥ ityādi vākyaiḥ saṃskṛta buddhi gamya sāmānya mātra buddhyā agamya prapañcam darśitam ācāryāt cacchāndogye upadekṣyanti jñānam jñāninaḥ tattva darśinaḥ gītāsu saṃvādena ati gahvara mahatā saṃrambheṇa tasmāḥ cilaṣṭa ākhyāyikā pakṣa siddhānta āpādya vasyu samarpaṇa artha ārambhaḥ ācāra vidhi upadeśa arthaḥ ācāravatoḥ vatt kṛśrokroḥ ākhyāyikā anugater athaḥ avagamyate kevala tarka budviniṣedha arthā ākhyāyikā tarkeṇa matiḥ āpaneyā tarka śāstra dagdhāya śruti smṛtibhyām śradvā sādhanam ākhyāyka arthaḥ gārgyā jāta śatravoḥ śradvālutāt dṛśyate ākhyāyikāyām śradvān labhate jñānam smṛtiḥ pakṣa vādī avidyā viṣaya dṛpta bālākiḥ dṛpate garvitaḥ asabhyak vittavādā iv balākāyā apatyam bālākiḥ dṛptaḥ bālākiḥ dṛpta bāla arkiḥ śabda etihyārtha ākhyāyikāyām anuvaca samarthaḥ vattkāvāk gamī gonnataḥ kvacid kāla viśeṣe ajātaśatrumajāta śatru nāmānam kāśi rājam abhigamya kathayāni uktaḥ dadbha pratyavocaḥ mātram gaḥ sahasra pradāne nimittam abhiprāyaḥ kathanam nimittam apekṣyate sahasra dāne itīyam nimittam apekṣyate ucyate śrutiḥ rājñaḥ abhiprāyam dātā vākya dvaye dvayam abhyasyate vaiśabdaḥ prasiddha avadyotana arthaḥ ditsurjanakaḥ śuśrūṣuḥ śuśrūṣavaḥ vivakṣavaḥ pati jighṛkṣavaḥ janādhāvanti abhigacchanti sambhāvitavān śuśrūṣum abhimukhībhūtam ya abhimānī dvāreṇa aaham bhoktā avasthitaḥ kārya karaṇa saṅghāte bravībhyupāḥsva uktaḥ pratyuvāca hastena vinivārayan brahmaṇi vijñeye ityābādhana vacanam samāne viṣaye āvayoḥ avijñānavata darśayatā bādhitāḥ syāma saṃvādam kārṣīḥ brahmaṇi jānāsi vaktum arhasi jñāyata manyase jānīṣe mātram viśeṣaṇa upāsana mantavyam jāne bravīṣi atītya tiṣṭhāti dīpti guma upeta viśeṣaṇaiḥ viśiṣṭam kārya karaṇa saṅghāte kartṛ bhoktṛ upāsa phalam viśiṣṭa upāsakasya ya guṇa upāsanam phalam saṃvādena brahmaṇi pratyākhyāte ajātaśatruṇā ya bhoktā pūrvavat viśeṣaṇam pāṇḍaram pāṇḍara ap abhimāninaḥ bhūtaḥ abhiṣūyate latā ātmakaḥ ekīkṛtya guṇam ya aharahar abhiṣutaḥ prakṛṣṭam sutarām vikāre ubhayavidha yajña anuṣṭhāna sāmarthyam arthaḥ ātmaka upāsakasya viśeṣaṇam phalam hāsya vidyutām aṅgīkaraṇāt prajāyām phala bāhulyam apravarti viśeṣaṇa dvayam pūrṇatva viśeṣaṇa phalam apravarti viśeṣaṇa phalam udvartata santānā vicchittiḥ viśeṣaṇam parameśvaraḥ aprasahyaḥ paraiḥ phalam rocanā ādhāra bāhulyāt phala bāhulyam gacchantam ya pṛṣṭhataḥ anīda jīvana hetuḥ ekīkṛtya aha jīvana hetuḥ guṇaḥ phalam yathopāttam phala paricchinna roga ādibhiḥ pīḍyamānam karṇayoḥ aviyukta bhāvaḥ viśeṣaḥ buddhau ātmavāni viśeṣaṇam phalam ātmavān hāsya buddhi bahula prajāyām sampādanam viśeṣaḥ parijñāta tvena krameṇa pratyākhyā brahmasu kṣīṇa vijñānaḥ apratibhāsamāna uttaraḥ abhoktā nirṇayaḥ nirdhārita viśeṣa gārgya abhipretasyaḥ satyenacchannaḥ ādiṣu anastamitaḥ nimlocatsu pāṇḍara asapatna sva vyāpāra ārūḍhaḥ nirjñāta ana stamita svabhāva anyasya kasyacid vyāpāraḥ gārgyeṇa abhipreyate virodhinaḥ sva āmantritena pratiboddhavyam pāriśeṣyāt gārgya abhipretasya abhoktṛ bhoktṛ svabhāvaḥ bhuñjīta viṣayam prāptam dagdhṛ svabhāvaḥ prakāśayitṛ svabhāvaḥ vahniḥ ulapa ādi dāhyam sva viṣayam prāptam dahati prakāśyam prakāśayati dahati prakāśayati prāptam viṣayam vahniḥ dagdhā prakāśayitā niścīyate prāpta śabda ādi viṣaya upalabdhṛ svabhāvaḥ gārgya abhipretaḥ pāṇḍara vāsa evamādi śabdam viṣayam upalabheta prāptam ulapa ādi vahniḥ dahet prakāśayet avyabhicāreṇa tadvat prāptānām śabda ādīnām apratibodhāt abhoktṛ svabhāva niścīyate svabhāvaḥ niścitaḥ vyabhicarati kadācid siddham abhoktṛ sambodhana artha viśeṣeṇa sambandha agrahaṇāt apratibodha āsīneṣu sva viśeṣeṇa sambandha āghrahaṇāt sambodhayati sambodhyamānaḥ viśeṣataḥ evamādīni ānītya gṛhīta sambandha sambodhana śabdam avijñātṛ abhyupagame aghrahaṇa anupapatteḥ ādi abhimāninī bhoktā abhyupagamyate saṃvyavahārāya viśeṣa sambandhaḥ avaśyam grahītavyaḥ anyathā āhvāna ādi viṣaye saṃvyavahāraḥ anupapannam vyatirikta pakṣe apratipattera yuktam vyatiriktaḥ bhoktā ādi sambodhane bṛhattva ādi viṣaya pratipattiḥ yuktā kadācid bṛhattva ādi śabdaiḥ sambodhitaḥ pratipadyamānaḥ dṛśyate akāraṇam abhoktṛ tve sambodhana apratipattiḥ tadvataḥ mātra abhimāna anupapatteḥ vyatiriktaḥ bhoktā abhimānaḥ sambodhane kṛtsnā abhimāninaḥ yuktā apratipattiḥ asādhāraṇa saṃyoge tvānabhimānāt sva prayoge apratipatti darśanāt ayuktam suṣuptasya laukikam devadatta ādi sambodhyamānaḥ kadācid bhoktā pratipadyata prāṇayoḥ supta asuptatva viśeṣa upapatteḥ suṣupta grasta uparatakaṇa prayujyamānam asuptasya bhoktṛtva uparata karaṇa sambodhana agrahaṇam yuktam aprasiddha sambodhanam ayuktam santi viṣayāṇi prasiddhāni ādi nāmā ni apohyaa prasiddhaiḥ bṛhattva ādi sambodhanam ayuktam laukika nyāya apohāt bhoktuḥ apratipattiḥ pratyākhyāna artha kevala sambodhana mātra apratipattyā asuptasya ādhyātmikasya abhokatṛ tve siddhe viṣayaiḥ sambodhanam bhoktā gārgyasya viśeṣa pratipatti nirākaraṇa laukika sambodhaneśakyam kartum grasta karaṇa antarāṇām pravṛtti anupapatteḥ bhoktṛtva anupapattiḥ antara abhāvāt nanu atiṣṭhā ādya vīti antena granthena guṇavat bhedasya darśita ekatva abhyupagamāt śrutiṣu arana abhinidarśanena bāhyasya anyasya anabhyupagamāt bhoktuḥ katama ekatva upapādanāt karaṇa bhedeṣu anāśaṅkā deha bhedeṣu smṛti jñāna di pratisandhāna anupapatteḥ anya smarati icchati pratisanda dhāti karaṇa bheda viṣayā bhoktṛtva mātra viṣayā kadācid upapadyate nanu saṅghāta bhoktā vyatirikta kalpanayā apeṣaṇe viśeṣa darśanāt saṅghāta mātraḥ bhoktā saṅghāta mātrā viśeṣāt sadā āpiṣṭasya anāpiṣṭasya pratibodhe viśeṣaḥ saṅghāta vyatirikte bha uktari saṅghāta sambandha viśeṣa aneka peṣaṇa apeṣaṇa kṛta vedanāyāḥ sukha duḥkha madhyama adhama uttama phala bheda upapatteḥ viśeṣaḥ yuktaḥ vijijñāpayiṣayā ārambhaḥ upakramya arekhalu upasaṃhārāt cātas antarāle vivakṣita m uktam anavasaraḥ sama guṇa bhāva anupagama udyasya viśeṣavataḥ upādhikasya saṃvyavahāra arthaḥ guṇa guṇi bhāvaḥ
