svābhāvyāt pracyutaḥ saṃsārī svabhāva vilakṣaṇa vivakṣayā pṛcchati gārgyam pratibhāna rahitam buddhi vyutpādanāya kuta gārgyeṇa praṣṭavyam gārgyeṇa pṛṣṭam udāste bodhayitavya pravartate pratijñāta vyutpādyamānaḥ bodhāt āgamanam vyutpede vaktum jñātavān vivakṣita artha samarpaṇāya ya ya kuta śṛṇu ucyamānam ātasmin ādīnām antaḥkaraṇa gata abhivyakti viśeṣa upādhi svabhāva janitena ādīnām sva sva viṣaya gata sāmarthyam ya madhye ya sva ucyate svābhāvike asāṃsārike kevala śruti antara sāmarthyāt satā somya sampannaḥ liṅga upādhi sambandha viśeṣa svarūpam utsṛjya aviśeṣe svābhāvike kevale vartata abhiprāyaḥyadā indriya adhyakṣatām utsṛjati sva vartata avagamyate prasiddhyā kāsau prasiddhiḥ ādeḥ vijñānāni ādatte prasiddham gauṇam ucyate sva piti prasiddhyā saṃsāra vilakṣaṇam avagamyate yuktiḥ āśaṅkya tatttra svāpa gṛhīta ghrāṇa ādi prakaraṇa at ādi sambandhe sati upādhi saṃsāra dharmi lakṣyate ādayaḥ upasaṃhṛtā upasaṃhṛteṣu ādiṣu kriyā kāraka phala bhāvāt sva stha abhavati avagamyate nanu darśana lakṣaṇāyām avasthāyām kārya karaṇa viyoge saṃsāra dharmitvam dṛśyate jāgarite sukhī duḥkhī bandhu viyuktaḥ muhyate ta dharmavān ādāyaḥ sukha duḥkha ādayaḥ kārya karaṇa saṃyoga janita bhrānti adhyāropitā mṛṣātvāt prakṛta darśana lakṣaṇayā vṛttyā vartate hāsya rāja rāja rāja brāhmaṇa uccam devatva ādi avacam tiryaktva ādi uccam avacam mṛṣā rāja ayaḥ śabda prayogāt vyabhicāra darśanāt bandhu viyoga ādi janita ādibhiḥ sambadhyata nanu jāgarite kāla avi abhicāriṇaḥ rāja ayaḥ kāla bhāvinaḥ kāla avyabhicāriṇa bhūtā avidyā adhyāropitā nanu kārya karaṇa avidyā adhyāropitam paramārtha ta vyatirikta maya pradarśanena pradarśitam dṛṣṭānta tvena mṛta ujjīviṣyan prādurbhaviṣyati maye vyatirikte kārya karaṇa ātmatva pradarśanam avidyā adhyāropitam śuktikāyām rajatatva darśanam siddhi ati vyatirikta astitva pradarśana nyāyena viśuddhi nyāya uktaḥ asan dṛṣṭāntaḥ kārya karaṇa ātmatva darśana lakṣaṇaḥ udbhāvyate nyāyaḥ viśeṣam apekṣamāṇaḥ apunaruktibhavati anubhūta rāja ayaḥ lokā bhūtāḥ anyasya prativimba darśanāt rāja vyasta suptāsu prakṛtiṣu paryaṅke śayānaḥ svapnān upasaṃhṛta karaṇaḥ upagata prakṛtim mabārājam yātrā gatam bhuñjānam bhogān mabārājasya paryaṅke śayanāt prakṛti upetaḥ viṣaye paryaṭan ahani prasiddhaḥ yamasau upasaṃhṛta karaṇasya ādimataḥ darśanam upapadyate dehe deha antarasya tulyasya deha sthasya darśanam nanu paryaṅke śayānaḥ pathi pravṛttam svapnān rāja upakaraṇa bhūtān bhṛtyān anyān upādāya sva ātmīya jaya ādinā upārjite icchātaḥ arthaḥ kriyā viśeṣaṇamprāṇān sthānebhya upasaṃhṛtya sva dehe karmabhyām udbhāsitāḥ anubhūta vastu sadṛśīḥ vāsanā arthaḥ mṛṣā adhyāropitā tvena lokā avidyamānā jāgarite pratyetavyam viśuddhaḥ akriyā kāraka phala ātmakaḥ maya siddham dṛśyante viṣaya bhūtāḥ kriyā kāraka phala ātmakāḥ kārya karaṇa lakṣaṇā dṛśyebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ ayaḥ viśuddhaḥ viśuddha hitvā darśana vṛttim suṣṭhu samprasādam svābhāvyena prasīdati kadā kasyana kiñcana arthaḥ ka syacana śabda ādeḥ sambandhi vastu kiñcana adhyāhāryam nyāyyam supte viśeṣa abhāvasya vivakṣita viśeṣa abhāve uktam krameṇa ucyate hitā hitā evaṃnāmnyaḥ śirā dehasya vipariṇāma bhūtāḥ sahasre adhike saptatiḥ piṇḍāt puṇḍarīka ākārāt hṛdaya pariveṣṭanam ācakṣatetat upalakṣitam abhipratiṣṭhanta kṛtsnam vyāpnuvatyaḥ aśvatthaparṇa rājaya mukhyaḥ pravṛttā arthaḥ buddheḥ antaḥkaraṇasya tatrastha buddhi tantrāṇi bāhyāni karaṇāni buddhiḥ vaśāt ādīni nāḍībhiḥ matsya jālavat karṇa śaṣkulya ādi sthānebhyaḥ prasārayati prasārya adhitiṣṭhati ayaḥ abhivyakta sva caitanya avabhāsa vyāpnoti saṅkocana anusaṅkucita mayasya svāpaḥ vikāsa anubhavaḥ buddhi upādhi svabhāva anuvidhāyī ādi pratibimba jala ādi anuvidhāyī buddheḥ viṣayāyāḥ nāḍībhiḥ pratyavasarpaṇam taptam loha piṇḍam aviśeṣeṇa saṃvyāpya agnivat saṃvyāpya vartata arthaḥ svābhāvika sva vartamānaḥ anugata buddhi anuvṛtti śeta ucyate suṣipti sambandhaḥ saṃsāra duḥkha viyuktā avasthā dṛṣṭāntaḥ atyanta bālaḥ atyanta vaśya prakṛtiḥ atyanta paripakva vinaya sampannaḥ ati ghnīm atiśayena ati ghnī avasthā sukha avasthā avatiṣṭheta kumāra ādīnām svabhāva sthānām sukam niratiśyam prasiddham vikriyamāṇānām svabhāvataḥ svābhāvikī avasthā dṛṣṭānta tvena upādīyate prasiddha svāpa abhipretaḥ svāpasya dārṣṭa antika tvena vivakṣita viśeṣa abhāvāt viśeṣe sati dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭa antika bhedaḥ svāpaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ maya śayanam kriyā viśeṣaṇa arthaḥ svābhāvike saṃsāra atītaḥ vartate svāpa kāla ūrṇanābhiḥ ūrṇanābhiḥ lūtākīṭa prasiddhaḥ sva apravibhaktena udgacchet udgamane svatas atiriktam kāraka rūpāt ekasmāt śrudrā alpā visphuliṅga asruṭayaḥ avayavā vividham uccaranti dṛṣṭāntau kāraka bheda abhāve pravṛttim darśayataḥ pravṛtteḥ svabhāvata mayasya pratibodhāt svarūpam arthaḥ prāṇā ādayaḥ lokā ādayaḥ adhiṣṭhātāraḥ ādayaḥ ādi stamba paryantāni eta ātmāna pāṭha upādhi samparka janita prabudhyamāna viśeṣa ātmāna arthaḥ sthāvara jabhgamam jagat visphuliṅgavat vyuccarati aniśam pralīyate jala budbudavat ātmakam vartate samīpam nigamayati abhidhāyakaḥ śabda ucatyate śāsra prāmāṇyāt śabda gataḥ viśeṣaḥ avasīyata upanigamayitṛ itya sarvatra upaniṣada laukikā artha durvijñeya arthā ācaṣṭe prāṇā vākyasya vyākhyānāya uttaram brāhmaṇa dvayam bhaviṣyati bhavatu vyākhyānāya uttaram brāhmaṇa dvayam uktam jānīmaḥ prakṛtasya mayasya pāṇi peṣaṇa utthitasya saṃsāriṇaḥ śabda ādi bhuja upaniṣadāhosvidasaṃsāriṇaḥ kasyacid kiñcātas saṃsāriṇaḥ saṃsāri vijñeyaḥ prāptiḥ śabda vācyaḥ asaṃsāriṇaḥ viṣayā bhāva āpattiḥ śāsra prāmāṇyāt bhaviṣyati kintu pakṣe avedaham ekatva pratipādikāḥ śrutayaḥ kupyeran saṃsāriṇaḥ anyasya abhāve upadeśa anarthakyāt yata paṇḍitānām anukta prativacana praśna viṣayam yathāśakti pratipādaka vākyeṣu vijijñāsūnām buddhi vyutpādanāya vicārayiṣyāmaḥ asaṃsārī pāṇi peṣaṇa pratibodhitāt śabda ādi bhujaḥ avasthā antara viśiṣṭāt utpatti praśāsita aśanāya ādi varjitaḥ abrahma pratijñāya pāṇi peṣam bodhayitvā dvāreṇa suṣupti ākhyam avasthā unnīya suṣupti avasthā viśiṣṭāt visphuliṅga ūrṇanābhidṛṣṭāntābhyām utpattim darśayati śrutiḥ ityādinā jagat utpatti kāraṇam antarāle mayasya prakaraṇam samāna prakaraṇe śruti antare kauṣītaki nāmāt ityādi prastutya bālāka puruṣāṇām vaitat veditavyaḥ prabuddhasya mayasya veditavyatām darśayati artha antarasya ya prasiddhaḥ draṣṭavya śrotavya mantavya nididhyāsitavya darśayati upanyāsa avedaham evamādi vākyānām ānulomyam parābhāve pūruṣaḥ vedānteṣu pratyagātma vedya pradarśyate vedya śabda ādivat pradarśyate kauṣītakinām vijijñāsīta vaktāram ityādinā ādi karaṇaiḥ vyāvṛttasya kartuḥ veditavyatām darśayati avasthā antara viśiṣṭaḥ asaṃsārī jāgarite śabda ādi bhuj suṣupta ākhyam avasthā gataḥ asaṃsārī praśāsitā adṛṣṭa evandharmakaḥ padārthaḥ vaināśika siddhāntāt gacchan śayānaḥ ādi jāti nyāyāt dharmakaḥ padārdhaḥ pramāṇena avagataḥ deśa kāla avasthā antareṣu dharmaka dharmaka vyabhicarati pramāṇa vyavahāraḥ lupyeta nyāya sāṅkhyamīmāṃsa kādayaḥ asaṃsāriṇaḥ abhāvam yukti śataiḥ pratipādayanti saṃsāriṇaḥ jagat utpatti laya kriyā kartṛtva vijñānasya abhāvāt ayuktam mahatā prapañcena sthāpitam bhavatā śabda ādi bhuj saṃsāri avasthā antara viśiṣṭaḥ jagata jagat utpatti laya kriyā kartṛtva śakti sādhana abhāvaḥ pratyakṣaḥ saṃsāriṇaḥ asmad ādiḥ saṃsārī cintayitum aśakyam ādi vinyāsa viśiṣṭam jagat nirminuyāt ayuktam śāsrāt śāsram saṃsāriṇaḥ jagat utpatti ādi darśayati śraddheyam pakṣaḥ sarvajñaḥ asaṅgaḥ sajjate antaryāmi puruṣāt ya vijaraḥ vimṛtyuḥ agra duḥkhena bāhyaḥ ityādi śruti śatebhyaḥ smṛteḥ prabhavaḥ mattaḥ pravartate asaṃsārī śruti smṛti nyāyebhyaḥ kāraṇam jagataḥ nan vevam ātmana itisaṃsāriṇa utpattim darśayati uktam ya hṛdaya parasya prakṛta ātmana yuktaḥ parasya parāmarśaḥ i praśnasya prativacana tvenā akāśa śabda vācyaḥ uktaḥ ya hṛdaya śeta satā somya sampannaḥ hara hargacchanti vidanti prājñenā atmanā sampariṣvaktaḥ saṃpratiṣṭhate ityādi śrutibhya niścīyate daharaḥ antara prastutya atma śabda prayogāt prakuta yuktam ātmana paramātmana saṃsāriṇaḥ sṛṣṭi saṃhāra jñāna sāmarthya abhāvam avotāma avedaham asmī prastutā viṣayañca bravāṇī jñapayiṣyāmī prārabdham asaṃsāri jagataḥ kāraṇam aśanāya ādi atītam nitya śuddha mukta svabhāvam viparītaḥ saṃsārī gṛhṇīyāt nikṛṣṭaḥ saṃsārya tvena smaran doṣa bhāj yuktam puṣpa udaka añjali stuti namaskāra bali upahāra svādhyāya dhyāna yoga ādibhiḥ ār irādhayiṣeta ārādhanena īśitṛ asaṃsāri saṃsārya tvena cintayet śīta tvenā akāśam mūrtimatvena ātmatva pratipādakam śāsram artha vādaḥ bhaviṣyati tarkaśāsra nyāyaiḥ avirodhaḥ mantra brāhmaṇa vādebhyaḥ praveśa śravaṇāt cakra prakṛtya āviśadi vicitya dhoraḥ abhivadan śākhāsu sahasraśas mantra vādāḥ sṛṣṭi kartuḥ asaṃsāriṇaḥ praveśam darśayanti brāhmaṇa vādāḥ anuprāviśat sīmānam vidārya dvārā prāpadyata devatemāsti satraḥ jīvenā atmanā gūḍha prakāśate ityādyāḥ śrutiṣu brahmaṇi śabda prayogāt śabdasya pratyagātmā abhidhāyaka antarātmā paramātma vyatirekeṇa saṃsāriṇaḥ abhāvāt advitīyam ityādi śrutibhyaḥ yuktam avadhārayitum sthitaḥ śāsra arthaḥ paramātmanaḥ saṃsaritvam sati śāsra anarthakyama saṃsāri tve upadeśa ānarthakyam spaṣṭaḥ doṣaḥ paramātmā antarātmā samparka janita duḥkhāni spaṣṭam parasya saṃsāri prāptam parasya asaṃsāritva pratipādikāḥ śrutayaḥ kupyeran smṛtayaḥ nyāyāḥ kathañcid sambandha jaiḥ duḥkhaiḥ sambadhyata śakyam pratipādayitum paramātmanaḥ sādhya parihārya abhāvāt upadeśa anarthakya doṣaḥ śakyate nivārayitum kecid parihāram paramātmā anupraviṣṭaḥ vikāra bhāvam āpannaḥ parasmāt ananyaḥ saṃsāritva sambandhī ananyaḥ avadhāraṇa arhaḥ aviruddham bhaviṣyati vikāra pakṣe etā gatayaḥ dravya vadane kadravya samāhārasya sāvayavasya paramātmana deśa vipariṇāmaḥ ghaṭa ādivat saṃsthāna avasthasya parasya vikriyate keśoṣara ādivat pariṇamet kṣīra ādivat samāna jātīya aneka dravya samūhasya dravya viśeṣaḥ samāna jātīya upacaritam paramārthataḥ sati siddhānta virodhaḥ nitya ayuta siddha avayava anugataḥ avayavī avasthasya saṃsārī avayava anugata avayavina avayava gataḥ doṣaḥ guṇa saṃsāritva doṣeṇa sambadhyata aniṣṭā kalpanā kṣīravat pariṇāma pakṣe śruti smṛti kopaḥ aniṣṭaḥ niṣkalam niṣkriyam śāntam divyaḥ amūrtaḥ bāhya abhyantaraḥ ākāśavat gataḥ kadācid avyaktaḥ ityādi śruti smṛti nyāya viruddhā pakṣāḥ acalasya paramātmana deśa pakṣe phalavat deśa saṃsaraṇa anupapattiḥ parasya saṃsāri uktam parasya visphuliṅgavat sphuṭitaḥ saṃsarati parasya avayava sphuṭanena kṣata prāptiḥ saṃsaraṇe paramātmanaḥ pradeśa antara avayava vyūhe chidra prāptiḥ avraṇatva vākya virodhaḥ avayava saṃsaraṇe paramātma śūnya pradeśa abhāvāt avayava antara nodana vyūhanābhyām hṛdaya śūlena paramātmanaḥ duḥkhitva prāptiḥ visphuliṅga ādi dṛṣṭānta doṣa jñāpaka śāsram padārthān anyathā kartum pravṛttam yathābhūtānām ajñātānām jñāpane kiñcātas śṛṇu bhūtā mūrta amūrta ādi padārtha prasiddhāḥ dṛṣṭānta upādānena avirodhi vastu jñāpayitum pravṛttam śāsram laukika vastu virodha jñāpanāya laukika vastu virodha jñāpanāya laukikam dṛṣṭāntam upādatte upādīyamānaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ anarthakaḥ dārṣṭa antikā saṅgateḥ hyāgniḥ śīta dṛṣṭānta śatena pratipādayitum śakyam pramāṇa anyathā adhigata vastunaḥ pramāṇam pramāṇa virudhyate pramāṇa antara aviṣayam pramāṇa jñāpayati laukika padārtha āśrayaṇa vyatirekeṇa āgamena śakyam ajñātam vastu avagamayitum prasiddha nyāyam anusara śakyā paramātmanaḥ avayava aṃśa aṃśitva kalpanā paramārthataḥ pratipādayitum kṣudrā visphuliṅgāḥ aṃśaḥ śrūyate smaryate ekatva pratyaya artha paratvāt visphuliṅgaḥ ekatva pratyaya arhe aṃśoṃ aśina ekatva pratyaya arhaḥ sati paramātma vikāra aṃśatva vācakāḥ śabdāḥ paramātma vikāra aṃśatva vācakāḥ śabdāḥ paramātmā ekatva pratyaya ādhitsavaḥ upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām upaniṣatsu pratijñāya dṛṣṭāntaiḥ hetubhiḥ paramātmanaḥ vikāra aṃśa ādi jagataḥ pratipādya pratijñāya utpatti laya hetu dṛṣṭāntaiḥ vikāra vikāritva ādi ekatva pratyaya hetūn pādya upasaṃhariṣyati upakrama upasaṃhariṣyati upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām arthaḥ niścīyate paramātmā ekatva pratyaya draḍhimna utpatti laya pratipādakāni vākyāni anyathā vākya bheda prasaṅgāt upaniṣatsu paramātmanā ekatva pratyayaḥ vidhīyata avipratipattiḥ vādinām vidhi vākya yoge utpatti ādi vākyānām pramāṇam phala kalpayitavyam utpatti ādi śrutaya ekatva pratipādana sampradāya vida ākhyāyikām sampracakṣate rāja pitraḥ jāta mātra pitṛbhyām apaviddhaḥ vyādha saṃvardhitaḥ amuṣya vaṃśyatām ajānan vyādha jāti pratyayaḥ vyādha jāti anuvartate rāja jāti anuvartate kāruṇikaḥ rāja putrasya rāja śrī prāpti yogyatām jānan amuṣya bodhayati vyādhaḥ amuṣya rājñaḥ kathañcid vyādha gṛham anupraviṣṭaḥ bodhitaḥ tyaktvā vyādha jāti pratyaya pitṛpaitāmahīm padavīm anuvartate parasmāt visphuliṅga ādivat jātiḥ vibhakta deha indriya ādi asaṃsārī deha indriya ādi saṃsāra anuvartate deha indriya saṅghātaḥ kṛśaḥ sthūlaḥ sukhī duḥkhī paramātma ajānan ātmakaḥ āsya saṃsārī pratibodhita ācāryeṇa hitvā traya anuvṛttim rāja putrasya rāja pratyayavat pratyayaḥ dṛḍhībhavati visphuliṅgava parasmāt bhraṣṭa ukte visphuliṅgasya bhraṃśāt ekatva darśanāt ekatva pratyaya dārḍhyāya suvarṇa maṇi loha visphuliṅga dṛṣṭāntāḥ utpatti ādi bheda pratipādana dhanavat prajñapti nairantarya avadhāraṇāt citra paṭavat vṛkṣa samudra ādivat utpatti ādi aneka vicitra vijigrāhayiṣitā ghanavat upasamahariṣyat prāyokṣyata ya anā nindā vacanam ekatva pratyaya dārḍhyāya anteṣu utpatti laya ādi kalpanā pratyaya karaṇāya niravayavasya paramātmanaḥ asaṃsāriṇaḥ saṃsāri deśa kalpanānyāyyā svatas adeśa paramātmanaḥ adeśasya parasya deśa saṃsāritva kalpanāyām saṃsārī kalpitam bhavet upādhikṛta parasya ghaṭa karaka ādi ākāśavat vivekinām paramātmā saṃvyavahāra bhāj buddhiḥ utpadyate avivekinām vivekinām upacaritā buddhiḥ dṛṣṭā vivekinām mithyā buddhi vivekinām saṃvyavahāra mātra ālambana artha kṛṣṇaḥ raktaḥ vivekinām kadācid kṛṣṇa rakta saṃvyavahāra mātra ālambana artha pratipadyata paramārthataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ raktaḥ bhavitum paṇḍitaiḥ svarūpa pratipatti viṣaye brahmaṇoṃ aśāṃśi deśa deśi vikāra vikāritva kalpanā kāryā kalpanā apanayana artha sāra paratvāt upaniṣadām hitvā kalpanām nirviśeṣa pratipattavyā ākāśavat gataḥ duḥkhena bāhyaḥ ityādi śruti śatebhyaḥ vilakṣaṇam kalpayet uṣṇa ātmaka śīta deśam prakāśa ātmake savitari deśam kalpanā apanayana artha sāra paratvāt upaniṣadām upādhi nimittā asaṃsāra dharmiṇi vyavahārāḥ vicitya abhivadan evamādi mantra varṇebhyaḥ svata saṃsāri alaktaka ādi upādhi saṃyoga janita rakta sphaṭika ādi buddhivat bhrāntam paramārthataḥ tiṣṭhantam śuni śvapāke ityādi śruti smṛti nyāyebhyaḥ paramātmanaḥ asaṃsāritā ata vikāraḥ śaktiḥ vikalpayitum niravayavatva abhyupagame viśeṣataḥ śakyate aṃśa ādi śruti smṛti vādāḥ ekatva arthāḥ bheda pratipādakāḥ vivakṣita artha vākya yogāt avocāma upaniṣadām paramātmā ekatva jñāpana paratve kimartham pratikūlor athaḥ bhedaḥ parikalpyata kāṇḍa prāmāṇya virodha parihārāya ekeca pratipādakāni vākyāni aneka kriyā kāraka phala bhoktṛ kartrāśrayāṇi bheda abhāve asaṃsāriṇa paramātmana ekatve iṣṭa phalāsu kriyāsu pravartayeyuḥ aniṣṭa phala abhyaḥ kriyā abhyaḥ nivartayeyuḥ baddhasya mokṣāya upaniṣadā ārabhyeta paramātmā ekatvau ādi pakṣe paramātmā ekatva upadeśaḥ upadeśa grahaṇa phalam baddhasya bandha nāśāya upadeśaḥ abhāva śa asram nirviṣayam ādi pakṣasya kāṇḍava ādi pakṣeṇa codya parihārayoḥ bheda abhāve kāṇḍam nirālambanam labhte prāmāṇyam prāmāṇye sva artha vidhātaḥ kāṇḍasya prāmāṇyam upaniṣadām prāmāṇya kalpanāyām sva artha vighātaḥ bhavet prāmāṇyam kāṇḍam pramāṇam apramāṇam bhavitum pradīpaḥ prakāśyam prakāśayati prakāśayati ādi pramāṇa vipratiṣedhāt kevalam pratipādayantyaḥ sva artha vighātam kāṇḍa prāmāṇya vighātam ādi niścita bheda pratipatti artha pramāṇaiḥ virudhyante aprāmāṇyam upaniṣadām anya artha vāstu ekatva pratipatti artha uttara pramāṇasya pramāṇa apramāṇa pramā utpādana anutpādana nimitm anyathā stambha ādīnām prāmāṇya prasaṅgāt śabda ādau prameye kiñcātas ekatva pratipatti pramām apramāṇam bhaveyuḥ vaktavyaḥ prāmāṇya pratiṣedha vākyam prāmāṇya pratiṣedham prakāśam bhavatu pratiṣedha pramāṇam vākyam prakāśa bhavet pratiṣedha vākya prāmāṇye upaniṣadām prāmāṇyam bhavantaḥ bruvantu parihāra nanu pratyatrā mada avākya prāmāṇya pratiṣedha artha pratipattiḥ prakāśana pratipattiḥ pramā pradveṣaḥ ekatva pratyaye pramām pratyakṣam kurvati iṣu upalabhyamānāsu pratiṣedha anupapatteḥ ādi nivṛttiḥ pratyakṣam phalam ekatva pratipatti pāramparya janitam avocāma uttara upaniṣadam pratyaprāmāṇya śaṅkā uktam sva artha vighāta kara aprāmāṇyam artha pratipatteḥ bādhaka abhāvāt upaniṣadbhyaḥ advitīyam pratipattiḥ uṣṇaḥ śītaḥ vākyāt viruddha artha dvaya pratipattiḥ abhyupagamya avocāma vākya prāmāṇya samaya nyāyaḥ ekasya vākyasya aneka artha sati aneka artha tve sva arthaḥ vighāta viruddhaḥ anyor athaḥ vākya pramāṇakānām viruddham aviruddham vākyam anekam pratipādayati samayaḥ artha vyeka vākyatā kānicid vākyāni ekatva pratiṣedham laukikam vākyam uṣṇaḥ śītaḥ vākyatā deśasya pramāṇa antara viṣaya anuvādi śīta vākyam uṣṇa pramāṇa antara anubhava smārakam artha avabodhakam śīta vākyatā pramāṇa antara anubhava smāraṇena upakṣīṇa viruddha artha pratipādakam vākyam śīta uṣṇa padābhyām padasā mānādhikaraṇya prayoga nimittā bhrāntiḥ ekasya vākyasya aneka artha laukikasya vaidikasya uktam kāṇḍa prāmāṇya vighāta vākyam anya artha ekatva pratipādana iṣṭa artha prāptau sādhana upadeśam niyogam vārayanti aneka arthatva anupapatteḥ kāṇḍa vākyānām sva arthe pramā utpadyate asādhāraṇe sva arthe pramām utpādayati vākyam kutaḥ virodhaḥ tve nirviṣaya pramāna utpadyata pramāyāḥ darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām svarga yajeta hantavyaḥ evamādi vākyebhyaḥ pratyakṣā pramā jāyamānā bhaviṣyati bodhayiṣyanti anumānam anumānam virodhe prāmāṇyam labhate pramā utpadyata prāptasya avidyā pratyupasthāpitasya kriyā kāraka phalasya āśrayaṇena iṣṭa aniṣṭa prāpti parihāra upāya sāmānye pravṛttasya viśeṣam ajānataḥ ācakṣāṇā śrutiḥ kriyākāraka phala bhedasya prasiddhasya asatya ācaṣṭe vārayati iṣṭa aniṣṭa phala prāpti parihāra upāya vidhi paratvāt kāmyeṣu pravṛttā śrutiḥ kāmānām mithyājñāna prabhava tve sati yathāprāptān upādāya sādhanāni vidhatte kāmānām mithyājñāna prabhava anartha vidadhāti nitya agnihotra ādi śāsram mithyājñāna prabhavam kriyākāraka bhedam yathāprāptam iṣṭa viśeṣa prāptim aniṣṭa viśeṣa parihāram prayojanam paśyat hotra ādīni vidhatte avidyā gocarāsa dvastu viṣayam pravartate kāmyeṣu puruṣā pravarteḥ vidyāvantaḥ dṛṣṭa kāminaḥ vidyāvatām adhikāra ekatva adhikāra virodhasya tve nirviṣaya upadeśena grahaṇa phala abhāva doṣa parihāra uktaḥ veditavyaḥ icchā rāga ādi vaicitryāt anekā puruṣāṇam icchāḥ rāga ādayaḥ doṣā vicitrāḥ bāhya viṣaya rāga ādi apahṛta cetasaḥ śāsram nivartayitum śaktam nā svabhāvataḥ bāhya viṣaya virakta cetasaḥ viṣayeṣu pravartayitum śaktam kintu śāsrāt iṣṭa sādhanam aniṣṭa sādhanam sādhya sādhana sambandha viśeṣa abhivyaktiḥ pradīpa ādivat ādi jñānam śāsram bhṛtyān balāt nivartayati niyojayati dṛśyante puruṣā rāga ādi gauravāt śāsram atikrāmantaḥ ati vaicitryam apekṣya sādhya sādhana sambandha viśeṣān anekadhā upadiśati yathāruci sādhana viśeṣeṣu pravartante śāsram savitṛ pradīpa ādivat udāsta kasyacid arthaḥ apuruṣa arthavat avabhāsate avabhāsaḥ tathārūpam anurūpāṇi sādhanāni upāditsate artha vādaḥ ityādiḥ jñāpayiṣyantaḥ vedāntā vidhi śāsrasya bādhakāḥ vidhi śāsram nirviṣayam kāraka ādi bhedam vidhi śāsram upaniṣadām prāmāṇyam nivartayati sva viṣaya śūrāṇi pramāṇāni ādivat paṇḍitaṃmanyāḥ kecid sva citta vaśāt pramāṇam itaretara viruddham tachā ādi virodham codayanti tve śabda ādayaḥ ādi viṣayā bhinnāḥ pratyakṣata upalabhyante bruvatām virodhaḥ sya at ādibhiḥ śabda ādi upalabdhāraḥ kartāraḥ adharmayoḥ pratiśarīram bhinnā anumīyante saṃsāriṇaḥ bruvatām anumāna virodhaḥ āgama virodham grāma yajeta paśu yajeta svarga yajeta evamādi vākyebhyaḥ grāma paśu svarga ādi sādhana ādi anuṣṭhātāraḥ bhinnā avagamyante ucyate kutarka dūṣita antaḥkaraṇā brāhmaṇa ādi varṇa apasadā anukampanīyā āgama artha vicchinna sampradāya buddhaya ādi dvāraiḥ śabda ādibhiḥ pratyakṣata upalabhyamānaiḥ brahmaṇa virudhyata vaktavyāḥ śabda ādīnām bhedena virudhyata viruddhyate virodhaḥ uktam pratiśarīram śabda ādi upalabdha āraḥ adharmayoḥ kartāraḥ bhinnā anumīyante tve anumāna virodha bhinnā kaiḥ anumīyanta praṣṭavyāḥ brūyuḥ asmābhiḥ anumāna kuśalaiḥ yūyam anumāna kuśalā pṛṣṭānām uttaram indriya mana ātmasu pratyekam anumāna kauśala pratyākhyāne indriya sādhanā anumāna kuśalāḥ aneka kāraka sādhya kriyāṇām anumāna kauśalebhavatām anekatva prasaṅgaḥ aneka kāraka sādhyā kriyā bhavadbhiḥ abhyupagatam anumānam kriyā indriya mana sādhanaiḥ kārakaiḥ kartṛkā nirvartyata pratijñātam anumāna kuśalā vadadbhiḥ indriya sādhanā pratyekam aneka abhyupagatam ahaḥ anumāna kauśalam darśitam apuccha śṛṅgaiḥ tārkika balī vardaiḥ mūḍhaḥ gatam jānīyāt anuminoti liṅgena svatas bheda pratipādakam liṅgena bhedam sādhayet liṅgāni bheda sādhanāya rūpavanti upanyasyanti gatāni upādhaya ghaṭa karaka apavaraka chidrāṇi bheda bheda labheta paratas viśeṣam abhyupagacchadbhiḥ tārkika śataiḥ bheda darśayitum śakyate svatas dūrāt apanītam aviṣaya tvena abhyupagacchati anyatva abhyupagamāt rūpayoḥ nirvahitā vyākaravāṇi utpatti pralaya ātmake vilakṣaṇam anumānasya aviṣaya kutaḥ anumāna virodhaḥ āgama virodhaḥ pratyuktaḥ uktam tve yasmā upadeśaḥ upadeśa grahaṇa phalam abhāvāt ekatva upadeśa ānarthakyam aneka kāraka sādhya kriyāṇām udyaḥ brahmaṇi nirupādhike upadeśaḥ upadeṣṭā upadeśa grahaṇa phalam upaniṣadām ānarthakyam abhyupagatam aneka kāraka viṣaya ānarthakyam codyate svatas ñabhyupagama virodhāt vādinām tārkika cāṭa bhaṭa praveśyam durgam alpabuddhi agamyam śāsra guru prasāda rahitaiḥ madāmadam mad devaiḥ vicikitsitam tarkeṇa matiḥ āpaneyā vara prasāda labhyatva śruti smṛti vādebhyaḥ ejati ejati dūre vantike ityādi viruddha samavāyitva prakāśaka mantra varṇebhyaḥ gītāsu mad sthāni vyāna varuṇaddhi śīrṣaṇyāḥ prāṇā viṣaya upalabdhi dvārāṇi prabhavā viṣaya rāgāḥ sahaja bhrātṛvyāḥ sva sthām dṛṣṭim viṣaya viṣayām dveṣṭāraḥ bhrātṛvyāḥ pratyak īkṣaṇa pratiṣedha kara kāṭhake uktam parāñci khāni vyatṛṇat svayambhūḥ parāṅpaśyati antarātman ityādi śiśva ādīn yāthātmyam avadhārayati bhrātṛ vyāna varuṇaddhi apāvṛṇoti vināśayati phala abhimukhībhūtāya madhye liṅga pañcadhā āviṣṭaḥ pāṇḍara uktaḥ prabhṛtīni karaṇāni viṣaktāni śaṅku ni darśanāt viṣayeṣu itara karaṇavat apaṭutva at sādhānam uktam śiśoḥ vatsa sthānīyasya karaṇa ātmana kārya ātmakam ādhīyate śiśoḥ adhiṣṭhānam karaṇāni adhiṣṭhitāni labdha ātmakāni upalabdhi dvārāṇi viṣaktāni darśitam ajāta śatruṇā upasaṃhṛteṣu karaṇeṣu ayaḥ upalabhyate deśa vyūḍheṣu karaṇeṣu maya upalabhamāna upalabhyate darśitam pāṇi peṣa pratibodhanena pradeśa viśeṣeṣu pratyādhīyata pāna janita aśaktiḥ paryāyaḥ bala avaṣṭambhaḥ darśanāt avaṣṭambha pakṣapātī kecid bhuktam pariṇamate ya sthūlaḥ pariṇāmaḥ dvayam mūtram purīṣam ādi śiśu sañjñakam kāraṇam upajanayat sthūṇa ākhya m pāśavat sadāmavat śarīrayoḥ nibandhanam akṣitaya upatiṣṭhantetam karaṇa ātmakam prāmam bandhanam cakṣuṣyūḍham etā vakṣyamāṇāḥ saṅkhyākā akṣiti hetu mantra karaṇe tiṣṭhatiḥ upapūrva īpadī abhidhānāni mantra sthānīyāni karaṇā ni tiṣṭhateḥ ātmanepadam viruddham kāḥ prasiddhāḥ akṣat nakṣaṇi lohitā rekhāḥ dvāra bhūtābhiḥ madhyamam anugataḥ akṣat nakṣaṇya dhūma ādi saṃyogena abhivyajyamānāḥ dvāra bhūtābhiḥ ñanugata upatiṣṭhata arthaḥ bhūtaḥ parjanye ānandinaḥ prāṇā śruti antarāt dṛś chaktiḥ kanīnakayā dvāreṇa madhyamam pakṣmaṇa adharatva sāmānyāt bhūtāḥ santatam phalam ya arthe mantraḥ camasa ityādiḥ mantra ācaṣṭe śrutiḥ camasa ityādiḥ mantra ācaṣṭe śrutiḥ camasa budhna camasa camasa ākāram mukhasya bila śirasaḥ budhna ākāra viśvarūpam śirasi viśvarūpam prāṇā ādayaḥ vāyavaḥ saptadhā prasṛtā mantraḥ śabda ādi jñāna hetu tīra parispanda ātmakāḥ ta prāṇau mantraḥ saṃvādam kurvatī hetum saṃvitta dakṣiṇaḥ uttaraḥ viparyayeṇa cakṣuṣī upadiśan uttaram viparyayeṇa upadiśan dakṣiṇaḥ puṭaḥ uttaraḥ pūrvavat adana kriyā yogāt saptamaḥ prasiddham attṛ adattiḥ ucyate jātasya atri nirvacana ādattā atta annena pratipadyata uktam ya uktam prāṇayāthātmyam bhū aādhāna pratyādhāna gataḥ bhoktā bhojyam bhojyād vyāvartata arthaḥ brāhmaṇam dvi pañcabhūta janita kārya karaṇa sambaddham mūrta amūrta ākhyam martya svabhāvam janita vāsanā sarvan jñam śakti upākhyam kriyā kāraka phala ātmakam vyavahāra āspadam vigata upādhi viśeṣam samyak darśana viṣayam ajam ajaram manasayoḥ aviṣayam advaita aneti nirdiśyate apoha dvāreṇa aneti nirdiśyate vāvaśabdaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ arthaḥ paramātmanaḥ rūpyate yābhyāma avidyā adhyāropyamāṇābhyām tathāmūrtam arthaḥ antarṇītasvātma viśeṣaṇe mūrta amūrte avadhāri kāni viśeṣaṇāni mūrta amūrtayoḥ maraṇa dharmi viparītam paricchinnam gati pūrvakam sthāsnu vyāpi aparicchinnam sthita viparītam viśeṣyamāṇa āsādhāraṇa viśeṣavat tyat viparītam atyat abhidhāna arham mūrcchita avayavam itaretara anupraviṣṭa avayavam ghanam saṃhatam arthaḥ dvayāt pariśeṣāt ādi mūrta ākhyam maraṇa dharmi paricchinnam artha samprayujyamānam virudhyate ghaṭaḥ stambha kuṇḍya ādinā paricchinnam artha antara sambandhi tator antara virodhāt viśeṣya māṇāsa ādhāraṇa dharmavat paricchinnam paricchinna mūrta martya sthita anyonya avyabhicārāt caturṇām dharmāṇām yatheṣṭam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ hetu hetum at bhāvaḥ darśayitavyaḥ sarvathā catuṣṭaya viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭam caturṇām gṛhīte viśeṣaṇe itarat viśeṣaṇam catuṣṭaya viśeṣaṇasya trayasya arthaḥ sāra arthaḥ trayāṇām sāriṣṭhaḥ savitā sārāṇi yata kṛta vibhajyamāna viśeṣaṇāni ādhidaivikasya kāryasya savitā trayasya mūrtaḥ savitā sāriṣṭhaḥ yadtva adhidaivikam karaṇam maṇḍalasya abhyantaram vakṣyāmaḥ adhunā ucyate pariśeṣitam dvayam amūrta avirudhyamānam kenacid amaraṇa dharmi sthita viparītam vyāpi aparicchinnam ayat aetat apravibhajyamāna viśeṣam tyat atyat abhidhāna arham pūrvavat yata catuṣṭaya viśeṣaṇasya yaeṣa karaṇa ātmakaḥ hiraṇyagarbhaḥ abhidhīyate dvayasya pūrvavat sāriṣṭhaḥ sāram cāmūrtam dvayamhairaṇyagarbha liṅga ārambhāya dvaya abhivyaktiḥ avyākṛtāt arthyāt sāram dvayam maṇḍala maṇḍalavat sāraḥ dvayasya maṇḍala sthasya dvayasya sādharmyam yuktam prasiddhavat vetu upādānam kāraṇam hiraṇyagarbha cetana kecid hiraṇyagarbha antarikṣayoḥ prayoktṛ ādhāram prayoktṛ sva antarikṣayoḥ prayoktā tayaḥ kāraṇam ucyata mūrta atulya trayasya trayasya traya samāna jātīyam cetanaḥ mūrtayoḥ bhūtayoḥ samāna jātīyena amūrtasena yuktam bhavitum vākya pravṛtteḥ tulya mūrta amūrte catuṣṭaya dharmavatī vibhajyete rasavatoḥ mūrta amūrtayoḥ tulyena nyāyena yuktaḥ vibhāgaḥ vaiśasam mūrta rase maṇḍala upādhiḥ cetanaḥ vivakṣyata atyalpam ucyate sarvatra mūrta amūrtayoḥ vivakṣita acetane anupapanna pakṣa puccha ādi viśiṣṭasya liṅgasya śabda darśanāt prajanayitum karavāma ta akurvan ādau maya ādiṣu śruti antare śabda prayogāt upasaṃhāraḥ adhyātma vibhāga ukti arthaḥ adhunā mūrtā mūrtayoḥ vibhāga ucyate cavāyoḥ antarabhyantare dvayam varjayitvā ārambhakam ityādi pūrveṇa ādhyātmikasya ārambhakasya kāryasya sāraḥ sāreṇa sāravat samastam maṇḍalena prāthamyāt cakṣuṣī prathame sambhavataḥ sambhavata niranartatā liṅgāt taijasam sāram taijasam sāram ādhyātmikam mūrtatva sāra tve hetu arthaḥ adhunā ucyate pariśeṣitam dvayam antarātman pūrvavat sāraḥ viśeṣa grahaṇam śāstra liṅgasya akṣṇi viśeṣataḥ adhiṣṭhātṛ śāsatrasya pratyakṣam śrutiṣu prayoga darśanāt pūrvavat viśeṣataḥ agrahaṇāt amūrtatva sāra tve hetu arthaḥ karaṇa liṅgasya vakṣyāmaḥ vāsanā mayam mūrta amūrta vāsanā maya saṃyoga janitam vicitram paṭa bhitti citravat māya indrajāla mṛga tṛṣṇikā upamam vyāmoha āspadam mātram vādinaḥ vaināśikā bhrāntāḥ vāsanā paṭa rūpavat dravyasya guṇa naiyāyikā vaiśeṣikāḥ sampratipannāḥ triguṇam svatantram pradhāna āśrayam arthena hetunā pravartata sāṅkhyāḥ aupaniṣadaṃmanyā kecid prakriyām racayanti mūrta amūrta rāśiḥ paramātma rāśiḥ uttamaḥ tṛtīyaḥ kartrā bhoktrā mayena ajāta śatru pratibodhitena samudāyaḥ prayoktā karmarāśiḥ prayojyaḥ uktaḥ mūrta amūrta rāśiḥ sādhanam tārkikaiḥ sandhim liṅga āśrayaḥ rāśiḥ tatasrasyantaḥ sāṅkhyatva bhayāt karmarāśiḥ puṣpa āśraya gandhaḥ puṣpa viyoge puṭa taila āśrayaḥ tadvat liṅga viyoge paramātmā deśam āśrayati paramātmā anyata āgatena guṇena guṇaḥ nirguṇaḥ bhoktā badhyate mucyate vaiśeṣika cittam anusaranti rāśiḥ rāśeḥ āgantukaḥ svatas nirguṇa paramātma deśatva at svata utthitā avidyā anāgantukā ūṣara vadanātma kalpanayā sāṅkhya cittam anuvartante tārkikaiḥ sāmañjasya kalpanayā ramaṇīyam lopa niṣad siddhāntam nyāya virodham uktā sāva yava tve paramātmanaḥ saṃsāritva vraṇatva phala deśa saṃsāritva vraṇatva phala deśa saṃsaraṇa anupapatti ādayaḥ doṣāḥ nitya bhede ekatva anupapattiḥ paramātmana upacarita deśa tvena kalpitam ghaṭa karaka bhū chidra ādivat liṅga viyoge paramātma deśa āśrayaṇam vāsanāyāḥ avidyāyāṣca svata utthānam ūṣaravat ityādi kalpanā anupapannā deśa vyatirekeṇa vāsanāyā vastu antara sañcaraṇam kalpayitum śakyam śrutayaḥ saṅkalpaḥ kāmā ityādyāḥ śrutīnām śrutādartha antara kalpanā nyāyyā brahmatva upapādana artha mātra artha upakṣaya upaniṣadām śruti artha kalpanā kuśalāḥ anyathā arthaḥ bhavatu dveṣaḥ adva rāśi traya pakṣe samañjasam mūrta amūrte janita vāsanāḥ mūrta amūrte rūpi antarāletadā anukūlam avadhāraṇam anyathā deśasya kalpyam paramātmanaḥ dvāreṇa dvivacanam asamañjasam vāsanābhiḥ bahuvacanam yuktataram mūrta amūrte vāsanāḥ mūrta amūrte paramātmanaḥ vāsanāḥ ātmana dvāreṇa vikriyamāṇasya paramātmanaḥ uyuktiḥ anarthikā vāsanāyā dvāra aviśiṣṭa vastu antara dvāreṇa vikriyata mukhyayā vṛttyā śakyam kalpayitum paramātmanaḥ vastu kalpanāyām siddhānta hānāt artha mūḍhānām sva citta prabhavā evamādi kalpanā akṣara bāhyāḥ akṣara bāhyaḥ arthaḥ artha upakārī nirapekṣa vedasya prāmāṇyam rāśi traya kalpanā asamañjasā ayaḥ liṅga prastutaḥ adhyātme adhidaive aya atasya prakṛta upādānāt upādīyate nanu mayasya rupāṇi mayasya prakṛta atasya prakṛta upādānāt mayasya arūpi tvena vijijñāpayiṣita ya di mayasya māhārajana ādīni syuḥ ava aneti aityana ākhyeya nanu anyasya āsādeśaḥ mayasya ṣaṣṭha upasaṃhārāt vijñāta āram mayam prastutya vijñāpayiṣyāmi pratijñāyā arthavat mayasya asaṃvyavahāryam svarūpam jñāpayitum pradhvasta upādhi viśeṣam pratijñā arthavatī jñāpitaḥ śāsra niṣṭhām aneti vyapadiśyate anyadadaḥ viparyayaḥ aātmānam avedaham atasya liṅga śasyai vaitāni paramātma svarūpe vaktavye niravaśeṣam vaktavyam viśeṣa vāsanāḥ tāsām prakṛtasya liṅga ātmana kāni mahārajanam haridrā raktam māhāra ādi viṣaya saṃyoge tādṛśam vāsanā rañjana ākāra mutpadyate cittasya rakta ucyate vasra ādivat pāṇḍu āvikam averidam āvikam ūrṇa ādi pāṇḍuram vāsanā indragopa atyanta raktaḥ vāsanā kvacid viṣaya viśeṣa apekṣayā rāgasya tāratamyam kvacid citta vṛtti apekṣayā bhāsvaram kvacid kasyacid vāsanā pumḍarīkam tadvat vāsanā kasyacid vidyuktam vidyotanam prakāśakam jñāna prakāśa vivṛddhi apekṣayā kasyacid vāsanā upajāyate vāsanā ādiḥ madhyam saṅkhyā nimittaṃvā avadhāryate asaṅkhyeya vāsanāyāḥ vāsanā hetūnām anantyāt ṣaṣṭhe ityādi svarūpa saṅkhyā avadhāraṇa arthā dṛṣṭāntāḥ ayathā māhāra aitya ādayaḥ prakāra pradarśana arthāḥ evamprakārāṇi vāsanā vāsanā abhihitam vidyotanam hiraṇyagarbhasya avyākṛtāt prādurbhavataḥ taḍitvat vyaktiḥ tadīyam vāsanā hiraṇyagarbhasya teva avadhāraṇa arthau khyātiḥ arthaḥ hiraṇyagarbhasya uktam vāsanā rūpamantyam niravaśeṣam sva abhidhāya avocāma svarūpa avadhāraṇa brahmaṇa ārabhyate svarūpa nirdeśa svarūpam nirdekṣyāmaḥ nirdeśaḥ nirdeśaḥ ucyate nirdeśaḥ nanu ābhyām aneti śabdābhyām nirdidikṣitam ucyate upādhi viśeṣa apohena viśeṣaḥ bhedaḥ jātiḥ guṇa dvāreṇa śabda pravṛttiḥ viśeṣaḥ brahmaṇi nirdeṣṭum śakyate spandate viṣāṇi nirdiśyate adhi āropita dvāreṇa nirdiśyate avijñānam avijñāna ghana evamādi śabdaiḥ svarūpam nirdidikṣitam nirasta upādhi viśeṣam śakyate kenacid prakāreṇa nirdeṣṭum abhyupāyaḥ prāpta nirdeśa pratiṣedha dvāreṇa aneti nirdeśaḥ nakāra dvayam vīpsā avyāpti yadyat prāptam niṣidhyate sati anirdiṣṭa parihṛtā anyathā nakāra dvayena prakṛta dvaya pratiṣedhe prakṛtāt pratiṣiddha dvayāt nirdiṣṭam kīdṛśam nivartiṣyate anarthakaḥ nirdeśaḥ vividiṣāyāḥ anivartaka abrahma vākyam aparisamāpta kāla ādi vividiṣā nivartitā upādhi nirākaraṇa dvāreṇa ghanavat ghanam ahaṃbrahma nivartate vividiṣā avasthitā vīpsā nakāra dvayam nanu mahatā yatnena parikara bandham yuktam nirdeśṭum bāḍham aityetasmāt vyāptavya prakārā nakāra dvaya viṣayā nirdiśyante grāmaḥ grāmaḥ ramaṇīya nirdeśanam nirdeśaḥ uktam atasya evaṃprakāreṇa yuktam uktam prāṇā brāhmaṇam maitreyīm sva bhāryām āmantritavān asyan pārivrājya ākhyam āśrama sambodhanam gārhasthyāt āśramāt gantum asmibhava āmi anumatim prārthayāmi kiñcā anyatte dvitīyayā bhāryayā vicchedam pati dvāreṇa yuvayoḥ sambandhasya vicchedam dravya vibhāgam saṃvibhajya yuvām uktā vitarke bhagoḥ sāgara parikṣiptā dhanena kathañcana ākṣepa arthaḥ praśna arthaḥ pūrṇa sādhyena hotra ādinā vyavahitena sambandhaḥ pratyuvāca ākṣepa anumodanam ākṣepa anumodanam praśnaḥ prativacana artha m syā sādhanavatām sukha upāya bhoga sampannam tadvat nāśā sādhyena uktā pratyuvāca kevalam amṛtatva sādhanam amṛtatva sādhanam mahyam sādhye amṛtatva sādhane pratyākhyāte sva abhiprāya sampattau tuṣṭa priyeṣāṭā anukampya asmākam bhavantī citta anukūlam ata ehyāḥ sva upaviśa amṛtatva sādhanam jñānaṃkathayiṣyāmi vyākhyānam kurvataḥ vākyāni arthataḥ niścayena dhyātum amṛtatva sādhanam vairāgyam upadidikṣuḥ pati ādibhyaḥ virāgam utpādayati saṃnyāsāya vaiśabdaḥ prasiddha smaraṇa arthaḥ prasiddham bhartuḥ prayojanāya jāyāyāḥ prayojanāya bhāryāyāḥ jāyāyāḥ ityādi āsanne prīti sādhane vacanam iṣṭatara vairāgyasya grahaṇa muktā anukta prasiddham atat upanyastam vṛtti sthānīyam prapañcitam prīti sādhana gauṇī prītiḥ mukhyā darśana arhaḥ darśana viṣayam āpādayitavyaḥ ācāryata āgamataḥ paḥ cāt tarkataḥ nididhya asitavyaḥ niścayena dhyātavyaḥ śravaṇa manana nididhi āsana sādhanaiḥ nirvartitaiḥ ekatva matāni upagatāni samyak darśanam ekatva viṣayam prasidati anyathā śravaṇa mātreṇa kṣatra ādi nimittam varṇa āśrama ādi lakṣaṇam adhyāropita pratyaya viṣayam kriyā kāraka phala ātmakam avidyā pratyaya viṣayam rajjavāmva sarpa pratyayaḥ upamardana khalvare nanu vidite doṣaḥ vyatirekeṇa vidite śrāvayati brāhmaṇa jātiḥ parādadhyāt parākuryāt ātmana svarūpa vyatirekeṇa brāhmaṇa jātiḥ parādadhyāt abrāhmaṇa jātiḥ anātma svarūpeṇa paramātmā kṣatriya jātiḥ anukrāntāni śrotavya prakṛtaḥ jāyata līyata mayam vyatirekeṇa agrahaṇāt grahītum śakyate cit mātra anugamāt sarvatra cit svarūpa gamyate dṛṣṭānta ucyate dṛṣṭānta ucyate svarūpa vyatirekeṇa agrahaṇam dṛṣṭāntaḥ bherī ādeḥ tāḍyamānasya daṇḍa ādinā bhūtān śabda viśeṣān śabda sāmānyāt niṣkṛṣṭān śabda viśeṣān śaknuyād grahītum śabdā eta śabda viśeṣā śabda sāmānya vyatirekeṇa abhāvāt dunduberāhananam āghātaḥ āghāta viśiṣṭasya śabda sāmānyasya gatā viśeṣā abhavanti ta nirbhidya grahītum śakyante viśeṣa abhāvāt vyatirekeṇa jāgaritayoḥ vastu viśeṣaḥ vyatirekeṇa abhāvaḥ yuktaḥ saṃyojyamānasya āpūryamāṇasya evamādi pūrvavat vīmāyā vādyamānāyāḥ aneka dṛṣṭānta upādānam sāmānya bahutva khyāpana aneke vilakṣaṇāḥ cetana acetana rūpāḥ sāmānya viśeṣāḥ pāramparya gatyā sāmānye antarbhāvaḥ pradarśayitavya śaṅkha śabda sāmānya viśeṣāṇām śabda tve antarbhāvaḥ sāmānya viśeṣa avyatirekāt śakyam avagantum ārdraiḥ edhobhiḥ iddhaḥ prakāram dhūma grahaṇam visphulihgādi pradarśana dhūma visphuliṅga āt ayaḥ vinirgacchanti dṛṣṭāntaḥ paramātmanaḥ prakṛtasya niśvasitam niśvasitam niśvasitam aprayatnena niśvāsaḥ niśvasitam ucyate yadṛgvedaḥ atharva aṅgirasaḥ caturvidham mantra itihāsa urvaśī purūra vasoḥ saṃvāda ādiḥ uru aśī apsarāḥ ityādi brāhmaṇam agra ityādi jana ādyā ityādyāḥ ślokā brāhmaṇa prabhavā mantrāḥ ityādayaḥ vastu saṅgraha vākyāni vede ityādīni mantra vivaraṇāni artha vādāḥ athavā vastu saṅgraha vākya vivaraṇāni caturtha adhyāye aātmā aanyaḥ adhyāya śeṣaḥ mantra vivaraṇāni aṣṭavidham brāhmaṇam mantra brāhmaṇayoḥ grahaṇam niyata racanāvataḥ vidyamānasya vedasya abhivyaktiḥ niśvāsavat buddhi prayatna pūrvakaḥ pramāṇam nirapekṣa sva arthe uktam pratipattavyam śreya icchadbhiḥ jñānam prakāśa vaśā rūpasya vikriyā vyavasthā rūpayoḥ paramātma upādhi bhūtayoḥ vyākriyamāṇayoḥ salila phenavat tattva anya tvena anirvaktavyayoḥ avasthayoḥ saṃsāra nāmna niśvasita uktam vacanena itarasya niśvasitatva siddheḥ athavā dvaita jātasya avidyā viṣaya uktam parādāti dam vedasya aprāmāṇyam āśaṅkyate nivṛtti uktam niśvāsavat aprayatna utthita pramāṇam grantha kevalam utpatti kālayoḥ vyatirekeṇa abhāvāt jagataḥ pralaya jala budbuda phena ādīnām salila vyatirekeṇa abhāvaḥ vyatirekeṇa kāryāṇām līyamānānām abhāvaḥ ghanam pratipattavyam ata pralaya pradarśanāya dṛṣṭāntaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ prakāreṇa nadī ivāpī taḍāga ādi gatānām abdhiḥ gamanam pralayaḥ avibhāga prāptiḥ arthaḥ yathāyām dṛṣṭāntaḥ mṛdu karkaśa kaṭhina picchila ādīnām tvak viṣayam sparśa sāmānya mātram praviṣṭāḥ sparśa viśeṣāḥ āpa samudram vyatirekeṇa abhāva bhūtāḥ saṃsthāna mātrā āsan sparśa sāmānya mātram śabda vācyam saṅkalpe viṣaya sāmānya viṣaya sparśa viśeṣāḥ praviṣṭam vyatirekeṇa abhāva viṣayaḥ buddhi viṣaya sāmānya vyatirekeṇa abhāva bhūtaḥ mātram pare brahmaṇi āpa pralīyate paramparā krameṇa śabda ādau grāhakeṇa karaṇena pralīne upādhi abhāvāt ghanavat ghanam ekarasam nirantaram vyavatiṣṭhate advayam pratipattavyam viśeṣāṇām ghrāṇa viṣaya sāmānyam abviśeṣāṇām viṣaya sāmānyam viṣaya sāmānyam pūrvavat ādi viṣaya sāmānyānām viṣaya sāmānye saṅkalpe viṣaya sāmānyasya buddhi viṣaya sāmānye mātram parasmin pralīyate karmendriyāṇām viṣayā vadana ādāna gamana visarga ānanda viśeṣāḥ kriyā sāmānyeṣu praviṣṭā vibhāga yogyā samudra abviśeṣāḥ sāmānyāni mātram mātram kauṣītakinaḥ adhīyate nanu sarvatra viṣayasya pralayaḥ abhihitaḥ karaṇasya abhiprāya bāḍham kintu viṣaya samāna jātīyam karaṇam śrutiḥ jāti viṣayasya sva grāhaka tvena saṃsthāna karaṇam viśeṣasya saṃsthānam pradīpaḥ karaṇam prakāśane viṣaya viśeṣāṇām sva viśeṣa prakāśaka tvena saṃsthāna antarāṇi karaṇāni pradīpavat karaṇānām pralaye yatnaḥ kāryaḥ viṣaya sāmānya ātmaka viṣaya pralayena pralayaḥ siddhaḥ karaṇānām aidam pratijñātam hetuḥ abhihitaḥ sāmānya ātmaja pralaya utpatti pralaya kāleṣu vyatirekeṇa abhāvāt prajñānam pratijñātam tarkatas sādhitam svābhāvikaḥ pralaya paurāṇikā buddhi pūrvakaḥ pralayaḥ nimittaḥ ātyantika avidyā nirodha dvāreṇa arthaḥ viśeṣa ārambhaḥ dṛṣṭānta upādīyate sindhoḥ vikāraḥ sindhu abhidhīyate syandanāt sindhuḥ vikāraḥ bhavaḥ khila sva arthe pratyayaḥ udeka sindhau sva yonauprastaḥ prakṣiptaḥ vilīyamānam anuvilīya ita bhauma taijasa samparkāt kāṭhinya prāptiḥ khilyasya sva yoni samparkāt apagacchati udakasya vilayanam tadanu vilīyata ucyate khilyasya pūrvavat grahītum samarthaḥ nipuṇaḥ anarthakaḥ samarthaḥ deśā svādayet lavaṇa āsvādam khilyam āvaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ maitreyidam paramātma ākhyam bhūtāt paricchinnā kārya karaṇa upādhi sambandhāt khilyam āvam āpannā martyā janma maraṇa pipāsā ādi saṃsāra dharmavatī kārya ātmikā amuṣya va khilya bhāvaḥ kārya karaṇa bhūna upādhi samparka bhrānti janitaḥ mahati bhūte sva yonau samudrasya ānīye ajare amare abhaye śudve vanavat rase anante apāre nirantare avidyā janita bhrānti meda varjite praveśitaḥ praviṣṭe sva yoni graste khilya bhāve avidyā bheda bhāve praṇāśite advaitam mahattara ādi kāraṇa viṣu kālepu svarūpa adhi abhicārāt pariniṣpannam vaikālikaḥ niṣṭhā pratyayaḥ athavā artha vācī pāramārthikam arthaḥ laukikam māyā himavat ādi parvata upamam artha vastu viśinaṣṭi abhūtam vidyata kadācid āpekṣikam viśinaṣṭaya pāramiti vijñaptiḥ ghana jāti antara pratiṣedha arthaḥ suvarṇa ayaḥ ghana avadhāraṇa arthaḥ anyan jāti antarāle vidyata arthaḥ advaitam paramārthataḥ svaccham saṃsāra duḥkha asampṛttkam kinnimitaḥ khilya bhāva sukhī duḥkhī evamādi lakṣaṇaḥ aneka saṃsāra upadrutaḥ ucyate kārya karaṇa vipaya ākāra pariṇatāni ātmakāni salliphena vudvuda upamāni svacchasya paramātmanaḥ salila upamasya yepām viṣaya paryantānām brahmaṇi artha viveka jñānena pravilāpanam uttakam nadī samudravata etabhyaḥ hetu śabda vācyebhyaḥ khilyavat adbhayaḥ ādi pratibimbaḥ svacchasya sphaṭikasya alattaka ādi upādhibhyaḥ rattka ādi bhāvaḥ kārya karaṇa upādhibhyaḥ viśepa khilya bhāvena samyak utthāya yebhyaḥ bhūtebhya utthitaḥ akārya karaṇa viṣaya ākāra pariṇatāni viśepa ātmakhilya hetu śāstra ācārya upadeśena vidyāyāḥ nadī samudravat pravilāpitāni vinaśyanti salila phena budbuda ādivat vinaśyatsu viśeṣa khilya bhāvaḥ vinaśyati udakālattphaka ādi hetu apanaye sārya sphaṭika ādi pratibimbaḥ vinaśyati ādi svarūpam paramārtha taḥ vyavatiṣṭhate tadvat ghanam svaccham vyavatiṣṭhate viśepa kārya karaṇa saṅghātebhyaḥ vimuttkasya viśeṣa amuṣya kṣetram dhanam sukhī duḥkhī evamādi lakṣaṇā avidyā kṛta avidyāyāḥ cabrahma niranvayataḥ nāśita kutaḥ viśeṣa caitanya svabhāva avasthitasya avasthitasya viśeṣa upapadyate kārya karaṇa vimuttkasya uttkavān artha darśanam maitreyyai bhāryāyai pratibodhitā uvācā uttkavatī etasmitreva vastuni brahmaṇi virudva dharmavattavam ācakṣaṇena bhagavatā pūjāvān am ūmuhat kṛta cān virudva dharmavat utkam ucyate ghana pratiśāya saṃśāsti ghana uṣṇaḥ śītaḥ mūḍha mohanam vākyam bravīm arthaḥ nanu virudva ghanam abhāvam vamiṃṇyamihitam tvayā virudva tvena vastu bhrāntyā uttkam uttkam avidyā pratyupasya apitaḥ kārya karaṇa sambandhī khilya bhāvaḥ nāśite nimittā viśeṣa ādi sambandhinī anyatva darśana lakṣaṇā kārya karaṇa saṅghāta upādhau pravilāpite naśyati hetu abhāvāt udaka ādi ādhāra nāśāt ādi pratibimba stad nimittaḥ prakāśa ādiḥ artha svarūpā nāśavat saṃsāri svarūpasya ghanasya nāśaḥ vijñā ghana uttkam jagataḥ paramārtha taḥ nāśān vināśī vināśī avidya khilya bhāvaḥ ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ śruti antarāt pāramārthikaḥ paryāptam ya yāvi ākhyātam vijñātum ucyate śṛṇu avidyā kalpite kārya karaṇa saṃghāta upādhi janite viśeṣa khilya bhāve at pāramārthataḥ advaite brahmaṇi bhinnam vastu ātmana upalakṣyate nanu dvaitena upamīyamāna dvaitasya pāramārthika avācā arambhaṇam vikāraḥ i ati śruti adekam advitīyam paramātmanaḥ khilya aparama arthaḥ udeḥ udaka ādi pratibimba ghrāta itareṇa dhrāṇena ghrātavyam itara kāraka pradarśana kriyā phalayoḥ abhidhānam chintti udyamya udyamya nipātanam chedasya dvaidhībhāva chinatti ekena abhidhīyate kriyā avasāna kriyā vyatirekeṇa phalasya anupalambhāt ghrāṇa itareṇa ghrāṇena ghratavyam pūrvavat avidyāvat avasthā avidyā nāśam upagamitā tatrā atma vyatirekeṇa anyasya abhāvaḥ ādi pravilāpitam saṃvṛttam karaṇena dhrātavyam paśya udvijānīyāt sarvatra kāraka sādhyā kriyā kāraka abhāve anupapattiḥ kriyāyāḥ kriyā bhāve phala abhāvaḥ avidyāyām satyām kriyā kāraka phala vyavahāraḥ nā atma vyatirekeṇa kārakam kriyā phalam nacānātmā kasyacid anāttma parikalpitam paramārtha ta vyatirekeṇa artha ekatva pratyaye kriyā kāraka phala pratyaya anupapattiḥ virodhāt kriyāṇām sādhanānām antyantam nivṛttiḥ kṣepa vacanam prakāra antara anupapatti darśana kenacid prakāreṇa kriyā karaṇa ādi kāraka anupapatteḥ kenatcit kañcitkāścid cit jivret arthaḥ avidyā avasthāyām karaṇasyavijñeye viniyukta jñātuśva jñeya jijñāsā nā atmani ivā atmā atmanaḥ viṣayaḥ aviṣaye jñātuḥ jñānam upapadyate karaṇena artha vivekinaḥ kevalaḥ advayaḥ vartate vijñāta āram prasiddhā ādi stamba paryantānām prāṇinām kāryam apūpaḥ anekaiḥ madhukaraiḥ nirvartita nirvartitā kāryam yaśva maya śvin mātra prakāśam ayaḥ ayaḥ amaraṇa bhavaḥ pūrvavat liṅga abhimānī upakāra karaṇa tvena caśabda sāmarthyāt catuṣṭayam kāryam kāryam kāraṇa pūrvaka ekasmāt kāraṇāt paramārtha taḥ itarat kāryam arambhaṇam vikāraḥ nāmadheya mātram paryāyāṇām arthaḥ saṃkṣepataḥ pratijñāta maitreyyā amṛtatva sādhanam uktam adhyāya ādau prakṛtam viṣayā ucyata viśeṣataḥ avasthānam viśeṣataḥ avasthānam ārambhaka tvena upakārān antargatānām maya ādīnām karaṇa tvena upakārāt uktam jyotīrūpa mayam adityaḥ śabda pratiśravaṇa velāyām viśeṣataḥ saṃnihitaḥ pratiśrutkāyām pratiśravaṇa velāyām bhavaḥ bhavaḥ stanayitnaḥ śabde bhavaḥ svare viśeṣataḥ akāśaḥ apratyakṣaḥ kāryeṇa prayuktena pratyakṣeṇa vyapadiśyate pratyakṣavat vyākhyātaḥ śruti smṛti lakṣaṇaḥ kṣatra ādīnām niyantā jagataḥ vaicitrya ādīnām pariṇāma hetu prāṇibhiḥ anuṣṭhīyamāna pratyakṣeṇa vyapadeśaḥ dharmayoḥ abhedena nirdeśaḥ śāsra ācāra lakṣaṇayoḥ idda bhedena vyapadeśa ekatve sati dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa bheda kārya ārambhaka adṛṣṭaḥ apūrva ākhyaḥ sāmānya viśeṣa adṛṣṭena kāryam ārabhate sāmānya ādīnām prayoktā viśeṣa kārya karaṇa saṃghātasya ādīnām prayoktari kārya karaṇa saṃghāta kartari bhavaḥ dṛṣṭena anuṣṭhīyamānenā acāra ākhyaḥ dvi prakāra sāmānya viśeṣa sāmānya ādi samavetaḥ viśeṣa kārya karaṇa saṃghāta samaveta ādi samavete vartamāna kriyā kārya karaṇa saṃghāta mavete bhavaḥ āvāti śruti antarāt satyābhyām prayuktaḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghāta viśeṣaḥ jāti viśeṣeṣa saṃyuktaḥ jāti viśeṣaḥ mānuṣa ādiḥ mānuṣa ādi jāti viśiṣṭā nikāyāḥ paraspara upakārya upakāraka bhāvena vartamānā dṛśyante mānuṣa ādi jātiḥ mānuṣa ādi jātiḥ bāhyā adhyātmikī ubhayathā nirdeśa bhāj kārya karaṇa saṃghātaḥ mānuṣa ādi jāti viśiṣṭaḥ nanu śārīra nirdiṣṭaḥ paryāya pārthiva aṃśasya grahaṇāt pratyasta mita adhyātma adhibhūta ādi viśeṣaḥ gaṇa viśiṣṭaḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghātaḥ ucyate ayamūrta ātmakaḥ nirdiśyate deśena ādiṣu nirdiṣṭaḥ adhyātma viśeṣa abhāvāt nirdiśyate pariśiṣṭaḥ ayaḥ arthaḥ deha liṅga saṃghāta ucyate pariśiṣṭaḥ ayaḥ amātmā avidyā kṛta kārya karaṇa saṅghāta upadhi viśiṣṭe vidyāyāḥ artha praveśite uttkaḥ kṛtastraḥ ghana bhūtaḥ sarvairūpāsyaḥ svatantraḥ kumāra mātyavat rājatva viśeṣaṇam rāja ucitaṣṭattim āśritya viśinaṣṭi muttkaḥ uttkam abrahma manuṣyā vedyasmāt vyākhyātam ātmānabheva tvena ācārya gamābhyām śrutvā matvā tarkataḥ darśitam evaṃlakṣaṇāt apibrahema abrahma bheva asarvam tāntu vijñanāt tiraskṛtya parisamāptaḥ śāstra arthaḥ arthaḥ prastutaḥ bhūte vidi jagat samarpitam arthe dṛṣṭānta upādīyate rathena cārāḥ samarpitā prasidvor athaḥ paramātma bhūte vidi ādi stambarī ādayaḥ ādayaḥ praṇā ādayaḥ eta jala candravat anupraveśinaḥ avidyā kalpitāḥ jagat samarpitam uttkam aaham bhāvaḥ vyākhyātaḥ upādhiḥ nirupādhiḥ nirupākhyaḥ ubhayaḥ acalaḥ asthūlaḥ anaṇuḥ evaṃviśeṣaṇaḥ anantaḥ tārkikāḥ kecid paṇḍitaṃmanyāḥ āgama śāstra artha virudvam manyamānā vikalpayantaḥ agādham upayānti manetrau anuvadataḥ anejat javīyaḥ ejati ejati taittirīyake kiñcat gāyan ityādi cchāndogye krīḍa n ramamāṇaḥ sayadi gandhaḥ ityādi āyarvaṇe sarvajñaḥ dūrāta sudūre antike kaṭhavallīṣu aṇoḥ aṇīyān mahīyān madāmadam vāvataḥ anyānatyeti tiṣṭhat gītāsu jagataḥ ādatte kasyacid avimattkam vibhatt kepu grasiṣṇu prabhaviṣṇu evamādi āgama artha virudvam pratibhā sva citta sāmarthyāt artha nirṇayāya vikalpayantaḥ akartā muttkaḥ badvaḥ kṣaṇikaḥ mātram śūnyam vikalpayantaḥ pāram adhigacchanti avidyāyāḥ virudvarrma darśi sarvatra ya śruti ācārya darśita mārga anusāriṇaḥ ta avidyāyāḥ pāram adhigacchanti ta samudrāt agādhāt uttariṣyanti sva vudvi kauśala anusāriṇaḥ anantara nirdiṣṭam vyapadiśati budvau sannihita vaiśabdaḥ smaraṇa arthaḥ ākhyāyikā nirvṛttaṃprakaraṇa antara abhihitam parokṣam vaiśabdena smārayan vyapadiśati pravargya prakaraṇe mūcitam āviṣkṛtam nirdiṣṭam aiyam aityādinā prakaraṇa sūcitam aṅ ābhyām brāhmaṇam dhāma indreṇa uttkaḥ asmayetat anyasmā anuvrūyāḥ chindyām chindyāt tadvām upaneṣya hocaturāvām trāsyāvahe trāsyethe upaneṣyase chittvā āhratya upanidhāsyāvaḥ śira āhrati pratidhāsya avaḥ avanuvakṣyasi avanuvakṣyasi chetsyati śira āhrati pratidhāsyāva upaninye upaninye śirat chittvā upanidadhutuḥ śira āhrati pratidadhatuḥ hābhyām anuvāca ābhyām anuvāca cit cheda śira āhrati pratidadhatuḥ pravargya abhihitam kakṣyam ajñāna ākhyam ākhyāyikā abhihitā stuti arthā pradarśyate aṅṅātharvaṇaḥ prapañcena ṛpiḥ śṛpiḥ mantraḥ upalabhamānaḥ uttkavān daṃsa vyavahitena sambandhaḥ daṃsa ki viśiṣṭam krūram yuvayoḥ he nara ākārau kinnimitam lābhāya lāma lubdha krūram ācarati upalabhyete soke tadāviḥ prakāśam karomi rahasi bhayām ucyate kāraḥ upariṣṭāt upacāra arthīyaḥ vede pratipedha arthaḥ yathāśvam yadvat vṛrṣṭi vṛrṣṭi prakāśayati stanayitnu ādi śabdaiḥ tadvat yuvayoḥ krūram āviṣkṛṇomi sambandhaḥ nanu aśvinoḥ stuti arthau mantrau syātām nindā vacanau epa doṣaḥ stutiḥ nindā vacanau īdṛśam atikrūram kurvatoḥ yuvayoḥ loma mīyata vīyata stutau nindām praśaṃsām laukikāḥ smaranti rūpā nindā prasidvā dadhyak anartha nipātaḥ kakṣyam jñāna lakṣaṇam āthavaṇaḥ yukābhyām śirasā prayat provāca anartha nipātaḥ ityādi pūrvavat mantra antara darśana mantraḥ ākhyāyikām anusaratisma dadhyak vidyata viśinaṣṭi dadhyak dadhīca he mantra dṛśaḥ vacanam aśvyama śvasya sva śira si chinne chittvā īdṛśam ati krūram aśvayam brāhmaṇam erayatam gamitavantau yuvām yuvābhyām pravocat pratijñātam kimartham jīvita sandeham āruhya pravocat ucyate śṛtāyan yata pratijñātam paripālayitum jīvitāt paripālanā gurutarā ityesya ki pravocat ucyate sambandhi chinnam pratisandhāna artha pravargya pravargya chedana pratisandhāna ādi viṣayam darśanam he dastraḥ dastrau balānām upakṣa payitārau śatrūṇām ahiṃsitārau kevalam sambandhi yuvābhyām kakṣyam gopyam rahasyam sambandhi brāhmaṇena uttkama dhyāya dvaya prakāśitam yuvābhyām pravocat anuvartate pūrvavat uttkau mantrau pravargya sambandhyākhyāyi upasaṃhartārau dvayoḥ pravargya arthayoḥ adhyāyayoḥ artha ākhyāyikā bhūtābhyām mantrābhyām prakāśitaḥ arthayoḥ adhyāyayoḥ artha auttarābhyām ṛgbhyām prakāśayitavyaḥ pravartate kakṣyam madhuttkavān yuvābhyām uttkam dat ucyate purāṇi śarīrāṇi yata acya akṛta vyākaraṇa prakriyā parameśvaraḥ avyākrate vyākurvāṇaḥ ādīm llokān kṛtavān dvi pāda palakṣitāni śarīrāṇi pakṣi śarīrāṇi tavā śarīrāṇi catuṣpād upalakṣitāni paśu śarīrāṇi purastān liṅga śarīrāṇi ācaṣṭe śrutiḥ asuyūrṣu śarīreṣu puriśeta ucyate kiñacana anāvṛta manāt śaditam kiñcana asaṃvṛtam antarananu praveśitam bāhya bhūtena antarbhūtena anāvṛtam nāmakhya antarvahiḥ bhāvena kārya karaṇa vyavasthitaḥ ityādi mantraḥ saṅkṣepata ācaṣṭā arthaḥ ityādi pūrvavat arthaḥ anurūpaḥ yādṛś saṃmathānau pitarau saṃsthānaḥ anurūpa dvipād catuṣpād parameśvaraḥ vyākurvāṇaḥ kimartha āgamanam ucyate pratikhyāpanāya vyākriyete nirūpa adhikam ana ghana ākhyam pratikhyāyeta kārya karaṇa vyāka pratikhyāyeta parameśvaraḥ prajñābhiḥ kṛta mithyā abhimānaiḥ paramārthataḥ gabhyate sanna prajñābhiḥ kāraṇāt yuttkā vājinaḥ sva vipaya prakāśanāya dasya haraṇāt indriyāṇi śatāni bheda bāhulyāt śatāna indriya vipaya bāhulyāt prakāśanāyā yuttkāna prakāśanāya parāñci khāni vyatṛṇat svayambhūḥ kāṭhake tasmātaiḥ vipaya svarūpaiḥ ghana sva tahi parameśvaraḥ haraya prāpte ucyate bhedasya anantyāt bahunā ya kāraṇam vidyata kāryam vidyata jāti antarāle vidyata analtaram vidyata avāhyam nirantaram pratyagātmā bodvā vedānta upadeśaḥ vedāntānām upasaṃhrator athaḥ parisamāptaḥ śāstra arthaḥ pañcamam brāhmaṇam ayedānīm arthasya madhuka aṇḍasya stuti arthaḥ vidyāyāḥ mantraḥ svādhyāya arthaḥ japa arthaḥ vaṃśa veṇuḥ parvaṇaḥ parvaṇaḥ bhidyate tadvat agrat prabhṛti āmūla prāpteḥ adhyāya catuṣṭayasya ācārya paramparā kramaḥ vaṃśa ucyate śiṣyaḥ pañcamayantaḥ ācāryaḥ hiraṇyagarbhāt ācārya paramparāna nityam svayambhū brahmaṇai svayambhuve ayedānīm arthasya madhuka aṇḍasya stuti arthaḥ vidyāyāḥ mantraḥ svādhyāya arthaḥ japa arthaḥ vaṃśa veṇuḥ parvaṇaḥ parvaṇaḥ bhidyate tadvat agrat prabhṛti āmūla prāpteḥ adhyāya catuṣṭayasya ācārya paramparā kramaḥ vaṃśa ucyate śiṣyaḥ pañcamayantaḥ ācāryaḥ hiraṇyagarbhāt ācārya paramparāna nityam svayambhū brahmaṇai svayambhuve ṣaṣṭham brāhmaṇam ādhḥYāYā vaideha ityādi yājñavalkoyam kāṇḍam ārabhyate upapatti pradhāna atikrāntena madhuka aṇḍena samāna artha tve sati punarukta ka aṇḍam āgema pradhānam āgama upapattī ekatva prakāśanāya pravṛtte śaknutaḥ kara tala gata bilvam darśayitum mantavya uktam āgama arthasya parīkṣā pūrvakam nirdhāraṇāya yājñavalkīyam kāṇḍam upapatti pradhānam ārabhyate ākhyāyikā stuti artha upāya vidhi prasiddhaḥ upāyaḥ vidvadbhiḥ śāstreṣu hṛyupanam prāṇinaḥ prabhūtam hiraṇyam gaḥ sahasra upalabhyate anya śāstreṇa prāpti upāya dāna pradarśana arthā akhyāyikā arabdhā vidya saṃyogaḥ taiśva vāda karaṇam prāpti upāyaḥ nyāya adyāye prābalyena pradarśyate pratyakṣā vidvat saṃyoge vṛddhiḥ prāpti upāya pradarśana arthā ākhyāyikā videhānām bhavaḥ śākhā antara prasiddhaḥ dakṣiṇaḥ bāhulyāt dakṣiṇa ucyate teneje ayajat nimantritā darśana kāmā kurūṇām deśānām viduṣām bāhulyam prasiddham abhisametā abhisaṃgatā vidvat mudāyam yajamānasya brahmiṣṭha viśeṣeṇa icchā anūcānāḥ ideṣām atiśayena anūcāna hānu ūcānatam aviṣaya utpad nijijñāsaḥ upāya vayasām avaru rodha goṣṭhe avarodham kārayāmāsa kiṃviśiṣṭāḥ avaruddhā ucyate pala caturtha bhāgaḥ pādaḥ suvarṇasya pādā ekaikasya goḥ ābaddhā pādā ekaikasmin śṛṅge gā brāhmaṇān he brāhmaṇā bhagavanta āmantratha yūyam brahmāṇaḥ atiśayena etā gā utkālayatu sva gṛham brāhmaṇā uktā brāhmaṇā brahmiṣṭha pratijñātum dadhṛ puḥ pragalbhāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ apragalbha brāhmaṇeṣu sva mātmīyam antevāsinam etā gā he somya udgamayā asmad he vidhim ator ayāt gā utkālitavān ācārya gṛham brahmiṣṭha paṇa svīkaraṇena brahmiṣṭha pratijñātā kruddhavantaḥ abhiprāyam ācaṣṭe asmākam ekaika pradhānānām kruddheṣu brāhmaṇeṣu yajamānasya ṛtvij aśvalaḥ yājñavalkyam brahmiṣṭha abhimānī rāja āśraya dhṛṣṭaḥ yājñavalkyam pṛṣṭavān asī plutiḥ bhartsana arthā namaskarmaḥ gaḥ brahmiṣṭha pratijñam brahmiṣṭha paṇa svīkaraṇāt dhṛtavān aśvalaḥ kāṇḍe pāḍaktena darśana saptuccitena yajamānasya atyayaḥ vyākhyāta udgītha prakaraṇe saṅkṣepataḥ parīkṣā viṣayaḥ ayamiti tadgata darśana viśeṣa arthaḥ vistara ārabhyate sādhana karmaṇa ṛtvigagni ādi lakṣaṇena svābhāvika āsaṅga sahitena jyāptam kevalam vyāptam abhiṣannam baśīkṛtam darśana lakṣaṇena sādhanena āptimati mṛtyu gacara atikramya mucyate svatantraḥ avaśaḥ arthaḥ nanu udgītha abhihitam atimucyatemukhya bāḍham uktam anuktaḥ viśeṣaḥ arthaḥ ārambha adoṣaḥ arthaṃvyācaṣṭe hetā atikāmati ucyate yajamānasya yajamānasya yāvāc adhiyajñe tatatrayeyaṃvan ga yajñasyayajamānasya prasiddhaḥ vyanna prakaraṇā ivyākhyātam hetā sādhana dvayam catviṅg adhiyajñam sādhana dvayam paricchinnam svābhāvikā jñāna āsaṅga prayuktena pratikṣaṇam anyathātvam āpadyamānam vaśīkṛtam adhidaivata adṛśyamānaṃ ayajamānasya sṛtyorati muktaye svarūpa darśanam sādhana dvayam gaśyati tadānīm svābhāvikādāsaṅgāt vimucyate ādhyātmikāt paricchinna rūpā dādhibhautikāt mukti sādhanam yajamānasya ati mukti sādhanam arthaḥ sādhana dvayasya paricchinnasya adhidevatā aparicchinnena dṛṣṭiḥ adhidevatā dṛṣṭiḥ adhyātma adhibhūta pariccheda viṣaya āsaṅga āspadam atikramya adhidevatā bhāvasya prāptiḥ phala bhūtā ucyate atimukteḥ sādhanam yajamānasya ati ādīnām ādi bhāva udgītha prakaraṇe vyākhyātam sāmānyena mukhya darśana mātram mukti sādhanam uktam viśeṣaḥ ādīnām ādi darśanam viśeṣaḥ varṇyate mṛtyu prāpti phala bhūtā yodgītha brāhmaṇena vyākhyātā amṛtyu pratikrāntaḥ ityādyā svābhāvikāda jñāna āsaṅga prayuktāt lakṣaṇāt ati vyākhyātā sāsaṅgasya āśraya darśa pūrṇamāsa ādi sādhanānām vipariṇāma hetuḥ ati nuṣṭhāna vyatirekeṇa prāk kriyāyāḥ sādhana vipariṇāma hetu tvena vyāpāra darśanāt ati vaktavyā ityata ahorātrābhyām dvi ahorātra ādi lakṣaṇāḥ tithi ādi lakṣaṇaḥ ahorātra ādi lakṣaṇāt atimuktim ahorātrābhyām vinaśyati yajña sādhanam yajamānasya śiṣṭāni pūrvavat neyāni yajamānasya sādhana dvayam adhyātma adhibhūta paricchedam hitvā adhidaivata bhāvena pūrvavat bhāvam āpannasya ahorātre sambhavataḥ tithi ādi lakṣaṇāt ati ucyate tithi ādi lakṣaṇāt ati ūcyate ahorātrayoḥ aviśiṣṭayoḥ ādīnām tithīnām tāsām vṛddhi kṣaya upagamanena pratipad prabhṛtīnām apācyā pakṣa apara pakṣa atyayaḥ apacyā ahorātra atyayavat yajamānasya audgātā udgītha avagatam avācā udak āyat nirdhāritam aatha jyotīrūpam prāṇauvāyu candramasām upasaṃhāre viśeṣaḥ manyamānā śrutiḥ adhidaivata nimittau vṛddhi kṣayau tithi ādi lakṣaṇasya kartuḥ kārayitā āpannaḥ tithi ādi atītaḥ upapannataram śruti antare dṛṣṭiḥ kāṇvānām sādhana dvayasya kāraṇa dṛṣṭiḥ śrutyoḥ virodhaḥ ati vyākhyātā yajamānasya atimucyamānaḥ avaṣṭambhena pariccheda viṣayam atotya phalam atimucyata ucyate prasiddham anārambaṇam anālambanam śabdāt tatrā alambanam jñāyata abhiprāyaḥ ajñāyamānam ālambanam pṛcchyate anyathā phala prāpteḥ asaṃbhavāt avaṣṭambhenā akrameṇa phalam pratipadyamānaḥ praśna viṣaya kenā akrameṇa ākramata phalam atimucyata arthaḥ akṣara nyāsaḥ pūrvavat yajamānasya prasiddham candramā prasiddham candramā brahmaṛtviktena paricchinnam manasa dvayam aparicchinnena avalambanena phalam atimucyata abhiprāyaḥ upasaṃhārātham vacanam evaṃprakārā ati mokṣāḥ sarvāṃṇi darśana prakārāṇi yajña viṣayāṇi avasara uktāni upasaṃhāra ati mokṣāḥ evaṃprakārā arthaḥ adhunā saṃpada kenacid sāmānyena agnihotra ādīnām mahatām phalavatām phalāya saṃpādanam phalasya utsāhena phala sādhana anuṣṭhāne prayatatām kenacid vaiguṇyena asaṃbhavaḥ āhitāgniḥ sanyat kiñcit agnihotra ādīnām yathāsaṃbhavam ādāyā alambanīkṛtya phala vidvattāyām satyām phala saṃpādayati anyathā rājasūya medha medha lakṣaṇānām adhikṛtānām traivarṇikānām asaṃbhavaḥ pāṭhaḥ svādhyāya artha kevalaḥ phala prāpti upāyaḥ kaścana sepadā phala prāptiḥ saṃpadām phalavat saṃpada ārabhyante abhimukhīkaraṇāya aya madya rgbhiḥ hetā saṅkhyā abhiḥ jātibhiḥ ayaṃha utar tvigasmin śastram śaṃsati jātibhiḥ ukkavantam pratyā hetaraḥ tāstiḥ tra saṅkhyeya viṣayaḥ praśnaḥ saṅkhyā viṣayaḥ puronuvākyāca yāga phālāt prayujyante jātiḥ ucyate yāga prayujyante jātiḥ śastra prayujyante jātiḥ kāścana stotriyā anyā etāsu tisṛṣu jātiṣu antarbhavanti saṅkhyā sāmānyāt phala sampādayati saṅkhī ādi sāmānyena hovāva pūrvavat katyaya madya yajña heṣyati āhuti prakārāḥ tastra tāstiḥ tra pūrvavat itara hūtā ājya āhutayaḥ hutā śabdam kuvanti māsa ādi āhutayaḥ hutā adhyādhaḥ bhūmeḥ āhutayaḥ nirvartitābhiḥ āhutibhiḥ āhutayaḥ hutā ujjvalana yuktā āhutayaḥ nirvartitāḥ phalam ākhyam ujjvalam sāmānyena maya ujjvalantya āhutayaḥ nirvartyamānāḥ phalasya ākhyam phalam nirvartyata sampādayati hutā āhutayaḥ kutsita śabda kartṛtva sāmānyena kutsita śabda kartṛtva sāmānyena sambaddhāyām saṃyamanyām puryām vaivasvatena yātyamānānāṃ ahā hatāḥ muñca muñca śabda ubhavati avadāna āhutayaḥ sāmānyāt nirvartyata sampādayati hutā ijayati bhūmi sambandha sāmānyāt agha uparitanān sādhyān apekṣya athavā gamanam apekṣya nirvartyata sampādayati hutā tābhijayati bhūmi sambandha sāmānyāt uparitanān sādhyān apekṣya athavā gamanam apekṣya nirvartyata sampādayati āhuti nirvartana pūrvavat ṛtvij brahmāsane sthitvā prāsaṅgikam vahuvacanam devatayā jñāte bahuvacanena praśnaḥ upapadyate jānataḥ pūrvayoḥ kaṇḍikayoḥ praśna prativacaneṣu tistra prasaṅgam bahuvacanena praśna upakramaḥ kriyate athavā prativādivyāmoha artha bahuvacanam itara sthitvā asane mana vyāpriyate dhyānena vartanī anyatarām saṃskaroti śruti antarāt mana vṛtti bhedena vaiśabdaḥ prasiddha avadyotana arthaḥ prasiddham manasa ānantyma ānantyā abhimāninaḥ ityādi śruti antarāt ānantya sāmānyāt pūrvavat stopyati stotriyā samudāyaḥ katipayānām ṛcām stotriya avāśamyāvāyāḥ kāścana sarvāstiḥ tra vyākhyātāḥ muronuvākyā śasya uktam prāṇabhṛta sāmānyena ucyate tāstiḥ tra paśabda sāmānyāt avānaḥ ānantaryāt prattam haviḥ grasanti yāgaḥ pradānam vyānaḥśasyā aprāṇan anapānat nṛcam abhivyāharati śrati antarāt vyākhyātam viśeṣa sambandha sāmānyam anuktam ucyate vyākhyātam sambandha sāmānyena madhyamatva sāmānyāt dyulokaṃśasyayā ūrdhvatva sāmānyāt praśna nirṇayāt aśvala asmad gecara adhyāye aśvala brāhmaṇam ākhyāyikā sambandhaḥ prasiddha ati vyākhyātā kāla lakṣaṇāt lakṣaṇāt ati vyākhyātā svābhāvikā jñāna āsaṅga āspadaḥ adhyātma adhibhūta aviṣaya paricchinnaḥ graha atigraha lakṣaṇaḥ paricchinna rūpāt atimuktasya aganyāt ityādīn yudgītha prakaraṇe vyākhyātāni aśvala praśneca tadgataḥ viśeṣaḥ jñāna sahitānām phalam sādhya sādhana rūpāt saṃsārāt mokṣaḥ kartavya atobandhana rūpasya svarūpam ucyate baddhasya mokṣaḥ kartavyaḥ atimuktasya sva uktam graha atigraha abhyām avinirmukta mṛtyu uktam aśanāya stham aṅgīkṛtya vahavā bhāva āpannaḥ āptimatimucyata ucyate graha atigrahau mṛtyu rūpau nastas jyotīrūpam amanaśva agrahaḥ atigrāheṇa atigrāheṇa atigrāheṇa vyanna vibhāge vyākhyātam asmābhiḥ vicāritam pravṛtti kāraṇam nivṛtti kāraṇam kecid nivṛtti kāraṇam kāgṇāt pūrvasmāt pūrvasmāt mucyate uttaram uttaram pratipadyamānaḥ vyāvṛtti tādarthyam ata dvaita kṣayāta dvaina kṣaye paramārtha āptimatimucyate āpekṣikī gauṇī antarāle evat abārhat āraṇyakam nanu mokṣaḥ bāḍham grāma yajeta paśu yajeta ityādi śrutīnām tādarthyam advaita artha grāma paśu svarga ādi artha grāma paśu svargāt ayaḥ gṛhyeran gṛhyante phala vaicitrya viśeṣāḥ vaidikānām tādarthyam saṃsāra abhaviṣyat tādarthye anuniṣpādita padārtha svabhāvaḥ saṃsāra darśana artha āloke tatrasthaḥ prakāśyata pramāṇa anupapatteḥ advaita artha tve vaidikānām sahitānām anya spānu niṣpādita tve pramāṇa anupapattiḥ pratyakṣam anumānam ata āgamaḥ ekena vākyena pradarśyata kulyā praṇayana āloka ādivat nevam vākya anupapatteḥ vākya gatasya arthasya pravṛtti nivṛtti sādhana avagantum śakyate kulyā praṇayana āloka ādau arthasya adoṣaḥ ucyate mantrā artheḥ dṛṣṭā arthaḥ pramāṇa agamyaḥ mantrāḥ artha āhosvit artha mṛgyam graha ati praha lakṣaṇaḥ bandhaḥ bhokṣaḥ vaktavya ata ārabhyate jānīmaḥ viṣaya sandhau antarāle avasthānam jaratīyam kauśalam atimucyata ukatvā graha atigrahau ucyete tacu artha sambandhāt sādhya sādhana lakṣaṇaḥ bandhaḥ graha atigraha avinirmokāt nigaḍe nirjñāte nigaḍitasya mokṣāya yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ tasmātādarthyena ārambhaḥ śabda aitihya arthaḥ aśvala uparate prakṛtam yājñavalkyam jaratkāru gotraḥ jāratkārava ṛta bhāgasya apatyam ārta bhāgaḥ abhimukhokaraṇāya pūrvavat praśnaḥ atigrahā vākya parisamāpti arthaḥ nirjñāteṣu graha atigraheṣu praśnaḥ anirjñāteṣu grahā nirjñātāḥ gatasya guṇasya saṃkhyāyāḥ nijñāta atigrahā saṃkhyā viṣayaḥ praśnaḥ upapadyate nirjñātāḥ saṃkhyeya viṣaya praśna atigrahā praṣṭavyam atigrahā praśnaḥ nirjñāta sāmānya keśu viśeṣa praśnaḥ kaṭhāḥ kāla apā graha atigrahā padārthāḥ kecana prasiddhāḥ viśeṣa arthaḥ praśnaḥ nanu atimucyata uktam graha gṛha utasya mokṣaḥ uktam prāptā grahā nanu grahā nirjñātā manāṃsi praśnaḥ upapadyate nirjñāta anavadhāraṇa artha catuṣṭvam vivakṣitam graha atigraha adarśane aṣṭhatva guṇa vivakṣayā katoti praśna upapadyata mukti atiktī ukte graha atigrahā siddhāḥ saṃkhyākā atigrahā pṛcchati itara grahā atigrahā grahā abhihitāḥ niyamena grahītavyā tatrā aha ghrāṇam ucyate prakaraṇāt sahitaḥ gandhena apāna saciva gandha ucyate apāna upahṛtam ghrāṇena ucyate adhyātma paricchinnayā asaṅga viṣaya āspadayā asatya anṛta asabhya bībhatsād ivacaneṣu vyāpṛtayā apahṛtaḥ vāggrahaḥ atigrāreṇa ākhyaḥ vaktavyena viṣayeṇa atigrāheṇa daighyam chāndasam vaktavya arthā vāktena vaktavyena arthena tādarthyena prayuktā vāktena vaśīkṛtā kāryam akṛtvā mokṣaḥ atigrāheṇa ucyate vakta vyāsaṅgena pravṛttā anarthaiḥ yujyate paryantā sparśa paryantāḥ atigrahā upasaṃhṛteṣu graha atigraheṣu vipadyate graha atigraha lakṣaṇena grastam kāsvitkā bhavet upasecanam śruti antarāt abhiprāyaḥ praṣṭuḥ anavasthā graha atigraha lakṣaṇāt mokṣaḥ upapadyate graha atigraha mṛtyu vināśe mokṣaḥ yāt bhavet graha atigraha lakṣaṇasya vināśaḥ durvacanam praśnam pṛcchati kāsvitsā nanu anavasthā anavasthā mṛtyu antara anupapatteḥ avagamyate dṛṣṭa vināśaka bhakṣyate gṛhāṇa graha atigraha bhakṣyate bandhane nāśite bhakṣite saṃsārāt mokṣa upapannaḥ bandhanam graha atigraha lakṣaṇam uktam mokṣa upapadyata prasādhitam bandha mokṣāya prayāsaḥ saphalaḥ mṛtyau bhakṣite paramātma muktaḥ mriyata udūrdhvam mriyamāṇāt prāṇā agadayaḥ grahā ādayaḥ atigrahā vāsanā rūpā antasthāḥ prayojakāḥ kāmatnī āhosvit pareṇā atmanā vibhāgam viduṣi kāryāṇi karaṇāni sva yonau tattave samavanīyanta ekībhāvena samavasṛjyante pralīyanta arthaḥ ūrmaya ida śruti śabda vācyānām parasmin pralayam darśayati paridraṣṭuḥ puruṣāyaṇāḥ gacchantī pareṇā atmanā vibhāgam darśitam ucchūnatām pratipadyata bāhyena dṛtivat niśceṣṭaḥ bandhana nāśe muktasya kvacid gamanam vākya arthaḥ muktasya prāṇā samavanoyanta āhosvit prayojakam prāṇā prayojakam prayojake vidyamāne prasaṅgaḥ ādi mokṣa upapadyata artha uttaraḥ praśnaḥ samavanīyata arthaḥ mātram līyata ākṛti sambandhāt nityam nitya anantyam nāmnaḥ ānantyā adhikṛtā anantā bai ānantya adhikṛtān viśvān tvena upetya tenā anantya graha atigraha bandhanam uktam mṛtyu mṛtyu sadbhāvāt mokṣaḥ upapadyate mokṣaḥ graha atigraha pralayaḥ pradīpa nirvāṇavat yadvat graha atigraha ākhyam bandhanam mṛtyu prayojakam svarūpa nirdhāraṇa ārabhyate kecid varṇayanti graha atigrahasya prayojakasya vināśe mucyate avaśiṣṭaḥ avidya uṣara sthānīyayā sva prabhavayā pa paricchinnaḥ bhojyāt jagataḥ vyāvṛtta ucchinna antarāle vyavatiṣṭhate paramātmā ekatva darśane dvaita darśanam apanetavyam paramātma darśanam ārabdhavyam apavarga ākhyām antarāla avasthām parikalya uttara grantha saṃbandham vaktavyam viśīrṇeṣu karaṇeṣu videhasya paramātma darśana śravaṇa manana nididhi āsanāni samavanīta mātra avaśiṣṭasya taiḥ ucyate śeta hayuktam manorathena upapādayitum śakyate jīvan avidyā mātra avaśiṣṭaḥ bhojyāt apāvṛtta parikalpyate kiṃnimittam vaktavyam samasta dvaita ekatva prāpti nimittam ucyate nirākṛtam sahitena dvaita ekatva sampannaḥ samavanīta jagat hiraṇyagarbha svarūpam prāpnuyāt asamavanīta bhojyāt jīvan vyāvṛttaḥ viraktaḥ paramātma darśana abhimukhaḥ prayatna niṣpādyena sādhanena labhyam hiraṇyagarbha prāpti sādhanam vyāvṛtti sādhanam paramātma abhimukhīkaraṇasya bhojyā dvaya āvṛtteḥ sādhanam hiraṇyagarbha prāpti sādhanam gati sādhanam gati nivṛtteḥ mṛtvā hiraṇyagarbham samavanīta avaśiṣṭaḥ paramātma jñāne adhikriyate asmad ādi paramātma jñāna upadeśaḥ anarthakaḥ arthāya upadiśyate ityādyayā śrutyā atyanta nikṛṣṭā śāstra bāhya kalpanā prakṛtam vartayiṣyāma prayuktam graha atigraha lakṣaṇam bandhanam nirdidha ārayiṣayā aha asamyak darśinaḥ pāṇi ādimataḥ sarvatra sambadhyate atrā atma adhiṣṭhānam hṛdaya ucyate apiyati nidhīyata ādāna sarvatra ādi parigṛhyante karaṇāni apakrāmanti prāk mokṣāt anadhiṣṭhitāni karaṇāni nyasta dātrā ādi upamānāni videhaḥ asvatantraḥ āśritaḥ pṛcchayate āśritaḥ āśrayam āśritya kārya karaṇa saṃghātam upādatte graha atigraha lakṣaṇam bandhanam prayujyate praśnaḥ ucyate svabhāvayadṛcchā kāla daiva mātra śūnyāni vādibhiḥ parikalpitāni aneka vipratipatti sthāna jalpa nyāyena vastu nirṇayaḥ vastu nirṇayam icchasyāhara sobhya hasta sārtabhāga tvad pṛṣṭasya nirūpayiṣyāvaḥ avāvayoḥ vastu jana samudāye nirṇetum śakyate ata ekānta gamiṣyāvaḥ vicāraṇāya ityādi śruti vacanam ārta bhāgau ekāntam cakratuḥ ucyate janāt deśān mantrayāñca krāte ādau laukika vādi pakṣāṇām parugṛhya vicāritavantau vicārya ū catuḥ apohya pakṣān śṛṇu aśrayam kārya karaṇa upādāna hetum ūcatur uktavantau kevalam kāla dā īśvareṣu abhyupagateṣu hetuṣu nirdhāritam prayuktam graha atigraha ādi kārya karaṇa upādānam śāstra vihitena viparotena viparītaḥ praśneṣu nirṇīteṣu aśakya prakampya jaratkārava adhyāye ārta bhāga brāhmaṇam graha atigraha lakṣaṇam bandhanam uktam prayojakāt muktaḥ mucyate baddhaḥ saṃsarati mokṣa upapadyate mṛyoḥ muktasya kvacid utsādaḥ mātra avaśeṣaḥ pradīpa nirvāṇavat avadhṛtam saṃsaratām mucyamānānām kārya karaṇānām sva kāraṇa saṃsarge samāne muktānām atyantam anupādānam saṃsaratām upādānam prayuktānām avadhāritam vicāraṇā pūrvakam kṣaye avaśeṣeṇa utsādaḥ mokṣaḥ ākhyam avadhārita saṃsāraḥ apuṇyena sthāvara jaṅgameṣu svabhāva duḥkha bahuleṣu naraka tiryak preta ādiṣu rāja vartmavat prasiddham śāstrī ādaraḥ kriyata śrutyā artha sādhanam śruti smṛti vādāḥ mokṣasya artha sādhyatā prāptā utkarṣaḥ phala utkarṣa prāptiḥ uttam utkarṣeṇa mokṣaḥ bhaviṣyati nivartayitavyā jñāna sahitasya prakṛṣṭasya karmaṇa etāvatī vyākṛta āspada phalasya akārye nitye avyākṛta dharmiṇya ātmake kriyā kāraka phala svabhāva varjite vyāpāraḥ vyāpāraḥ saṃsāra arthasya pradarśanāya brahmaṇam ārabhyate kaiścid ucyate sahitam nirabhisaṃdhi mantra śarkarā ādi yukta viṣada dhyādivat kārya ārabhata anārabhya mokṣasya bandha nāśa mokṣaḥ kārya bhūtaḥ bandhanam avidyā avocāma avidyāyāḥ nāśa upapadyate dṛṣṭa viṣayatva acva sāmarthyasya utpatti āpti vikāra saṃskārā sāmarthyasya viṣayāḥ utpādayitum prāpayitum vikartum sāmarthyam vyatirikta viṣayaḥ sāmarthyasya aprasiddha mokṣa padārthānām anyatamaḥ avidyā mātra vyavahita avocāma bāḍham bhavatu kevalasya karmaṇa evaṃsvabhāva saṃyuktasya nirabhisaṃdheḥ anyathā svabhāvaḥ anya śakti tvena nirjñātānām padārthānām viṣa ādīnām mantra śarkarā ādi saṃyuktānām anya viṣaye sāmathyam pramāṇa abhāvāt karmaṇa viṣaya vyatirekeṇa viṣaya antare sāmarthya astitve pramāṇam pratyakṣam anumānam upamānam arthāpattiḥ nanu phala antara abhāve codanāni anupapattiḥ pramāṇam nityānām nyāyena phalam kalpyate phalam codyante pāriśeṣyāt mokṣaḥ phalam gamyate anyathā puruṣā pravarteran nanu viśvajit nyāya ayātaḥ mokṣasya phalasya kalpita mokṣe phale akalpite puruṣā pravarteran mokṣaḥ phalam kalpyate śruta artha āpattyā viśvajiti nanu sati ucyate viśvajit nyāyaḥ phalam kalpyate nyāyaḥ vipratiṣiddham abhidhīyate mokṣaḥ phalam pratijñāhānāt kārya viṣadadhi ādivat ārabhata pratijñātam mokṣaḥ kāryam phalam pratijñā hīyeta kārya tve mokṣasya svarga ādi phalebhyaḥ viśeṣaḥ vaktavyaḥ kāryam nityānām phalam mokṣa asyā vacana vyakteḥ kor vaktavyam kārya phala śabda bheda mātreṇa viśeṣaḥ śakyaḥ kalpayitum aphalam mokṣaḥ nityaiḥ kriyate nityānām phalam kāryam eṣor athaḥ vipratiṣiddhaḥ abhidhīyate śīta jñānavat jñānasya kāryam mokṣaḥ jñānena akriyamāṇaḥ ucyate tadvat kāryatvam ajñāna nivartaka jñānasya ajñāna vyavadhāna nivartaka jñānasya mokṣaḥ jñāna kāryam upacaryate nivartayitavyam ajñānam ajñāna vyatirekeṇa mokṣasya vyavadhāna kalpayitum śakyam nitya mokṣasya sādhaka svarūpa avyatirekāt nivartyeta ajñānam nivartayati vilakṣaṇa anabhivyaktiḥ ajñānam abhivyakti lakṣaṇena jñānena virudhyate tājñānena virudhyate jñāna vilakṣaṇam jñāna abhāvaḥ saṃśaya jñānam viparīta jñānam ucyate ajñānam jñānena nivartyate anyatamena virodha abhāvāt adṛṣṭam ajñāna nivartaka kalpyam jñānena ajñāna nivṛttau gamyamāna āyām dṛṣṭa nivṛtti kalpanā anupapatteḥ avaghātena vrīhīṇām tuṣa nivṛttau gamyamānāyām hotra ādi nityakarma kārya adṛṣṭā kalpyate tuṣa nivṛttiḥ tadvat ajñāna nivṛttiḥ nitya kārya adṛṣṭā kalpyate jñānena viruddha asakṛt avocāma aviruddham jñānam prāpti nimittam uktam kalpye phale nityānām śrutānām virudhyate dravya guṇa kāryam kalpyatām sāmarthyam kiṃvā sāmarthyam phalam aviruddham kalpyatām pravṛtti jananāya avaśyam phalam kalpayitavyam aviruddha viṣaya śruta arthāpatteḥ kṣīṇa mokṣaḥ phalam kalpayitum śakyaḥ vyavadhāna ajñāna nivṛttiḥ aviruddha dṛṣṭa sāmarthya viṣaya pāriśeṣya nyāyāt mokṣa kalpayitavya phalam itara phala vyatirekeṇa phalam kalpanā yogyam pariśiṣṭaḥ mokṣaḥ ceṣṭaḥ phalam kalpayitavya phala vyaktonām ānantyāt pāriśeṣī anyāya anupapatteḥ icchā viṣayāṇām kenacid asarva jñena avadhṛtam sādhanānām icchānām aniyata deśa kāla nimitta icchā viṣaya sādhanānām iṣṭa phala prayukta pratiprāṇi icchā vaicitryāt sādhanānām cā anantya siddhiḥ ānantyāt aśakyam puruṣaiḥ ajñāte sādhana phala tve mokṣasya pariśeṣa siddhiḥ phala jāti pāriśeṣyam sati icchā viṣayāṇām sādhanānām cā anantye phala jāti tulyam mokṣa satva phala pariśiṣṭaḥ pariśeṣāt yuktaḥ kalpayitum nitya phalatva abhyupagame phala samāna jātīyatva upapatteḥ pariśeṣa anupapattiḥ anyathā upapatteḥ kṣīṇā śruta arthāpattiḥ utpattaya āpti vikāra saṃskārāṇām anyatam nityānām phalam upapadyata kṣīṇā śruta arthāpattiḥ caturṇām anyatama mokṣa utpādyaḥ nitya ata avikāryaḥ asaṃskāryaḥ āta asādhana dravya ātmaka sādhana ātmakam dravyam saṃskriyate pātra ājya ādi prokṣaṇa ādinā saṃskriyamāṇaḥ saṃskāra nirvartyaḥ yūpa ādivat pāriśeṣyāt āpyaḥ nā aḥ svabhāva ekatvāt itaraiḥ vailakṣaṇyāt nityānām phalena vilakṣaṇena bhavitavyam tvasā lakṣaṇyāt lakṣaṇam phalam itara phalaiḥ nimitta vailakṣaṇyāt kṣāmavatī ādibhiḥ samāna gṛha dāha ādau nimitte kṣāmavatī ādi iṣṭiḥ bhinne skanne evamādau naimittikeṣu karmasu mokṣaḥ phalam kalpyate taiḥ aviśeṣāt naimittika tvena jīvana ādi nimitte śravaṇāt nityānām mokṣaḥ phalam ālokasya darśana sādhanatva ulūka ādaya ālokena ulukā ādi vailakṣaṇyāditara cakṣurbhiḥ ādi viṣaya parikalpyate ādi viṣaye sāmarthyasya adṛṣṭa viṣaye sāmarthyam viśeṣaḥ kalpayitavyaḥ punaruktam mantra śarkarā ādi saṃyukta viṣada ādivat nityāni kārya ārabhanta ārabhyatām viśiṣṭam kāryam iṣṭa avirodhaḥ nirabhisaṃdheḥ saṃyuktasya viśiṣṭa kārya antara ārambhe virodhaḥ yājya yājinoḥ viśeṣa śravaṇāt aśreyān yājī atyādau ayat karotī atyādau paramātma darśana viṣaye manunā yāji asamam yājī atyatra yājī arthaḥ athavā gatyā ātmayājya saṃskāra nityāni saṃskriyate gārbhaiḥ hemaiḥ ādi prakaraṇe kārya karaṇa saṃskāra artha nityānām darśayati saṃskṛtaḥ ya yājī taiḥ draṣṭum samarthaḥ janmāntare darśanam utpadyate svārājyam adhigacchati eṣor athaḥ yāji gatyā prayujyate jñāna yuktānām nityānām jñāna utpatti sādhanatva pradarśana viśvasṛjaḥ avyaktam uttamām sāttvikīm gatim manīṣiṇaḥ sārṣṭi vyatirekeṇa apyayam darśayati pāṭham viṣaye paricchinna buddhi adoṣaḥ arthavāda adhyāyasya brahmānta vipāka arthasya tadvayati rikta jñāna arthasya kāṇḍa bhayām tulya arthatva darśanāt vihita akaraṇa pratiṣiddha sthāvara śva sūkara ādi phala darśanāt vānta āśya ādi preta darśanāt śruti smṛti vīrīta pratiṣiddha vyatirekeṇa vihitāni pratiṣiddhān ivā kenacid avagantum śakyante akaraṇāt anuṣṭhānāt preta śva sūkara sthāvara ādīni anumānābhyām upalabhyante akarma phala kenacid abhyupagamyate vihita akaraṇa pratiṣiddha sevānām vipākāḥ preta tiryak sthāvara ādayaḥ utkṛṣṭeṣu anteṣu vipāka vapām udakhidat arodīdi brahmatva ādīni nityāni nirabhisaṃdhīni saṃskāra arthāni jñāna utpatti arthāni brāhmī kriyate tanuḥ smaraṇāt ārāt upakāraka mokṣa sādhanāni virudhyate arthaḥ ṣaṣṭhe ākhyāyikā samāptau vakṣyāmaḥ antaḥkaraṇa vṛttiḥ kriyata vinaśyati dṛṣṭiḥ uṣṇa prakāśa ādi vatsā draṣṭaḥ svarūpa vinaśyati kriyamāṇayā upādhi bhūtayā saṃsṛṣṭā vyapadiśyate bhedavat dṛṣṭiḥ laukikī dṛṣṭiḥ dvārā uparaktā jāyamānā avidyā viṣaya jihāsitavya vyutthānam vidhitsitam nanu upaniṣada jñāna paratvāt vyutthāna śrutiḥ stuti arthā vidhiḥ vidhitsita samāna kartṛkatva śravaṇāt akartavyena kartavyasya samāna kartṛka tvena
