svabhāve satyau guru patana svabhāve saṃyukta viyoga svabhāve cetanāvat abhimāni adhiṣṭhita svatantre vartete akṣa vyavasthā maryādā vidharaṇam praśāsanam atikrāmataḥ siddham astitvam avyabhicāri niyate vartete cetanāvantam praśāsitāram asaṃsāriṇam yuktam ugrā dṛṣṭā mantra varṇāt nimeṣā muhūrtā kāla avayavāḥ atīta anāgata vartamānasya janimataḥ kalayitāraḥ prabhuṇā niyataḥ gaṇakaḥ māyam vyayam apramattaḥ gaṇayati prabhu sthānīya kāla avayavānām niyantā prācayaḥ prāgañcanāḥ diggamanā sravanti himavat ādibhyaḥ giribhyaḥ gaṅgā ādyā pravartitā niyatāḥ pravartante anyathā pravartitum utsahantyaḥ praśāstuḥ pratīcīm añcanti sindhva ādyā anupravṛttāḥ vyabhicaranti siṅgam dadataḥ hiraṇya ādīn prayacchata pīḍām kurvataḥ pramāṇa jñā dīyate pratigṛhmanti samāgamaḥ vilayaḥ anvakṣaḥ dṛśyate adṛṣṭaḥ samāgamaḥ manuṣyā dadatām dāna phalena saṃyogam pramāṇa jña phalena saṃyojayitari kartuḥ phala vibhāga jñe praśāstari asati dāna kriyāyāḥ vināśi dāna kartṛṇām phalena saṃyojayitā sadbhāve pramāṇa anupapatteḥ praśastuḥ āgamatātparyasya siddha ava ucāma dyāgamasya vastu paratvāt apūrva kalpanāyām arthāpatteḥ kṣayaḥ anyathā upapatteḥ sevā phalasya sevyāt prāpti darśanāt sevāyāḥ kriyā sāmānyāt adānahoma ādīnām sevyād īśvara ādeḥ phala prāptiḥ upapadyate dṛṣṭa kriyā sāmarthyam aparityajya phala prāpti kalpanā upapattau dṛṣṭa kriyā sāmarthya parityāgaḥ nyāyyaḥ kalpanā ādhikyāt kalpvaḥ apūrvā kriyāyāḥ svabhāvaḥ sevyāt phala prāptiḥ dṛṣṭā apūrvāt adṛṣṭam kalpayitavyam phala dātṛ tve sāmarthyam sāmarthye sati abhyadhikam īśvarasya sevyasya sadbhāva mātram kalpyam phala dāna sāmarthyam dātṛ sevyāt phala prāpti darśanāt anumānam darśitam avāpṛthivyau aityādi īśvarāḥ jīvana arthe anugatāḥ cara puroḍāśa ādi upajīvana prayojanena anyathā utsahantaḥ kṛpaṇām dīnām vṛttim āśritya sthitāḥ praśāstuḥ praśāsanāt darvī darvīhomam anugatā arthaḥ smāt ajñāne niyatā saṃsāra upapattiḥ bhavitavyam vicchedaḥ nyāya upapatteḥ nanu kriyāta vicchittiḥ he aviditvā avijñāya yajata phalam phala upabhoga kṣīyanta kārpaṇya atyayaḥ saṃsāra vicchedaḥ abhāvāt kṛta phalasya upabhoktā janana maraṇa prabandha ārūḍhaḥ saṃsarati praśāsitṛ ucyate gārgya paṇakrīta dāsa ādiḥ ya dahana prakāśaka svābhāvikasya praśāstṛ acetanasya ityata adṛṣṭam kenacid aviṣaya dṛṣṭi svarūpa aviṣaya śruti svarūpa tathāmatam aviṣaya mantṛmati svarūpa avijñātam buddheḥ aviṣaya svarūpa akṣarāt darśana kriyā kartṛ darśana kriyā kartṛ sarvatra sarvatra sarvatra dvāreṇa kriyā kartṛ buddhi dvāreṇa kriyā kartṛ acetanam pradhānam gārgyākāśa braṅma ya aśanāya ādi saṃsāra atītaḥ kāṣṭhā ādeḥ antasya he brāhmaṇā śṛṇuta madīyam manyedhvam namaskāram arthaḥ jayaḥ āśaṃsanīyaḥ kāryataḥ madhye kadācid yājñavalkyam udyam jetā cena mahyam jetā bhavitā pratijñātam niścayaḥ udyam pratyetat tulyaḥ vidyata vācakna vyupararāma antaryāmi uktam vidiḥ vidurye darśanāt akriyā kartṛ tvena cetana ādi dhātuḥ uktam viśeṣaḥ sāmānyam kecid parasya samudra sthāna ayasya apracalitatva rūpasya īṣat pracalita avasthā atyanta pracalita avasthā kṣetrajñaḥ vedāntaryāmiṇam avasthāḥ parikalpayanti avasthā śaktaya etā śaktimat vikārā avasthā śaktī upapadyeta aśanāya ādi saṃsāra atītatva aśanāya ādi atīta aśanāya ādi dharmavat avasthāvat ekasya yugapad upapadyate śaktimat vikāra avayava tve doṣāḥ pradarśitāḥ caturthe etā asatyāḥ kalpanāḥ meda upādhikṛta brūmaḥ svata medaḥ amedaḥ ghanavat dhana svāmāvyāt vāhya abhyāntaraḥ ātharvaṇe nirūpa adhikasya nirūpa ākhyātvāt nirviśeṣa vyapadeśaḥ avidyā viśiṣṭa kārya karaṇa upādhiḥ saṃsārī jiva ucyate nitya niratiśaya jñāna śakti upādhiḥ antaryām ī īśvara ucyate nirūpa ādhiḥ kevalaḥ śudvaḥ svabhāvena ucyate hiraṇyagarma avyākṛta jāti piṇḍa tiryak preta ādi kārya karaṇa upādh ibhiḥ viśiṣṭaḥ ākhyaḥ arūpaḥ ejati ejati vyākhyātam ta antarātmā gūḍhaḥ tavam ityādi śrutayaḥ virudhyante kalpanā antareṣu śrutayaḥ upādhi medena ela medaḥ anyathā aekam advitīyam avadhāraṇāt sarveṣa niṣatsu adhyāyeṣṭamam akṣara brāhmaṇam ādīnām sūkṣma tāratamya krameṇa pūrvasya pūrvasya uttarasmin uttarasminnota prota bhāvam kathayan prakāśitavān vyākṛta viṣaye sūtra medeṣu niyantṛ uktam vyākṛta viṣaye vyaktaram aparokṣa tve niyantavya meda saṃkoca vikā dvāreṇa adhigantavye arya brāhmaṇam āramyate vidagdha nāmataḥ śakalasya apatyam saṃkhyākā he vakṣyamāṇayā saṃkhyām saṃkhyām pṛṣṭavān saṃkhyākā śastrasya nivid saṃkhyā vācakāni mantra padāni kānicid vaiśvadeve śastre śasyante nivid saṃjñakā ni śrūyante tāvantaḥ nivid nivid padāni pradarśyante śatāni sahasrāṇ etāvantaḥ madhyamā saṃkhyā samyaktayā jñātā tepām saṃkoca viṣayām saṃkhyām pṛcchati śata saṃkoca vikāsa viṣayām saṃkhyām pṛṣṭvā saṃkhyeya svarūpam pṛcchati sahasra vibhūtayaḥ trayastriṃśataḥ śata ityādayaḥ paramārthataḥ ucyate trayastriṃśataḥ pūraṇau vasava svarūpam pratyekam pṛchcyate ādyā prāṇinām phala āśraya tvena kārya karaṇa saṃghāta nivāsa tvena vipariṇamantaḥ jagat vāsayanti vāsanti e vasava rudrā buddhīndriyāṇi mana ekādaśānām pūraṇaḥ prāṇā prāṇinām phala pabhoga kṣaye sambandhinaḥ sambandhinaḥ rudrā katama ādityā avayavāḥ prasiddhāḥ parivartamānāḥ prāṇinām āyūṃṣi phalam ādadānā gṛhyanta upādadataḥ ādadānā ādityā katama stanayiti uḥ vajram prāṇinaḥ pramāpayati yajña paśava sādhanāni arūpa paśu sādhana āśraya yajña ucyate agnyādayaḥ tvena paṭhitāḥ varjayitvā ṣaṭa saṃkhyā viśiṣṭāḥ ādi uktam eta ādi vistara ṣaṭasu antarbhavati arthaḥ ima lokā ekokṛtya ekīkṛtya tṛtīyaḥ antarbhavanti ta nairuktānām keṣāñcid pakṣaḥ anayoḥ uktānām antarbhāvaḥ adhyargha codayanti adhyardha idaṃ madhya ardhnot sati madhya ardhna udadhi ṛddhim adhyardha katama ātmaka tyat tyat brahmācakṣate āmidhāyakena anantānām nivid saṃkhyā viśaṣṭeṣu antarbhāvaḥ śada ādi pu uttara uttareṣu ekasya saṅkhyātaḥ vistaraḥ anantaḥ saṃkhyā viśiṣṭaḥ ekasya karna guṇa śakti medaḥ adhikāra medāt aṣṭadhā meda upadiśyate āśrayaḥ lokayati arthaḥ manojyotiḥ saṃkalpa vikalpa ādi kāryam manojyotiḥ śarīraḥ darśanaḥ saṃkalpayitā abhimānī kārya karaṇa saṃghātavān arthaḥ ya viśiṣṭam ātmana ādhyātmikasya kārya karaṇa saṃghātasya paramayanam āśrayaḥ mātṛ jena rudhira kṣetra sthānīyena bīja sthānīyasya jasya asthi śukra rūpasya ayanam karaṇa ya vetti itya abhiprāyaḥ ajānan paṇḍita abhimāni ami prāyaḥ labhyate kathayasi śākalyasya vacanam draṣṭyam kiṃviśeṣaṇaḥ ya pārdhiva aṃśe bhavaḥ mātṛ jakośa traya arthaḥ e tvayā pṛṣṭaḥ he kintu vaktavyam viśeṣaṇa pṛcchā arthaḥ he prakṣobhitaḥ amarpa vaśa ga tottrādinta gajaḥ śarīrasya niṣpadyate prakaraṇe vivakṣitaḥ bhuktasya annasya mātṛ jasya niṣpatti hetuḥ vayan arasāt niṣpadyate striyām śritam mayam bīja āśrayam vyatikāra abhilāṣaḥ arthaḥ hradayam hradayena budvayā ya maya striya strītaḥ kāmasya dīptiḥ śukla kṛṣṇa ādīni ya viśiṣṭam kāryam satyām satyām ucyate avyātmataḥ adhidaivatasya niṣpatti ya śrotraḥ bhavaḥ śrotraḥ pratiśravaṇa velāyām viśeṣataḥ kādevatā diśa ādhyātmikaḥ niṣpadyate tama tama śārvadi andhakāraḥ parigṛhyate ām ayaḥ ajñāna apidaivatam niṣpatti kāraṇam ādhārāni uktāni prakāśakāni viśiṣṭāni gṛhyante āyatanasya viśeṣa pratibimba ādhāram ādarśa ādi pratibimba ākhyasya niṣpattirasoḥ āpa sādhāraṇāḥ āpa vāpī kūpa taḍāga ādi āśrayāsu viśeṣa avasthānam varuṇāt saṅghāta karñyodhi ātmam āpa ādi apam niṣpatti kāraṇam reta ya ayaḥ viśeṇa reta āyatanasya putrasya asthi mañjā śukāṇi pituḥ prajñāpatiḥ ucyate pitṛtaḥ putrasya utpattiḥ aṣṭakā bhedena tridhā tridhā pravibhajya avasthita bheda upāsana artha vyapadiṣṭaḥ adhunā vibhāgena pañcadhā pravibhaktasya ātmānayupasaṃhāra tūṣṇīmbhūtam śākalyam graheṇa āveśayan vitarke nūnam aṅgārāvakṣaṇam aṅgārā avakṣīyante sandaṃśa ādau aṅgārāvakṣaṇam nūnam kṛtavantaḥ budhyase dahyamānam abhiprāyaḥ kuruṣañcalānām brāhmaṇān ati uktavān bhītāḥ aṅgārāva kṣayaṇam kṛtavanta adhikṣipasi brāhmaṇān viṣayam jāne kvalam diśa devā devaiḥ adhiṣṭhātṛbhiḥ pratiṣṭhābhiḥ itara saphalam tvayā pratijñātam kindevataḥ digbhṛtasya pañcadhā dvāreṇa jagat tvena upagamya vyavasthitaḥ abhimukhaḥ vacanāt pratijñā pṛcchati kindevataḥ sarvatra vede dvapāḥ bhūtaḥ pratipadyata adevaḥ adhiṣṭhātrī kayā devatayā prāpī sampanna arthaḥ itara devata devā uktam vaktavyam pratiṣṭhita adhyātmataḥ cakṣuṣa niṣpanna mantra brāhmaṇa vādāḥ cakṣoḥ cakṣuṣa ityādayaḥ kāryam kāraṇe ātmakam cakṣu prayuktam prayuktam taiḥ ārabdham prācyā diśā sthaiḥ sarvai bhūtā hṛdaya hṛdaya ārabdhāni ākāreṇa pariṇatam buddhi ekīkṛtya nirdeśaḥ smaraṇam vāsanā ātmanām arthaḥ kindevataḥ pūrvavat devata dakṣiṇa ādiś pratiṣṭhita yajña agṛhyaḥ karaṇa gocaram vastu grahaṇa gocaram viparītam tattvam aśīryaḥ dhi saṃhatam ādi viparītaḥ āsaṅgaḥ mūrtaḥ mūrta sambadhyamānaḥ viparītaḥ abaddhaḥ mūrta vadhyate viparīta abaddha grahaṇa viśaraṇa sambandha kārya rahita hiṃsām āpadyate vinaśyati arthaḥ kramam atikramya aupaniṣadasya ākhyāyikātas apasṛtya śrutyā tvarayā nirdeśaḥ ākhyāyikām aśriti uktāni āyata nāni apṛthivī evamādīni aupaniṣadaḥ aśanāya ādi varjitaḥ upaniṣatsu vijñeyaḥ anya pramāṇa gamyaḥ abhimāninam vispaṣṭam kathayiṣyasi vijñātavān vipatitaḥ samāpta ākhyāyakā śrutevacanam mena ityādi hāsya taskarā saṃskāra artha śiṣyenīyamānāni pratyapajahaḥ apahratavantaḥ kinnimittam dhanam nīyamānam vṛttā ākhyāyikā sūcitā aṣṭādhyāya śākalyena samāna saṃvādaḥ nivṛttaḥ śāpaḥ dattaḥ pure atithye mariṣyasi prāpsyanti mamāra brāhmaṇān gaḥ dhanam irtavyam nyāyam matvā tūṣṇīmbhūteṣu brāhmaṇeṣu he brāhemaṇā bhagavanta sambodhya madhye icchati yājñavalkyam pṛcchat yūyam pṛcchami yuṣmān brāhmaṇā brāhmaṇā uktā pragalbhāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ pratyuttaram vaktum apragalbha brāhmaṇeṣu vakṣyamāṇaiḥ pṛṣṭavān vṛkṣasya viśeṣaṇam amṛpā amṛpā lomā ni itarasya vanaspateḥ parṇā ni tvagasya vahiḥ itarasya vanaspateḥ tvaca sakāśāt dṛḍham snāvnaḥ kināṭasya abhyantaratas kāṣṭhā ni vanaspateḥ majjopamā majjāyāḥ viśeṣaḥ arthaḥ vanaspateḥ vanaspateḥ chinnaḥ prādurbhavati punarnavataraḥ pūrvasmāt abhinavataraḥ viśeṇāt prāk vanaspateḥ praṣṭavyam aniṣyamāṇasya praṣṭavyaḥ jātasya jāta āta upasmin viṣaye praśna dyata jāyata anyathā akṛta abhyāgama kṛta nāśa prasaṅga at mṛtam vijajñuḥ jagataḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ brahmiṣṭha hratā jitā samāptā ākhyāyikā jagataḥ vyapadiśyate brāhmaṇān pṛṣṭavān śrutiḥ abhyam vijñaptiḥ viṣaya vijñānavat duḥkha anuvidvam prasannam śivam atulam anāya asaṃnitya tṛptame karasamiti arthaḥ umaya viśeṇavat rāteḥ paṣṭha yatha prathamā dhanasya arthaḥ dhanasya yajamānasya phalasya pradātṛ eṣaṇābhyasyasmin brahmāṇi akarma vetti vicca vida arthaḥ vicāryate ānanda sukha vācī prasidvaḥ viśeṣaṇa tvena ānanda śrūyate śruti antare vyajānāt syāta bhūmā sukham evamādyāḥ saṃvedye sukhe ānanda prasidvaḥ brahmānandaḥ saṃvedyaḥ yuktā brahmaṇi ānanda śabdāḥ nanu śruti prāmāṇyāt saṃvedya ānanda svarūpam vicāryam virudva śruti vākya darśanāt ānanda brahmaṇi śrūyate pratiṣedhaḥ ekatve bhūmā sampariṣvaktaḥ kiñcana ityādi virudva śruti vākya darśanāt kartavyaḥ vicāraḥ yuktam vāki artha nirṇayāya vicārayitum mokṣa vādi vipratipatteḥ sāṃkhyā vaiśeṣikāḥ mokṣa vādinaḥ mokṣe sukham saṃvedyam vipratipannāḥ nigtiśayam sukham sva saṃvadya miti yuktam ānanda ādi śravaṇāt jakṣata krīḍan ramamāṇaḥ asayāda bhavata sarvajñaḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ mokṣe sukham saṃvedyam nanu tve kāraka vimāgamāvād anupapattiḥ kriyāyāḥ ane kakārakrasādhyā vijñānasya kriyā doṣaḥ śabda prāmāṇyāt bhavet ānanda viṣaye ityādīni ānanda svarūpasya asaṃvedya tve anupapannāni vacanāni avocāma nanu vacanena śaityam udakasya cauṣbhyam kriyate jñāpaka vacanānām deśa antare śīta śakyate jñāpayitum agamye deśa antare uṣṇam pratyak ānanda darśana at avijñānam aitvevam ādīnām vacanānām śītaḥ ityādi vākyavat ādi virudva artha pratipādaka anubhūyate avirudva artha sukhya ham sukha ātmakam vedayate sutarām pratyakṣā virudvārtha ātmakam vedayate ānanda pratipādikāḥ śrutayaḥ samañjasāḥ syuḥ ajakṣat krīḍan ramamāṇaḥ evamādyāḥ uktāḥ kārya karaṇa abhāve anupapatteḥ vijñānasya viyogaḥ mokṣa ātyantikaḥ bhāve karaṇa anupapattiḥ āśraya abhāva at anupattiḥ ākārya karaṇa deha dyabhāve utpattau kārya karaṇa upādāna ānarthakya prasaṅgaḥ ekatva virodhāt ānanda ātmakam nitya nityam saṃsāri saṃsāra vinirmuktaḥ svābhāvyam pratipadyeta jalāśaya udaka añjaliḥ kṣiptaḥ pṛthaktvena vyavatiṣṭhate ānanda ātmaka mukta ānanda ātmakam vedayate anarthakam vākyam muktaḥ vedayate pratyak ānanda svarūpa ekatva virodhaḥ sati śruti virodhaḥ kalpanā upapadyate nirantara ānanda avijñāna kalpanā narthakyam nirantaram ānanda viṣayam svabhāva kalpanā anupapanna prasaṅge kalpanāyāḥ arthavat vetti iṣu ādya āsakta nairantaryeṇa ūṣu jñāna ajñāna kalpanāyā arthavat vicchinnam vijñānasya chidre anya viṣayatva prasaṅgaḥ naśya vikriyāvat anityatva prasaṅgaḥ svarūpa anvākhyāna śrutiḥ ānanda saṃvedyatva artha ajakṣat krīḍan ādi śruti virodhaḥ asaṃvedyatva ekatve prāpta anuvādi muktasya bhāve sati kvacid yogiṣu jakṣaṇa ādi prāptam yathāprāptam anūdyate bhāvāt bhāva mokṣa stutaye prāpta anuvadi tve duḥkhi yogi ādiṣu yathāprāpta jakṣaṇa ādivat sthāvara ādiṣu yathāprāpta duḥkhi kṛta kārya karaṇa upādhi samparka janita bhrānti adhyāropita sukhitva duḥkhi ādi viśeṣasya parihratam virudva śrutīnām viṣayam avocāma itivat sarvāṣya ānanda vākyāni draṣṭavyāni adhyāye navamam brāhmaṇam vaideha āsān sambandhaḥ ādyān bhedanena pañcadhā vyāhya pratyūhya anyonya pratiṣṭham ādi paḍhta vṛtya ātmake samāna ākhye jagat ātmanu sūtra upasaṃhṛtya jagat sūtra upasaṃhṛtya jagat anaṃśarīra hṛdaya sūtra avastham atikrāntavān ya aupaniṣadaḥ vyapadiṣṭaḥ akṣāñcopādāna kāraṇa svarūpeṇa nirdiṣṭaḥ avijñānam ādi dvāreṇa adhigamaḥ kartavya adhigamana upāya antara arthaḥ ārambhaḥ brāhmaṇa dvayasya ākhyāyikā ācāra pradarśana arthā vaideha āsān kṛtavān āsthāyikām dattavān arthaḥ darśana kāmebhyaḥ rājñaḥ avasare āgatavān yogakṣema rājñaḥ vivadiṣām anugraha āgatam yajñavalkyam yathāvat pūjām uktavān he kimartham āgataḥ āhosvit sūkṣma sūkṣma vastu nirṇaya mattaḥ śrotum he vājapeya ājñayā rājyam mantraṇam he samastasya bhāratasya varṣasya kintu ācāryaḥ aneka ācāryaḥ aneka ācārya sevī itara abravadīt uktavān āacāryaḥ nāmataḥ śilinasya apatyam śaili nirvāgvai vāgdevatā āhetapaḥ putrasya samyak anuśāstri anuśāsana kartrī ata anuśāstā upanayanāt samāvartanāt ācāryaḥ anuśāstā śuddhi traya hetu saṃyuktaḥ sādhāda ācāryaḥ kadācid apu prāmāṇāt vyabhicarati śiṣyāya śaili niruktavān avadataḥ mūkasya amutra kiñcana kintu uktavāḥ brahmaṇa kāleṣu ya āśrayaḥ itara ekapād pādaḥ ekapād pādaiḥ śūnyam upāsyamānam phalāya arthaḥ sannaḥ asmabhyam he cā aha ayatanam vāgdevasya karaṇam avyākṛta ākhyaḥ utpatti laya kāleṣu itīyam caturthaḥ pādaḥ ki nimittam ayatana vyatirikte tadvat katha uktavān vyatiriktā prajñāti ucyate asmākam ukte prajñāyakate rgvaidādi yāga nimitta homa nimittam āśitamanna dā ni m ittam pāna dāna nimitta mayam janma pratipattavyam janma vaisamrāj nānam vidam bali dāna ādibhiḥ pāta uttara ya niṣkriya tulya gaḥ sahasretat hastṛṣabham ananuśiṣya śiṣyam kṛtārtham akṛtvā śiṣyāt dhanam abhiprāyaḥ nāmataḥ śulbasya apatyam śaulbasya apatyam pūrvavat ayanam he arthāya aya patita ādikam apratigṛhyasya ugrādeḥ nimittam āśaṅkam arthaḥ taskara ādi ākīrṇām ba dha aśahkā tve nāmataḥ vṛṣṇasya apatyam ityādityaḥ hastinam anyau brūyat vyabhicarati avyabhicāri gardabhī vipīta nāmataḥ gotrataḥ diśa śrotrasyā anantyam prācīm udīcām kāñcid asyā antaṅgacchati kañcid apu anantā ān antyam ṣa anantyam satyakāma nāmataḥ jabālāyāḥ apatyam candramā ānanda upaniṣati mana anandaḥ samrāṭa abhikāmayamānaḥ abhihāryate prārthayata arthaḥ abhikāmayamānaḥ abhihāryate anurūpaḥ ānanda hetuḥ nirvartyate mana ātmakāni hṛdaya āśrayāṇi avocāma bāhmaṇe hṛdaya vadhṛtaye sravāṇi viśeṣaṇāni brahmāṇi ācāryaka hitvā āsana viśeṣāt utthāya samīpam avasarpa nyādayoḥ nipatan arthaḥ uktavān he anuśādhi arthaḥ vākya parisamāpti arthaḥ he gamiṣyan sothalena gamiṣyat āvam jalena gamiṣyan brahmāṇi yuktāni upāsīnaḥ tmāsi atyantam saṃyukta kevalam pūjyaḥ cā aḍhyaḥ daridra arthaḥ adhītaḥ uktāḥ upaniṣada ācāryaiḥ am ka vibhūtati saṃpannaḥ sanbhayaya madhyaḥ cha paramāt jñānena vinākṛta artha arthaḥ vetsi deha ādi mucyamāna toratha sthānīyābhiḥ vastu prāpsyasi vastu pūjā vanveda jāne jānīṣe gataḥ kṛtārthaḥ syā prasannaḥ śṛṇu indha evaṃnāmā antara gta akṣat nakṣaṇi viśeṣeṇa vyavasthitaḥ nāmā dīpti guṇa pratyakṣam indha āca kṣateparokṣeṇa grahaṇam dviṣanti vaiśvānaram saṃpannaḥ vaiśvānaram saṃpannaḥ bhoktuḥ bhogyā bhogya cāttā ya antara hṛdaya piṇḍasya madhye vakṣyamāṇam bhojyam hetuḥ ya eṣe piṇḍa ākāra āpannā pariṇamate punarā pacyamānam pariṇamate lohitāt akrameṇa pāñcabhautikam piṇḍam upacinoti aṇiṣṭhaḥ piṇḍa liṅga mithunībhūtasya taijasam indrāṇi oḥ mithunībhūtayoḥ sūkṣmāsu nāḍīṣu anupraviṣṭaḥ hetuḥ ucyate ityādi pravāraṇam bhuktavatoḥ svapatoḥ sāmānyam kalpayati śrutiḥ ki aneka chidra bahula mārgaḥ saṃcanarataḥ svapnat deśa āgamana mārgaḥ ahṛdaya deśāt abhimukhī sati parimāṇam ucyate atyanta sūkṣmaḥ sūkṣmā dehasya saṃbandhinyaḥ hitā hitā khyātā nāḍyāḥ māsaṃpiṇḍe pritiṣṭhitā viprarūḍhāḥ sarvatra kadamba kesa pavat nāḍobhiḥ atyanta sūkṣmābhiḥ annama asravat gacchat annena bhūtena upacīyamānam sthūlena annena upacitaḥ piṇḍa sūkṣmeṇa annena upacitam piṇḍa upacaya karam praviviktam mūtra purīṣa ādi apekṣya liṅga karam sākṣmataram āhāraḥ āhārāt āhāratara liṅga ivā vaiśvānarāt sūkṣmāt upacitaḥ hṛdaya bhūtaḥ sūkṣma bhūtena vidhriyamāṇaḥ viduṣaḥ krameṇa vaiśvānarāt taijasam prāptasya hṛdaya āpannasya hṛdaya āpannasya prāk gatāḥ digdakṣiṇe kreṇa ātmakam tvena upagataḥ pratyak upasaṃhṛtya draṣṭu bhāvam krameṇa ityādi vyākhyātam janma maraṇa ādi nimitta bhaya śūnyam he uktavān uktam he pūjau jñāpayasi prāpitavān upādhi kṛta ajñāna vyavadhāna apanayanena arthaḥ niṣkriya prayacchāmi dattavate yatheṣṭam bhujyanta āmayam dāsa bhāve sthitaḥ yatheṣṭam rājyam pracati padyasva arthaḥ abhisaṃbandhaḥ maya draṣṭi tyādi śrutibhyaḥ vadana ādi liṅgaḥ vyatirikta kāṇḍe ajāta śatru saṃvāde ādi kartṛtva bhoktṛtva pratyākhyānena adhigataḥ prāṇana ādi upanyasya auṣasta praśne prāṇana ādi liṅgaḥ sāmānyena adhigataḥ ityādinā draṣṭa ādinālupta śakti svabhāvaḥ adhigataḥ upādhi nimittaḥ saṃsāraḥ rajjūṣara śuktikā gagana ādiṣu sarpet akaraja malinatva ādi parādhi āropaṇa nimittam svatas nirupādhikaḥ nirupākhyaḥ vyapadeśyaḥ antara praśasta aupaniṣadaḥ adhigatam indhasajñaḥ āhāraḥ liṅga jagat upādhiḥ pravilāpya jagadātmānam upādhi rajju ādau sarpa ādikam adhigatam pariprāpitaḥ yājñavalkyenā agamataḥ saṃkṣepataḥ suṣupta turīyāṇi upani anya prasaṅgena svapnāt vāreṇa mahatā tarkeṇa vistarataḥ adhigamaḥ kartavyaḥ prāpayitavyam sadbhāvāḥ cā atmanaḥ vipratipatti nirākaraṇa dvāreṇa vyatirikta śuddha svayan jyotiṣṭvam alupta śakti svarūpa niratiśaya ānanda svābhāvyam advaita adhigantavyam ārabhyate ākhyāyayikā saṃpradāna grahaṇa vidhi prakāśana arthā stutaye viśeṣataḥ vara dāna ādi sūcanāt gacchan cintitavān apu rājñe gamana prayojanam yogakṣema vadiṣya evaṃsaṃkalpaḥ pṛṣṭavān hetuḥ saṃkalpitasya anyathā karaṇa atrā akhyāyikām ācaṣṭe pūrvatra yājñavalkyoḥ saṃvāda nimitte agnihotra viṣayam upalabhya parituṣṭaḥ janakāya varanda dau praśnam vṛtavān vara pradāna sāmarthyena avyācikhyāsum apidau yājñavalkyam uṣṇaim anuktiḥ vidyāyāḥ viruddha vidyāyāḥ svātantryāt svatantrā sahakāri sādhana antara nirapekṣā artha sādhana he saṃbodhya abhimukhīkaraṇāya kiñjyotiḥ vyavaharati kiñjyotiḥ prākṛtaḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghāta pāṇi ādimān pṛcchyate sva avayava asaṃghāta bāhyena vyavaharati āhosvit svāvayava saṃghāta madhya pātinā jyotiṣkārya mayam nirvartayati abhipretya pṛcchati kiñcātaḥ vyatiriktena avyatiriktena jyotiṣkāryam nirvartayati śṛṇu kāraṇam vyatiriktena jyotiṣkārya nirvartaka svabhāvaḥ nirdhāritaḥ adṛṣṭa jyotiṣkārya viṣaye anumāsyāmahe vyatirikta nimittam kāryam avyatiriktena sva vyavaharati apratyakṣe jyotiṣi jyotiṣkārya darśane abyatiriktam anumeyam aniyama vyatiriktam avyatiriktam vyavahāra hetuḥ anadhyavasāya viṣaya pṛcchati yājñavalkyam kiñjyotiḥ nanu anumāna kauśale praśnena pratipadyata liṅga liṅgi saṃbandha viśeṣāṇām atyanta saukṣmyāt duravabodhyatām bahūnām apu paṇḍitānām ekasya ata sūkṣma nirṇaye pariṣad vyāpāra iṣyate viśeṣaḥ apekṣyate avarā pariṣattrayaḥ anumāna kauśalam rājñaḥ yuktaḥ kauśala tāratamya upapatteḥ puruṣāṇām athavā śrutiḥ akhyāyikā vyājena anumāna mārgam upanyasya bodhayati matimanusartī abhiprāya bhijña vyatiriktam bodhayiṣyan vyatirikta pratipādakam prasiddham sva avayava ghāta vyatiriktena anugrāhakeṇa prākṛtaḥ āsta upaviśati prayeti kṣetram bāhi aneka pradarśanam liṅgasya avyabhicāritva darśana ita kiñjyotiḥ candramā vāgjyotiḥ parigṛhyate viṣayeṇa indriye saṃpradīpte viveka upajāyate bāhyām ceṣṭām ova śṛṇotī brāhmaṇam purvāc ujyotiṣṭvam aprasiddham ata ī anugṛhītaḥ ayaṭam vyavaharati prasiddham jyotiṣṭvam prāvṛṣi prāyeṇa medhā andhakāre pratyasta maye prāṇiḥ hastaḥ vispaṣṭam nirjñāyate ceṣṭā nirodhe prāpte bāhya jyotiṣaḥ abhāvāt śvā bhaṣati rauti upaiva manasoḥ naiḥ antayam jyotiṣkārya pratipadyeta upanyā sannihitaḥ arthaḥ vipalya vāgyotiṣaḥ grahaṇam gandha ādīnā anupalakṣaṇa gandha ādibhiḥ ghrāṇa ādiṣu anugṛhīteṣu pravṛtti nivṛtya ādayaḥ taiḥ anugrahaḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghātasya śāntāyāḥ gandha ādiṣu śānteṣu bāhyeṣu anugrāhakeṣu pravṛtti nirodhaḥ uktam viṣaye bahirmukha karaṇāni ādīni ādityādi jyotirbhiḥ anugṛhyāmāṇāni sphuṭataraḥ saṃvyavahāraḥ puruṣasyadṛṣṭā manyāmahe bāhya pratyasta maye suṣupta jāgarite tādṛś avasthāyām sva avayava saṃghāta vyatiriktena jyotiṣkārya siddhiḥ dṛśyate jyotiṣkārya siddhiḥ bandhu saṃgamana viyoga darśanam deśa antra gamana ādi suṣuptat utthānam sukham asva apsam avediṣam vyatiriktam ucyate kārya karaṇa sva avayava saṃghāta vyatiriktam kārya karaṇa avabhāsakam ādityādi bāhi jyotiḥvat anavabhāsyamānam abhidhīyate stham pāriśeṣyāt kārya karaṇa vyatiriktam siddham kārya karaṇa vyatiriktam kārya karaṇa saṃghāta anugrāhakam bāhyaiḥ ādi karaṇaiḥ upalabhyamānam ādibhiḥ upalabhyata ādi jyotiḥṣu uparateṣu kāryam jyotiṣaḥ dṛśyote aste vipalya nūnam antaraḥstham avagamyate kiñcā adityādi vilakṣaṇam abhautikam hetuḥ ādi agrāhyam ādivat samāna jātīyena ādityādi kārya karaṇa saṃghātasya bhautikasya bhautikena upakāraḥ kriyamāṇaḥ dṛśyate duṣṭam anumeyam kārya karaṇāt artha upakārakam āt itya ādivat jyotisthā kārya karaṇa saṃghāta samāna jātīyam anumeyam kārya karaṇa ghāta upakāraka ādityādi jyotiḥvat stha apratyakṣa vailakṣaṇyam ucyate ādi jyotirbhiḥ anaikāntikam apratyakṣāṇi sthāni ādi jyotīṃṣi bhautikāni manoratha mātram vilakṣaṇam siddham kārya karaṇa saṃghāta bhāva bhāvi saṃghāta anumīyate jyotiṣaḥ sāmānyatas dṛṣṭasya anumānasya vyabhicāri aprāmāṇyam sāmānyatas dṛṣṭa balena āt itya ādivat vyatiriktam sādhayati kārya karaṇebhyaḥ pratyakṣam anumānena bādhitum śakyate kārya karaṇa saṃghātaḥ pratyakṣam upakārakam āt ityādivat atmā syajyotiḥ ādivat ya pratyakṣam darśana kriyām atmā kārya karaṇa saṃghātaḥ virodhe anumānasya aprāmāṇyāt nanu darśana ādi krāya atmā saṃghātaḥ avikalasya darśana ādi kriyā kartṛ kadācid kadācid doṣaḥ dṛṣṭa anupapannam khadyote prakāśa aprakāśa tvena dṛśyamāne kāraṇa anumeyam anumeya tve kenacid sāmānyāt sarvatra anumeyam aniṣṭam padārtha svabhāvaḥ uṣṇa svābhāvyam anya nimittam udakasya śaityam adharma ādi apekṣam adharma ādeḥ nimitta antara apekṣa svabhāva prasaṅgaḥ anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ aniṣṭaḥ smṛtyoḥ dṛṣṭasya darśanāt uktam svabhāva vādinā dehasya darśana ādi kriyā vyatiriktasya dehasya darśana ādi kriyā dṛṣṭasya darśanam andhaḥ dṛṣṭa śāka dvīpa ādi gatam adṛṣṭa cetat siddham dṛṣṭa vastu vidyamāne at rākṣīt deha dehaḥ draṣṭāsa adrākṣīt uddhṛte dṛṣṭa prasiddhiḥ himavataḥ śṛṅgam uddhṛta cakṣuṣām andhānām apu anuddhṛte cakṣuṣiḥ dṛś deha avagamyate smṛtau dṛṣṭṛ smartroḥ ekatve sati ya draṣṭāsa smartā nimīlita sman dṛṣṭa dṛṣṭavat nimīlitam draṣṭṛyat nimīlite smarat animīlite avagamyate mṛte dehe avikalasya ādi darśana abhāvāt draṣṭru tve mṛte darśana ādi kriyā tasmādi apāye dehe darśanam dbhāve darśana ādi kriyā kartṛ avagamyate ādīni darśana ādi kriyā kartṝṇi spṛśāmi bhinna kartṛka tve pratisaṃghāna anupapatteḥ viṣaya ādivat dṛṣṭṛtva ādi anupapatti stham vyatiriktam ādivat siddham uktam kārya karaṇa saṃghāta samāna jātīyam anumeyam ādityādibhiḥ samāna jātīyaiḥ upakriyamāṇa upakārya upakāraka bhāvasya aniyama darśanāt pārthivaiḥ indhanaiḥ pārthavatu asamāna jātīyaiḥ ulapa ādibhiḥ prajvalana upakāraḥ kriyamāṇaḥ dṛśyate samāna jātīyaiḥ prajvana upakāraḥ sarvatra anumeyaḥ udakena prajvalana upakāraḥ bhinna jātī yona vaidyutasya jāṭharasya kriyamāṇaḥ dṛśyate upakārya upakāraka bhāve samāna jātīya asamāna jātīya niyamaḥ kadācid samāna jātīyā manuṣyā manuṣyaiḥ upakriyante kadācid sthāvara paśu ādibhiḥ bhinna jātīyaiḥ ahetuḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghāta māna jātīyaiḥ ādi jyotirbhiḥ upakriyamāṇa it i ādibhiḥ ādi jyotiḥvat adṛśya hetuḥ antarasya stha vailakṣaṇyam sādhayati ādibhiḥ anaikāntika ādi karaṇebhyaḥ anya tve sati hetoḥ viśeṣaṇatva upapatteḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghāta jyotiṣa uktam anumāna virodhāt ādi jyotiḥvat kārya karaṇa saṃghātāt artha anumānam uktam virudhyata pratijñā kāraya karaṇa saṃghāta jyotiṣa bhāva bhāvi asiddham mṛte dehe jyotiṣaḥ adarśanāt sāmānyatas dṛṣṭasya anumānasya aprāmāṇye sati pāna bhojana ādi vyavahāra lopa prasaṅgaḥ aniṣṭaḥ pāna bhojana ādiṣu kṣudh pipāsā ādi nivṛttim upalabdha vasaḥ sāmānyāt pāna bhojana ādi upādānam dṛśyamānam dṛśyante upalabdha pāna bhojanāḥ sāmānyatas pāna bhojana antaraiḥ kṣudh pipāsā ādi nivṛttim anum invantaḥ tādartheyana pravartamānāḥ mayam dehaḥ darśana ādi kriyā parihṛtam smṛti oḥ dehāt artha antara bhūtaḥ antarasya pratyuktam khadyota ādeḥ kādācid prakāśa aprakāśa pakṣa ādi avayava saṃkoca vikāsa nimititta prakāśa aprakāśa punaruktam adharmayoḥ avaśyam phala dātṛ svabhāvaḥ abhyupagantavya abhyubagame siddhānta hānāt anavasthā doṣaḥ pratyuktaḥ vyatiriktam stham vyatiriktatva ādi siddham samāna jātīya anugrāhakatva darśana nimitta bhrāntyā karaṇānām anyatamaḥ vyatiriktaḥ avivekataḥ pṛcchati katama nyāya sūkṣma tāyāḥ durvijñeya upapadyate bhrāntiḥ athavā vyatirikte siddhe karaṇa vijñānavantī vivekata anupalabdha katama deha indriya manaḥsu ayā asta uktam athavā tvayā abhipretaḥ prāṇā samuditeṣu brāhmaṇeṣu tejasvinaḥ katama ṣaḍaṅga pūrvasmin vyākhyāne katama praśna vākyam ayaḥ katama edatantam maya śabdasya praśna vākyam ayaḥ katama edatantam maya śabdasya nirdhārita artha viśeṣa viṣaya katama śabdasya praśna vākya parisamāpti artha vyavahita saṃbandham yuktam katama praśna vākyam ityādi prativacanam niścīyate nirdeśaḥ ayaḥ prāyaḥ buddhi upādhi saṃprakā vekāt maya ucyate buddhi saṃpṛkta upalabhyate rāhuḥ saṃpṛktaḥ buddhiḥ artha karaṇam pradīpaḥ purovasthitaḥ śṛṇotī uktam buddhi āloka viśiṣṭam viṣaya upalabhyate purovasthita pradīpa āloka viśiṣṭam dvāra mātrāṇi karaṇa buddheḥ viśeṣyate maya vijñapti vikāra vyākhyānam ayaḥ maya ādau maya śabdasya anya artha darśanāt aśrauta artha tāvasīyate saṃdigdhaḥ padārathaḥ niścita prayoga darśanāt nirdhārayitum śakyaḥ vāśya śeṣāt niścata nyāya balāt uttaratra pāṭhāt vacana āt yuktam prāya vyatireka pradarśa arthā saptamī vṛkṣeṣu pāṣāṇa sāmīpya lakṣaṇā vyātiḥ avyatireka saṃdihyata prāṇebhyaḥ vyatirikta arthaḥ yeṣu vyatiriktaḥ pāṣāṇeṣu atat jātīya buddhiḥ ata hṛdat puṇḍarīka ākāraḥ puṇḍaḥ tātthyāt buddhiḥ hṛd tasyā buddhau buddhi vṛtti vyatireka pradarśana avabhāsa ātmaka ucyate avabhāsakenā atmanā aste cenāvān kārya karaṇa prakāśa ghaṭaḥ marakata ādiḥ maṇiḥ kṣīra ādi dravye prakṣiptaḥ parīkṣaṇāya chāyam kṣīra ādiḥ dvyam tādṛś eda ātmajya pabuddheḥ sūkṣma hṛdyantaḥstham hṛdaya ādikam kārya karaṇa saṃghātam ekīkṛtyā atma pūrṇa niratiśayam svayan jyotiṣṭvam avabhāsaka anya anava bhāsya svabhāvaḥ pṛcchasi katama bāhyānām karaṇa anugrāhakāṇām pratyasta maye antaḥkaraṇa dvāreṇa anugrāhakaḥ karaṇānām uktam bāhya karaṇa anugrāhakāṇām ādityādi bhāvaḥ ādityādi artha kārya karaṇa saṃghātasya ācaitanye sva artha anupapatteḥ sva artha jyotiṣa anugraha abhāve kārya karaṇa saṃghātaḥ vyavahārāya kalpate anugraheṇa saṃvyavahāraḥ caittasaṃjñānam ityādi śruti antarāt abhimānaḥ saṃvyavahāpaḥ abhimāna hetum marakata maṇi dṛṣṭāntena avocāma tattha viṣaye karaṇa agocara jyotiṣaḥ buddhi ādi bāhya abhyantara kārya viśuddhiḥ śūnya vādi pakṣaḥ pramāṇa vipratiṣiddha nirākaraṇāya nā adaraḥ kriyate dehe mṛtyaḥ kārya karaṇāni atikramya sva ātmajyetiṣyāḥ ta prakṛtaḥ ajāyamānaḥ jāyamāna ucyate deha indriya saṃghātam abhyām anavaracam saṃcarati parokau janma maraṇābhyām kārya karaṇa upādāna parityāga anavaratam pratipadyamāna saṃsāra mokṣāt saṃcarati siddham asyā atma yajyotiṣaḥ anya kārya karaṇa rūpebhyaḥ upādānam satyatrāyam puraṣaḥ svayan ucyate doṣaḥ viṣaya darśayitum śakyaḥ anyathā asati viṣaye kasmiṃścid suṣupta kāla bhā vāsanā ātmikā viṣaya upalabhyamānā asiḥ kośāt niṣkṛṣṭaḥ saṃsarga rahitam ādi kārya karaṇa vyāvṛtta svarūpam alupta dṛś avabhāsayat puruśaḥ svayan siddham nanu svayan jāgarata grāhya grāhaka ādi lakṣaṇaḥ vyavahāraḥ dṛśyate ādi anugrāhakāḥ cā ādyā dṛśyante jāgarite viśeṣa āśrayam dṛśyate jyotiṣaḥ dṛśyate alupta dṛśaḥ kevalam asiḥ kośāt vivivaktam tatrā sukha viśeṣā harṣā ādi lābha nimittāḥ ta prakorṣa upetāḥ cā ananda ādīn veśa antāḥ palvalāḥ taḍāgāḥ sravanti aḥ veśānta ādīn vāsanā mātra rūpān tdava āsana aśracitta vṛti udbhava nimitta hetu tvena avocāma kartṛ kriyā sādhana abhāvāt kārakam kriyā hasta pāda ādīni kriyā kārakāṇi saṃbhavanti ka vidyante jāgarite alupta dṛś ādi śakti svābhāvyāt vasana ākāra udbhūta anantaḥkaraṇa vṛtya āśrayā nbāhya ādhyātmikān ela bhāvān pratyastamitān suptā anabhicākaśītya lupyā atma dṛṣṭyā avabhāsati arthaḥ jyotiṣmad indriya mātra punor hiraṇmaya caitanya svabhāvaḥ haṃsa sva pneha ādīn vṛttinā paripālayan anyathā mṛta bhrāntiḥ nikṛṣṭam aneka aśuci saṃghāta atyanta bībhatsam nīḍam stha saṃbandha abhāvāt stha bahiścaritvā avidyāyāḥ satatva avadhāraṇa kaṇḍikā arabhyate pāṇi ādi lakṣaṇasya etā hitā parimāṇena tvena tāśṭa rasasya śuklatva ādibhī viśeṣaiḥ arthaḥ ethe varṇa viśeṣā vāta pitta śleṣmaṇām itaretara saṃyoga udbhāsita antaḥkaraṇa vṛtya āśrayā duḥkha svarūpa vṛtyā āśrayā duḥkha svarūpa kiṃbahunā ādi lakṣaṇam bhaya vinā ādi avidyā vāsanayā mṛṣā udbhūtayā avidyā apakṛṣyamāṇā utkṛṣyamāṇā kiṃviṣayā kiṃlakṣaṇā ucyate viṣayā udbhūtā udbhūtayā vāsanayā ivā ucyate rājya abhiṣiktaḥ rāja vāsanā vāsitaḥ atyanta prakṣīyamāṇā udbhūtā viṣayā bhāvitaḥ bhāvaḥ atmanaḥ bhāvaḥ svābhāvakaḥ bhāvāt bāla agra mātram anya tvena dṛśyate avasthā vidyī pratyupasthāpitā anātma bhāvā aparamāḥ sthāvara antāḥ saṃvyavahāra viṣayān apekṣma bhāvaḥ samastaḥ apakṛṣyamāṇāyām avidyāyām kāṣṭām gatāyām bhāvaḥ mokṣaḥ svayan jyotiṣṭvam pratyakṣata upalabhyate avidyā kārye bhāvaḥ paricchinna bhāvaḥ śuddhayā asarvaḥ anyatas cad pravibhaktaḥ pravabhaktaḥ virudhyate viruddha hanyate vicchādyate asarva viṣaya tve bhinna samastaḥ sankutaḥ bhidyate virudhyetaviroda abhāve hanyate vicchādyate ata avidyāyāḥ sattvam uktam asarva tvena grāhayati anyadhaḥ tvaram avidyamānam pratyupasthāpayati asarvam āpādayati viṣayaḥ bhidyate kāmataḥ kriyām upādatte phalam uktam vakṣyamāṇam itara ityādi avidyāyāḥ sata kāryeṇa pradarśitam vidyāyāḥ kāryam bhāvaḥ pradarśitaḥ avidyāyāḥ viparyeṇa avidyā nā atmanaḥ svābhāvikaḥ utkṛṣyamāṇāyām apacīyamānā gatāyām vidyāya aṃpari niṣṭhite bhāve nivartate rajjvām sarpa jñānam rajju niścaye uktam ityādi nā atma avidyā svābhāvikasya ucchittiḥ kadācid upadyate uṣṇya prakāśayoḥ mokṣa aupapadyate bhāvaḥ mokṣaḥ phalam kriyā kāraka phala śūnyam pratyakṣataḥ nirdiśyate avidyā santi prastutam kañcana kañcana paśyāti bhāvaḥ asaḥ uktaḥ aticchandā aticchandam arthaḥ paratvāt chandaḥ atigataḥ candaḥ rūpāt aticchandam sāntar chandaḥ ādi chanda uvācī vacanaḥ aticchandā pāṭhaḥ svādhyāya vacana prayuttkaḥ chanda asvacchandaḥ aparacchandaḥ ādau aaticchandam upaneyam varjitam arthe ṣabdena adharmau ucyete uttka adharma varjitam avidyā kāryam aavidyayā uttkam kārya dvāreṇa kāraṇa pratiṣedhaḥ āvidyā varjitam phalam sarvatma bhāvaḥ itad chanda saṃsāra varjitam ate upanyasyam atīta anantara brahmaṇa samāptau āgamataḥ tarkataḥ prapañcitam darśita āgama artha pratyaya dārḍhyāya caitanya svabhāvaḥ caitanya avabhāsayati ramatecarati uttkam nyāyataḥ nityam svarūpam caitanya jyotiṣṭvam yātma avinaṣṭaḥ vartate svapnayoḥ ucyate śṛṇvātra ajñāna hetum ajñāna hetuḥ ucyate dṛṣṭāntena pratyakṣībhavati vivakṣitor iṣṭāyāḥ sampariṣvattakaḥ samyak pariṣvattkaḥ kāmayantyā kāmukaḥ kiñcana mattaḥ vastu sukhī duḥkhī apariṣvatt kastu pravibhatt bheva brāhyam ābhyantaram pariṣvaṅga uttara kālantu ekatva āpatteḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ mātra asaṃsargataḥ khilyavat pravibhattkaḥ jala ādau ādi pratibimbavat kārya karaṇa prajñena arthena svābhāvikena sampariṣvattkaḥ samyak pariṣvakta ekībhūtaḥ nirantaraḥ kiñcana vastu āntaram sukhī duḥkhī caitanya svabhāva tve aprākṣīḥ hetuḥ uttka strīpuṃsayoḥ sampariṣvattkayoḥ arthān viśeṣa hetuḥ uttkam nānātve kāraṇ vastavantarasya pratyupasthāpikā avidyā uktam avidyāyā praviviktaḥ jñāna jñeya ādi kāraka vibhāge asati kutaḥ viśeṣa prādurbhāvaḥ svābhāvike svarūpstha jyotiṣi atmanaḥ svayan sva bhavasya yasma ātmaḥ āptāḥ kāmā sya anya tvena pravibhaktaḥ anāpta avasthāyām devadatta ādi kutaścid pravibhajyate vastu antarāt pravibhajyata āhosvit vastu antaramata yata kāmā pravibhaktā anya tvena kāmyamānā svapnayoḥ tasyā atmā anyatva pratyupasthāpaka hetoḥ avidyāyāḥ abhāvāt ata kāmya viṣaya abhāvāt śāka chidram śūnyam madhyam sarvathā varjitam arthaḥ prakṛtaḥ svayan avidyā vinirmukta uktam asaṅga āgantuka caitanya svabhāva tve sati ekībhāvāt strīpuṃsayoḥ saṃpariṣvaktayoḥ uktam prāsaṅgikam uktam krama ādivat svayan jyotiṣṭvam asyā atmanaḥ svabhāvaḥ upalabhyata āśaṅkāyām prāptāyām nirākaraṇāya strīpuṃsayoḥ dṛṣṭānta upādānena vidyamānasya svayan jyotiṣṭvasya suṣupte agrahaṇam ekībhāvāt hetoḥ ādivat āgantukam prāsaṅgikam abhidhāya prakṛtam anupravartayati prakṛtam avidyā vinirmuktam suṣupta pratyakṣata yathābhūtam abhihitam saṃbandha atītam suṣupta atichchanda janayitṛ nimittam asaṃbaddhaḥ saṃbandha nimittāt vinirmukta apitā pituḥ aputra ubhavati sāmarthyāt gamyate ubhayoḥ saṃbandha nimittam tamayatikrāntaḥ vartate uktam amātā jetavyā jitāḥ saṃbandha abhāvāt lokā alokāḥ bhūtāḥ saṃbandha atyayāt devā adevāḥ sādhya sādhana saṃbandha abhidhāyakā mantra lakṣaṇāḥ abhidhāka tvena bhūtā adhītā adhyetavyāḥ nimittam saṃbadhyante puruṣeṇa atikramaṇāt vedā avedāḥ saṃpadyante kevalam śubha saṃbandha atītaḥ aśubhaiḥ atyanta ghoraiḥ asaṃbaddha vartata atam arthām brāhmaṇa suvarṇa hartā ghnā pāṭhāt avagamyate ghoroṇa vinirmuktaḥ mahāpātakī stena ucyate abhrūṇa cāṇḍālaḥ kevalam pratyutpannena vinirmuktaḥ sahajena atyanta nikṛṣṭa jāti prāpakeṇa vinirmukta cāṇḍālaḥ brāhmaṇyām utpannaḥ caṇḍāla cāṇḍālaḥ jāti nimittena saṃbaddha acāṇḍālaḥ pulkasa kṣatriyāyām utpannaḥ apulkasaḥ aśrama lakṣaṇaiḥ asaṃbagaddhaḥ ucyate parivrāḍyat nimittaḥ vinirmukta aśramaṇaḥ pāpasaḥ vānaprasthaḥ atāpasaḥ varṇa āśrama ādīnām upalakṣaṇa ubhayoḥ grahaṇam bahunā ananva āgatam asaṃbandham śāstra vihitena vihita akaraṇa pratiṣiddha kriyā lakṣaṇena napuṃsaka rūpiti anuvartate asaṃbaddha tve kāraṇam hetuḥ ucyate evaṃrūpaḥ śokāḥ iṣṭa viṣaya prārthanā viṣaya viyoge āpadyate viṣayaṃma prāptam viyuktam uddiśya cintayānaḥ guṇān saṃtapyate śokaḥ ratiḥ paryāyāḥ sarava atītaḥ kañcana aticchandā uktam prakriyā āpatatas śahdaḥ vacana bhavitum hetuḥ yathākāmaḥ krayuḥ atitīrṇa yuktam ānan vāgatam ityādi puṇḍarīka ākāraḥ stham antaḥkaraṇam buddharhṛdayam ucyate tāt sthān mañcakrośanavat buddheḥ śokāḥ buddhi saṃśrayā ityādi mana ati kāmā saṃśraya bhrānti apanodāya vacanam śritā śokā hṛdaya karaṇa saṃbandha atītaḥ mṛtyaḥ uktam hṛdaya karaṇa sahandhā atīta saṃśraya saṃbandha atītaḥ yuktataram vacanam vādinaḥ kāmā vāsanāḥ hṛdaya saṃbandhinam ātmanam upasṛpya upaśliṣyanti hṛdaya viyoge cā atmani avatiṣṭhante puṭa tailasya puṣpa ādi gandha haryova śokā ityādīnām vacanānām ānarthakyam hṛdaya karaṇa utpādya śritā viśeṣaṇāt karaṇa mātra tve śritā vacanam samañjasam viśaddeḥ vivakṣita hṛt śrayaṇa vacanam yathārtham yuktam śrureḥ anyā artha asaṃbhavāt kāmā śritā viśeṣaṇāt āśrayā santi anāśrita apekṣa atrā aśraya apekṣya viśeṣaṇam anāśritāḥ apekṣya viśeṣaṇam aprarūñā bhaviṣyā bhūtāḥ pratipakṣataḥ nivṛttāḥ saṃbhāvyante yuktam apekṣya viśeṣaṇam prarūḍhā vartamānā viṣaye pramucyanta viśeṣaṇa ānarthakyam yatat mādhikyāt heya artha itaratha aśrutam aniṣṭam cakalpitam āśraya kāmānām kañcana kāmayata prāpta pratiṣedhāt āśraya kāmānām sadhīḥ nimitta āśrayatva prāpteḥ asaṅga vacanāt āśraya tve asaṅga vacanam upapadyate avocāma viṣayaḥ vyatirikta abhāva artha vaiśeṣika ādi tantra nyāya upapannam ādi āśraya śritā ityādi viśeṣa śruti virodha anapekṣyāḥ veśeṣikā ādi tantra upapattayaḥ śruti virodhe nyāya bhāsatva upagamāt svayan jyotiṣṭva bādhanāt ādīnām kevala dṛśi mātra viṣaya svayan jyotiṣṭvam siddham bādhyeta samavāyi tve dṛśyatva anupapatteḥ gata viśeṣavat dṛśyam artha antara svayan jyotiṣṭvam siddham bādhitam ādi āśraya parikalpyet śāstra artha vipratiṣedhāt parasya deśa kalpanāyām ādi āśraya tve śāstra artha kupyeta vistareṇa caturthe avocāma mahatā prayatnena ādi āśrayatva kalapnājha pratiṣeddhavyā ekatva śāstra artha siddhayeḥ kalpanāyām kriyamāṇāyām śāstra bādhitaḥ yathecca adhīnām kalpayantaḥ vaiśeṣikā naiyāyikāḥ śāstra artha bādhanāt nā adaraṇīyā puṃsayoḥ uktam svayan svayan svan jyotiṣṭvam caitanya svabhāva uṣṇatva ādivat caitanya svabhāva ekatve svabhāvam jahyāt jānīyāt suṣupte vipratiṣiddham caitanyam svabhāvaḥ vipratiṣiddham upapadyata suṣupte suṣupte jānīṣe gṛhṇīyāḥ nanu ānam suṣupte jānīme darśane karaṇam vyāpṛtam vyāpṛteṣu darśana śravaṇa ādiṣu vyavahāraḥ vyāpṛtāni karaṇāni paśyāmaḥ dṛṣṭa kartuḥ dṛṣṭiḥ vināśaḥ auṣṇyam nanu vipratiṣiddham abhidhīyate dṛṣṭiḥ viparilupyata ita aśakyam vaktum nanu viparilupyata vacanāt avināśinī vanacasya jñāpaka nyāya vināśaḥ kṛtakasya vacana śatena vārayitum śakyate vacanasya jñāpaka nyāya vināśaḥ kṛtakasya vacana śatena apu vārayitum śakyate vacanasya yathāprāpta artha jñāpaka doṣaḥ ādi prakāśaka tvavat darśana upapatteḥ adityādayaḥ nitya prakāśa svabhāvā svābhāvikena nityena prakāśena prakāśayanti aprakāśa prakāśam prakāśayanti svabhāvena nityena prakāśena viparilupta svabhāvayā dṛṣṭyā nityayā gauṇam draṣṭu mukhyatva upapatteḥ anyathā draṣṭu draṣṭu gauṇa darśana prakāraḥ mukhyam draṣṭu upapadyate anyathā adityādīnām prakāśayitṛ nityena sva bhāvikena akriyamāṇena prakāśakena prakāśayitṛ mukhyam prakāśayitṛtva antara anupapatteḥ dṛṣṭiḥ viparilupyata ita vipratiṣedha gandhaḥ nanu anitya kriyā kartṛ viṣaya tṛd pratyaya antasya śabdasya prayogaḥ chettā bhettā gantā prakāśayitā dṛṣṭa bhavatu prakāśakeṣu anyathā saṃbhavān dṛṣṭi aviparilopa anubhava darśanāt karaṇa vyāpāra viśeṣa apekṣa uddhṛta cakṣuṣām svapn aviparulopadarśanāt avipulupta svabhāva atmanaḥ atasya avipariluptayā dṛṣṭyā svayan svabhāvayā suṣupte ucyate viṣaya kiṃvaśiṣṭam draṣciḥ anya tvena upalabheta viśeṣa darśana kāraṇam antaḥkaraṇam cakṣū anyatvena pratyupasthāpitam kāla ekībhutam pariṣvaṅgāt paricchinnasya viśeṣa darśanāya karaṇam anya tvena vyatiṣṭhate saṃpiṣvaktaḥ prājñenā atmanā pṛthaktvena vyavasthitāni karaṇāni viṣayāḥ abhāvāt viśeṣa darśanam karaṇa ādi nā atma pratyavabhāsate ta bhrāntiḥ dṛṣṭiḥ parilupyataca manana vijñānayoḥ dṛṣṭi ādi sahakāri tve sati ādi nirapekṣe vartamāna viṣaya vyāpāraḥ vidyata grahaṇam dṛṣṭi ādīnām auṣṇya prakāśana jvalana ādivat bheda āhosvit abhinnasya upādhi nimittam anyatvam kecid vyācakṣate vastunaḥ svata goḥ godravya anumeyam sarvatra avyabhicāra darśanāt tadvat dṛṣṭi ādīnām parasparam anya paratvāt dṛṣṭi ādi bheda pradarśa vākyam ityādi caitanya suṣupte nūnam caitanya ātmajyotiḥ prāptau nirākaraṇayā ārabdham ityādi svapnayoḥ ādi aneka upādhi dvāram caitanya svābhāvyam upalakṣitam dṛṣṭi ādi abhidheya vyavahāra āpannam suṣuptam upādhi bheda vyāpāra nivṛttau anudbhāsyamāna anupalakṣyamāṇa svabhāvam upādhi bhedena bhinnam prāpta anuvādena vidyam āntavam ucyate dṛṣṭi ādi bheda kalpanā vivakṣita artha anabhijña ghanavat ghana śruti virodhāt anandam jñānam prajñānam ityādi śrutibhyaḥ śabda pravṛteḥ laukikaḥ śabda pravṛttaḥ śabdam rasanena annasya sarvatra dṛṣṭi ādi śabda abhidheyānām śabda vācyatām darśayati śabda pravṛttiḥ pramāṇam dṛṣṭānta upapatteḥ svaccha svābhāvya yuktaḥ sphacikaḥ nimittam kevalam harita nīla ādi upādhi bheda yāgāt ākāra śakyante ādi upādhi bheda saṃyogat ghana svabhāvasya atma jyotiṣaḥ dṛṣṭi ādi śakti bheda upalakṣyate ghanasya svaccha svābhāvyāt sphaṭika svaccha svābhāvyavat svayan jyotiṣṭvāt śakti bheda upalakṣyate cā jyotiravabhāsya bhedaiḥ saṃyujyamānam harita nīla pīta ādi bhedaiḥ avibhāgyam ākāra abhāvam kṛtsnañjagat avabhāsayat ādīni ākāram uktam asta ityādi nivayaveṣu aneka śakyate kalpayitum dṛṣṭānta abhāvāt gatatva ādi bhedaḥ parikalpyate paramāṇu ādīnām gandha ādi aneka guṇa nirīpyamāṇam upādhi nimittam ākāśasyatāvat sarvaga svatas upādhi saṃśrayāt sarvatra sattvam apekṣya sarvagatva vyavahāraḥ kvacid gataḥ vāgataḥ svatas gamanam deśa antara sthasya deśa saṃyoga kāraṇam kriyā aviśeṣe bhedā santi paramāṇu ādau paramāṇuḥ gandha ghanāyāḥ sūkṣmaḥ avayavaḥ gandha ātmaka purgandhavattva śakyate kalpayitum ādima abādi saṃsa sarga nimitta niravayavasya aneka dharmavat tve dṛṣṭāntaḥ sti dṛś ādi śakti bhedānām cakṣu ādi bhedena pariṇāma bheda kalpanā prayuktā svapnayoḥ pravibhaktam anya tvena uktam suṣupte viśeṣamṣa nanu svabhāvaḥ kiṃnimittam viśeṣa svabhāva parityāgena viśeṣa svabhāvaḥ viśeṣam ucyate śṛṇu yasmiḍh jāgarite ivā atmanaḥ vastu pratyupasthāpitam avidyā pratyupasthāpitāt ivā manyamānaḥ asati pravibhakte vastu antare asati pravibhakte upalabheta darśitam pratyakṣataḥ manvāti avidyā suṣupte vastu antara pratyupasthāpikā śāntā anya tvena avidyā pravibhaktasya vastunaḥ abhāvāt aatmanā sva yan svabhāvena samastaḥ saṃprasanna salilavaḥ tvad śībhūtaḥ salila dvitīyasya abhāvāt avidyāyāḥ dvitīyasya abhāvāt bhma vyāvṛtta kārya karaṇa upādhi bhedaḥ sva jyotiṣi śānta saṃbandhaḥ vartate he anuṣṭavān śruti vacanam mayasya anyā deha graha lakṣaṇā ādi stamba paryantā avidyā kalpitāḥ gatayaḥ aparamā avidyā viṣaya devatva ādi gatīnām sādhyānām uttamā samasta bhāvaḥ anya dvijānāti saṃpadām vibhūtīnām svābhāvika kṛtakā phala āśrayā aparamāḥ kenacana mīyate svābhāvika eṣosya aparama viṣaya indriya saṃbandha janitāni ānanda apekṣya nitya bhūmā sukham śruti antarāt paśyanyat apekṣya ānanda unitya bhūmā sukham śruti antarāt paśyat alpam amukhyam kṣukham viparītam eta evai aanandasya kalām avidyā pratyupasthāpitām viṣaya indriya saṃbandha kāla vibhāvyām kāni anandāt avidyathā pravibhajyamāna svarūpāṇi anya tvena parikalpyamānāni santi viṣaya indriya saṃparka dvāreṇa vibhāvyamānām paramān dasya mātrā avayavā ādibhiḥ paryantaiḥ bhūtaiḥ upajīvyante ānanda mātrāt vāreṇa mātriṇam adhijigami yiṣan lavaṇa śakalaiḥ lavaṇaśailam madhye saṃsiddhaḥ avikalaḥ samagra avayava arthaḥ samṛddha upabhoga upakaraṇa saṃpannaḥ samāna jātīyānām svatantra māṇḍalikaḥ samastaiḥ divya bhoga upakaraṇa nivṛti bhoga upakaraṇāni taiḥ saṃpannānām atiṣayena saṃpannaḥ saṃpannatamaḥ tatrā ananda andita uḥ abheda nirdeśāt artha antara ānandarasya viṣaya aviṣayyākareṇa mātrā prasṛtā hayuktam ityādi vākyena yuktaḥ ānanda abheda nirdeśaḥ yudhiṣṭhira ādi tulyaḥ rājātra udāharaṇam ānandaram ādim śataguṇa uttara krameṇa unnīya bhedaḥ nivartate adhigamayati śataguṇa uttarottara krameṇa vardhamānaḥ vṛddhi kāṣṭām gaṇita bhedaḥ nivartate anya darśana śravaṇa mananā bhāvāttam vivakṣan evaṃprakārāḥ ānanda bhedāḥ viśeṣaṇam śrāddha ādi pitṝn toṣayitvā pitṛṇām ānanda śata guṇīkṛta parimāṇa śata guṇīkṛtaḥ śata guṇīkṛtaḥ agnihotra ādi śrauta prāpnuvanti devaiḥ evai aajāna ājānata utpattita avaḍa jinaḥ vṛjinam rahitaḥ kāriti arthaḥ akāma vīta tṛṣṇa abhyor avāgyāvantaḥ viṣayāḥ evaṃbhūtasyā ajāna devaiḥ samāna ānanda anvākṛṣyate śabdāt śata guṇīkṛta parimāṇaḥ vijñānavān āvṛjina ityādi pūrvavat śata guṇīkṛta parimāṇa hiraṇyagarbha ityādi pūrvavat gaṇita nivṛttaḥ ānanda prayuktaḥ ānanda jasya ādyānandā mātrā udadheḥ vipruṣaḥ śataguṇa uttara uttara vṛddhi upetā ānandā yānti śrotriya pratyakṣaḥ saṃprasāda lakṣaṇaḥ athaḥ bhūmā bhūma viparītāḥ śrotrayitvādvṛjina tve tulye akāma hatatva viśeṣa ānanda śataguṇa vṛddhi hetuḥ sādhanāni śrotriyatva āvṛjinatva akāma hata tvāni anandasya prāptau artha ādi bhihita karmāṇgnihotra ādīni devatva prāptau śrotriyatva āvṛjinatva lakṣaṇe adhara bhūmiṣu samāne uttara ānanda prāpti sādhane abhyupeyete akāma hata vairāgya tāratamya upapatteḥ uttarottara bhūmi ānanda prāpti sādhanam avagamyate vitṛṣṇa śrotriya pratyakṣaḥ adhigataḥ vedavyāsaḥ sukham divyam sukham tṛṣṇā kṣaya sukhasya arhataḥ ṣoḍaśīm kalām he evanuśiṣṭaḥ ata ūdhvam vyākhyātam vākye bibhayāñcakāra bhītavān bhaya kāraṇam śrutiḥ vaktṛtva sāmarthya abhāvāt bhīta vān ajñānāt praśna nirṇayavasānebhya udarautsīdāvṛṇot avarodham kṛtavān arthaḥ yadyāt nirṇītam praśna vimokṣa deśa tvena praśnasya paryanuyuṅktta medhāvi bhaya kāraṇam madīyam praśna vyājena upāditsati svayan pradarśitaḥ antabudvānta saṃcāreṇa kārya karaṇa vyatirittka pravivekaḥ asaṅga matsya dṛṣṭāntena pradarśitaḥ avidyā kāryam dhnanta ityādinā pradarśitam arthāt avidyāyāḥ tattvaṃnirdhīritam atat varma adhyāropaṇa anātma vidyāyāḥ kāryam pradarśitam sarvatma bhāvaḥ pratyakṣataḥ bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ avidyā ādi saṃsāra saṃbandha atītam suṣupte gṛhyata ena t vijñāpitam svayan vidyāyā viṣayaḥ saṃprasādaḥ sukhasya kāṣṭhā antena granthena vyākhyātam caid vimokṣa padārtha vimokṣa padārthasya dṛṣṭānta bandhanasya mokṣa bandhane hetuke prapañce nirdiṣṭe avidyā kārye dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭa antika sthānīye mokṣa handhane hetuke praśna artha bhūte tvayā vatt kavye parthanuyuṅttke ata matsya vatsu abuddha antauvasaṅgaḥ saṃcarati svayan uktam kārya karaṇa mṛtyu parityajan upāda matsyavat taiḥ mṛtyu saṃyujyate viyujyate saṃcaraṇam buddhanta anusaṃcārasya dārṣṭa antika tvena sūcitam vistareṇa nimittam saṃcaraṇam varṇayitavyam arthaḥ ārambhaḥ antāt anupraveśitaḥ saṃprāsāda mokṣa dṛṣṭanā pracyāvya saṃsāra vyavahāraḥ pradariśyitavya saṃbandhaḥ antāt spna krameṇa saṃprasanna sthitvā īṣat pracyutaḥ ityādi pūrvavat bundāya adravati ita ārabhya saṃsāraḥ varṇyate antāt āgata dehat deha pratipatsyata dṛṣṭāntam śakaṭam suṣṭhu bhṛśam bhāṇḍa upaskaraṇena ulūkhala musala śūrpa piṭhara ādinā annādyena saṃpannam saṃbhāreṇā akrana arthaḥ bhāra ākrāntam utsarjat śabdam kurvat yayāt gacchet śā kaṭikena adhiṣṭhitam uktaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ śarīraḥ śārīre bhavaḥ liṅga upādhiḥ āvivi janma maraṇābhyām saṃsarga viyoga lakṣaṇābhyām utkramaṇam ādi utkramaṇam pareṇā atmanā sva yan svabhāvena anvārūṭhaḥ adhiṣṭhitaḥ avabhāsyamānaḥ uktam āttam anaiva aste palyayata utsarjan caitanya bhāsye liṅge pradhāne upādhiḥ śruti vaham ityādi ata uktam prājñenā atmanā anvārūṭha anyathā ekībhūtaḥ śakaṭavat utsarjan liṅga upādhiḥ utsarjan marmasu nikṛtyamāneṣu duḥkha vedanayār aatas śabdam kurvan kāla ucyate kriyā viśeṣaṇam ucchāsita arthaḥ dṛśyamānasya anuvadanam vairāgya ga hetoḥ kaṣṭaḥ saṃsāraḥ utkrānti marmasu utkṛtyamāneṣu smṛti lopaḥ duḥkha vedanā ārtasya artha sādhana pratipattau asāmarthyam vaśīkṛta cittasya avasthā nā agamiṣyati artha sādhana karvyatāyām apramattaḥ bhavet kāruṇyāt śrutiḥ ucchvāsi kiṃnimittam kimartham ucyate prākṛtaḥ pāṇi ādimān ayamaṇi mānam aṇoḥ bhāvam kārśyam arthaḥ kiṃnimittam kāla pakva phalavat jīrṇaḥ kārśyam upatapati upatapan jvara ādi rogaḥ upatapyamānaḥ hirogeṇa viṣama agnitayā bhuktam jarayati anupacīyamānaḥ kārśyam āpapadyate ucyata atyanta kārśyam pratipannaḥ jarā ādi nimittaiḥ uccha vāsī bhṛśa āhita saṃbhāra śakaṭavat utsarjan jaribhā abhavaḥ roga ādi pīḍanam kārśyāpattiḥ śarīravataḥ avaśyaṃbhāvina anarthā vairāgyāya ucyate utsarjanyāti vimuñcati dṛṣṭānta ucyate yatāmram phalam vāphalam viṣama aneka dṛṣṭānta upādānam maraṇasya aniyata nimittatva khyāpana aniyatāni maraṇasya nimittāni asaṃkhyātāni vairāgya aneka maraṇa nimittavān vartata badhyate vṛntena bandhana kāraṇaḥ badhyata vṛntam ucyate bandhana rasāt vṛntāt vāta ādi aneka nimitam liṅga liṅga upādhirebhyaḥ ādi deha avayavebhyaḥ samyak nirlepena pramucya suṣupta gamana kāla upasaṃhṛtya śabandāt dedāt deha asakṛt gatavān purgacchati pratigamanam yathāgatam arthaḥ yoni śruta ādi vaśādādravati kimartham vyūhāya arthaḥ prāṇayā viśeṣaṇam anarthakam vyūhāya gamanam dehāt deha phala upabhoga artha siddhiḥ sattā mātreṇa tādarthāyartham yuktam viśeṣaṇam vyūhāya parityajya anyasya deha antarasya upādāne sāmarthyam deha indriya viyogāt bhṛtya sthānīyā gṛham rājñe pratīkṣamāṇā vidyante sati antara upādānam ucyate jagatsva phala upabhoga sādhana tvāya upāttam sva phala upabhogāya pravṛttaḥ dehāt deha pratipitsuḥ jagatsva prayuktam phala upabhoga ayogyam sādhanam pratīkṣata abhijāyate svapnāt jāgaritam pratipitsoḥ prasiddhaḥ dṛṣṭānta ucyate rājya abhiṣiktam āyāntam sva rāṣṭra ugrā jāti viśeṣāḥ krūra pratenasi karmaṇi niyuktāḥ taskara ādi daṇḍanādau niyuktāḥ sūtāḥ grāma netāraḥ rājña āgamanam buddhvā bhojya bhakṣya ādi prakāraiḥ madirā ādibhiḥ āvasathaiḥ prāsāda ādibhiḥ niṣpannaiḥ pritīkṣante ayāti dṛṣṭānta phalasya veditāram saṃsāriṇam arthaḥ phalam prastutam evaṃśabdena parāmṛśyate kartṝṇi karaṇa anugrahītṝṇi cā adityādīni prayuktāni kṛtaiḥ phalaḥ babhoga sādhanaiḥ pratīkṣante bhoktṛ kartṛ asmākam pratīkṣanta arthaḥ jigamiṣum gacchante kriyā praṇunnā āhosvit vaśāt kartṝṇi ucyate dṛṣṭāntaḥ tatat prakarṣeṇa yātum icchantam ābhumikhyena samāyanti ekībhāvena abhimukhā āyanti anājñaptā kevalam jigamiṣa abhijñāḥ bhoktāram antakāle maraṇa prāṇā ādayaḥ ātat vyākhyātam ayamam saṃsāra upavarṇanam prastutam uktam saṃpramokṣaṇam kathe vistaram saṃsaraṇam varṇayitavyam āpabhyate prastutaḥ abala bhāvam ni dehasya daurbalyam ātmana daurbalyam uparyate svatas amūrta abala bhāvam saṃmūṭha saṃmohaḥ viveka abhāvaḥ saṃmūḍha svatas saṃmohaḥ asaṃmohaḥ nitya caitanya svabhāva utkrānti karaṇa upasaṃhāra nimittaḥ vyākulībhāva ātmana lakṣyate laikikaiḥ vaktāraḥ saṃmūḍhaḥ saṃmūḍhaḥ ubhayatreva śabda prayogaḥ yojyaḥ nyet ubhayaḥ upādhi nimittatva aviśeṣāt samāna kartṛka nirdeśāt kāla prāṇā ādaya ātmanam śārīrasyā atmanaḥ saṃpramoṇam saṃpramokṣaṇam prakāreṇā ucyate tejasā vayavā ādi prakāśaka ādīni karaṇāni arthaḥ samabhyāda samyak nirlepena abhyādadāna ābhimukhyena ña adadānaḥ saṃharamāṇaḥ apekṣayā viśeṣaṇam samiti nirlepena samyāga ādānam ādāna mātram agṛhītā aasya aśukram ādāye atyādi vākyebhyaḥ puṇḍarīka ākāram anvakrāmati anvāgacchati abhivyakta vijñānaḥ arthaḥ buddhi ādi vikṣepa upasaṃhāpe sati svatas calanam vikṣepa upasaṃhāra ādi vikriyā uktvāt buddhi ādi upādhi dvārā vikriyā adhyāropyatetasmin kadā mātra abhyādām ucte bhavaḥ cākṣuṣa jāditya aṃśaḥ bhoktuḥ prayuktaḥ yādavat deha dhāraṇam anugraham kurvan vartate maraṇa anugraham parityajati āditi uktam ādityāmi tyādi deha grahaṇa saṃśrayiṣyanti svapsyataḥ prabudhyataḥ āhi parāṅparyāvartate parisamantāt parāṅvyāvartata arūpajñaḥ mumūrṣū ādi samabhyāda svapnkāla karaṇa liṅga evana pārśva sthā ghrāṇa nivṛttau ghrāṇam liṅga jihvāyām nivṛti apekṣayā rasayata upalakṣyate nivṛttiḥ karaṇānām hṛdaya ekībhāvaḥ hṛdaya upasaṃhṛteṣu karaṇeṣu antarvāya pāraḥ kathyate prakṛtasya hṛdaya chidrasya nirgama dvāram kāla mātra ādāna kṛtena svonāva atmanā tenā atma hṛdaya agreṇa ayaḥ liṅga upādhiḥ nigracchati niṣkramāti atharvaṇe vaham utkrānta utkrāntaḥ bhaviṣyāmi pratiṣṭhate pratiṣṭhāsyāmi cā atma caitanya abhivyaktataram upādhi dvārā janma maraṇa gamana āgamana ādi vikriyā lakṣaṇaḥ saṃvyavahāraḥ ātmakam dvādaśavidham karaṇam buddhi ādi jīvanam antarātmā jagataḥ tasthuṣaḥ hṛdaya agra prakāśena niṣkramamāṇaḥ mārgeṇa ucyate cakṣuṣṭaḥ prāpti nimittam jñānam prāpti nimittam avayavebhyaḥ yathākarma yathāśrutam prasthitam udbhūta ākūtam artha adhikāri sthānīyaḥ rājña ādayaḥ prāṇām pradhānān khyāseyam krameṇa sārthavat gmanam vivakṣitam vijñānaḥ svapn viśeṣa vijñānavān vaśāt n svatantraḥ svātantryeṇa tve kṛtakṛtyaḥ labhyate ata aha vyāsaḥ sadā bhāva bhāvitaḥ udbhāvyamānena antaḥkaraṇa vṛtti viśeṣa āśrita vāsanā ātmaka viśeṣa vijñānaḥ gantavyam anvavakrām atyagacchati viśeṣa udbhāsitam arthaḥ svātantrya yoga anusevanam parisaṃkhyāna abhyāsaḥ viśiṣṭa upayaḥ śraddhadhānaiḥ arthibhiḥ apramattaiḥ kartavya śāstrāṇām yatnataḥ vidheyor athaḥ duścaritāt uparamaṇam śakyate sampādayitum nīyamānasya svātantrya abhāvāt apuṇyaḥ atyuktam anarthasya upaśama upāya vidhānāyā śākhā pravṛttāḥ vihita upāya anusevanam muktvā atyanti anarthasya upaśama upāyaḥ vihita upāye yatna paraiḥ bhavitavyam prakaraṇa arthaḥ śakaṭa taṃbhṛ saṃbhāram utsarjanyāti uktam pravṛttasya pathdanam śākaṭika saṃbhāra sthānīyam bhuṅkte ādi ārambhakam ucyate gacchantam srava prakārā vihitā pratiṣiddhā avihita apratiṣiddhā vihitam pratiṣiddham avihita pratiṣiddham samyak anvārabhete anvālabhete anugacchataḥ anubhūta viṣayā atīta phala anubhava vāsanā arthaḥ vāsanā rambhe vipāke aṅgam anvāpabhate vāsanayā vinā kartum phalam upabhoktum śakyate anabhyaste viṣaye kauśalam indrayāṇām anubhava vāsanā pravṛttānām indriyāṇām abhyāsam anantareṇa kauśalam upapadyate dṛśyate keṣāñcid kāsu cid kriyāsu citrakarma ādi lakṣaṇāsu vinā abhyāsena janmata kauśalam kāsucid atyanta saukarya yuktāsu akauśalam koṣāñcid prajñayā vinā karmaṇi phala upabhoge kasyacid pravṛttiḥ upapadyate śākaṭika sambhāra sthānīyam pathya dana pūrvaprajñā ākhyam kramaṇī pūrvapjñā deha antara pratipati upabhoga sādhanam tasmat ādi śubham samātaret iṣṭa deha sambhoga upabhogau syātām prakaraṇa arthaḥ ādi sambāra samphṛtaḥ deha pratipadyamānaḥ muktvā deham vṛkṣa deha athavā ativāhikena phala janma deśam nīyate atrasthasya gatānām karaṇānām vṛtti lābhaḥ āhosvit śarīraḥsya saṃkucitāni karaṇāni bhinna ghaṭa pradīpa prakāśavat vyapya deha antara ārambhe saṅkocam upagacchanti mātram vaiśeṣika samaya deha antara ārambha deśam kiṃvā kalpanānā vedānta samaya ucyate ta ātmakāni karaṇāni ātmaka saṃśrayāt ādhyāmika ādhibhautika paricchedaḥ jñāna bhāvanā nimittaḥ vaśāt svabhāvataḥ sargatānām anantānām karjñāna vāsanā anurūpeṇa dehān nara ārambha vaśāt vṛttiḥ saṃkucati vikasati uktam sama vacanam anukūlam anupāste ityādi vāsanā ākhyā tantrā jalūkavat saṃtatā kāla dehāt deha ārabhate deha antara ārambhe deha āśrayam vimuñcati arthe dṛṣṭānta upādīyate deha antara sañcāra nidarśanam prakāreṇa tṛṇajalūkā avasānam ākramyata ākramaḥ tamākramam ākramyā aścityā upabhoga yogyam prajāpatyam brahmaṇa yathākarma yathāśrutam anyeṣa aṃvā sambandhi abhisambanyate bandhana saṃjñakā upādhi bhūtāḥ saṃyuttkaḥ maye vibhāvyate padārthāḥ puñjīkṛtya ekatra pratinirdiśyante udbhave budvi dvāreṇa ādi karaṇa ārambhaka ādi ayaḥ pārthiva ārambhe pṛthivīmayaḥ ādi āpi aśarīra ārambha vāyavya ārambhe akāśa ārambha ayaḥ taijasāni śarīrāṇi ārabhyamāṇeṣu vyatiriktāni paśu ādi śarīrāṇi naraka preta ādi śarīrāṇi atejaḥ mayāni apekṣyā aha atejaḥ maya kārya karaṇa saṃghāta prāptavyam vastu prāpta madaḥ prāptavyam viparīta pratyayaḥ abhilāṣaḥ ayaḥ kāme doṣam viṣaya abhilāṣa praśāme citam prasannam akaluṣam śāntam akāma vihate kām ekena acid tvena pariṇamate bhavan krodhaḥ kenacid upāyena nivartitaḥ prasannam anākulam citam akrodha ucyate abhyāma akrodhābhyām ayaḥ adharma ādibhiḥ vinā ādi pravṛtti rūpapadyate kāmasya ceṣṭitam smaraṇāt ayaḥ adharmayaḥ ayaḥ samastam adharmayoḥ kāryam yāvartki cit adharmayoḥ phalam pratipadyāmānaḥ bahunā sidvam gṛhyamāṇa viṣayādi daṃmayaḥ ada parokṣam kāryeṇa gṛhyamāṇena nirdiśyate anantā antaḥkaraṇe bhāvanā viśeṣāḥ viśeṣataḥ nirdeṣṭum śakyante tasmiḥ kṣaṇe kāryataḥ avagamyanta hradi vartate adosyate gṛhyamāṇa kāryeṇa idaṃmaya nirdiśyate parokṣaḥ vyavahāraḥ maya saṃkṣepataḥ kartum caritum śīlam cārī karaṇam niyatā kriyā vidhi pratiṣedha ādi gamyā caraṇam aniyatam viśeṣaḥ yathākārīti viśeṣaṇam tāt śīlya pratyaya upādānāt atyanta tātparyatā maya mātreṇa uti āśaṅkayā aha mātreṇa maya tāt śīlyam apekṣate tāt śīlye mayatva atiśaya viśeṣaḥ ādi pūrvaka kāritā maya tve hetuḥ saṃsārasya kāraṇam dehāt deha antara saṃcārasya prayuktaḥ deha upādatte apuṇye saṃsārasya kāraṇam viṣayau vidhi pratiṣedhau śāstrasya sāphalyam athaḥ bandha mokṣa kuśalāḥ ādi pūrvake apuṇye grahaṇa kāraṇam prayuktaḥ puṇye upacinoti prahāṇe mānam puṇyepa caya karam upacite puṇye śūnye phala ārambhake saṃsārasya cektam ātharvaṇe kāmānyaḥ manyamānaḥ kāmabhiḥ maya anya maya akāraṇam vidyānam aptaḥ avadhārayati maya sanyādṛśena yathākāmaḥ bavati yogyam nirvartayati tadīyam phalam maya tve saṃsāri tve hetuḥ artha mantra upi sakta āsaktaḥ udbhūta abhilāṣaḥ arthaḥ phala āsaktaḥ sannakara uttena phalam liṅga pradhāna liṅgasya ucyate athavā liṅgayate avagamyate avagacchati niścayena saktam udbhūta abhilāṣam saṃsāriṇaḥ abhilāṣaḥ kṛtavān abhiṣaṅga vaśāt phala prāptiḥ etasi dvam saṃsārasya ata ucchinna kāmasya vidyamānāni vandhya prasavāni paryāpta saya kṛtātmanaḥ pravilītanti bhuktvā avasānam phalam bhuktvā pradhānaḥ tenā aha karmaṇa karaṇāya phala āsaṅga vaśāt saṃsarati ya māt kāmayamāna saṃsarati akāmayamānaḥ kvacid saṃsarati phala āsaktasya uktā akāmasya kriyā anupapatteḥ akāmayamānaḥ mucyata punakāmaya mānaḥ akāmayamānaḥ akāma ucyate niṣṭakāmaḥ nirgatāḥ kāmā nirgacchanti ya āptāḥ kāmā āpyante kāmā tvena yasyā ama kāmayitavyaḥ vastu antara bhūtaḥ padārthaḥ ghana ekarasaḥ tiryak kāmayitavyam vastu vaivam jñāyamānaḥ anya tvena padārthaḥ kāmayitavyaḥ vida kāmasya ya atmakāma apta akāmayamānaḥ mucyate yasyā atmā anātmā kāmayitavyaḥ anātmā kāmayitavyaḥ cā atmā vipra tiṣidvam darśinaḥ kāmayitavya abhāvāt anupapattiḥ pratyavāya parihāra kalpayanti pratyavāyasya jihāsita vyasyā atmanaḥ anyasya abhipreta aśanāya ādi atītaḥ nityam pratyavāya saṃbadvaḥ vidita vidam brūmaḥ nityam aśanāya ādi atītam ātmanam jihāsita vyam upādeyam śakyata saṃbaddhu m abrahma vitasya pratyavāya parihāra virodhaḥ abhāvāt akāmayamānaḥ mucyata akāmayamānasya abhāve gamana kāraṇa abhāvāt prāṇā ādayaḥ dehāt bhūtaḥ dṛṣṭānta tvena pradarśitam dārṣṭa antika bhūtaḥ artha upasaṃhriyate akāmayamāna ityādinā evaṃbhūtaḥ mucyata ucyate suṣupta avastham nirviśeṣam advaitam alupta cit svabhāvam akāmayamānasya bhāve gamana kāraṇa bhāvat prāṇā ādayaḥ kintu saiha dehāvān lakṣyate abrahmatva pariccheda hetavaḥ santi pātettara viduṣaḥ bhāva antara āpattiḥ anya bhāvaḥ deha antara pratisaṃdhāna abhāva mātreṇa ucyate bhāva antarārāpattau mokṣasya upaniṣa nid vivakṣitor ekatva ākhyaḥ bādhitaḥ bhavet hetukaḥ mokṣaḥ jñāna nimitta aniṣṭaḥ anitya mokṣasya kriyā nirvṛttor athaḥ mokṣaḥ abhyupagamyate mantra varṇāt svābhāvikāt svabhāvāt nityam kalpayitum śakyam svābhāvikaḥ udātmanaḥ svabhāvaḥ śakyate vyāpāra anubhāvī vaktum auṣṇyam prakāśaḥ agnu vyāpāra anantara anubhāvī vyāpāra anubhāvī svābhāvikaḥ vipratiṣiddham jvalana vyāpāna anubhāvi uṣṇa prākāśa guṇābhyām abhivyajyate epa īkṣayā anya auṣṇya prakāśau dharmau vyavahitai kasyacid dṛṣṭyā asaṃbadhyamānau jvalana apekṣayā vyadhāna apagame abhivyajyete apekṣayā bhrāntiḥ upajāyate jvalana pūrvakau etauviṣṇa prākāśau dharmau jātau uṣṇa prakāśayoḥ svābhāvika svābhāvaki udāhariṣyāmaḥ svābhāvikaḥ padārthānām śakyam vaktum nigaḍa bhaṅga abhāva bhūtaḥ mokṣaḥ bandhana nivṛttiḥ upapadyate paramātmā ekatva abhyupagamāt aekam advitīyam baddhaḥ nigaḍa nivṛttivat bandhana nivṛttarmokṣaḥ vyatirekeṇa anyasya abhāvam vistareṇa avādiṣma avidyā nivṛtti mokṣa vyavahāra avocāma rajju ādau sarpa ādya jñāna nivṛttau sarpa ādi nivṛttiḥ mokṣe ānanda abhivyajyata sairvaktavyaḥ abhivyakti śabda arthaḥ laukikikī upalabdhi viṣaya vyāptiḥ abhivyakti śabda arthaḥ vaktavyam vidyamānam abhivyajyate avidyamānam vidyamānam muktasya abhivyajyate tasyā atma upalabdhi vyavadhāna anupapatteḥ nitya abhivyakta muktasya abhivyajyata viśeṣa vacanam arthakam kadācid abhivyajyata upalabdhi vyavadhānāt anātma anyatas abhivyakti prasaṅgaḥ abhivyakti sādhana apekṣayā upalabdhi samāna āśraya tve vyavadhāna kalpanā anupapatteḥ abhivyakti prasaṅgaḥ abhivyakti sādhana apekṣa upalabdhi samāna āśraya tve vyavadhāna kalpanā anupapatteḥ abhivyaktiḥ anabhivyaktiḥ antarāla kalpanāyā pramāṇam samāna āśrayaṇām ekasyā atma dharmāṇām itaretara viṣaya viṣayi sukha yoṣca abhivyakteḥ saṃsāri abhivyakti uttara mukta tvaṃsya parasmāt nitya abhivyakta jñāna svarūpāt atyanta vailakṣaṇyāt śaityam auṣṇyāt paramātma bheda kalpanāyāñca vaidikaḥ kṛtāntaḥ parityaktaḥ mokṣasya nirviśeṣa tve artha adhika yatna anupapattiḥ śāstra vaiyarthyam avidyā bhrama apoha āptha vastu tas muktā muktatva aviśeṣaḥ nityāka kintu viṣaya avidyā apohyate śāstra upadeśa janita prāk upadeśa prāpteḥ arthaḥ prayatna upapadyata avidyāvataḥ avidyā nivṛtya nivṛtti veśeṣa avidyā kalpanā viṣayatva abhyupagamāt rajjūṣara śuktakāgaganānām udaka rajata malinatva ādivat adoṣa avocāma timira atimitara dṛṣṭivat avidyā kartṛtva akatṛ akṛta viśeṣaḥ dhyāti svatas avidyā kartṛtva sva pratiṣiddha aneka vyāpāra sannipāta janita avidyā bhramasya viṣatva upapatteṣca avidyā bhramaḥ ghaṭa ādivat viviktaḥ avidyā bhramavān jāne mugdhe pratyata darśanāt avidyā bhramava viveka grahaṇāt vivekena grahītā bhrānta ucyate viveka grahaṇam bhrama vipratiṣiddham jāne mugdhaḥ dṛśyata bravīṣi darśinaḥ ajñānam mugdha dṛśyata darśanasya viṣayaḥ āpadyata kartṛ svarūpa dṛśi viśeṣaṇa jñānam ugdhate syātām dṛśi viśeṣaṇa syātām dṛśinā vyāpyete kartṛ kriyayā vyāpyamānam vyāpyam vyāpakam vyāpyate jñānam ugdhate dṛśi viśeṣaṇe syātām ajñāna aviveka darśī ajñānam upalabhamāna upalabdhṛ tvena gṛhmāti kārśya dādavat sukha duḥkha icchā prayatna ādīn grahītuḥ vivaktatā abhyupagatā jāne tvad uktam mugdha bhavatu ajñaḥ mugdhaḥ evandarśū jñam amugdham pratijānīmahe vyosena uktam icchā ādi kṛtsnam kṣetram kṣetrī prakāśayati tiṣṭhantam parameśvaram vinaśyat vinaśyantam ityādi śataśa uktam nā atmanaḥ svatas baddha mukta jñāna viśeṣaḥ sama svābhāvya abhyupagamāt tvataḥ anyathā atma vastu parikalpya bandha mokṣa ādiśāstriṃ artha vādam āpādayanti ta utsahante khe śākunam draṣṭum muṣṭinā akraṣṭum carmavat veṣṭitum kartum aśaktāḥ sarvādā samaikaram vaitam avikriyam ajam ajaram amaram tattvam vedānta niścitor pratipadyāmahe upacāra mātram vipīratagrahavat deha saṃtateḥ ccheda mātram phalam apekṣya gamana dṛṣṭāntasya dārṣṭa antikaḥ saṃsāraḥ varṇitaḥ saṃsāra hetuḥ varṇitā upādhi bhūtaiḥ kārya karaṇa lakṣaṇa bhūtaiḥ pariveṣṭitaḥ saṃsāri uktāni prayojakau adharvau pakṣam avadhāritam brahmaṇena arthaḥ ayavadhārita mantreṇa bandham bandha kāraṇam upasaṃhṛtam prakaraṇam kāmayamāna akāyamāna ārabhya suṣupta dṛṣṭanātasya dārṣṭa antika bhūtaḥ bhāvaḥ mokṣa uktaḥ mokṣa kāraṇam cā atma uktam sāmartha āyadana jñānam antareṇā atmaka āmaya apta sāmarthyāt mokṣa kāraṇam uktam uktam mokṣa kāraṇa viparyayeṇa bandha kāraṇam avidyā ityet uktam mokṣaḥ mokṣa sādhanam brāhmaṇena uktam dṛḍhīkaraṇāya mantra udāhriyate śloka śabda vācyaḥ artha mantraḥ samastāḥ tṛṣṇā prabhedāḥ kāmya mūlataḥ viśīryante prasiddhā amutra arthāḥ lakṣaṇā prasiddhasya buddhau śritā āśritāḥ maraṇa viyogāt mūlataḥ vartamānaḥ bhāvam mokṣam pratipadyata arthaḥ mokṣaḥ deśa antara gamana ādi apekṣate viduṣaḥ prāṇā avasthitā sva kāraṇe mātram avaśiṣyata uktam samanavīteṣu dehe sva kāraṇe pralīne muktaḥ sanvartamānaḥ pūrvavat dehi saṃsāritva lakṣaṇam pratipadyata ucyate dṛṣṭāntaḥ ahiḥ sarpaḥ nirmekaḥ sarpa āśraye valmīka ādau arthaḥ prakṣiptān bhāvena sarpeṇa parityaktā varte dṛṣṭānta sarpa sthānīyena muktena anātma bhāvena parityaktam mṛtam sarpa sthānīyaḥ muktaḥ sarmātama bhūtaḥ sarpavat vartamānaḥ aśarīra pūrvavtupanaḥ śarīraḥ prayukta bhāvena śarīraḥ viyogāt ata vakṣyamāṇe śloke bandhanam somya śruti antare prakaraṇa vākya sama arthāt atmā śabda vācyaḥ paramātmā teja yenā atma jagat avabhāsyamānam netram jyotiṣmad avibraṃśadvartate praśnaḥ vimokṣa arthaḥ dattaḥ janakāya hetukaḥ bandha mokṣa artha lakṣaṇaḥ dṛṣṭāntika bhūtaḥ nirṇītaḥ vistaraḥ ākhyāyikā dhāriṇyā śrutyā saṃsāra vimokṣa upāya uktaḥ prāṇibhyaḥ śrutiḥ aha niṣkriya janakena uktam ovam vimokṣitaḥ tvayā niṣkriya uvācā uktavān kasmdā vimokṣa padārthe nirṇīte videha rājyam nivedayati deśa uktau abhiprāya kecid varṇayanti adhyātma rasikaḥ artam mantraiḥ śuśrūṣati nivedayati śrutvā abhipretam nivedayiṣyāmi nivedayāmi nivṛtta abhilāṣaḥ śravaṇāt matvā ślokān navakṣyati bhayāt sahasra śuśrūṣā liṅga jñāpanāya pramāṇa bhūtāyāḥ vyāja anupapatteḥ artha śeṣa upapatteḥ vimokṣa padārtha ukte jñāna sādhana jñāna śeṣa bhūtaḥ sarveṣaṇā parityāgaḥ saṃnyāsa ākhyaḥ vaktavyor śeṣaḥ śloka mātra śuśrūṣā kalpanā anṛjvaḥ agatikā puvarukta artha kalpanā ayuktā satyām gatau stuti mātram avocāma nanu satyata vaktavyam dauṣaḥ jñānavat aprayojakaḥ saṃnyāsaḥ pakṣe pratipatti karmavat saṃnyāsena tanum tyajet smṛteḥ sādhutva āpakṣe ata praśnam mokṣa sādhana bhūtātma jñāna paripāka artha kāmasya mokṣa arthe mantra ukte vistara pratipādakā ślokā bhavanāti sūkṣmaḥ panthā durvijñeya vitatas vistīrṇaḥ vispaṣṭa taraṇa hetu vitara pāṭhā antarāt mokṣa sādhanaḥ jñāna mārgaḥ cirantanaḥ nitya śruti prakāśita tārkika buddhi prabhava kudṛṣṭi mārgavadarvāk kālikaḥ labdha arthaḥ labhyate saṃbadhyate ayaḥ lakṣaṇaḥ mokṣa mārgaḥ labdha spṛṣṭa ucyate kevalam labdhaḥ kintu anuvedanam vidyāyāḥ paripāka apekṣayā phala avasāna niṣṭhā prāptiḥ bhujeḥ tṛpti avasāna jñāna prāpti saṃbandha mātram viśeṣaḥ asā ena mantra dṛś phalam prāptavān mayāva avadhārayati doṣaḥ phalam sākṣikam anuttamam vidyāyāḥ stuti paratvāt kṛtārtha abhimāna karam pratyaya sākṣikam jñānam anyatsyāt stauti puranyaḥ phalam artha aha mārgeṇa prajñāvantaḥ vida arthaḥ apiyantpigacchanti phalam mokṣam svarga śabda viṣṭapa vācyam prakaraṇāt mokṣa abhidhāyakaḥ pātāt jīvanta mokṣa sādhana mārge vipratipattiḥ mumukṣūṇām vimalam kecid mumukṣavaḥ yathādarśanam suṣumna ādyāḥ śleṣma ādiḥ asaṃsaṃpūrṇāḥ ityādi mokṣa mārgam evaṃvidham śukla nīlaḥ ādi śruti antārāt darśana mārgasya śukla ādi varṇa asaṃbhavāt sarvathā prakṛtāt mārgāt anya śukla ādayaḥ nanu adhvataiya mārgaḥ nīla pūta ādi śabdaiḥ varṇa vācakaiḥ anudravaṇāt śukla ādīn yoginaḥ mokṣa pathān mokṣa mārgāḥ saṃsāra viṣayā ve deśebhya śarīdeśāt niḥsaraṇa saṃbandhāt ādi prāpakāhi mokṣa mārgaḥ ya ātkāma tvenā aptakāma sarvakāmakṣe gamana anupapattau pradīpa nirvāṇavat ādīnām kārya karaṇānām samavanaya jñāna mārgaḥ panthā paramātma svarūpeṇa brāhmaṇena tyakta sarvaiśaṇenana mārgeṇa kīdṛśaḥ ucyate tyaktu ādi eṣaṇaḥ parātma saṃyojya abhinirvṛttaḥ taijam asaḥ cā atma arthaḥ mārgeṇa ādi samuccaya kāriṇaḥ grahaṇam virodhāt avocāma apuṇya uparame punarbhava nirbhāḥ śāntāḥ saṃnyāsinaḥ yānti mokṣa smṛteḥ tyaja adhramam ityādi puṇyā tyāga upadeśāt nirāśiṣam anārambham nirnamaskāram astutum akṣoṇam kṣīṇa karmāṇam brāhmaṇam etādṛśam sama satyatā śīlam daṇḍa nidhānam ārjavam ta uparamaḥ kriyābhyaḥ ityādi smṛtibhyaḥ upadekṣyati brahmaṇasya prayojana abhāve hetum uktavā dānta ityādinā kriyā uparamam yathāvyākhyātam kṛtvam athavā kṛta ejasaḥ sutiḥ kṛti taijase yogini mahābhāgyam prasiddham satūyate prakhyāta mahābhāgya adarśana ātmakam saṃsāra niyāmakam vidyātaḥ sādhya sādhana lakṣaṇam anuvartanta arthaḥ bhūya bahutaram ya avidyā vastu pratipādikāyām arthāyām trayyām ratā abhiratāḥ vidhi pratiṣedha artha anapekṣiṇa arthaḥ adarśana lakṣaṇam pravisanti doṣa ucyate anandā anānandā asukhā adarśana lakṣaṇena avṛtā vyāptāḥ ajñāna gocarāḥ mṛtvā abhigacchanti abhiyānti avidvāṃsaḥ sāmānyena avidvattā mātreṇa ucyate abudhaḥ budheḥ avagamana arthasya dhātoḥ kvippratyaya antasya avagama varjitā arthaḥ prakṛtā janana dharmiṇaḥ prāṇimanīṣita jñam hṛd stham aśanāya ādi atītam udyadi sahasreṣu vidyāyā durlabha darśayati pratyaya sākṣī ityāt yuktaḥ nitya śuddha mukta svabhāvaḥ bhavāmi pūruṣaḥ sava vyatiriktam anya t phala kimicchankasya vānyasyā atmanaḥ vyatiriktasya prayojanāya tasyā atmana eṣṭavyam phalam anyosti icchati kimicchankasya anusaṃjvaret bhraṃśet upādhi kṛta anuduḥkhī tāpam anutapyeta anātma darśinaḥ vyatirikta vastavantara īpsoḥ putrasya bhāryāyāḥ īhamānaḥ janana maraṇa prabandha rūḍhaḥ rogam rujyate darśinaḥ asaṃbhava anulabdhaḥ sākṣātkṛtaḥ pratyagātma tvena avagata saṃdahye saṃdehe aneka anartha saṃkaṭa upacaye viṣame aneka śata sahasra viveka pratipakṣe viṣame pratibodhena arthaḥ viśvasya viśvakṛttavam viśvakṛt āśaṅkyā aha mātram kevalam viśvakṛt prayuktaḥ anyā ucyate śabdenā atmā ucyate ña atmā arthaḥ ya brāhmaṇena pratyagātmā pratibuddhatayā anuvitta anartha saṃkaṭe saṃsārī kintu viśvasya sarvasyā atmā advitīyaḥ anusaṃdhātavya śloka arthaḥ āleka artha saṃkule bhavantaḥ jñāna dīrgha nidrā mohitāḥ kathañcid tattvam tvena vijānīmaḥ prakṛta mahaḥ kṛtārthā abhiprāyaḥ vijānīmaḥ viditavantaḥ vedanam vedī vedyā vedira doṣaḥ mahati parimāṇā janma maraṇa ādi lakṣaṇā vinaśanam ahaḥ vinaśanāt nirmuktā advayam viditavanta arthaḥ vinaśanāt vipramuktā evaṃye ta vidbhyaḥ abrahma vida arthaḥ janma maraṇa ādi lakṣaṇam kadācid aviduṣām vinivṛttiḥ arthaḥ ta tvena upagacchanti kathañcid kāruṇikam kañcid ācāryam labdha prayādaḥ sākṣātkaroti dyotanavantam dātāram anurūpam sāvāminam kāla trayasya īśānāt devāt viśeṣeṇa jugupsate gopāyitum icchati leka īśvarāt guptam icchati bhedeḥ śī ekatvadarśī kutaścana atma tvena nindati evaṃpaśyan kamasau nindyāt īśānāt arvāgi anya viṣaya arthaḥ kāla janimataḥ paricchettā paricchindan vartate sva avayavaiḥ ahorātraiḥ arthaḥ ādityādi avabhāsaka upāsane āyuṣmantaḥ āyuṣkāmenā ayuḥ guṇena upāsyam arthaḥ brahmaṇi pañcajanā ādayaḥ saṃkhyātā gandharvāḥ asurā rakṣāṃsi niṣāda pañcamā varṇā avyākṛta ākhyaḥ imotam pratiṣṭhita gārgyākāśa uktam anya tvena jāne sanna jñāna mātreṇa āsam apagamāt caitanya avabhāsyamānaḥ bhūtena śrautrasya brahmam aśaktyodhiṣṭhitānām ādīnām darśana ādi sāmarthyam svatas kāṣṭha loṣṭa samāni caitanya śūnyāni mana adāvyāpāra anumitāstivam pratyāga viṣaya niścayena jñātavantaḥ cirantanam bhavam ātharvaṇe edhā ekena prakāreṇa ghana prakāreṇā akāśavat nirantareṇa aprameyam pramīyata aprameyam nityam kūṭastham avicālī arthaḥ nanu viruddham ucyate aprameyam jñāyata jñāyata pramāṇaiḥ mīyata arthaḥ aprameyam pratiṣedhaḥ doṣaḥ avastuvat anāgama pramāṇa prameyatva pratiṣedha artha vastūni āgama nirapekṣaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ viṣayīkriyante ātmata pramāṇa viṣayīkartum śakyate āamatve vijīnāyat pramātṛ pramāṇa ādi vyāpāra pratiṣedhena agamaḥ vijñāpayati abhidhāna abhidhelakṣaṇa vākya aṅgīkaraṇena nā agamanā svarga meru ādivat pratipādyate pratipādayitra pratipādayituḥ pratipādanasya pratipādya viṣaya bhede sati jñānam parātbhāva nivṛttiḥ bhāvaḥ kartavye vidyamānvāda bhavasya bhāvaḥ ātat viṣaya pratyavabhasate atad viṣaya avabhāsa nivṛtta vyatirekeṇa bhāvaḥ vidhīyate anyātbhāva nivṛttau bhāvaḥ sva svābhāvikaḥ kevalaḥ jñāyata ucyate svatas aprameyaḥ pramāṇa viṣayīkriyata uccayate svatas aprameyaḥ pramāṇa viṣayīkriyata aviruddham vigata adharma ādi malam rahita vyatiriktaḥ sūkṣmaḥ vyāpī akāśāt avyākṛta ākhyāt janma pratiṣedhāt uttare bhāva vikārāḥ pratiṣiddhāḥ janma ādi parimāṇataḥ mahatatraḥ īdṛśam dhāmān upadeśataḥ śāstrataḥ śāstra ācārya upadiṣṭa viṣayām jijñāsā pari samāpti karīm karaṇa sādhanāni saṃnyāsa śama dama uparama titikṣā samādhānāni kuryīt arthaḥ anucintayet prabhūtān bahutva pratiṣedhāt kevala ātmakatva pratipādakāḥ alpāḥ śabdā anujñāyante dhyāyatha anyā vimiñcatha cā atharvaṇe viśeṣeṇa glāni karam śrama karam śabda abhidhyānam hetukau bandha mokṣau abhihitau mantra brāhmaṇabhyām mokṣa svarūpam vistareṇa pratipāditam viṣaye upayuktaḥ vaktavyam artheyam kaṇḍikā arabhyate prapāṭhake abhihitam prayojanam anūdyātra upayogaḥ kṛtsnasya vedasya kāmya rāśi varjitasya artha anuvādaḥ ityādiḥ parāmarśa arthaḥ uktaḥ parāmṛśyate nirdiśati ya maya atīntara vākya saṃpratyayaḥ ya katama ucyate uttara vākya ulliṅganam saṃśaya nivṛti uktam praśna ārambhe katam ityādi uktam ityādinā vākyena pratipāditaḥ svayan avidyānām anātma dharmatva pratidāpādana dvāreṇa mokṣitaḥ paramātma bhāvam āpāditaḥ anya uktaḥ yathāvyākhyāta artha ya hṛdayepuṇḍarīka madhye hṛdaya puṇḍarīka madhye ya atmā nirupādhikaḥ mayasya sva svabhāḥ sva svabhāve ākhye sete vyākhyātam prativacana tvena indrāt eḥ vaśe vartate uktam praśāsana kevalam īśāna īśitā brhama prabhṛtīnām īśitṛ kadācid jāti rāja balavattarān bhṛtyān tadvat adhiṣṭhāya pālayitā svatantra arthaḥ rāja putravat amātya ādi bhṛtya tantraḥ vaśitva ādi hetu hetumat adhiṣṭāya pālayati pratīṣṭa prasiddham kica evaṃbhūtaḥ ayaḥ śāstra vihitena avasthātaḥ kenacid śāstra priṣiddhena asādhunā alpa taraḥ avasthātaḥ hīyata arthaḥ adhiṣṭhāna pālana ādi kurvan anugraha pīḍā kṛtena adharma ākhyona yujyate abhāva ucyate īśitum śīlam saṃbandhyate kiñcāṣa ādi stambha paryantānām pālayitā rakṣitā kiṃviśiṣṭa varṇa āśrama ādi vyavasthāyāḥ vidhārayitā ādīnā antānām asaṃbhedāya asaṃbhinna maryādāyai parameśvareṇa setuvat avidhāryamāṇā saṃbhinna maryādāḥ syuḥ asaṃbhedāya setu bhūtaḥ parameśvaraḥ svayan jyoḥ ityādi vidyāyāḥ phalam nirddiṣmaṭam kijyetiḥ iyaṃpuruṣa evamādi ṣaṣṭha prapāṭhaka vihitāyām evaṃphalāyām kāmya deśa varjitam kṛtsnam kāṇḍam tādarthyena vaniyujyate ucyate mantra brāhmaṇa adhyayanena nitya svādhyāya lakṣaṇena veditum brāhmaṇa grahaṇam upalakṣaṇa aviśiṣṭaḥ adhikāraḥ trayāṇām varṇānām athavā kāṇḍena mantra brāhmaṇena vivijiṣanti vividiṣantī ucyate ityādi ya mantra brāhmaṇa lakṣaṇena prakāśyamānam vividaṣanti vyācakṣate āraṇyaka mātram anuvacanam karmakāṇena prakāśyate taḥ tvaipaniṣadam viśeṣa aviśeṣita samasta grāhi dam vacanam deśa utsarhe yuktaḥ nanu tvad pakṣe varjam deśa nā vyākhyāne avirodhāt pakṣe doṣaḥ anuvacana svādhyāyaḥ vidhīyate upaniṣada pu anuvacana śabda artha parityaktaḥ yajña ādi pāṭhāt yajña ādīni anukramiṣyan anuvacana śabdam prayuṅkte krama anuvacana ucyata gamyate nitya svādhyāyaḥ nitya svādhyāya ādibhiḥ vividaṣanti prakāśanayanta dodhaḥ viśuddhi hetu saṃskṛtā viśuddha śaknuvanti prakāśitam apratibandhena veditum ātharvaṇe viśuddha sattvaḥ paśyate niṣkalam dhyāyamānaḥ smṛtiḥ jñānam utpadyate puṃsām kṣayāt pāpasya ityādiḥ nityāni saṃskāra arthāni avagamyate yājī aṅgam saṃskriyata aṅgam upadhīyate ityādi smṛti śāstreṣu saṃskāra arthāni acakṣate aṣṭācatvāriṃśat saṃskārā ityādiṣu gītāsu daina pāvanāni manīṣiṇām yajña yajña kṣapita kalmaṣāḥ dravya yajñā jñāna saṃskāra arthāḥ saṃskṛtasya viśuddha satvasya jñāna utpattiḥ apratibandhena bhaviṣyati vividiṣṭi kṣaya hetu vṛddhi hetu tapa aviśeṣeṇa kṛcchra cāndrāyaṇa ādi prāptau viśeṣaṇam anāśakam bhojana nivṛttiḥ bhojana nivṛttau mriyata nā atma vedanam anuvacana yajña dāna nityam upalakṣyate kāmya varjitam nityam jñāna utpatti dvāreṇa mokṣa sādhana pritapadyate kāṇḍena vākya tauvagatiḥ uktena nyāyena prakāśitam mananāt yogī artha nanu anya vedane muni avadhāryata bāḍham anya vedane bhavet kitu anya vedane karmi bhavet karmī asādhāraṇam muni vivakṣitam avadhārayati vidite kriyā sambhavāt mananam ecamevā prārthayantaḥ pravrajana śīlāḥ pravraḍanti prakarṣeṇa vrajanti saṃnyasyanti arthaḥ icchanta avadhāraṇāt bāhya lokatraya īpsūnām pārivrājya udhikāra gamyate gaṅgādvāram pratipitsuḥ kāśī deśa nivāsī abhimukhaḥ bāhya traya arthinām apara sādhanam ityādi athaḥ arthibhiḥ ādi sādhanam pratyākhyāya pārivrājyam pratipattum yuktam atad sādhana pārivrājyasya yuktam avadhāraṇam prāptiḥ avidyā nivṛttau sva avasthānam icchaci kriyā uparama atma valoka sādhanam mukhyam antaraṅgam ādiḥ bāhya trayasya ādi pratyasādhana asambhavena viruddha avocāma prvrajanti kriyā abhyaḥ nivarterannā arthaḥ bāhya traya arthinaḥ pratiniyatāni ādīni sādhanāni vihatāni arthanaḥ nivṛttiḥ pārivrājyam vidhīyata ta arthanaḥ pravraḍanti ucyate artha vāda vākya hotum darśayatu pārivrājye kāraṇam ucyate itikrānta kālīnā vidvāṃsa jñāḥ apara upalabhitam bāhya traya sādhanam nirdiśyate kāmayante ādi traya sādhanam anutiṣṭhanti arthaḥ nanu apara darśam anutiṣṭhanti balāt vyutthānam apavādāt parāda āt anyatrā atmanaḥ parāda darśam apavadati apara madhya antararbhāvāt apara bāhya antara darśana pratiṣedhāt vijīnāyīt nā atma darśana vyatirekeṇa vyutthāna kāraṇam apekṣate abhiprāya ucyate prayojanam phalam sādhyam kariṣyāmaḥ sādhanena bāhya sādhanam nirjñātā bāhya asmākam vyatiriktaḥ asmākam bhūtāḥ nā atma kenacid sādhanena utpādya āpyaḥ vikāryaḥ saṃskāryaḥ saṃskāra kārya karaṇa darśana viṣayam aṅgam saṃskriyata aṅgitva ādi śravaṇāt ghana nairantarya darśinaḥ aṅgi saṃskāra upadhāna darśanam praḍādi sādhanaiḥ kariṣyāmaḥ aviduṣām pradāji sādhanaiḥ karvyam phalam mṛgatṛṣṇikāyām udaka pānām udaka darśī pravṛtta uṣara mātram udaka abhāvam paśyeta pravṛttiḥ yuktā asmākam artha darśinām ādi sādhana sādhye mṛgatṛṣṇikā ādi avidvat darśana viṣaye pravṛttiḥ yuktā abhiprāyaḥ ucyate asmākam artha darśinām aśanāya ādi vinirmuktaḥ byāma vikāryaḥ phalam abhipratam cā atmanaḥ sādhya sādhana ādi saṃsāra vinirmuktasya sādhanam eṣitavyam sādhyasya sādhana anveṣaṇā kriyate asādhyasya sādhana anveṣaṇāyām jala buddhyā sthala taraṇam khe śākuna anveṣaṇam prvjeyuḥ brāhmaṇā karmā arabheran arthaḥ brāhnā akāmayamānāḥ ta sādhya sādhana saṃvyavahāram nindantaḥ avidvat viṣayaḥ kṛtavanta ucyate aṣaṇāyāḥ vista lokāṣaṇāyāḥ canaranti ityādi vyākhyātam pravrajeyuḥ vidhiḥ artha vādena saṃgacchate sārtha tutya abhimukhyam upapadyate arthavāda ityādiḥ uttaraḥ granthaḥ arthavādaḥ arthavāda apekṣeta apekṣate ityādi artha vādam ādi karmabhyaḥ nivṛttāḥ pravjitavanta ava adhunātanā pravjeyuḥ sambadhyamānam lokastiti abhimukham bhavitum samāna kartṛkatva upadeśa ādityānauvocāma anuvacana ādi sahapāṭhāt atma vedana sādhana tvena vihitānām anuvacana ādīnām yathārtha arthavāda taiḥ paṭhitasya pārivrājyasyā atma prāpti sādhana tvena arthavāda ayuktam phala vibhāga upadeśāt bāhyāt phala antara tvena pravibhajati eṇa ḍayyaḥ pārpatat stuti pradhānavat artha vāda apekṣam abhrāntiḥ stiti anuṣṭheyena pārivrājyena stutuḥ upapadyate di pārivrājyam anuṣṭheyam anya stuti darśa pūrṇamāsa ādīnām anuṣṭhāyānām stuti artha kartavyatā viṣaya ārjñātā yata stuti arthaḥ bhavet kvacid vidhiḥ parikalpyeta pārivrājyasya mukhyaḥ anadhikṛta viṣaye pārivrājyam parikalpyate vṛkṣa ādi ārohaṇa ādya pu pārivrājyat kalpyeta kartavya tvena anirjñātatva aviśeṣāt stutitva gandhaḥ aapi śakyaḥ kalpayitum yadyayātmā iṣyate kimartham prāpti sādhana tvena nā abheran pārivrājyena ucyate atma asaṃbandhāt pravrajeyuḥ sādhana tvena phala tvena utpādyatva ādi prakārāṇām anyatamatvena apu vartate vidam m vakṣyamāṇe tarataḥ prāpnuta yuktam vākya śeṣaḥ ucyate nimittāt dhāraṇa ādi hetoḥ apuṇyam kṛtavān kaṣṭam narakam pratipatsya kṛtavataḥ paritāmapaḥ phala viṣaya kāmāt nimittāt yajña dāna ādi lakṣaṇam śobhanam kṛtavān jataḥ phalaṃsukham upabhokṣya deha antara harṣaḥ lakṣaṇe saṃnyāsina janmani apūrve nā arabhyete kṛta akṛte nitya anuṣṭhānam akṛtam akriyā kṛta akṛte tapataḥ anātma jñam phala akṛtam pratyavāya utpādanena tapataḥ bhasmīkaroti yathedhāṃsi samidvaḥ ityādi smṛteḥ ārambhakayoḥ upabhogena kṣayaḥ vida saṃbandhī vastu brāc maṇena uktam mantreṇa prakāśitam ityādi lakṣaṇaḥ anityāḥ vilakṣaṇaḥ svābhāvika tyakta sarveṣaṇasya kutaḥ nitya hetum śubha lakṣaṇena kṛtena vṛdvilakṣaṇām vikriyām prāpna aśubhena apakṣaya lakṣaṇām vikriyām upacaya apacaya hetu bhūtā vikriyā pratiṣidhyante avikriya nitya mahimnaḥ bhavet padasya vettā gamyate jñāyata mahimnaḥ svarūpam padasya vedanena ucyate mahimānam saṃbadhyate adharma lakṣaṇena pāpakam viduṣaḥ akarma saṃbandhi ityādi
