uktaḥ samuccityā asyā kaṇḍikāyām nirdiśyata samasta āraṇyaka artha jīryata vipariṇamata arthaḥ mriyata jīryate vinaśyati ajara ata jani prabhṛtiḥ bhāva viripaiḥ varjitaḥ itaraiḥ bhāva vikāraiḥ kṛtaiḥ ādibhiḥ mṛtyu vījata ata viśeṣaṇaḥ tasmasmāt bhaya varjitaḥ avidyā kāryam kārya priti ṣedhena bhāva vikāra pratiṣedhena avidyāyāḥ pratiṣedhaḥ siddhaḥ veditavyaḥ abhaya evaṅguṇa viśiṣṭaḥ parivṛḍham niratiśayam arthaḥ prasiddham yuktam evaṅguṇa viśiṣṭa ya yathoktam saṃkṣiptor uktaḥ artha s samyak prabodhāya utpatti pralaya ādi kalpanā kriyā kāraka phala adhyāropaṇā cā atmani apohena adhi āropita aviśeṣa apanaya dvāreṇa tatvam āveditam prabhṛti apara saṃkhyā svarūpa parijñānāyāḥ rekhā adhyāropaṇam ekeyam rekhā daśeyam śateyam sahasreyam grāhayati avagamayati saṃkhyā svarūpam kevalam saṃkhyāyāḥ rekhā ākāra ādīni grāhayati utpati ādi aneka upāyam āsthāya tattvam āveditam kalpita upāya janita viśeṣa pariśodhana tattva upasaṃhāraḥ upasaṃhṛtam pariśuddham kevalam saphalam jñānam kaṇḍikāyām brāhmaṇam āgama pradhānena madhuka aṇḍena tattvam nirdhāritam upatti pradhānena yājñavalkīyena kāṇḍena pakṣa pratipakṣa parigraham vigṛhya vādena vicāritam śaiṣya ācārya saṃbandhena ṣaṣṭhe praśna prativacana nyāyena vistaram vicārya upasaṃhṛtam nigamana sthānīyam brāhmaṇam ārabhyete nyāyaḥ vākya kovidaiḥ parigṛhītaḥ hetu apadeśāt pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam nigamanam athavā agama pradhānena madhuka aṇḍena amṛtatva sādhanam saṃnyāsa bha jñānam abhihitam tarkeṇa amṛtatva sādhanam saṃnyāsam jñānam adhigamyate tarka pradhānaṃhi yājñavalkīyam kāṇḍam śāstra tarkābhyām niścitam jñānam saṃnyāsam amṛtatva sādhanam śāstra śraddhāvadbhiḥ amṛtatva pratipitsubhiḥ pratipattavyam āgama upapattibhyām niścitor athaḥ śraddheyaḥ avyabhicārāt akṣarāṇām caturthe vyākhyātor athaḥ pratipattavyaḥ avyākhyātāni vyākhyāsyāmaḥ hetu upadeśa anantarya pradarśana arthaḥ hetu pradhānāni vākyāni atītāni āgama pradhānena pratijñātor athaḥ nigamyate brāhmaṇena vṛttāvadyotakaḥ patnyau āstām nāmata aparā nāmataḥ bhāryayoḥ vadana śīlā babhūvā asīt striyām yocitā gṛha prayojana anveṣaṇā lakṣaṇā kāla sati pūrvasmāt gārhasthya lakṣaṇāt vṛttāt pārivrājya lakṣaṇam upācikīrṣuḥ he jyeṣṭhām bhāryām āmantrayāmāsa āmanñya pāni vrājyam gārhasthyāt bhavāmi anujānīhi icchasi karavāṇotyādi vyākhyātam uktā sādhyena ahaḥ ityādi asmabhyam avṛdha dvardhitavatī nirdhāritavatī tuṣṭaḥ icchasi amṛtatva sādhanam he mṛtatva sādhanam khalvare dṛṣṭa ucyate ācārya āgamābhyām tarkeṇa upapattayā vicārite śravaṇam āgama mātreṇa mata upapattyā anyathā nirdhārite ucyata vyatirekeṇa abhāvāt ayatha artha darśitam parākuryāt kaivalyā saṃbandhinam anātma svarūpeṇa aparādhāt bhāvaḥ caturthe śabda niḥśvāsena ādi artha niḥśvāsaḥ sāmarthyāt iktaḥ uktaḥ śāstra saṃhāram kṛtvār arthaḥ spaṣṭīkartavya ucyate kārya pralaye nimitte ghanavat avāhyaḥ dhana avatiṣṭhate mānna asaṃsarga viśeṣat labdha viśeṣa vijñānaḥ pravilāpite viśeṣa nimitte saṃsarge uktā vastuni ghana madhyama apī pidāpī dava gamitavān saṃsohitavān arthaḥ lakṣaṇam vivekata vinaṣṭum śīlam vināśī vināśya vināśī vinā vikriyā vināśī avikriya arthaḥ prakṛtaḥ anucchitti ucchittiḥ uccheda ucchedaḥ vināśa ucchittiḥ ucchittiḥ ardharmā dharmānucchitti vikriyā lakṣaṇaḥ apaccheda lakṣaṇaḥ vīnāśaḥ vidyata arthaḥ caturṣu prapāṭhakeṣu tulyaḥ nirdhāritaḥ upāya viśeṣaḥ adhigame upeyaḥ atmā caturthe ata nirdiṣṭaḥ pañcame paṇa upanyāsena saṃvāde nirdhāritaḥ pañcama samāptau saṃvāde samāptau caturṇām prapāṭhakānām niṣṭhatā antarāle vivakṣiter pradarśana āya upasaṃhāraḥ ityādiḥ prakāra śatena nirūpyamāṇe tave niṣṭhā anya upalabhyate tarkeṇa agamena amṛtatva sādhanam parijñānam saṃnyāsaḥ upasaṃjihīrṣan mātram advaita darśanam anya sahakāri kāraṇa nirapekṣam amṛtatva sādhanam pṛṣṭatī amṛtatva sādhanam evetu vijñeyam tvayā amṛtatva sādhanam jñānam priyāyai bhāryāyāḥ saṃnyāsa paryavasānā upadeśa niṣṭhā artha karta vyatānta vicāryate śāstra artha viveka pratipattaye yata ākulāni vākyāni dṛśyante yāvajjīvam hotram jīvam darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām yajeta kurvan jijīviṣet jarā maryam agnihotram ityādīnyā āśrami ājñāpakānyāni cā aśrama antara pratipādakāni vākyāni samāpya gṛhī bhavet grahāt vanī pravrajet vetarathā brahmacaryāt pravrajet gṛhāt vanāt dhanena tyāgena ekemṛtatva mānaśuḥ ityādīni smṛtayaḥ brahmacaryavān pravrajati aviśīrṇa brahmacaryaḥ icchat tamāvasā aśramam avikalpam ekebruvate vaidānanadhītya brahmacaryeṇa pautrān pāvana pitṛṇām agnīn vidhivat ceṣṭa vanam praviśya bubhūṣet prājāpatyām nirupya iṣṭim vesa agnīn samāropya pravrajet gṛhāt ityādyāḥ vyutthāna vikalpa kramayata iṣṭa āśrama pratipatti pratāpādakāni śruti smṛti vākyāni śataśa upalaṃbhyanta itaretara viruddhāni ācāraḥ vipratipattiḥ śāstra artha pratapat tṝṇām śakyate śāstra arthaḥ manda buddhibhiḥ vivekena pratipattum pariniṣṭhata śāstra nyāya buddhibhiḥ oṣām vākyānām viṣaya vibhāgaḥ śakyate avadhārayitum viṣaya vibhāga jñāpanāya buddhi sāmarthaṃya vicārayiṣyāmaḥ jīva śruti ādi vākyānām anya artha asaṃbhavāt kriyā vasāna ava artha yajña pātraiḥ dahanti antya śravaṇāt jarā marya śravaṇāt liṅgāt pārivrājya pakṣe śarīrasya smṛtiḥ niṣeka ādi śmaśāna mantraiḥ uditaḥ vidhiḥ śāstre adhikāraḥ jñeyaḥ anyasya kasyacid mantrakam vedena vidhīyate śmaśāna darśayati smṛtiḥ adhikāra abhāva pradarśanāt atyantam śruti adhikāra abhāvaḥ akarmiṇaḥ gamyate udvāsanā apavādāt avīra udvāsayate nanu vyutthāna ādi vijhadhānāt vaikalpikam kriyā avasāna arthasya anya artha vyutthāna ādi śrutīnām ayāvat jīvam at nihotram yāt jīvam darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām yajeta evamādīnām śrutīnām jīvana mātra nimitta śakyate anya artha kalpayitum vyutthāna ādi vākyānām anadhikṛta viṣayatva saṃbhavāt kurvan jijīvaṣet mantra varṇāt mucyate jarā mṛtyubhyām viyogāt chidrā saṃbhavāt karmiṇām śmaśāna vaikalpikam kāṇa kubja ādayaḥ karmaṇi anadhikṛtā anugrāhyā śrutyā vyutthāna ādi āśrama antara vidhānam anupapannam pārivrājya ākrama vidhānasya anavakāśa sarvamedhayoḥ jīva vidhi apavāda jīva agnihotra ādi vidheḥ sarvamedhayoḥ apavādaḥ krama pratipatti saṃbhavaḥ samāpya gṛhī bhavet gṛhāt vanī pravrajet i virodha anupapatteḥ evaṃviṣaya tve pārivrājya kama vidhāna vākyasya virodhaḥ krama pratipatteḥ anya viṣaya parikalpanāyām bādhaḥ nā atma jñānasya amṛtatva hetutva abhyupagamāt ārabhya antena granthena upasaṃhṛtam jñānam amṛtatva sādhanam abhyupagatam bhavatā amṛtatva sādhanam anya nirapekṣam mṛṣyate kimartham jñānam marṣayati śṛṇu kāraṇam yathāsvarga kāmasya svarga prāpti upāyam ajānataḥ agnihotra ādi svarga sādhanam abhyupagamyate jñānam jñāpyate tatā amṛtatva sādhanam jñānam abhyupagantum yuktam tulya prāmāṇyāt ubhaya tra hetu upamardaka jñānasya udbhave nivṛttiḥ dāra saṃbaddhānām hotra ādi bheda buddhi viṣaya saṃpradāna kāraka sādhya anya buddhi chedyām ādi saṃpradāna kāraka amantreṇa nirvartyate saṃpradāna kāraka buddhyā saṃpradāna kārakam sādhana tvena upadiśyate nivartyate anyatrā atmanaḥ mṛtyaḥ ya anā ityādi śrutibhyaḥ deśa kāla nimitta dyapekṣa vyavasthita vastu viṣaya jñānasya kriyāyāḥ tantra deśa kāla nimitta ādi epekṣa jñānam vastu tantra deśa kāla nimitta ādi apekṣate uṣṇa amūrta atma apu nanu sati prāmāṇa karvidheḥ nirodhaḥ tulya pramāṇayoḥ itaretara nirodhaḥ yuktaḥ svābhāvika bheda buddhi mātra nirodhaka vidhi antara nirodhakam jñānam svābhāvika bheda buddhi mātram niruṇaddhi hetu apahārāt anupapatteḥ vidhainirodha pratiṣedhāt kāmya pravṛtti nirodhavat adoṣāt svarga yajeta svarga sādhane yāge pravṛttasya pratiṣevidheḥ kāme vihate kāmya yāga anuṣṭhāna pravṛttiḥ nirudhyate kāmya vidhiḥ niruddhaḥ pratiṣedha vidhinā kāmya vidheḥ anarkatva jñānāt pravṛti anupapattiḥ ananuṣṭheya tve anuṣṭha ātuḥ abhāvāt anuṣṭhāna vidhyā narthakyāt aprāmāṇyam vidhīnām jñānāt pravṛti upapatteḥ svābhāvikasya kriyā kāraka phala bheda vijñānasya jñānāt hetu upapadyata viṣaye doṣa utpatteḥ prāk kāmya pravṛtti hetu svarga ādi icchāyāḥ svābhāvikyāḥ tadvāt sati anartha arthaḥ artha anarthayoḥ abhiprāta tantra mokṣam varjayitvā anyasya avidyā viṣaya tvāta abhiprāya tantrau ārtha anarthau maraṇa ādi kāmya iṣṭa darśanāt jñāna vidheḥ ābhimukhyam vidhaya nā atma jñāna sahabhāvi siddham jñānam amṛtatva sādhanam nirapekṣa jñānasya viduṣaḥ pārivrājyam siddham saṃpradāna ādi kāraka jāti ādi śūnya avikriya dṛḍha pratipatti mātreṇa vacanam nyāyataḥ vyākhyātam ātmāyam hotu vacanena vidvāsaḥ akāmayamānā vyuttiṣṭhanti pārivrājyam viduṣām avabodhāt vividiṣā uḥ apu siddham pārivrājyam vacanāt avidvat viṣaya avocāma avidyā viṣaye utpatya āpti vikāra saṃskārthāni saṃskāra dvaireṇā atma jñāna sādhana avocāma yajña ādibhiḥ vividaṣanti eta viṣayāṇām āśrama bala abala vicāraṇāyām jñāna utpādanam pradhāna anām amānitva ādīnām mānasānām dhyāna jñāna vairāgya ādīnām sannipatya upakāra hiṃsā rāga dveṣa ādi bāhulyāt kliṣṭa vimiśritā itara pārivrājyam mumukṣūṇām tyāga uktānām vairāgyam mokṣasya avadhiḥ dhanena bandhubhiḥ dāraiḥ brāhmaṇa mariṣyasi anviccha guhā praviṣṭam gatāḥ ākhya yoga śāstreṣu saṃnyāsaḥ jñānam pratyāsanna ucyate pravṛtti abhāvāt pravṛtteḥ jñāna pratikūla śāstreṣu prasiddhā viraktasya mumukṣoḥ vinā jñānena brahmacaryāt pravrajet ādyu upapannam nanu avakāśa anadhikṛta viṣayam uktam jīva śruti uparodhāt doṣaḥ nitarām avakāśa jīva śrutīnām avadvid kāmi kartavya avocāma nirapekṣam jīvana nimittam kartavyam prāyeṇa bahulāḥ aneka viṣayaḥ aneka sādhana sādhyaḥ aneka phala sādhanāni vaidikāni dāra saṃbandha kartavyā anuṣṭhīyamāna phala kṛṣi ādivat śata samāptīni gārhasthye apekṣayā jīva śrutayaḥ akurvan mantra pakṣe sarvamedhayoḥ parityāgaḥ pakṣe jīva anuṣṭhānam śmaśāna śarīrasya itara varṇa apekṣayā jīva śrutiḥ kṣattriya vaiśyayaḥ pārivrājya pratipattiḥ amantraiḥ uditaḥ vidhiḥ aaika āśramyam ācāryā evamādīnām kṣatriya vaiśya apekṣa śasām arthaya jñāna vairāgya ādi apekṣayā vyutthāna vikalpa krama pārivrājya pripatta prakārā virudhyante anadhikṛtānām vidhānāt pārivrājya s asnāta vāsnātakaḥ utsanna anagni ve atyādinā siddha āśrama antarāṇi adhikṛtānām pañcamam brāhmaṇam yājñavalkīyasya kāṇḍasya vaṃśa ārabhyate madhuka aṇḍasya vyākhyānam pūrvavat nama pañcamaḥ adhyāyaḥatha pañcama adhyāyasya brāhmaṇam pūrṇamadaḥ kutaścid vyāvṛttam vyāpi niṣṭhā kartari draṣṭavyā ada abhidhāyi sarvanāma arthaḥ sampūrṇam ākāśavat vyāpi nirantaram nirupādhikam upādhikam sthaṃ vyavahāra āpannam vyāpi upādhi paricchinnena viśeṣa viśeṣa āpannam kārya ātmakam kāraṇa ātmana udacyata udricyata udgacchati kārya udricyate svarūpam pūrṇa paramātma bhāvam jāhāti udricyate kārya pūrṇa pūrṇa sva āpadya avidyā bhūtamātra upādhi saṃsarga jamanyatva avabhāsam tiraskṛtya avāhyam ghana svabhāvam kevalam uktam agra mantrasya arthaḥ arthaḥ pūrṇamada agra arthaḥ śruti amutrayat amutra śabda vācyam kārya stham upādhi saṃyuktam udriktam artha svarūpāt pratyavabhāsamānam ahamadaḥ tiraskṛtya āpūrṇa svarūpa avidyā kṛtām upādhi saṃparka jām kevalam uktam arthaḥ mantreṇa anūdyata uttara sambandha sādhana tvena vakṣyamāṇāni sādhanāni uṅkāra dama dāna dayā ākhyāni vidhitsitāni khila prakaraṇa sambandhāt upāsana varṇayanti kāraṇāt kāryam udricyate udriktam kāryam vartamāna artha vastu dvaita pralaya kāryasya pūrṇa ādāyā atmani kāraṇa utpatti pralayeṣu kāleṣu kārya kāraṇayoḥ pūrṇa pūrṇa kārya kāraṇayoḥ bhedena vyapadiśyate dvaitādvaita ātmakam jala taraṅga phena budbuda ādi ātmaka jalam udbhavāḥ taraṅga phela budbuda ādayaḥ samudra bhūtā avirbhāva tirobhāva dharmiṇaḥ artha satyā artha jala taraṅga ādi sthānīyam samudra jala sthānīyam dvaitasya tve kāṇḍasya prāmāṇyam avidyā mṛgatṛṣṇikāvat advaitam paramārthataḥ kāṇḍam viṣaya abhāvāt apramāṇam virodha deśa pramāṇam artha advaita vastu pratipādaka apramāṇam kāṇḍam dvaita viṣaya virodha parijihīrṣayā śrutyā uktam kārya kāraṇayoḥ samudravat pūrṇa mada ityādinā viśiṣṭa viṣaya apavāda vikalpayoḥ asambhavāt vivakṣitā kalpanā kriyā viṣaya utsarga prāptasya deśe apavādaḥ kriyate ahiṃsan tīrthebhya hiṃsā viṣaya utsargeṇa nivāritā tīrthe viśiṣṭa viṣaye jyotiṣṭoma ādau anujñāyate vastu viṣaya advaitam utsargeṇa pratipādya deśe apavaditum śakyate advaita deśa anupapatteḥ vikalpa anupapatteḥ atirātre ṣoḍaśinam atirātre ṣoḍaśinam grahaṇa agrahaṇayoḥ adhīna vikalpaḥ vastu viṣaye advaitam vikalpaḥ apuruṣa tantra vastunaḥ virodhāt dvaita advaita tvayoḥ ekasya vivakṣitā kalpanā śruti nyāya virodhāt ghanavat ghanam nirantaram apara bāhya abhyantara bheda vivarjitam bāhya abhyantaram ajam asthūla manaṇva ajaram evamādyāḥ śrutayaḥ niścita arthāḥ saṃśaya viparyāsa rahitāḥ prakṣiptāḥ syuḥ akiñcitkara nyāya virodhaḥ sāvayavasya aneka ātmakasya kriyāvataḥ nityatva anupapatteḥ nitya cā atmanaḥ smṛti ādi darśanāt anumīyate virodhaḥ anitya tve kalpanā narthakyam sphuṭam pakṣe kāṇḍa ānarthakyam akṛta abhyāgama kṛta vipraṇāśa prasaṅgāt nanu dvaitādvaita ātmaka tve samudra ādi dṛṣṭāntā vidyante ucyate bhavatā ekasya dvaitādvaita viruddham anya viṣaya nitya aniravayava vastu viṣayam viruddha avocāma dvaita advaita kārya viṣaye avayave śruti smati nyāya virodhāt anupapanneyam kalpanā kalpanāyāḥ parityāga adhyeya astra artheyam kalpanā janana maraṇa ādi anartha śata sahasra bheda samākulam samudra vana ādivat sāvayavam aneka dhyeya tvena vijñeya tvena śrutyā upadiśyate ghana upadiśati anekadhā darśana apavādāt ya anā śrutyā ninditam kartavyam kriyate śāsra arthaḥ aneka anekadhātvam dvaita nindita draṣṭavyam śāsra arthaḥ draṣṭavya praśastam praśasta śāstra arthaḥ bhavitum uktam deśasya aprāmāṇyam viṣaye dvaita abhāvāt advaite prāmāṇyam prāpta upadeśa artha advaitam vastu jāta mātram jñāpayitvā upadiśati śāsram upadeśa arham jāta mātra buddhi gamya dvaitasya anṛtatva buddhiḥ acid dvaitasya upadiśya prāmāṇyam pratipādayet śāsram pāṣaṇḍibhiḥ prasthāpitāḥ śāsrasya prāmāṇyam gṛhṇīyuḥ yathāprāptam avidyā svābhāvikam upādāya svābhāvikyā yuktāya rāga dveṣa ādi doṣavate abhimata artha sādhanam upadiśati prasiddha kriyā kāraka phala svarūpa doṣa darśanavate biparīta audāsīnya svarūpa avasthāna phala arthine upāya bhūtām ekatva darśana ātmikām upadiśati sati audāsīni svarūpa avasthāne phale prāpte śāsrasya prāmāṇyam pratyarthi nivartate abhāvāt śāsrasya śāsra nivartata parisamāptam śāsram śāsra virodha gandhaḥ advaita jñāna avasāna śāsra śiṣya śāsana ādi dvaita bhedasya anyatama avasthāne virodhaḥ avasthitasya itara itara apekṣa śāsra śiṣya śāsanānām anyatamaḥ avatiṣṭhate samāptau viredha āśaṅkyeta advaite kevale śive siddhe avirodha tāta abhyupagamya brūmaḥ dvaitādvaita ātmaka tve śāsra virodhasya tulya samudra ādivat dvaita ātmakam virudhyate dvaita viṣaye anyonya upadeśaḥ samudra dṛṣṭāntaḥ viruddhaḥ samudra udaka ekatvavat tve upadeśa grahaṇa ādi kalpanā hasta ādi dvaitādvaita ātmake devadatte vākkarṇayoḥ devadatta deśa bhūtayoḥ upadeṣṭrī karṇaḥ kevala upadeśasya grahītā devadattaḥ upadeṣṭā upadeśasya grahīta kalpayitum śakyate samudra udaka tvavat vijñānava devadattasya śrati nyāya virodhaḥ abhipreta artha asiddhiḥ evaṅkalpanāyām yathāvyākhyāta asmābhiḥ pūrṇamada mantrasya arthaḥ mantraḥ aviniyukta brāhmaṇena dhyāna karmaṇi viniyujyate viśeṣya abhidhānam viśeṣaṇam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyena nirdeśaḥ nīlotpalavat bṛhat vastu mātra āspadaḥ aviśeṣitaḥ viśeṣyate uṃśabda vācyamoṃ śabda svarūpam evavā ubha sāmānādhikaraṇyam aviruddham upāsana sādhanatva artha m oṃ prayuktaḥ śruti antarāt ālambanam ālambanam yuñjīta akṣareṇa abhidhyāyīta dhyāyatha ādeḥ anya artha asaṃbhavāt upadeśasya anyatrom śaṃsati udgāyati evamādau svādhyāya ārambha apavargayoḥ uṅkāra prayogaḥ viniyogāt avagamyate tathār avagamyate dhyāna sādhana tvena uṅkāra śabdasya upadeśaḥ ādi śabdā vācakāḥ śruti prāmāṇyāt nediṣṭham abhidhānam oṅkāraḥ ata pratipattau sādhanam dvi prakāreṇa pratīka tvena abhidhāna tvena pratīka tvena viṣṇu ādi pratimā abhedena oṅkāraḥ pratipattavyaḥ oṅkāra ālambanasya prasīdati ālambanam ālambanam ālambanam jñātvā mahīyate bhautike khe pratītiḥ ciratanam arthaḥ paramātma ādya viṣaya nirālambanam aśakyam grahītum bhaktibhyām bhāva viśeṣeṇa uṅkāra āveśayati viṣṇu aṅkitāyām śilā ādi pratimāyām viṣṇum am vidyata am kha mātram ucyate kauravyāyaṇī vāyure khe mukhyaḥ sva śabda vyavahāraḥ mukhe saṃpratyayaḥ yukta nirūpa adhi svarūpam am upādhikam sarvathā oṅkāraḥ pratīka tvena pratimāvat sādhana satyakāma uṅkāraḥ śruti antarāt kevalam sva śabda arthe vipratipattiḥ oṅkāraḥ oṅkāraḥ vācakaḥ abhidhānam abhidhānena prakāśyamānam abhidhīyamānam sādhakaḥ upalabhate brāhmaṇā brāhyaṇānām abhidhāna tvena sādhana abhipretam oṅkārasya athavā ādi artha vādaḥ oṅkāraḥ pratīka tvena sāmāna adhikaraṇyāt stutiḥ tvena oṅkāra prabhava ātmakaḥ ādi bheda bhinna oṅkāraḥ śaṅkunā ityādi śruti antarāt oṅkāraḥ oṅkāraḥ itarasya vedasya ata viśiṣṭaḥ oṅkāraḥ sādhana tvena pratipattavya athavā brāhmaṇā viduroṅkārāt praṇava udgotha ādi vikalpaiḥ vijñeyaḥ prayujyamāne sādhana tvena prayuktaḥ adhunā dama ādi sādhana traya vidhāna arthoṃ ārambhaḥ saṃkhyākāḥ prajāpatyāḥ apatyāni prajāpattau śiṣyatva vṛtteḥ brahmacaryasya prādhānyāt śiṣyāḥ uṣitavanta arthaḥ viśeṣataḥ manuṣyā akurvan ucyate kathayatu asmabhyam tebhya arthibhyaḥ varṇa mātram upadeśa abhihitasya vijñātavanta āhosvit vijñātavantaḥ ucyatām uktam abhyata adāntā yūyam svabhāvataḥ dāntā bhavatā kathayati itara āhomiti samyak svabhāvataḥ lubdhā yūyamatas yathāśakti saṃvibhajata asurā krūrā yūyam hiṃsā ādi prāṇiṣu anuvartata ādīn anuśāsti daivyā stanayitnu lakṣaṇayā śrūyate kāsau vākyānām upalakṣaṇāya dakāra uccāryate anukṛtiḥ stanayitnu saṃkhyā niyamasya aprasiddha anuśāsti kāraṇāt ucyate upādadyāt asmābhiḥ kartavyam kartavyam matim smṛtiḥ trividham narakasya dvāram aśatam krodhaḥ lobhaḥ tyajet vidheḥ śeṣaḥ ādīn uddiśya kimartham dakāra uccāritavān anuśāsana arthibhyaḥ vivekena pratipannāḥ manogatam samānena dakāra varṇa mātreṇa abhiprāya jñā vikalpayanti adāntatva tṛtīya phalam bhuktam kalpayitvā icyate pāda traya pāda traya phalasya kṣaya kāraṇam anyasya doṣasya kartṛ tve kṣamam dātā pratigrahītā stutaye kalpyate dātā pratigrahītā saṃbhāvyate pratigrahaḥ aparādha kṣamaḥ abhyadhikam artha avaśiṣṭam caturtha pāda viṣayam darśayati parorajā ya kenacana kenacid pratigraheṇā am prāpyam arthaḥ uktāni padāni apyāni kenacid kalpayitvā uktam paramārthataḥ kuta ananurūpam pratigraha doṣeṇa hastaḥ bhūtaḥ smāritaḥ gāyatryā he samrāṇna vidāñcakāra vijñātavān āhga vikala aphalam śṛṇu gāyatryā indhanam laukikāḥ indhanam gāyatryā vetti evaṃvitsyāt agnimukhaḥ pratigraha ādi doṣam bhakṣayitvā agnivat pratigraha doṣāt jñāna samuccaya kāla prārthayati prasaṅgaḥ turīyaḥ pādaḥ prakṛtam prārthyate hiraṇya mayena mayena vastu apidhīyata ākhyam mayena maṇḍalena arthaḥ darśanāya ityādīni nāmānya āmantraṇa arthani ekarṣa darśanāt jagata mantra varṇāt jagataḥ saṃyamanam tvad suṣṭhu vīrayate jagata īśvarasya apatyam hiraṇyagarbhasya he vigamaya saṃkṣipā atmanaḥ śaknuyām tvad svarūpam draṣṭam vidyotana ata upasaṃhara kalyāṇānām atiśayena paśyāmaḥ vacana vyatyayena bhūrbhuvaḥ vyāhṛtya vayavaḥ ākṛti bhavāmi aharam upaniṣada cākṣuṣayoḥ parāmṛśyate saṃbandhaḥ ādiṣṭā prāpyate prārthyate punaruktiḥ ādara arthā he prāpaya śobhanena mārgeṇa dhanāya phala prāptaya arthaḥ kṛṣṇena punarāvṛtti yuktena śuklena he prajñānāni prāṇinām apanaya viyojaya asmad asmad taḥ vivakṣitam khila kāṇḍasya pūrvatra anuktam viśiṣṭa phalam viṣayam upāsanam vaktavyam āvadhāraṇaṛchai jyeṣṭha śreṣṭha guṇam vakṣyamāṇam phalena pralobhitaḥ praśnāya amukhībhūtaḥ cā aha avagamyate niṣeka kāla śukra śoṇita saṃmbandhaḥ ādi kalāpasya aviśiṣṭaḥ aprāṇam virohati prathamaḥ vṛtti lābhaḥ ādibhyaḥ vayasā niṣeka kāla dārabhya labdha vṛttau ādīnām vṛtti lābhaḥ yuktam jyeṣṭha ādiṣu guṇa icchati jyeṣṭha śreṣṭha darśī nanu vayenimittam jyeṣṭha icchātaḥ ucyate doṣaḥ prāṇavat vṛtti lābhasya jyeṣṭha vivakṣita darśana anurūpeṇa phalam jñāti vyatirekeṇa bhavitum icchati ucyatām kāsau vāsayati atiśayena vāggminaḥ dhanavantaḥ atiśayena ācchādana arthasya vaseḥ abhibhavanti vāggminaḥ anyān guṇavat parijñānāt guṇa darśana anurūpam phalam guṇavatīm phalam deśe viṣame durgamane deśe durbhikṣa ādau viṣame ucyatām kāsau pratiṣṭhātvam dṛṣṭavā anurūpam phalam ya sampadam sampad guṇa yuktam phalam saṃpadyate guṇakam guṇa ucyate sati vedā abhisampannāḥ indriyavataḥ adhyeya vihita āyattāḥ anurūpam phalam saṃ ya āśrayaḥ ya vedā ayatanam ucyate āśraya indriyāṇām viṣayāṇām manaā āśritā viṣayā bhogya saṃkalpa vaśāni indriyāṇi pravartante nivartante mana indriyāṇām darśana anurūpeṇa phalam ya sampannaḥ prajanana upalakṣyate anurūpam phalam ya heme prāṇā ādayaḥ śreyā prayojanāya vivadamānā biruddham vadamānā gatavantaḥ śabda vācyam uktavantaḥ asmākam madhye asmākam madhye vāsayati taiḥ pṛṣṭam sadhā uvācoktavat madhya nirgate pūrvasmāt atiśayena pāpīyaḥ pāpataram aneka aśuci saṃdhāta kaṣṭataram vairāgya ucyate pāpīya madhye bhaviṣyati jānan vasiṣṭham prajāpatirta uvācāyam itareṣām apriya parihārāya ta uktā prāṇā vīrya parīkṣaṇāya krameṇa ucca kramuḥ ucca krāma utkrāntavatī proṣitā śaktavantaḥ yūyam mad vinā ta uktā akalā mūkā avadantaḥ prāṇana vya darśana vyāpāram kārya akārya ādi viṣayam prajāyamānā putrān utpādayanta uttarā avasiṣṭha buddhvā het cakrāma ityādi pūrvavat atirita utkramamam tadānīm sva pracalitā ādayaḥ suhayaḥ mahāsu śobhanaḥ lakṣaṇa upetaḥ parimāṇataḥ sindhu deśe bhavaḥ abhijanataḥ śaṅkūn pāda bandhana śaṅkūn paḍvīśāḥ śaṅkavaḥ udyacchet yugapad utkhanet āroha ārūḍhe parīkṣaṇāya ima anvāc ādīn saṃvavarhet yatavān sva bhraṃśitavān ādayaḥ he bhagavat utkram īryasmāt tvad vinā śreṣṭha bhavadbhiḥ karam karam prayacchata samvādaḥ kalpitaḥ viduṣaḥ śreṣṭha parīkṣaṇa prakāra upadeśaḥ prakāreṇa śreṣṭha parīkṣaṇam parīkṣaṇa prakāraḥ samvāda bhūtaḥ kathyate anyathā saṃhatyakāriṇām satām saṃvatsara mātram ekaikasya nirgamana ādi upapadyate prakāreṇa vicārayati ādīnām pradhāna bubhutsurupāsanāya prārthitāḥ pratijñātavantaḥ bali dānāya pravṛttā uvācā uktavatī guṇena sampad āyatana atitva giṇān krameṇa samarpitavantaḥ dattavantaḥ bhavantaḥ brūta ma evaṅguṇa viśiṣṭasya vāsa āpyā śvabhya kṛmibhya śva kṛbhyannam pataṅga kiñcitprāṇibhiḥ adyamānam dṛṣṭiḥ vidhīyate kecitu bhakṣaṇe doṣa abhāvam śāsra pratiṣiddha vikalpa avidhāyaka anannam vijñānasya vihitasya stuti vākyata āpatteḥ śāsra antara vihitasya bādhane sāmarthyam anya mātrasya darśanam ihi vidhitsitam bhakṣayet bhakṣaṇe doṣa abhāva jñānam mithyā pramāṇa abhāvāt viduṣaḥ upapatteḥ sāmarthyāt adoṣa aśeṣān natva anupapatteḥ kāryata karaṇa saṃghātena viśiṣṭasya vidvattā kārya karaṇa saṃghātena kṛmi ādi aśeṣa bhakṣaṇam upapadyate aśeṣa bhakṣaṇe doṣa abhāva jñāpanam anarthakam aprāpta aśeṣa bhakṣaṇa doṣasya nanu sanbhakṣayati kṛmi ādi bāḍham kintu viṣayaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ daiva raktam kiṃśukam doṣa abhāvaḥ doṣa abhāva jñāpanam anarthakam aprāpta aśeṣa bhakṣaṇa deṣasya kārya karaṇa saṃghāta sambandhena pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate sambandhena pratiprasavaḥ pratiṣedha atikrame doṣa anya viṣaya ādeḥ brāhmaṇa ādi śarīrasya sarvānnatva darśanam vidhīyate kintu mātrasya sāmānyena annasya kasyacid jīvana hetuḥ viṣam viṣa jasya krimeḥ anyasya doṣam utpādayati maraṇa ādi lakṣaṇam annasya pratiṣiddha bhakṣaṇe brāhmaṇatva ādi deha saṃbandhāt doṣa mithyājñānam abhakṣya bhakṣaṇe doṣa abhāva jñānam vāsa bhakṣamāṇā sthānīyāḥ prāṇasyā vāsa darśanam vidhīyate kārye viniyoktum śakyāḥ yathāprāpte abbhakṣaṇe darśana mātram kartavyam anannam anadanīyam bhuktam ānadanīyam bhukta madanīyam bhuktam kṛta doṣeṇa lipyata āstutiḥ avocāma anannam apratighrāhyam hastyādi pratigrāhyam apratigrāhya pratigraha doṣeṇa lipyata stuti ya anasya phalam ātmabhāva phala abhiprāyeṇa stuti abhiprāyeṇa nanu phalam darśinaḥ ātmabhāva phalam anadanīyam ādyam apratigrāhyam pratigrāhyam yathāprāptam upādāya stūyate phala vidhi sarūpa vākyasya śrotriyā aśiṣyantaḥ bhokṣyamāṇā acāmanti bhuktyā uttara ācāmatām abhiprāya anam yoyasmai karomi cā vāsa uktam pibāmi kartavyam nanu bhokṣyamāṇaḥ bhuktavān prayataḥ bhaviṣyāmi anagna karaṇa artha tve dvi kārya acamanasya kārya dvayam ācamanasya ekasya yuktam prāyatya anagnatā anagnatā prāyatya ācamana anagna karaṇāya bhavatu kriyā dvitva upapatteḥ kriye bhotryamāṇasya bhuktavataḥ ācamanam smṛti vihitam prāyatya kriyā mātram prāyatyam darśana ādi apekṣate cā acamana bhūtāsu kartavya codyate kriyamāṇa ācamanasya prāyatyartha vādhyate kriyā antara ācamanasya bhokṣyamāṇasya bhuktavataḥ ācamanam darśana mātram vidhīyate aprāpta anyatas saṃbandhaḥ khila adhikāraḥ anuktam ucyate saptama adhyāya jñāna samuccaya kāriṇā mārga yācanam supatha anekeṣām pathām sadbhāvaḥ mantreṇa sāmarthyāt pradarśitaḥ supatha viśeṣaṇāt kṛta vipāka pratipatti mārgāḥ ityādi vipāka pratipatti mārgā saṃsāra gati upasaṃhāra arthaḥ ārambhaḥ etāvatī saṃsāra vipākaḥ svābhāvikasya śāsrīyasya vijñānasya dvayā prājāpatyā svābhāvikaḥ sūcitaḥ kāryam vipākaḥ pradarśitaḥ śāsrīyasya vipākaḥ pradarśitaḥ pratipatti antena ārambhe vairāgyasya vivakṣita kevalena saṃyuktena uktam mārgeṇa uktam khila prakaraṇe aśeṣataḥ vaktavyam ata ārabhyate upasaṃhāraḥ śāsrasya iṣṭaḥ uktam amṛtatva hetuḥ uktaḥ arthaḥ ārambhaḥ nitye tve vyāpāraḥ amṛtatva sādhanam sāmarthyāt hetu saṃpadyate uktam utkrātim gatim tṛptim punarāvṛtim pratyutthāyinam prativacane āhutī hute utkrāmata ityādinā āhuteḥ kāryam uktam kartuḥ āhuti lakṣaṇasya phalam kartāram anāśrityā ahuti lakṣaṇasya svātantryeṇa utkrānti ādi kārya ārambha upapadyate kartṛ artha kārya ārambhasya sādhana āśraya agnihotra stuti artha agnihotrasya kāryam uktam ṣaḍ prakāram kartuḥ phalam upadiśyate prakāram phala vijñānasya vivakṣita dvāreṇa darśanam uttara mārga pratipatti sādhanam vidhitsitam aśeṣa saṃsāra gati upasaṃhāraḥ kāṇḍasya niṣṭhā dvayam didarśayiṣuḥ ākhyāyikām praṇayati nāmataḥ aruṇasya apatyam apatyam śabda aitihya arthaḥ niścaya arthaḥ prathanāya rājñaḥ jeṣyāmi garveṇa jīvalasya apatyam jevalim pañcāla rājam pravāhaṇa anaṃsu abhṛtyaiḥ paricaraṇam kārayantam abhimāna garvam śrutvā vinetavyaḥ matvā utprekṣyā agata mātram abhyuktavān kumārā saṃbodhya bhartsana arthā plutiḥ uktaḥ bhoiti bhoitya kṣattriyam pratyuktavān kruddhaḥ anuśāsitaḥ bhavasi itara oṃm bāḍham saṃśayaḥ vijānāsi prakāreṇa prasiddhāḥ mriyamāṇā vipratipadyanta vicāraṇa arthā plutiḥ samānena mārgeṇa gacchantīnām mārga dvaividhyam kāścid mārgeṇa kāścid vipratipattiḥ vetthā arthaḥ āpadyantauiti āgacchanti prasiddhena nyāyena asakṛt mariyamāṇaiḥ yathāyena prakāreṇa saṃpūryatāiti saṃkhyā kāyām āhutau hutāyāmāpaḥ yāsām vāktāḥ śabda vācyā ākāra pariṇatāḥ samyak utthāya udbhūtāḥ vadantī ākāra pariṇatāḥ samyak utthāya udbhūtāḥ vadantī mārgasya pratipattām pratipad chabda vācyam viśiṣṭam arthaḥ mārgam pratidyante pratipad icyate pratipatti sādhanam vetthā arthaḥ arthasya prakāśakam mantrasya vākyam mantraḥ arthasya prakāśakaḥ vidyata arthaḥ mantra ucyate mārgau śṛtavān pitṛṇām prāpikā saṃbaddhā sṛtyā arthaḥ vyavahitena saṃbandhaḥ utāpi saṃbandhini anyā prāpayati punarubhābhyām sṛtibhyām pitṝn ucyate saṃbandhinyau manuṣyā sṛtibhyām arthaḥ sṛti hyām samastam gacchat saṃgacchate yayoḥ pitroḥ madhya arthaḥ kau pitarau āvaṇḍa kapāle vyākhyātam brāhmaṇena aṇḍa kapālayoḥ madhye saṃsāra viṣaye nā atyantika amṛtatva gamanāya itara praśna samudāyāt ekañcana praśnam apanīya abhimāna garvam prakṛtam śvetaketum prayojanena upamantrayāñcakre vasantu bhavantaḥ pādyam arpyam cā anīyatām upamantraṇam kṛtavān anādṛtya pratigatavān cā ajagāma samāvagatavān cā ajagāma samāvartana sarvābhiḥ vidyābhiḥ upālambham putrasya śrutvā aha katha prakāreṇa upajātam he śobhanā medhā sumedhāḥ śṛṇu saṃkhyākān praśnāt rājanya bandhū rājanyā bandhavaḥ paribhava vacanam pṛṣṭavān naikañcana vijñātavān rājñāḥ pṛṣṭāḥ praśnā uktaḥ ta mukhāni praśnānām udāhṛtavān kruddham upaśamayan prakāreṇa he tāta vatsa jānīthā gṛhṇīthā tatubhyam taraḥ tvad taḥ arthaṃrakṣiṣye jānāmi pṛṣṭam prehya āgaccha rājñi nirīkṣitum utsahe gotrataḥ jaivalerāsā asanam āsthāyikā ṣaṣṭhī dvayam āsthāne gautamāyāḥ agatāyā asanam anurūpam bhṛtyaiḥ āhāra yāñcakāra asmā ardhyam purodhasā kṛtavān mantravat madhuparkam pūjām dadbha gaḥ śva ādi lakṣaṇam pratijñātaḥ tvayā pratijñāyām dṛḍhī kurva putrasya samīpe praśna rūpām vara prārthayase anyatamam prārthaya bhavatā prārthitena kṛtyam ditsasi hiraṇyasya prabhūtasya prāptam gaḥ aaśvānānām āpāttam sarvatra anuṣaṅgaḥ parivārāṇām vidyamānam tvattaḥ prārthanīyam tvayā deyam pratijñātaḥ tvayā jānīṣe yuktam pratijñā rakṣaṇīyā abhiprāyaḥ abhyasmān kevalān sarvatra vadānyaḥ avadān kadaryaḥ arthaḥ prabhūtasya phalasya aparisamāptikasya pautra ādi gāmikasya īdṛśasya pratyeva kevalam ādātā bhūdbhavān ādeyam he nyāyena śāsra vihitena matta icchāsā icchā anvāptum uktaḥ upagacchāmi śiṣya tvena kṣattriyān arthinaḥ vaiśyān kṣattriyā vaiśyān āpadyupayanti śiṣya vṛttyā upacchanti śuśrūṣā ādibiḥ kortyā upagamana kīrtana mātreṇa uṣitavān upāyanam gautamenā antara ukte pīḍitam matvā kṣāmayan aparādhā aparādham kārṣīḥ asmadīyaḥ aparādhaḥ grahītavya arthaḥ pitāmahā asmad pitāmaheṣu yata aparādham jagṛhuḥ pitāmahānām asmāsu bhavatā rakṣaṇīyam arthaḥ tvayā prārthitetaḥ tvad saṃpradānāt prāk brāhmaṇa uṣitavatī jānīṣe kṣattriya parayeyam agatā rakṣaṇīyā śakyata uktam ādeyaḥ vara itaḥ śakyate rakṣitum vakṣye ityādi caturthaḥ praśnaḥ prāthamyena nirṇīyate krama bhaṅgaḥ nirṇaya āyatta itara prasna nirṇayasya he dṛṣṭiḥ anagnau vidhīyate yoṣit puruṣayoḥ samindhanāt samidhyate samidha uththāna sāmānyāt nirgatāḥ samidhaḥ uttiṣṭhati ahararciḥ prakāśa sāmānyāt aṅgārā upaśama sāmānyāt diṣaḥ visphuliṅgā visphuliṅgavat vikṣepāt evaṅguṇa viśiṣṭe ādayaḥ āhuti dravya sthānīyām prakṣipanti āhutyā āhuteḥ kiṃvā ākhyam haviḥ ata uktam asmābhiḥ saṃbandhe utkrāntim ādi padārtha ṣaṭka nirṇaya agnihotra uktam agnihotra āhutī hute satyau utkrāmataḥ āviśataḥ āhavanīyam kurvāte samidham marīcīḥ śukrām āhutim antarikṣan tarpayataḥ utkrāmataḥ āviśataḥ āhavanīyam kurvāte samidham evamādi uktam hotra āhutī sādhane utkrāmataḥ sādhanaiḥ viśiṣṭe jñāyete āhavanīya samiddhūma aṅgāra visphuliṅga āhuti dravyaiḥ utkrāmataḥ tvena samittvena dhūma tvena aṅgārā aṅgāra tvena visphuliṅga tvenā ahuti dravyam paya ādya āhuti dravya tvena sarga ādau avyākṛta avasthāyām sūkṣmeṇā atmanā vyavatiṣṭhate vidyamānam sādhanam agnihotra lakṣaṇam apūrveṇā atmanā vyavasthitam vyākaraṇa ādīnām āhavanīya ādi ādi bhāvam kurvat vipariṇamate agnihotra ākhyam hotra āhuti apūrva vipariṇāma ātmakam jagat āhutyoḥ stuti artha tvena utkrānti ādyā pratyutthāyinā antāḥ ṣaḍ padārthāḥ prakaraṇe nirṇītāḥ kartuḥ vivakṣāyām ādi ārabhya darśanam uttara mārga pratipatti sādhanam viśiṣṭa phala upabhogāya vidhitsitam ādi darśanam prastūyate ya ādhyātmikāḥ prāṇā agnihotrasya hotāraḥ ta adhidaivika tvena pariṇatāḥ santa ādayaḥ ta hotāraḥ agnihotrasya phala bhogāya hotram hutavantaḥ ta phala pariṇāma phala bhoktṛ hotṛ vipariṇamamānā śabda vācyāḥ dravyam agnihotra āśraya ihā ahavanīye prakṣiptam bhakṣitam adṛṣṭena sūkṣmema vipariṇatam kartrā yajamānena dhūma ādi krameṇa dyulokam sūkṣmā āpa āhuti kārya bhūtā agnihotra samavāyinyaḥ kartṛ sahitāḥ śabda vācyāḥ kartuḥ antara ārambhāya praviśantyaḥ praviśya kartuḥ ārabhante ucyate hutāyāmāpaḥ vadantoti praśnaḥ nirṇaya viṣaye prastutam samāvāyinyaḥ kartuḥ ārambhikāḥ śabda vācyā niścīyate bhūyas tvādāpaḥ puruṣavāca vyapadeśaḥ santi prayuktaḥ ārambhaḥ apsamavāyi prādhānyam kartṛ tve cā puruṣavāca vyapadeśaḥ janma ārambhaḥ sarvatra agnihotra āhuti stuti dvāreṇa utkrānti ādayaḥ prastutāḥ padārthā vaidikāni agnihotra prabhṛtīni lakṣyante dāra saṃbaddham prastutya uktam dvitīya āhuti ādhāra āhutyoḥ āvṛtti krameṇa vṛṣṭi upakaraṇa abhimānī saṃvatsara saṃvatsareṇa śarad ādibhiḥ grīṣma antaiḥ sva avayavaiḥ va parivartamānena dhūma prabhava dhūmavat upalakṣya prakāśa sāmānyāt upaśānta kāṭhinya sāmānyābhyām hlādunayaḥ stanayitnu śabdā visphuliṅgāḥ vikṣepa anekatva sāmānyāt āhuti adhikaraṇa nirdeśaḥ ta hotāraḥ abhinirvṛttaḥ dvitīye parjanya hūyate āhuteḥ janma upabhoga āśrayaḥ kriyā kāraka phala viśiṣṭaḥ tṛtīyaḥ aneka upabhoga saṃpannayā samidhyate āśraya utthāna sāmānyāt indhana dravyam āśritya uttiṣṭhati āśrayena saṃbandha prabhava sāmānyāt saṃbandhena saṃbandhena śarvarī chāyām śārvaram candramā prabhavatva sāmānyāt prabhavanti rātrau upaśāntatva sāmānyāt visphuliṅgāḥ bisphuliṅgavat vikṣepa sāmānyāt ityādi pūrvavat āhuteḥ vṛṣṭi prabhavatu prasiddha yava ādeḥ annasya prasiddhaḥ pāṇi ādimān caturthaḥ vivṛtam vivṛtena vacana svādhyāya ādau samidhā utthāna sāmānyāt uttiṣṭhati vākya vyañjakatva sāmānyāt vyañjakam abhidheya vyañjakaḥ aṅgārā upaśama sāmānyāt prakāśa āśraya visphuliṅgā vikṣepa sāmānyāt nanu juhvataḥ dṛśyante doṣaḥ devatva upapatteḥ adhidaivam ādayaḥ annasya prakṣeptāraḥ āhute pariṇāmaḥ yoṣa srī pañcamaḥ homa adhikaraṇaḥ upastha samidhyate utthāna sāmānyāt varṇa sāmānyāt aṅgārā karaṇam maithuna vyāpāraḥ aṅgārā vīrya upaśama hetutva sāmānyāt vīrya ādi upaśama kāraṇam maithunam aṅgāra bhāvaḥ upaśama kāraṇam sukha lavāḥ kṣudratva sāmānyāt visphuliṅgāḥ āhuteḥ dyuparjanyāyaṃloka yoṣa agniṣu kramema hūyamānāḥ vṛṣṭi bhāvena sthūla tāratamya kramam āpadyamānāḥ śabda vācyā śabdam ārabhante praśnaḥ caturthaḥ hutāyāmāpaḥ puraṣavācaḥ vadantī nirṇītaḥ pañcamyām āhutau yoṣa bhūtā krameṇa kiyantam ucyate nimittam arthaḥ kṣaye yasmi mṛtam antyāhutyai śratvijaḥ ahuti prasiddhaḥ homa adhikaraṇam parikalpyaḥ prasiddhā aṅgārā aṅgārā visphuliṅgā visphuliṅgā yathāprasiddham arthaḥ antya āhutim āhutyā āhuteḥ atiśaya dīptimān niṣeka ādibhiḥ anti āhuti antaiḥ saṃskṛta niṣpadyate praśna nirākaraṇa ya uktam darśanam śabdāt samiddhūma aṅgāra visphuliṅga ādi viśiṣṭāḥ agnayaḥ nirdiṣṭāḥ agnīn arthaḥ nanu hotra āhuti darśana viṣayam darśanam uktam utkrānti ādi padārtha ṣaṭka nirṇaye ahavanīyam kurvāte ityādi amuṣya samit ityādi sāmyam śeṣam darśanam prasna prativacana parigrahāt praśnasya prativacanasya parigrahaḥ evaṃśabdena parāmraṣṭum yuktam anyathā praśna anarthakyān nirjñāta saṃkhyāyāḥ agnaya vaktavyāḥ nirjñātam anūdyate prāptasya anuvadanam yuktam upalakṣaṇa arthaḥ ādyena antyena upalakṣaṇam yuktam śruti antarāt samāne prakaraṇe chāndogya śrutau agnīn saṃkhyāyā upādānāt anagnihotra śeṣam darśanam ādi sāmānyam agnihotra stuti avocāma utkrānti ādi padārtha ṣaṭka parijñānāt arcira ādi pratipattiḥ prakṛta upādānena ādi pratipatti vidhānāt ya gṛhasthā nanu yajña ādi sādhanena dhūma ādi pratipattiḥ vidhitsita anevaṃvidām gṛhasthānām yajña ādi sādhana upapatteḥ bhikṣuvānaprasthayoḥ araṇya saṃbandhena grahaṇāt gṛhastha saṃbaddha darśanasya brahmacāriṇa gṛhyante uttare pathi praveśaḥ smṛti prāmāṇyāt aṣṭāśīti sahasrāṇām ūrdhvaretasām uttareṇa āryamṇaḥ bhejire gṛhasthā agnijaḥ apatyam krameṇa agnibhyaḥ cāmī vānaprasthāḥ parivrājakāḥ araṇya niṣṭhāḥ snataḥ hiraṇyagarbha gṛhasthāḥ ādi āhuti krameṇa pañcamyām āhutau yoṣa jātāḥ pratyutthāyinaḥ agnihotra ādi anuṣṭhā tāraḥ dhūma ādi krameṇa parjanya ādi krameṇa āvartante yoṣa jātāḥ ghaṭīyantravat gati āgatibhyām āvartante ghaṭīyantra bhramaṇāt vinirmuktāḥ jvālā mātram abhimāninī śabda vācyā uttara mārga lakṣaṇā vyavasthitā parivrājakānām arciṣā saṃbandhaḥ parigṛhyate śabda vācyā maraṇa kāla niyama anupapatteḥ āyuṣaḥ kṣaye maraṇam evaṃvidāhani martavyam maraṇa niyantum śakyate rātrau pretāḥ pratīkṣante kṣipyet śruti antarāt ahna āpūryamāṇa pakṣam devatayā ativāhitā āpūryamāṇa pakṣa śukla pakṣa āpūryamāṇa pakṣa ādyān udaṅṅuttarām savitā śukla pakṣa devatayā ativāhitāḥ bahuvacanāt saṃgha cāriṇyaḥ uttarāyaṇa māsa ativāhitā abhimāninīm abhimāninīm prāptān vāsī sṛṣṭaḥ etyāḥ agatya aniti adhara uttara bhūmi bhedena bhinnā gamyante bahuvacana prayogāt upāsana tāratamya upapatteḥ puruṣeṇa gamitāḥ prakṛṣṭāḥ prakṛṣṭāḥ saṃvatsarān anekān anekān kalpān arthaḥ gatānām punarāvṛttiḥ saṃsāre āgamanam śākhā antara pāṭhāt ākṛti mātra grahaṇam śvaḥ bhūte paurṇamāsīm yadvat viśeṣaṇā narthakyāt nā avartanta grahaṇam anarthakam śvobhūte paurṇamāsīm paurṇamāsyāḥ śvobhūta anuktaṃna jñāyata yukta viśeṣayitum śvaākṛtiḥ śabda arthaḥ vidyata śva virarthaka prayujyate viśeṣaṇa śabde prayukte anviṣyamāṇe viśeṣaṇa phalam gamyate yuktaḥ nirarthaka tvena utsraṣṭum viśeṣaṇa satyām viśeṣaṇa phala avagatau kalpāt gamyate utkrānti ādi agnihotra saṃbandha padārtha ṣaṭkasya veditāraḥ kevala karmiṇaḥ agnihotra ādinā vedi bhikṣamāṇeṣu dravya saṃvibhāga lakṣaṇena vedi ādi vyatiriktena kṛcchra cāndrāyaṇa ādinā bahuvacanāt phala ramyam abhipretam uttara mārga dhūma ādi śabda vācyāḥ dhūma pratipadyanta arthaḥ ātivāhika tadvat rātri apakṣīyamāṇa pakṣa māsa viśeṣān bhūtānyathā yajña ṛtvija āpyāyasvāpakṣīyasva prāptān karmiṇaḥ bhṛtyān svāminaḥ upabhuñjate āpyāyasvāpakṣīyasva mantraḥ āpyāyyā apyāyya camasa stham bhakṣaṇena apakṣayam arthaḥ labdha śarīrān karmiṇa upakaraṇa bhūtān viśrāmayantaḥ anurūpam phalam prayacchantaḥ āpyāyanam somasyā apyāyanam upabhuñjata upakaraṇa bhūtān karmiṇām yajña dāna ādi lakṣaṇam prāpakam parigacchati parikṣīyata arthaḥ prasiddham śabda vācyā hutā ākāra pariṇatā yābhiḥ karmiṇām upabhogāya ārabdham ap mayam kṣayāt himapiṇḍa ivā atapa saṃparkāt pravilīyante pravilīnāḥ sūkṣmā bhūtā ucyata aakāśam abhiniṣpadyanta karmiṇaḥ śarīrāḥ purovāta ādinā itāḥ amutas nīyante uktam parjanya vṛṣṭi bhūtā patanti yava ādi uktam āhutyā bhūtā sici bhūtā yoṣa pratyutthāyinaḥ pratyuttiṣṭhantaḥ agnihotra ādi anutiṣṭhanti dhūma ādinā ta karmiṇaḥ ghaṭīyantravat cakrībhūtā baṃbhram anti arthaḥ uttara mārgāya sadyas muktaye saṃsarati uktam ya uttaram uttarasya dakṣiṇasya pratipattaye jñānam anutiṣṭhanti arthaḥ ucyate pataṅgā daṃśam aśakam saṃsāra kaṣṭa āsyām nimagnasya uddhāra durlabhaḥ śruti kṣudrāṇi asakṛt āvartīni jāyasva mriyasva utsāhena yathāśakti svābhāvika jñāna hānena dakṣiṇa uttara mārga pratipatti sādhanam śāsrīyam jñānam anutiṣṭhet vākya arthaḥ uktam durniṣprapataram jugupseta śruti antarāt mokṣāya prayateta arthaḥ uttara mārga pratipatti sādhana yatnaḥ kartavya gamyate anuparivartanta praśnāḥ nirṇītāḥ esau ārabhya caturthaḥ praśnaḥ ityādiḥ prathamyena pañcamaḥ dvitīya tvena dakṣiṇa uttara mārga pratipatti sādhana kathanena prathamaḥ ābhya kecid kecid vipratipattiḥ punarāvṛttiḥ praśna ādi krameṇa āgacchanti pataṅga ādi pratipatteḥ keṣāñcid tṛtīyaḥ praśnaḥ nirṇītaḥ jñāna karmaṇoḥ uktā jñānam svatantram daiva mānuṣa dvaya āyattam upārjanīyam apratyavāya kāriṇā upāyena mantha ākhyam karmā arabhyate mahattva prāptaye tve satyartha siddham ucyate arthī karmaṇi adhikṛtaḥ arthaḥ mantha vidhitsitasya abhidhīyate udagayana sarvatra prāptau āpūryamāṇa pakṣasya śukla pakṣasya sarvatra prāptau anukūla siddhi kara arthaḥ puṇye anukūle cikīrṣati arabhya upasadvratī upasatsu upasadaḥ prasiddhā jyotiṣṭome stana upacaya apacaya dvāreṇa bhakṣaṇam anupasaṃhārāt kevalam itikartavya śūnyam bhakṣaṇa mātram upādīyate nanu upasadaḥ vigrahaḥ itikartavya grāhyam parigṛhyata ucyate smārta smārtam mantha nanu śruti vihitam smārtam bhavitum smṛti anuvādinīhi śrutiḥ śrauta tve prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ prākṛta grāhi vikāra śrauta ata cā avasathya vidhīyate cā avṛtsmārtā upasadvratī sannīti arthaḥ audumbara udumbara vṛkṣa maye viśeṣaṇam kaṃsa ākāre camasa ākāre vaudumbara ākāre vikalpaḥ audumbara tve etra samūham yathāsambhavam yathāśakti samāhṛtya grāmyāṇām niyamena grāhyā yava ādyā vakṣyamāṇāḥ adhika grahaṇe doṣaḥ grāmyāṇām yathāsambhavam yathāśakti samasta sambhāra upacaya pradarśana arthaḥ sambharaṇīyam arthaḥ kramaḥ gṛhya uktaḥ parisamūhana parilepane bhūmi saṃskāraḥ vacanāt āvasathye gamyate vacanāt upasamādhāna śravaṇāt vidyamānasya upasamādhānam darbha anāvṛtā smārta āvṛt parigṛhyate ajyam puṃnāmnā puṇyāha saṃyuktena auṣadha phala piṣṭam upasicya upamanthanya upamaṃmathya madhye saṃsthāpya audumbareṇa sruveṇā avāpa sthāna mantraiḥ ityādyaiḥ ārabhya āhutī sruva avalepanam saṃsrāvayati ityādi liṅgāt jyeṣṭha śreṣṭha ādi vida karmaṇi adhikāraḥ retasa ārambha ekām āhutim aparayā upamanthanyā mathnāti mantreṇa ucchati ām aṃsya amaṃhi bhakṣayati pādena madhumatyā vyāhṛtyā prathamayā grāsam dvitīya pādena madhumatyā dvitīyayā dvitīya vyahṛtyā grāsam tṛtīyena pādena tṛtīyayā madhumatyā tṛtīyayā vyāhṛtyā grāsam madhumatīruktvā bhūrbhavaḥ samastam bhaśrayati caturbhiḥ grāsaiḥ dravyam parisamāpyate nirupyet pātra avaliptam nirṇijya pivet saṃdhyām upāsyā adityam mantreṇa yathāgatam etyā agatya antevāsina ya niṣiñcej jāyerañ chākhāḥ bhrhūp paiṅgyaś bhāga antevāsina ya niṣiñcej jāyerañ chākhāḥ bhrhūp bhāga vittiḥ jānakaya āyaḥ sthūṇāya antevāsina ya niṣiñcej jāyerañ chākhāḥ bhrhūp jānakir antevāsina ya niṣiñcej jāyerañ chākhāḥ bhrhūp uddālaka ityādi antevāsibhya ya prabhṛti ekaika ācārya krama āgatam satyakāma ācāryaḥ bahubhyaḥ antevāsibhya ucyate ya gata bhakṣaṇāya saṃskṛtam prakṣipet jāyeu utpadyeran śākhā avayavā vṛkṣasya sthāṇoḥ sidhyet dhruva phalam stuti adhigame ṣṭa tīrthāni darśanasya mantha vijñānasya adhigame tīrthe anujñāyete antevāsī vyākhyātam grāmyāṇām dhānyānām niyamena grāhyā avocāma ta nirdiśyante māṣā priyaṅgavaḥ aṇavaḥ śabda vācyāḥ kvacid deśe priyaṅgavaḥ prasiddhāḥ kaṅgu khalvā niṣpāvā valla śabda vācyā khala kulāḥ kulatthāḥ vyatirekeṇa yathāśakti auṣadha grāhyāḥ avocāma aya ajñikāni varjayitvā saṃbhūtam śruti antarāt yata sāratamam yogyā sraṣṭā ī kṣāñcake sriyam maithuna ākhyam adhaupāsanam kṛtavān sriyam śreṣṭha anuśrayaṇā vājapeya sāmānyakḷptim prakṛṣṭa gati yuktam abhiṣava upala sthānīyam kāṭhinya sāmānyāt prajanana udapārayat utpūritavān srī vyañjanam sriyam abhyasṛjat abhisaṃsargam kṛtavān uddālaka āruṇirāha adhā upahāsa ākhyam maithuna vājapeya sampannam arthaḥ ta ujyate maryā maraṇa dharmiṇaḥ manuṣyā brāhmaṇā ayanam ayanā brahmabandhavaḥ jāti mātra upajīvina nirindriyā viśliṣṭa indriyā vigata sukṛta karmāṇaḥ avidvāṃsau maithuna āsaktā arthaḥ paribhraṣṭā maithuna atyanta hetu darśayati ya avidvāṃsaḥ adhopahāsam śrīmantham patnyā ṛtu brahmacaryeṇa pratīkṣate ida rataḥ alpam rāga prābalyāt uddālaka āruṇirāha adhā upahāsa ākhyam maithuna vājapeya sampannam arthaḥ maudgālya ta ucyate maryā maraṇa dharmiṇaḥ manuṣyā brāhmaṇā ayanam brāhmaṇāyanā brahmabandhavaḥ jāti mātra upajīvina nirindriyā viśilaṣṭa indriyā vigata sukṛta karmāṇaḥ avidvāṃsau maithuna āsaktā arthaḥ paribhraṣṭā maithuna atyanta hetu darśayati ya avidvāṃsaḥ adhopahāsam śrīmantham patnyā śratu brahmacaryeṇa pratīkṣate ida rataḥ alpam rāga prābalyāt anumantrayeta anujapet arthaḥ reta antena mantreṇa madhye bhruveḥ stanayoḥ kadācid udaka chāyām atri mantreṇa teja patnā srīṇām madhye udvāsā udgata malavat śrīmatīm abhigatya adyā avābhyām kāryam utpādanam āplutām maithunam kartum utpādanam jñāpayet maithunāya śāpsyāmi durbhagām kariṣyāmi prakhyāpya mantreṇa upagacchet yaśa ādada abhiśāpāt vandhyā durbhagā khyātāyaśā anuguṇa bhartuḥ mantreṇa upagaccha yaśa sva bhāryām prajanana nikṣipya mantram dhārayet pūrvavat abhiprāṇanam reta ādada mantreṇa āretā arthaḥ ityādi pūrvavat viparyayeṇa reta jāra upapatiḥ abhicariṣyāmi manyeta iṣīkāḥ aktā ghṛta abhyaktā ādyā āhutīrante grahaṇam pratyekam evaṃvidyā vigata karmā śrotrisya narmā śatruḥ arthaḥ ṛtu bhāvam prāpnuyāt evamādi granthaḥ srīṇām sāmarthyāt kaṃsena snātām asnātām upahanyāt upaspṛśet samāptau snātvā hata vāsā vyavahitena saṃbandhaḥ āplutām avaghātāya viniyuñjyāt ya varṇataḥ kṣīra āśvarau samarthau janayitum dadhnā carum dvidevam icchati aśana niyamaḥ kevalam svābhāvikam udagrahaṇam anya prasaṅga nivṛtti atham duhituḥ gṛha tantra viṣayam vede anadhikārāt kṛtaram vividham gītaḥ prakhyāta arthaḥ samitiṅgamaḥ sabhām pragalbha arthaḥ pāṇḍityasya grahaṇāt śrotum iṣṭām ramaṇīyām saṃskṛtāyāḥ arthavatyā arthaḥ niyama aukṣem māṃsena ukṣā secana samarthaḥ puṅgavaḥ tadīyam māṃsam adhikavayāḥ tadīyam ārṣabham māṃsam āmi avaghāta nirvṛttān taṇḍulān sthālī pāka vidhinā ajyam ajya saṃskāram carum śrapayitvā sthālī pākasya āahutīḥ ityādyāḥ gārhyaḥ vidhiḥ caru śeṣam patnyai ucchiṣṭam udakena abhyukṣatyena mantreṇa uttiṣṭhāta mantra uccāraṇam abhimantrya kṣīra odana ādi apatya bhuktvā kramaḥ saṃveśana ityādi mantreṇa ityādi pūrvavat ena am prabhṛti ityādi pratimantram prasava sukha prasavana mantreṇa garbha jātakarma aṅka saṃmīya saṃyojya ādi āvāpa vāk anantarhitena avyavahitena hiraṇyena mantraiḥ pratyekam sva aṅka stham stana ityādi mantreṇa abhimantrayata vidhinā pitāmaham atiśeta niṣṭhām stutyaḥ arthaḥ adhyāhāryam samasta pravacana srīprādhānyāt guṇavān prastutam srī viśeṣaṇena viśeṣaṇāt ācārya paramparā kīrtyate avyāmiśrāṇi brāhmaṇena athavā tānī śuddhāni ārabhya pautimāṣī adhomukhaḥ niyata ācārya kramaḥ samāna māsāṃjīvīputrāt pravacana
